  <div class="issue-tab-bar" id="issueTabBar" style="display:none"></div>

  <!-- Row Hover Preview Tooltip -->
  <div class="row-preview-tip" id="rowPreviewTip"></div>

  <!-- Batch Operations Toolbar (injected above tables) -->

  <script>

// ============================================================
// NOTIFICATION CENTRE
// ============================================================
const Notif = {
  _items: [],
  _unread: 0,

  init: function() {
    try {
      var stored = localStorage.getItem('tt_notifications');
      this._items = stored ? JSON.parse(stored) : [];
      this._unread = this._items.filter(function(n){ return !n.read; }).length;
      this._updateBadge();
    } catch(e) { this._items = []; }

    // Close on outside click
    document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
      var wrap = document.getElementById('notifWrap');
      if (wrap && !wrap.contains(e.target)) {
        var panel = document.getElementById('notifPanel');
        if (panel) panel.classList.remove('open');
      }
    });
  },

  push: function(text, type, issueId) {
    var item = {
      id: Date.now(),
      text: text,
      type: type || 'info',
      issueId: issueId || null,
      time: new Date().toISOString(),
      read: false
    };
    this._items.unshift(item);
    if (this._items.length > 50) this._items = this._items.slice(0, 50);
    this._unread++;
    this._save();
    this._updateBadge();
    this._render();
  },

  toggle: function() {
    var panel = document.getElementById('notifPanel');
    if (!panel) return;
    var isOpen = panel.classList.toggle('open');
    if (isOpen) this._render();
  },

  markAllRead: function() {
    this._items.forEach(function(n){ n.read = true; });
    this._unread = 0;
    this._save();
    this._updateBadge();
    this._render();
  },

  _updateBadge: function() {
    var badge = document.getElementById('notifCount');
    if (!badge) return;
    if (this._unread > 0) {
      badge.textContent = this._unread > 9 ? '9+' : this._unread;
      badge.style.display = 'flex';
    } else {
      badge.style.display = 'none';
    }
  },

  _render: function() {
    var list = document.getElementById('notifList');
    if (!list) return;
    if (this._items.length === 0) {
      list.innerHTML = '<div class="notif-empty">&#x2714; All caught up!</div>';
      return;
    }
    var icons = { info: 'ℹ', success: '✓', warning: '⚠', error: '✕', assigned: '◆', mention: '@', review: '✔', sla: '⚠' };
    var self = this;
    list.innerHTML = this._items.slice(0, 20).map(function(n) {
      var timeAgo = App.relativeTime ? App.relativeTime(n.time) : new Date(n.time).toLocaleTimeString();
      return '<div class="notif-item ' + (n.read ? '' : 'unread') + '" onclick="Notif._click(\'' + n.id + '\',\'' + (n.issueId||'') + '\')">' +
        '<div class="notif-icon">' + (icons[n.type] || 'ℹ') + '</div>' +
        '<div class="notif-body">' +
          '<div class="notif-text">' + n.text + '</div>' +
          '<div class="notif-time">' + timeAgo + '</div>' +
        '</div></div>';
    }).join('');
  },

  _click: function(id, issueId) {
    this._items.forEach(function(n){ if (n.id == id) n.read = true; });
    this._unread = Math.max(0, this._unread - 1);
    this._save();
    this._updateBadge();
    if (issueId) {
      App.navigate('issue-detail', { id: issueId });
      var panel = document.getElementById('notifPanel');
      if (panel) panel.classList.remove('open');
    }
  },

  _save: function() {
    try { localStorage.setItem('tt_notifications', JSON.stringify(this._items)); } catch(e) {}
  }
};

// ============================================================
// SMART SEARCH
// ============================================================
const Search = {
  _debounce: null,
  _cache: null,

  open: function() {
    var panel = document.getElementById('smartSearchPanel');
    var backdrop = document.getElementById('searchBackdrop');
    var input = document.getElementById('smartSearchInput');
    if (panel) panel.classList.add('open');
    if (backdrop) backdrop.classList.add('open');
    if (input) { input.focus(); input.select(); }
    if (!this._cache && App.allIssues && App.allIssues.length) {
      this._cache = App.allIssues;
    }
  },

  close: function() {
    var panel = document.getElementById('smartSearchPanel');
    var backdrop = document.getElementById('searchBackdrop');
    if (panel) panel.classList.remove('open');
    if (backdrop) backdrop.classList.remove('open');
  },

  init: function() {
    var self = this;
    var input = document.getElementById('smartSearchInput');
    if (!input) return;

    input.addEventListener('input', function() {
      clearTimeout(self._debounce);
      var q = input.value.trim();
      if (!q) {
        document.getElementById('smartSearchResults').innerHTML = '<div class="search-empty">Start typing to search...</div>';
        return;
      }
      self._debounce = setTimeout(function() { self.search(q); }, 300);
    });

    input.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
      if (e.key === 'Escape') self.close();
    });

    // Cmd+Shift+F
    document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
      if ((e.metaKey || e.ctrlKey) && e.shiftKey && e.key === 'F') {
        e.preventDefault(); self.open();
      }
    });
  },

  search: function(query) {
    var results = document.getElementById('smartSearchResults');
    if (!results) return;
    var q = query.toLowerCase();
    var issues = App.allIssues || [];

    if (!issues.length) {
      results.innerHTML = '<div class="search-empty">Load the issue list first for search to work</div>';
      return;
    }

    // Score each issue
    var scored = issues.map(function(i) {
      var score = 0;
      var title = (i.title || '').toLowerCase();
      var desc  = (i.description || '').toLowerCase();
      var id    = (i.id || '').toLowerCase();

      if (id === q) score += 100;
      if (title.includes(q)) score += 50;
      if (desc.includes(q)) score += 20;
      // word-level matching
      q.split(' ').forEach(function(word) {
        if (word.length > 2 && title.includes(word)) score += 10;
        if (word.length > 2 && desc.includes(word)) score += 5;
      });
      // Priority boost
      if (i.priority === 'Critical') score += 5;
      if (!['Resolved','Closed'].includes(i.status)) score += 3;

      return { issue: i, score: score };
    }).filter(function(s){ return s.score > 0; })
      .sort(function(a,b){ return b.score - a.score; })
      .slice(0, 12);

    if (!scored.length) {
      results.innerHTML = '<div class="search-empty">No results for "' + query + '"</div>';
      return;
    }

    var html = '<div class="search-result-group">';
    html += '<div class="search-group-label">Issues (' + scored.length + ')</div>';
    scored.forEach(function(s) {
      var i = s.issue;
      var highlight = function(text) {
        if (!q) return text;
        var re = new RegExp('(' + q.replace(/[.*+?^${}()|[\]\\]/g,'\\$&') + ')', 'gi');
        return text.replace(re, '<mark style="background:var(--accent-dim);color:var(--accent);border-radius:2px;">$1</mark>');
      };
      html += '<div class="search-result-item" onclick="App.navigate(\'issue-detail\',{id:\'' + i.id + '\'});Search.close();">' +
        '<div class="search-result-id">' + i.id + '</div>' +
        '<div class="search-result-title">' + highlight(i.title.substring(0,60)) + '</div>' +
        '<div style="display:flex;gap:6px;flex-shrink:0;">';
      if (App.priorityBadge) html += App.priorityBadge(i.priority);
      html += '</div></div>';
    });
    html += '</div>';
    results.innerHTML = html;
  }
};

// ============================================================
// AI ISSUE ASSISTANT
// ============================================================
const AIAssist = {
  _issueId: null,
  _history: [],

  open: function(issueId, issueTitle) {
    this._issueId = issueId;
    this._history = [];
    var panel = document.getElementById('aiAssistPanel');
    if (panel) panel.classList.add('open');
    var msgs = document.getElementById('aiAssistMessages');
    if (msgs) msgs.innerHTML = '<div class="ai-msg assistant">Hi! I\'m reviewing <strong>' + (issueTitle||issueId) + '</strong>. Ask me anything   root cause, suggested fix, status update draft, or similar resolved issues.</div>';
    this._showSuggestions(issueId);
    var input = document.getElementById('aiAssistInput');
    if (input) input.focus();
  },

  close: function() {
    var panel = document.getElementById('aiAssistPanel');
    if (panel) panel.classList.remove('open');
  },

  _showSuggestions: function(issueId) {
    var sug = document.getElementById('aiAssistSuggestions');
    if (!sug) return;
    var suggestions = [
      'What\'s the likely root cause?',
      'Suggest a fix',
      'Draft a status update',
      'Find similar resolved issues',
      'Should this be escalated?'
    ];
    sug.innerHTML = suggestions.map(function(s) {
      return '<div class="ai-chip" onclick="AIAssist.sendText(\'' + s.replace(/'/g,"\\'") + '\')">' + s + '</div>';
    }).join('');
  },

  sendText: function(text) {
    var input = document.getElementById('aiAssistInput');
    if (input) input.value = text;
    this.send();
  },

  send: async function() {
    var input = document.getElementById('aiAssistInput');
    var text = (input ? input.value : '').trim();
    if (!text || !this._issueId) return;
    if (input) input.value = '';

    var msgs = document.getElementById('aiAssistMessages');
    if (!msgs) return;

    // Add user message
    msgs.innerHTML += '<div class="ai-msg user">' + App._esc(text) + '</div>';
    msgs.innerHTML += '<div class="ai-msg assistant loading" id="aiAssistTyping">&#x2736; Thinking...</div>';
    msgs.scrollTop = msgs.scrollHeight;

    // Call backend AI
    var context = 'Issue ID: ' + this._issueId + '\nUser question: ' + text;
    var r = await App.callAsync('processAIQuery', context);

    var typing = document.getElementById('aiAssistTyping');
    if (typing) typing.remove();

    var answer = 'I couldn\'t get a response right now. Please try again.';
    if (r && r.success && r.result && r.result.message) {
      answer = r.result.message;
    }

    msgs.innerHTML += '<div class="ai-msg assistant">' + App._esc(answer) + '</div>';
    msgs.scrollTop = msgs.scrollHeight;
    this._history.push({ user: text, assistant: answer });
  }
};

const OfflineMonitor = {
  init: function() {
    var self = this;
    window.addEventListener('online',  function() { self._setOffline(false); });
    window.addEventListener('offline', function() { self._setOffline(true); });
    this._setOffline(!navigator.onLine);
  },
  _setOffline: function(isOffline) {
    var banner = document.getElementById('offlineBanner');
    if (banner) banner.classList.toggle('visible', isOffline);
  }
};


const AI = {
  _debounce: null,
  _history: [],
  _issueCache: null,

  SUGGESTIONS: [
    'Show critical issues',
    'Find login bug',
    'Summarize open issues',
    'Create: API timeout error on checkout',
    'Issues assigned to me',
    'Show SLA breaches',
    'Bugs in API module',
    'Show resolved this week'
  ],

  init: function() {
    var self = this;
    var bar = document.getElementById('aiBar');
    if (!bar) return;

    bar.addEventListener('input', function() {
      clearTimeout(self._debounce);
      var q = bar.value.trim();
      if (!q) { self.close(); return; }
      self._debounce = setTimeout(function() { self.process(q); }, 420);
    });

    bar.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
      if (e.key === 'Escape') self.close();
      if (e.key === 'Enter') {
        clearTimeout(self._debounce);
        var q = bar.value.trim();
        if (q) self.process(q, true);
      }
    });

    bar.addEventListener('focus', function() {
      if (!bar.value.trim()) self.showSuggestions();
    });

    document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
      if ((e.metaKey || e.ctrlKey) && e.key === 'k') {
        e.preventDefault();
        bar.focus();
        if (!bar.value.trim()) self.showSuggestions();
      }
    });

    this.checkKeyOnInit();
  },

  showSuggestions: function() {
    var panel = document.getElementById('aiPanel');
    var backdrop = document.getElementById('aiBackdrop');
    if (!panel) return;

    var chips = this.SUGGESTIONS.map(function(s) {
      return '<div class="ai-chip" onclick="AI.runSuggestion(\'' + s.replace(/'/g, "\\'") + '\')">' + s + '</div>';
    }).join('');

    panel.innerHTML =
      '<div class="ai-panel-header">' +
        '<div class="ai-panel-title">\u2736 Gemini AI Command</div>' +
        '<button class="ai-panel-close" onclick="AI.close()">\u2715</button>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<div class="ai-panel-body">' +
        '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-bottom:10px;line-height:1.6">' +
          'Type in plain English. AI understands search, filters, summaries, and can pre-fill new issues.' +
        '</p>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<div class="ai-suggestions">' + chips + '</div>';

    panel.style.display = 'block';
    backdrop.style.display = 'block';
  },

  runSuggestion: function(text) {
    var bar = document.getElementById('aiBar');
    if (bar) {
      bar.value = text.replace(/^[^\w\u2736]+/, '').trim();
      this.process(bar.value, false);
    }
  },

  process: async function(query, immediate) {
    var self = this;
    this.setLoading(true);

    // Always run local classifier instantly (zero latency)
    if (!this._issueCache) {
      var r = await this._callBackend('getIssues', null);
      this._issueCache = (r && r.success) ? r.issues : [];
      setTimeout(function() { self._issueCache = null; }, 60000);
    }
    var local = this.classifyLocally(query, this._issueCache);

    // Try backend AI (Gemini runs server-side   no key in browser)
    try {
      var backendResult = await new Promise(function(resolve) {
        var t = setTimeout(function() { resolve(null); }, 12000);
        google.script.run
          .withSuccessHandler(function(r) { clearTimeout(t); resolve(r); })
          .withFailureHandler(function() { clearTimeout(t); resolve(null); })
          .processAIQuery(query);
      });

      self.setLoading(false);
      if (backendResult && backendResult.success && backendResult.result) {
        self.render(backendResult.result, query);
      } else {
        // Fallback to local + direct Gemini if backend key not set
        try {
          var geminiResult = await self.askGemini(query, local);
          self.render(geminiResult, query);
        } catch(e) {
          self.render(local, query);
        }
      }
    } catch(err) {
      self.setLoading(false);
      self.render(local, query);
    }
  },

  classifyLocally: function(query, issues) {
    var q = query.toLowerCase();

    if (/^(create|new|add|report|log|raise)[\s:]/i.test(query)) {
      var desc = query.replace(/^(create|new|add|report|log|raise)[\s:]*/i, '').trim();
      var priority = /critical|urgent|p0|blocker/i.test(desc) ? 'Critical'
        : /high|p1|important/i.test(desc) ? 'High'
        : /low|minor|p3/i.test(desc) ? 'Low' : 'Medium';
      var mod = /\bapi\b/i.test(desc) ? 'API' : /auth|login/i.test(desc) ? 'Authentication'
        : /dashboard/i.test(desc) ? 'Dashboard' : /report/i.test(desc) ? 'Reports' : '';
      return { intent: 'create', title: desc, priority: priority, module: mod, description: desc };
    }

    if (/summar|overview|how many|count|total/i.test(q)) {
      var open = issues.filter(function(i) { return i.status === 'Open'; }).length;
      var critical = issues.filter(function(i) { return i.priority === 'Critical' && i.status !== 'Resolved' && i.status !== 'Closed'; }).length;
      var breached = issues.filter(function(i) { return i.slaBreached; }).length;
      var resolved = issues.filter(function(i) { return i.status === 'Resolved' || i.status === 'Closed'; }).length;
      return { intent: 'summary', stats: { open: open, critical: critical, breached: breached, resolved: resolved, total: issues.length } };
    }

    var filtered = issues.slice();
    var filtersApplied = [];

    if (/critical/i.test(q))     { filtered = filtered.filter(function(i) { return i.priority === 'Critical'; }); filtersApplied.push('Critical priority'); }
    if (/high priority/i.test(q)){ filtered = filtered.filter(function(i) { return i.priority === 'High'; }); filtersApplied.push('High priority'); }
    if (/sla breach/i.test(q))   { filtered = filtered.filter(function(i) { return i.slaBreached; }); filtersApplied.push('SLA breached'); }
    if (/\bopen\b/i.test(q))     { filtered = filtered.filter(function(i) { return i.status === 'Open'; }); filtersApplied.push('Status: Open'); }
    if (/in progress/i.test(q))  { filtered = filtered.filter(function(i) { return i.status === 'In Progress'; }); filtersApplied.push('In Progress'); }
    if (/resolved/i.test(q))     { filtered = filtered.filter(function(i) { return i.status === 'Resolved' || i.status === 'Closed'; }); filtersApplied.push('Resolved'); }
    if (/my issues|assigned to me/i.test(q) && App.currentUser) {
      var me = App.currentUser.email;
      filtered = filtered.filter(function(i) { return i.assignedTo === me || i.raisedBy === me; });
      filtersApplied.push('Assigned to me');
    }

    var mods = ['API','Dashboard','Reports','Authentication','Database','UI','Integration','Backend','Frontend','DevOps'];
    for (var mi = 0; mi < mods.length; mi++) {
      if (q.indexOf(mods[mi].toLowerCase()) !== -1) {
        var m = mods[mi];
        filtered = filtered.filter(function(i) { return i.module === m; });
        filtersApplied.push('Module: ' + m);
        break;
      }
    }

    var keywords = q.split(' ').filter(function(w) {
      return w.length > 3 && ['show','find','issues','bugs','list'].indexOf(w) === -1;
    });
    if (keywords.length && filtersApplied.length === 0) {
      filtered = filtered.filter(function(i) {
        return keywords.some(function(k) {
          return (i.title||'').toLowerCase().indexOf(k) !== -1 || (i.description||'').toLowerCase().indexOf(k) !== -1;
        });
      });
      filtersApplied.push('Search: ' + keywords.join(' '));
    }

    return { intent: 'filter', issues: filtered.slice(0, 20), filters: filtersApplied };
  },

  askGemini: async function(query, localResult) {
    var apiKey = this.getGeminiKey();
    if (!apiKey) throw new Error('No Gemini API key set');

    var issuesSummary = (this._issueCache || []).slice(0, 40).map(function(i) {
      return (i.id||'') + '|' + (i.title||'') + '|' + (i.priority||'') + '|' + (i.status||'') + '|' + (i.module||'') + '|' + (i.assignedTo||'');
    }).join('\n');

    var userName = (App.currentUser && App.currentUser.name) ? App.currentUser.name : 'Unknown';
    var userRole = (App.currentUser && App.currentUser.role) ? App.currentUser.role : 'Unknown';

    var prompt = 'You are an AI assistant for TechTrack, an engineering issue tracker.\n' +
      'User: ' + userName + ' (' + userRole + ') | Today: ' + new Date().toDateString() + '\n' +
      'Query: ' + query + '\n\n' +
      'Reply with ONLY a raw JSON object, no markdown, no explanation:\n' +
      '{"intent":"create|filter|summary|unknown","confidence":0.9,"message":"what you did",' +
      '"filters":[],"issues":[{"id":"","title":"","priority":"","status":"","module":""}],' +
      '"create":{"title":"","description":"","priority":"Medium","module":"","environment":"","impact":""},' +
      '"summary":{"open":0,"critical":0,"breached":0,"resolved":0,"total":0}}\n\n' +
      'Issue data (id|title|priority|status|module|assignee):\n' + issuesSummary + '\n\n' +
      'Intent rules: create/new/add/log=create intent; show/find/list/search=filter intent; how many/count/summary=summary intent\n' +
      'For filter: return matching issue rows from data above.\n' +
      'Return ONLY the JSON object.';

    var response = await fetch(
      'https://generativelanguage.googleapis.com/v1beta/models/gemini-2.0-flash:generateContent?key=' + apiKey,
      {
        method: 'POST',
        headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },
        body: JSON.stringify({
          contents: [{ parts: [{ text: prompt }] }],
          generationConfig: {
            temperature: 0.2,
            maxOutputTokens: 1200,
            responseMimeType: 'application/json'
          }
        })
      }
    );

    if (!response.ok) {
      var errData = await response.json().catch(function() { return {}; });
      throw new Error((errData && errData.error && errData.error.message) || ('Gemini API error ' + response.status));
    }

    var data = await response.json();
    var text = (data.candidates && data.candidates[0] && data.candidates[0].content &&
                data.candidates[0].content.parts && data.candidates[0].content.parts[0] &&
                data.candidates[0].content.parts[0].text) ? data.candidates[0].content.parts[0].text : '{}';
    var clean = text.replace(/```json|```/g, '').trim();
    return JSON.parse(clean);
  },

  getGeminiKey: function() {
    try { return localStorage.getItem('tt_gemini_key') || ''; } catch(e) { return ''; }
  },

  setGeminiKey: function(key) {
    try { localStorage.setItem('tt_gemini_key', key); } catch(e) {}
  },

  render: function(result, query) {
    var panel = document.getElementById('aiPanel');
    var backdrop = document.getElementById('aiBackdrop');
    if (!panel) return;

    var intentLabels = {
      create: 'Create Issue', filter: 'Filter Results',
      summary: 'Summary', update: 'Update', unknown: 'Unknown'
    };
    var intentClass = result.intent || 'unknown';
    var bodyHtml = '';

    if (result.intent === 'create') {
      var c = result.create || {};
      var title = c.title || query.replace(/^(create|new|add|report|log|raise)[\s:]*/i,'').trim();

      var priorityOpts = ['Critical','High','Medium','Low'].map(function(p) {
        return '<option value="' + p + '"' + (p === (c.priority||'Medium') ? ' selected' : '') + '>' + p + '</option>';
      }).join('');
      var envOpts = ['','Production','Staging','Development','QA'].map(function(e) {
        return '<option value="' + e + '"' + (e === (c.environment||'') ? ' selected' : '') + '>' + (e||'Select...') + '</option>';
      }).join('');
      var impactOpts = ['','Revenue','Customer','Internal','Performance','Security'].map(function(im) {
        return '<option value="' + im + '"' + (im === (c.impact||'') ? ' selected' : '') + '>' + (im||'Select...') + '</option>';
      }).join('');

      bodyHtml =
        '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-bottom:10px">' +
          (result.message || 'I\'ll pre-fill a new issue. Review and confirm:') +
        '</p>' +
        '<div class="ai-confirm-form" id="aiCreateForm">' +
          '<div class="ai-confirm-row">' +
            '<div class="ai-confirm-key">Title</div>' +
            '<input class="ai-confirm-edit" id="aiTitle" value="' + this._esc(title) + '">' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="ai-confirm-row">' +
            '<div class="ai-confirm-key">Description</div>' +
            '<input class="ai-confirm-edit" id="aiDesc" value="' + this._esc(c.description || title) + '">' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="ai-confirm-row">' +
            '<div class="ai-confirm-key">Priority</div>' +
            '<select class="ai-confirm-edit" id="aiPriority">' + priorityOpts + '</select>' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="ai-confirm-row">' +
            '<div class="ai-confirm-key">Module</div>' +
            '<input class="ai-confirm-edit" id="aiModule" value="' + this._esc(c.module||'') + '">' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="ai-confirm-row">' +
            '<div class="ai-confirm-key">Environment</div>' +
            '<select class="ai-confirm-edit" id="aiEnv">' + envOpts + '</select>' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="ai-confirm-row">' +
            '<div class="ai-confirm-key">Impact</div>' +
            '<select class="ai-confirm-edit" id="aiImpact">' + impactOpts + '</select>' +
          '</div>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="ai-actions">' +
          '<button class="btn-primary" onclick="AI.confirmCreate()">Create Issue</button>' +
          '<button class="btn-secondary" onclick="AI.openCreatePage()">Open Full Form</button>' +
          '<button class="btn-secondary" onclick="AI.close()">Cancel</button>' +
        '</div>';
    }

    else if (result.intent === 'summary') {
      var s = result.summary || result.stats || {};
      bodyHtml =
        '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-bottom:10px">' +
          (result.message || 'Current system summary:') +
        '</p>' +
        '<div class="ai-summary-grid">' +
          '<div class="ai-summary-stat"><div class="ai-summary-val" style="color:var(--status-open)">' + (s.open||0) + '</div><div class="ai-summary-lbl">Open</div></div>' +
          '<div class="ai-summary-stat"><div class="ai-summary-val" style="color:var(--critical)">' + (s.critical||0) + '</div><div class="ai-summary-lbl">Critical</div></div>' +
          '<div class="ai-summary-stat"><div class="ai-summary-val" style="color:var(--critical)">' + (s.breached||0) + '</div><div class="ai-summary-lbl">SLA Breach</div></div>' +
          '<div class="ai-summary-stat"><div class="ai-summary-val" style="color:var(--low)">' + (s.resolved||0) + '</div><div class="ai-summary-lbl">Resolved</div></div>' +
          '<div class="ai-summary-stat"><div class="ai-summary-val">' + (s.total||0) + '</div><div class="ai-summary-lbl">Total</div></div>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="ai-actions">' +
          '<button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.navigate(\'dashboard\');AI.close()">Open Dashboard</button>' +
        '</div>';
    }

    else {
      var issues = result.issues || [];
      var filters = (result.filters || []).join(' \xB7 ');
      var rows = '';
      if (issues.length > 0) {
        for (var ri = 0; ri < issues.length; ri++) {
          var iss = issues[ri];
          rows += '<div class="ai-issue-row" onclick="App.navigate(\'issue-detail\',{id:\'' + (iss.id||'') + '\'});AI.close()">' +
            '<div class="ai-issue-id">' + (iss.id||'') + '</div>' +
            '<div class="ai-issue-title">' + this._esc(iss.title||'') + '</div>' +
            '<span class="badge priority-' + (iss.priority||'').toLowerCase() + '">' + (iss.priority||'') + '</span>' +
            '<div class="ai-issue-meta">' + (iss.module||'') + '</div>' +
          '</div>';
        }
      } else {
        rows = '<div class="empty-state" style="padding:24px"><div class="empty-state-icon">Search</div><p>No issues matched</p></div>';
      }

      bodyHtml =
        (filters ? '<p style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-bottom:10px;font-family:var(--font-mono)">' + filters + '</p>' : '') +
        '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-bottom:12px">' +
          (result.message || ('Found ' + issues.length + ' issue' + (issues.length !== 1 ? 's' : ''))) +
        '</p>' +
        '<div>' + rows + '</div>' +
        (issues.length > 0 ? '<div class="ai-actions"><button class="btn-secondary" onclick="AI.applyToIssueList()" style="font-size:11px">Open in Issue List \u2192</button></div>' : '');
    }

    var chips4 = this.SUGGESTIONS.slice(0,4).map(function(s) {
      return '<div class="ai-chip" onclick="AI.runSuggestion(\'' + s.replace(/'/g, "\\'") + '\')">' + s + '</div>';
    }).join('');

    panel.innerHTML =
      '<div class="ai-panel-header">' +
        '<div class="ai-panel-title">' +
          '<span class="ai-intent ' + intentClass + '">' + (intentLabels[intentClass]||'AI') + '</span>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<button class="ai-panel-close" onclick="AI.close()">\u2715</button>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<div class="ai-panel-body">' + bodyHtml + '</div>' +
      '<div class="ai-suggestions">' + chips4 + '</div>';

    panel.style.display = 'block';
    backdrop.style.display = 'block';
  },

  confirmCreate: async function() {
    var issueData = {
      title:       (document.getElementById('aiTitle') || {}).value || '',
      description: (document.getElementById('aiDesc') || {}).value || '',
      priority:    (document.getElementById('aiPriority') || {}).value || 'Medium',
      module:      (document.getElementById('aiModule') || {}).value || '',
      environment: (document.getElementById('aiEnv') || {}).value || '',
      impact:      (document.getElementById('aiImpact') || {}).value || ''
    };
    if (!issueData.title.trim()) { App.showToast('Title is required', 'warning'); return; }
    App.showToast('Creating issue via AI...', 'info');
    var result = await App.call('createIssue', issueData);
    if (result.success) {
      this.close();
      App.showToast('Issue ' + result.issueId + ' created!', 'success');
      App.navigate('issue-detail', { id: result.issueId });
    } else {
      App.showToast('Failed: ' + result.error, 'error');
    }
  },

  openCreatePage: function() {
    var title = (document.getElementById('aiTitle') || {}).value || '';
    this.close();
    App.navigate('create-issue');
    setTimeout(function() {
      var el = document.getElementById('issueTitle');
      if (el) el.value = title;
    }, 400);
  },

  applyToIssueList: function() {
    this.close();
    App.navigate('issue-list');
  },

  setLoading: function(on) {
    var bar = document.getElementById('aiBar');
    var icon = document.getElementById('aiBarIcon');
    if (bar) bar.classList.toggle('loading', on);
    if (icon) icon.classList.toggle('spinning', on);
  },

  close: function() {
    var panel = document.getElementById('aiPanel');
    var backdrop = document.getElementById('aiBackdrop');
    if (panel) panel.style.display = 'none';
    if (backdrop) backdrop.style.display = 'none';
    this.setLoading(false);
  },

  saveKeyFromBanner: function() {
    var key = (document.getElementById('geminiKeyInput') || {}).value || '';
    key = key.trim();
    if (!key) { App.showToast('Please enter your Gemini API key', 'warning'); return; }
    this.setGeminiKey(key);
    var banner = document.getElementById('geminiBanner');
    if (banner) banner.style.display = 'none';
    App.showToast('Gemini API key saved! AI commands are now active.', 'success');
  },

  showKeyBanner: function() {
    var banner = document.getElementById('geminiBanner');
    if (banner) banner.style.display = 'block';
  },

  checkKeyOnInit: function() {
    var self = this;
    if (!this.getGeminiKey()) {
      setTimeout(function() { self.showKeyBanner(); }, 2000);
    }
  },

  _esc: function(str) {
    if (!str) return '';
    return String(str)
      .replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;')
      .replace(/"/g,'&quot;').replace(/'/g,'&#039;');
  },

  _callBackend: function(fn, arg) {
    return new Promise(function(resolve) {
      google.script.run
        .withSuccessHandler(resolve)
        .withFailureHandler(function(err) { resolve({ success: false, error: err.message }); })
        [fn](arg);
    });
  }
};



// ============================================================
// THEME SYSTEM
// ============================================================

const Themes = {
  THEMES: ['midnight','arctic','forest','sunset','ocean','slate','uiux'],
  LABELS: {
    midnight: 'Midnight',
    arctic:   'Arctic Light',
    forest:   'Forest',
    sunset:   'Sunset',
    ocean:    'Ocean',
    slate:    'Slate Pro',
    uiux:     'UIUX',
    neon:     'Neon',
    rosegold: 'Rose Gold',
    nova:     '✦ Nova',
    clarity:  '⬡ Clarity'
  },
  ICONS: {
    midnight:'■', arctic:'○', forest:'▲', sunset:'●', ocean:'□', slate:'◆', uiux:'◈',
    neon:'◉', rosegold:'◇', nova:'✦', clarity:'⬡'
  },

  current: 'midnight',

  init() {
    const saved = (typeof localStorage !== 'undefined' && localStorage.getItem('tt_theme')) || 'midnight';
    this.apply(saved, false);
  },

  set(name, el) {
    this.apply(name, true);
    // Update active states
    document.querySelectorAll('.theme-option').forEach(o => o.classList.remove('active'));
    if (el) el.classList.add('active');
    this.toggle(); // close panel
  },

  apply(name, save) {
    document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', name);
    this.current = name;
    const icon = document.getElementById('themeIcon');
    const label = document.getElementById('themeLabel');
    if (icon) icon.textContent = this.ICONS[name] || '•';
    if (label) label.textContent = this.LABELS[name] || 'Theme';
    // Mark active option
    document.querySelectorAll('.theme-option').forEach(o => {
      o.classList.toggle('active', o.dataset.themePick === name);
    });
    if (save) {
      try { localStorage.setItem('tt_theme', name); } catch(e) {}
    }
  },

  toggle() {
    const picker = document.getElementById('themePicker');
    if (picker) picker.classList.toggle('open');
  }
};

// Close theme picker when clicking outside
document.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
  const picker = document.getElementById('themePicker');
  const btn = document.getElementById('themeToggleBtn');
  if (picker && !picker.contains(e.target) && btn && !btn.contains(e.target)) {
    picker.classList.remove('open');
  }
});

/* ============================================================
   FOLLOW-UP TRACKER  — localStorage-based per issue
   ============================================================ */
const FollowUp = {
  _key: id => 'tt_fu_' + id,

  get(id) {
    try { return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(this._key(id)) || '[]'); }
    catch(e) { return []; }
  },

  add(id, note) {
    const list = this.get(id);
    list.push({ ts: new Date().toISOString(), note: (note || '').trim() });
    try { localStorage.setItem(this._key(id), JSON.stringify(list)); } catch(e) {}
    return list;
  },

  count(id) { return this.get(id).length; },

  /* Small flag button used in table rows & kanban cards */
  renderBtn(id) {
    const n = this.count(id);
    const hasCls = n > 0 ? ' has-fu' : '';
    const countHtml = n > 0 ? ` <span class="fu-count">${n}</span>` : '';
    const tip = n > 0 ? `${n} follow-up${n>1?'s':''} logged` : 'Log follow-up';
    return `<button class="followup-btn${hasCls}" title="${tip}" data-fu-id="${id}"
              onclick="event.stopPropagation(); FollowUp.openModal('${id}')">🚩${countHtml}</button>`;
  },

  /* Full modal dialog */
  openModal(issueId) {
    const existing = document.getElementById('fuModal');
    if (existing) existing.remove();

    const overlay = document.createElement('div');
    overlay.className = 'fu-modal-overlay';
    overlay.id = 'fuModal';
    overlay.innerHTML = this._modalHtml(issueId);
    document.body.appendChild(overlay);
    overlay.addEventListener('click', e => { if (e.target === overlay) overlay.remove(); });
    overlay.querySelector('.fu-note-input')?.focus();
  },

  _modalHtml(issueId) {
    const list = this.get(issueId);
    return `<div class="fu-modal">
      <div class="fu-modal-header">
        <span class="fu-modal-title">🚩 Follow-up Tracker &nbsp;—&nbsp; ${issueId}</span>
        <button class="fu-modal-close" onclick="document.getElementById('fuModal').remove()">×</button>
      </div>
      <div class="fu-modal-body">
        <div class="fu-log-section">
          <div class="fu-log-title">Log New Follow-up</div>
          <textarea class="fu-note-input" id="fuNoteInput"
            placeholder="Optional note — e.g. 'Pinged dev team on Slack, awaiting ETA'" rows="2"></textarea>
          <button class="fu-log-btn" onclick="FollowUp._logAndRefresh('${issueId}')">+ Log Follow-up</button>
        </div>
        <div class="fu-history-section">
          <div class="fu-history-title">
            History
            <span class="fu-count-label" id="fuCountLabel">${list.length} follow-up${list.length!==1?'s':''}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="fu-history-list" id="fuHistoryList">${this._historyHtml(list)}</div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>`;
  },

  _historyHtml(list) {
    if (!list.length) return '<div class="fu-empty">No follow-ups yet. Log your first one above.</div>';
    return list.slice().reverse().map((fu, ri) => {
      const idx = list.length - ri;
      const dt = new Date(fu.ts);
      const dateStr = dt.toLocaleDateString('en', {day:'numeric',month:'short',year:'numeric'});
      const timeStr = dt.toLocaleTimeString('en', {hour:'2-digit',minute:'2-digit'});
      return `<div class="fu-item">
        <div class="fu-item-top">
          <span class="fu-num">#${idx}</span>
          <span class="fu-ts">${dateStr} · ${timeStr}</span>
        </div>
        ${fu.note ? `<div class="fu-note">${fu.note}</div>` : ''}
      </div>`;
    }).join('');
  },

  _logAndRefresh(issueId) {
    const note = document.getElementById('fuNoteInput')?.value || '';
    const list = this.add(issueId, note);

    /* Refresh modal history */
    const histEl = document.getElementById('fuHistoryList');
    if (histEl) histEl.innerHTML = this._historyHtml(list);
    const lblEl = document.getElementById('fuCountLabel');
    if (lblEl) lblEl.textContent = `${list.length} follow-up${list.length!==1?'s':''}`;
    const inp = document.getElementById('fuNoteInput');
    if (inp) inp.value = '';

    /* Refresh all flag buttons for this issue in the page */
    document.querySelectorAll(`[data-fu-id="${issueId}"]`).forEach(btn => {
      const n = list.length;
      btn.className = 'followup-btn' + (n > 0 ? ' has-fu' : '');
      btn.title = n > 0 ? `${n} follow-up${n>1?'s':''} logged` : 'Log follow-up';
      btn.innerHTML = '🚩' + (n > 0 ? ` <span class="fu-count">${n}</span>` : '');
    });

    /* Refresh inline detail panel if visible */
    const detailCount = document.getElementById('fuDetailCount');
    if (detailCount) detailCount.textContent = list.length;
    const detailHistory = document.getElementById('fuDetailHistory');
    if (detailHistory) detailHistory.innerHTML = this._historyHtml(list);

    if (typeof Toast !== 'undefined') Toast.show('Follow-up logged ✓', 'success');
  }
};
