const App = {
  currentUser: null,
  currentPage: 'dashboard',
  issueFilters: { status: 'all', priority: 'all', module: 'all', assignedTo: 'all' },
  allIssues: [],
  users: [],
  modules: [],

  // ============================================================
  // INIT
  // ============================================================
  
  async init() {
    // Cycle through loading messages while waiting
    const messages = [
      'Authenticating session...',
      'Connecting to Google Sheets...',
      'Loading your workspace...',
      'Almost ready...'
    ];
    const msgEl = document.querySelector('.loader-msg');
    let msgIdx = 0;
    const msgTimer = setInterval(() => {
      msgIdx = (msgIdx + 1) % messages.length;
      if (msgEl) msgEl.textContent = messages[msgIdx];
    }, 1800);

    // Hard timeout   if google.script.run never responds, show clear error
    const timeoutId = setTimeout(() => {
      clearInterval(msgTimer);
      this.showError(
        'Connection timed out. Please check:\n' +
        '1. Your Spreadsheet ID is set in Code.gs\n' +
        '2. You ran initializeSpreadsheet() from the Apps Script editor\n' +
        '3. The Web App is deployed with "Execute as: Me"\n\n' +
        'Try refreshing the page.'
      );
    }, 12000);

    try {
      const result = await this.call('getCurrentUser');
      clearTimeout(timeoutId);
      clearInterval(msgTimer);

      if (!result.success) {
        this.showError(result.error || 'Access denied. Contact your administrator.');
        return;
      }

      this.currentUser = result.user;

      // Load feature flags early — they control what gets rendered
      try {
        const flagsResult = await this.call('getAllFeatureFlags');
        this.featureFlags = (flagsResult && flagsResult.success) ? flagsResult.flags : {};
      } catch(fe) {
        this.featureFlags = {};
      }

      this.setupUI();
      this.navigate('dashboard');

    } catch (err) {
      clearTimeout(timeoutId);
      clearInterval(msgTimer);
      this.showError('Initialization failed: ' + err.message);
    }
  },
  
  setupUI() {
    // Init theme from saved preference
    Themes.init();
    // Init AI command bar
    AI.init();
    this.initKeyboardShortcuts();
    Notif.init();
    Search.init();
    OfflineMonitor.init();
    this.applyFeatureFlags();
    this.initContextMenu();
    this.loadAnnouncements();

    document.getElementById('loading-screen').style.display = 'none';
    document.getElementById('main-app').style.display = 'flex';
    
    // Set user info
    const u = this.currentUser;
    document.getElementById('userAvatar').textContent = '\u{1F464}';
    document.getElementById('userName').textContent = u.name || u.email;
    document.getElementById('userRole').textContent = u.role + ' · ' + u.team;
    
    // Show admin nav
    if (u.role === 'Admin') {
      document.getElementById('adminNav').style.display = 'block';
    }
    
    // Nav click handlers
    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(item => {
      item.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        e.preventDefault();
        this.navigate(item.dataset.page);
      });
    });
    
    // Sidebar toggle
    document.getElementById('sidebarToggle').addEventListener('click', () => {
      document.getElementById('sidebar').classList.toggle('collapsed');
    });
    
    // Check SLA alerts
    this.checkSLAAlerts();
    setInterval(() => this.checkSLAAlerts(), 60000);
  },

  // ============================================================
  // NAVIGATION
  // ============================================================
  
  showPageError: function(area, message) {
    if (!area) return;
    area.innerHTML =
      '<div class="card" style="max-width:600px;border-color:var(--critical-dim);">' +
      '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;margin-bottom:12px;">' +
      '<span style="font-size:14px;font-weight:700;color:var(--critical);">Failed to load</span></div>' +
      '<p style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text-secondary);line-height:1.6;margin-bottom:14px;">' + (message || 'Could not connect to backend.') + '</p>' +
      '<div style="background:var(--bg-elevated);border-radius:8px;padding:12px;font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);font-family:var(--font-mono);line-height:1.8;">' +
      'If you just updated Code.gs:<br>' +
      '1. Apps Script → Deploy → Manage deployments<br>' +
      '2. Edit → New version → Deploy<br>' +
      '3. Also run initializeAll() once to create new sheets' +
      '</div></div>';
  },

  setPage(title, breadcrumb) {
    const el = document.getElementById('pageTitle');
    const bc = document.getElementById('breadcrumb');
    if (el) el.textContent = title;
    if (bc) bc.textContent = breadcrumb || '';
  },

  navigate(page, params = {}) {
    this.currentPage = page;
    
    const titles = {
      'dashboard': 'Dashboard',
      'create-issue': 'Create Issue',
      'issue-list': 'All Issues',
      'my-issues': 'My Issues',
      'issue-detail': 'Issue Detail',
      'admin-panel': 'Admin Panel',
      'user-management': 'User Management',
      'sla-settings': 'SLA Settings',
      'system-settings': 'System Settings',
      'ai-intelligence': 'AI Intelligence',
      'kanban': 'Kanban Board',
      'analytics': 'Analytics',
      'workload': 'Workload Balancer',
      'oncall': 'On-Call Schedule',
      'custom-fields': 'Custom Fields',
      'release-notes': 'Release Notes',
      'audit-trail': 'Audit Trail',
      'admin-settings': 'Settings',
      'escalations': 'Escalation Rules',
      'recurring': 'Recurring Templates',
      'integrations': 'Integrations',
      'leaderboard': 'Dev Leaderboard',
      'cfd': 'Cumulative Flow',
      'forecast': 'Issue Forecast',
      'repeat-offenders': 'Repeat Offenders',
      'first-response': 'First Response Time',
      'root-causes': 'Root Cause Clusters',
      'recurring': 'Recurring Templates',
      'workload-board': 'Developer Workload Board',
      'leadership': 'Leadership Dashboard'
    };
    
    document.getElementById('pageTitle').textContent = titles[page] || page;
    
    const breadcrumbs = {
      'dashboard': '',
      'create-issue': 'Issues / New Issue',
      'issue-list': 'Issues / All Issues',
      'my-issues': 'Issues / My Issues',
      'issue-detail': 'Issues / Detail',
      'admin-panel': 'Admin / Overview',
      'user-management': 'Admin / Users',
      'sla-settings': 'Admin / SLA',
      'system-settings': 'Admin / Settings'
    };
    const bcEl = document.getElementById('breadcrumb');
    if (bcEl) bcEl.textContent = breadcrumbs[page] || '';
    
    document.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(i => {
      i.classList.toggle('active', i.dataset.page === page);
    });
    
    const content = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    content.innerHTML = '<div style="padding:40px;text-align:center;color:var(--text-muted)"><div class="loader-bar" style="width:180px;margin:0 auto"><div class="loader-fill"></div></div></div>';
    
    this.updateMobileNav(page);
    switch(page) {
      case 'dashboard': this.renderDashboard(); break;
      case 'create-issue': this.renderCreateIssue(params); break;
      case 'issue-list': this.renderIssueList(); break;
      case 'my-issues': this.renderMyIssues(); break;
      case 'issue-detail': this.renderIssueDetail(params.id); break;
      case 'admin-panel': this.renderAdminPanel(); break;
      case 'admin-settings': this.renderAdminSettings(); break;
      case 'user-management': this.renderUserManagement(); break;
      case 'sla-settings': this.renderAdminSettings('sla'); break;
      case 'system-settings': this.renderAdminSettings('features'); break;
      case 'ai-intelligence': this.renderAdminSettings('ai'); break;
      case 'kanban': this.renderKanban(); break;
      case 'analytics': this.renderAnalytics(); break;
      case 'workload': this.renderWorkload(); break;
      case 'oncall': this.renderOnCall(); break;
      case 'custom-fields': this.renderCustomFields(); break;
      case 'release-notes': this.renderReleaseNotes(); break;
      case 'audit-trail': this.renderAuditTrail(); break;
      case 'escalations': this.renderEscalations(); break;
      case 'recurring': this.renderRecurring(); break;
      case 'integrations': this.renderIntegrations(); break;
      case 'leaderboard': this.renderLeaderboard(); break;
      case 'cfd': this.renderCFD(); break;
      case 'forecast': this.renderForecast(); break;
      case 'repeat-offenders': this.renderRepeatOffenders(); break;
      case 'first-response': this.renderFirstResponse(); break;
      case 'root-causes': this.renderRootCauseClusters(); break;
      case 'workload-board': this.renderWorkloadBoard(); break;
      case 'leadership': this.renderLeadershipDashboard(); break;
    }
  },

  // ============================================================
  // DASHBOARD
  // ============================================================

  async renderDashboard() {
  const area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
  // skeleton while loading
  area.innerHTML = `<div class="tt-dash-container">
    <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(4,1fr);gap:14px;margin-bottom:24px">
      ${[1,2,3,4].map(()=>`<div class="skeleton" style="height:88px;border-radius:14px"></div>`).join('')}
    </div>
    <div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:16px">
      ${[1,2,3,4].map(()=>`<div class="skeleton" style="height:280px;border-radius:14px"></div>`).join('')}
    </div>
  </div>`;

  const [statsRes, settingsRes] = await Promise.all([
    this.call('getDashboardStats'),
    this.call('getSettings')
  ]);

  if (!statsRes.success) {
    this.showPageError(area, statsRes.error || 'Failed to load dashboard data.');
    return;
  }

  const s        = statsRes.stats;
  const settings = settingsRes.success ? settingsRes.settings : {};
  const trend    = statsRes.trend || [];
  const wl       = Object.entries(statsRes.devWorkload || {}).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1]).slice(0,6);
  const pc       = statsRes.priorityCount || { Critical:0, High:0, Medium:0, Low:0 };
  const modCount = statsRes.moduleCount   || {};
  const total    = s.total || 1;
  const extractIssueArray = (value) => {
    if (Array.isArray(value)) return value;
    if (!value || typeof value !== 'object') return [];
    if (Array.isArray(value.rows)) return value.rows;
    if (Array.isArray(value.items)) return value.items;
    if (Array.isArray(value.nodes)) return value.nodes;
    return [];
  };

  const totalIssues = extractIssueArray(statsRes.issues)
    || extractIssueArray(statsRes.allIssues)
    || extractIssueArray(statsRes.issueList)
    || extractIssueArray(statsRes.data?.issues)
    || [];

  const wipCount = ((typeof s.wip === 'number' ? s.wip : 0) + (typeof s.inProgress === 'number' ? s.inProgress : 0))
    || totalIssues.filter(i => {
      const statusText = normalizeStatus(getIssueStatus(i));
      return statusText.includes('wip') || statusText.includes('in progress');
    }).length;
  const combinedOpenWIP = (s.open || 0) + wipCount;

  // Optionally load dev perf
  let perfRows = '';
  if (settings.DEV_PERFORMANCE_ANALYTICS_ENABLED === 'true') {
    const perfRes = await this.call('getDevPerformance');
    if (perfRes.success && perfRes.performance.length) {
      perfRows = perfRes.performance.map(d => `
        <tr>
          <td style="padding:10px 14px;font-size:12px;color:var(--text-secondary);font-family:var(--font-mono)">${d.email}</td>
          <td style="padding:10px 14px;text-align:center;font-weight:700;color:var(--text-primary)">${d.resolved}</td>
          <td style="padding:10px 14px;text-align:center;color:var(--text-secondary)">${d.avgResolutionHours}h</td>
          <td style="padding:10px 14px;text-align:center;color:${d.reopened>0?'var(--critical)':'var(--text-dim)'}">${d.reopened}</td>
        </tr>`).join('');
    }
  }

  const resolveValue = (value) => {
    if (value == null) return '';
    if (typeof value === 'string' || typeof value === 'number' || typeof value === 'boolean') return String(value);
    if (Array.isArray(value)) return value.map(resolveValue).join(' ');
    if (typeof value === 'object') {
      return resolveValue(value.name || value.label || value.value || value.email || value.id || value.type || value.status || value.priority || value.title || '');
    }
    return '';
  };

  const getIssueStatus = (issue) => resolveValue(issue.status || issue.state || issue.stage || issue.ticketStatus || issue.statusName || issue.stateName || issue.workflowState || issue.issueStatus || issue.ticket_status || issue.status_text);
  const getIssuePriority = (issue) => resolveValue(issue.priority || issue.severity || issue.priorityLevel || issue.priority_level || issue.severity_level || issue.severityName || issue.priorityName || issue.priority_text);
  const getIssueAssignee = (issue) => {
    const assignee = issue.assigned_to || issue.assignedTo || issue.assignedBy || issue.assignee || issue.owner || issue.user || issue.responsible;
    const resolved = resolveValue(assignee);
    return resolved || 'Unassigned';
  };
  const getIssueCreatedDate = (issue) => resolveValue(issue.createdDate || issue.created_at || issue.createdAt || issue.dateCreated || issue.created || issue.timestamp || issue.openedDate);

  const normalizePriority = (priority) => {
    const key = String(priority||'').trim().toLowerCase();
    if (key === 'critical') return 'Critical';
    if (key === 'high') return 'High';
    if (key === 'medium') return 'Medium';
    return 'Low';
  };

  const normalizeStatus = (status) => String(status||'').trim().toLowerCase();
  const isInProgressStatus = (status) => {
    const key = normalizeStatus(status);
    return key.includes('wip') || key.includes('in progress') || key.includes('inprogress') || key.includes('working') || key.includes('active') || key.includes('ongoing');
  };

  const inProgressIssues = totalIssues.filter(i => isInProgressStatus(getIssueStatus(i)));

  const closedCount = s.closed || s.resolved || s.resolvedCount || 0;
  const statusChartLabels = ['Total','In Progress','Resolved'];
  const statusChartValues = [s.total || totalIssues.length || 0, wipCount, closedCount];
  const statusChartColors = ['#378add','#7F77DD','#2ed573'];

  const prioLabels = ['Critical','High','Medium','Low'];
  const prioValues = prioLabels.map(p => pc[p] || pc[p.toLowerCase()] || totalIssues.filter(i => normalizePriority(getIssuePriority(i)) === p).length);
  // Use server-side severityInProgress aggregation (already computed by getDashboardStats)
  const prioInProgressValues = prioLabels.map(p => {
    if (statsRes.severityInProgress && statsRes.severityInProgress[p] != null) return statsRes.severityInProgress[p];
    return inProgressIssues.filter(i => normalizePriority(getIssuePriority(i)) === p).length;
  });
  const prioColors = ['#ff4757','#f5a623','#74b9ff','#2ed573'];

  const devWorkloadTotal = {};
  const devWorkloadInProgress = {};
  totalIssues.forEach(issue => {
    const devKey = getIssueAssignee(issue) || 'Unassigned';
    const dev = String(devKey).split('@')[0] || 'Unassigned';
    const prio = normalizePriority(getIssuePriority(issue));
    devWorkloadTotal[dev] = devWorkloadTotal[dev] || { Critical: 0, High: 0, Medium: 0, Low: 0 };
    devWorkloadTotal[dev][prio] += 1;
    if (isInProgressStatus(getIssueStatus(issue))) {
      devWorkloadInProgress[dev] = devWorkloadInProgress[dev] || { Critical: 0, High: 0, Medium: 0, Low: 0 };
      devWorkloadInProgress[dev][prio] += 1;
    }
  });

  const buildDevChartData = (devMap) => {
    const rows = Object.entries(devMap)
      .map(([dev, counts]) => ({
        dev,
        counts,
        total: Object.values(counts).reduce((sum, value) => sum + value, 0)
      }))
      .sort((a,b) => b.total - a.total)
      .slice(0, 6);

    return {
      labels: rows.map(r => r.dev),
      datasets: prioLabels.map((prio, idx) => ({
        label: prio,
        data: rows.map(r => r.counts[prio] || 0),
        backgroundColor: prioColors[idx],
        stack: 'workload'
      }))
    };
  };

  // Build dev chart data from backend-aggregated severity maps (devWorkloadSeverityTotal / devWorkloadSeverityInProgress)
  const buildDevChartDataFromServer = (devMap) => {
    const rows = Object.entries(devMap || {})
      .map(([email, counts]) => ({
        dev: email.split('@')[0],
        counts,
        total: Object.values(counts).reduce((s, v) => s + v, 0)
      }))
      .sort((a, b) => b.total - a.total)
      .slice(0, 6);
    return {
      labels: rows.map(r => r.dev),
      datasets: prioLabels.map((prio, idx) => ({
        label: prio,
        data: rows.map(r => r.counts[prio] || 0),
        backgroundColor: prioColors[idx],
        stack: 'workload'
      }))
    };
  };

  const devTotalData = Object.keys(statsRes.devWorkloadSeverityTotal || {}).length
    ? buildDevChartDataFromServer(statsRes.devWorkloadSeverityTotal)
    : Object.keys(devWorkloadTotal).length ? buildDevChartData(devWorkloadTotal)
    : { labels: wl.map(([e]) => e.split('@')[0]), datasets:[{ label:'Tickets', data: wl.map(([,n]) => n), backgroundColor:'#74b9ff', stack:'workload' }] };

  const devInProgressData = Object.keys(statsRes.devWorkloadSeverityInProgress || {}).length
    ? buildDevChartDataFromServer(statsRes.devWorkloadSeverityInProgress)
    : Object.keys(devWorkloadInProgress).length ? buildDevChartData(devWorkloadInProgress)
    : { labels: [], datasets: [] };

  // Use server-side aging buckets (already computed by getDashboardStats for WIP issues)
  const backendAging = statsRes.aging || {};
  const ageBuckets = [
    { label:'0–2d',  key:'0–2 days',  min:0,  max:2 },
    { label:'3–5d',  key:'3–5 days',  min:3,  max:5 },
    { label:'6–10d', key:'6–10 days', min:6,  max:10 },
    { label:'10+d',  key:'10+ days',  min:11, max:Infinity }
  ];
  const agingValues = ageBuckets.map(bucket => {
    if (backendAging[bucket.key] != null) return backendAging[bucket.key];
    return inProgressIssues.filter(issue => {
      const dateValue = getIssueCreatedDate(issue);
      const createdTs = new Date(dateValue).getTime();
      const age = Number.isFinite(createdTs) ? Math.max(0, Math.floor((Date.now() - createdTs) / 86400000)) : 0;
      return age >= bucket.min && age <= bucket.max;
    }).length;
  });

  // Use server-computed open-age stats (added to getDashboardStats)
  const avgOpenAge = (typeof s.avgOpenAge === 'number' ? s.avgOpenAge : null)
    ?? (() => {
      const openIssues = totalIssues.filter(i => {
        const statusKey = normalizeStatus(getIssueStatus(i));
        return ['open','in progress','inprogress','wip','acknowledged','blocked','need info','reopened'].includes(statusKey);
      });
      return openIssues.length ? Math.round(openIssues.reduce((sum, i) => {
        const createdTs = new Date(getIssueCreatedDate(i)).getTime();
        return sum + ((Date.now() - createdTs) / 86400000);
      }, 0) / openIssues.length) : 0;
    })();
  const oldestOpenAge = (typeof s.oldestOpenAge === 'number' ? s.oldestOpenAge : null)
    ?? (() => {
      const openIssues = totalIssues.filter(i => {
        const statusKey = normalizeStatus(getIssueStatus(i));
        return ['open','in progress','inprogress','wip','acknowledged','blocked','need info','reopened'].includes(statusKey);
      });
      return openIssues.length ? Math.round((Date.now() - Math.min(...openIssues.map(i => new Date(getIssueCreatedDate(i)).getTime()))) / 86400000) : 0;
    })();

  const trendLabels = trend.map(t => {
    const d = new Date(t.date);
    return ['Sun','Mon','Tue','Wed','Thu','Fri','Sat'][d.getDay()];
  });
  const trendValues = trend.map(t => t.count);

  const devLabels = wl.map(([e])=>e.split('@')[0]);
  const devValues = wl.map(([,n])=>n);
  const devMax    = Math.max(...devValues, 1);
  const devColors = devValues.map(v => v >= devMax*0.8 ? '#ff4757' : v >= devMax*0.55 ? '#f5a623' : '#2ed573');

  const modTop   = Object.entries(modCount).sort((a,b)=>b[1]-a[1]).slice(0,7);
  const modLabels = modTop.map(([m])=>m);
  const modValues = modTop.map(([,n])=>n);

  const legendHTML = (labels, colors) =>
    `<div class="tt-legend">${labels.map((l,i)=>
      `<div class="tt-legend-item"><div class="tt-legend-dot" style="background:${colors[i]}"></div>${l}</div>`
    ).join('')}</div>`;

  area.innerHTML = `
  <div class="tt-dash-container">
    <div class="tt-header">
      <h1>Dashboard</h1>
      <p>Live engineering metrics &middot; auto-refreshes every 60s</p>
    </div>

    <div class="tt-kpi-grid">
      <div class="tt-kpi-card" style="--tt-kpi-color:#378ADD">
        <div class="tt-kpi-icon">📋</div>
        <div>
          <div class="tt-kpi-value">${s.total}</div>
          <div class="tt-kpi-label">Total issues</div>
          <div class="tt-kpi-sub">all time</div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="tt-kpi-card" style="--tt-kpi-color:#7F77DD">
        <div class="tt-kpi-icon"> </div>
        <div>
          <div class="tt-kpi-value">${wipCount}</div>
          <div class="tt-kpi-label">WIP / In Progress</div>
          <div class="tt-kpi-value">${combinedOpenWIP}</div> <div class="tt-kpi-label">Open + WIP</div> <div class="tt-kpi-sub">${Math.round((combinedOpenWIP/total)*100)}% of total</div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="tt-kpi-card" style="--tt-kpi-color:#ff4757">
        <div class="tt-kpi-icon">⚠️</div>
        <div>
          <div class="tt-kpi-value">${s.critical}</div>
          <div class="tt-kpi-label">Critical open</div>
          <div class="tt-kpi-sub">${s.slaBreached} SLA breached</div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="tt-kpi-card" style="--tt-kpi-color:#2ed573">
        <div class="tt-kpi-icon">✅</div>
        <div>
          <div class="tt-kpi-value">${s.resolved}</div>
          <div class="tt-kpi-label">Resolved</div>
          <div class="tt-kpi-sub">${s.closed} closed</div>
        </div>
      </div>
      <div class="tt-kpi-card" style="--tt-kpi-color:#f5a623">
        <div class="tt-kpi-icon">⏱️</div>
        <div>
          <div class="tt-kpi-value">${avgOpenAge}d</div>
          <div class="tt-kpi-label">Avg open age</div>
          <div class="tt-kpi-sub">Oldest ${oldestOpenAge}d</div>
        </div>
      </div>
    </div>

    <div class="tt-charts-grid">

      <div class="tt-chart-card">
        <p class="tt-chart-card-title">Ticket status snapshot</p>
        <p class="tt-chart-card-sub">Total tickets, in progress, and closed</p>
        <div style="position:relative;height:200px;margin-top:8px">
          <canvas id="ttC1" role="img" aria-label="Bar chart of total tickets, in progress tickets, and closed tickets">Status snapshot.</canvas>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="tt-chart-card">
        <p class="tt-chart-card-title">Severity breakdown</p>
        <p class="tt-chart-card-sub">All tickets by priority</p>
        ${legendHTML(prioLabels, prioColors)}
        <div style="position:relative;height:220px;margin-top:8px">
          <canvas id="ttC2" role="img" aria-label="Doughnut chart of total tickets by priority">Priority breakdown.</canvas>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="tt-chart-card">
        <p class="tt-chart-card-title">In progress severity</p>
        <p class="tt-chart-card-sub">In progress tickets by priority</p>
        ${legendHTML(prioLabels, prioColors)}
        <div style="position:relative;height:220px;margin-top:8px">
          <canvas id="ttC3" role="img" aria-label="Doughnut chart of in progress tickets by priority">In progress severity.</canvas>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="tt-chart-card">
        <p class="tt-chart-card-title">Developer workload</p>
        <p class="tt-chart-card-sub">All tickets per developer by priority</p>
        <div style="position:relative;height:260px;margin-top:8px">
          <canvas id="ttC4" role="img" aria-label="Stacked bar chart of developer workload for total tickets">Developer workload total.</canvas>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="tt-chart-card">
        <p class="tt-chart-card-title">In progress developer workload</p>
        <p class="tt-chart-card-sub">In progress tickets per developer by priority</p>
        <div style="position:relative;height:260px;margin-top:8px">
          <canvas id="ttC5" role="img" aria-label="Stacked bar chart of developer workload for in progress tickets">Developer workload in progress.</canvas>
        </div>
      </div>

      <div class="tt-chart-card">
        <p class="tt-chart-card-title">Aging for in progress tickets</p>
        <p class="tt-chart-card-sub">How long active tickets have been open</p>
        <div style="position:relative;height:220px;margin-top:8px">
          <canvas id="ttC6" role="img" aria-label="Bar chart of aging buckets for in progress tickets">Ticket aging.</canvas>
        </div>
      </div>

    </div>

    ${settings.BUG_HEATMAP_ENABLED === 'true' && modTop.length > 0 ? `
    <div class="tt-chart-card" style="margin-bottom:16px">
      <p class="tt-chart-card-title">Bug heatmap by module</p>
      <p class="tt-chart-card-sub">Issue count per module</p>
      <div style="position:relative;height:180px;margin-top:8px">
        <canvas id="ttC7" role="img" aria-label="Bar chart of issues per module">Module distribution.</canvas>
      </div>
    </div>` : ''}

    ${perfRows ? `
    <div class="tt-chart-card">
      <p class="tt-chart-card-title">Developer performance</p>
      <p class="tt-chart-card-sub">Resolution metrics this period</p>
      <table style="width:100%;border-collapse:collapse;margin-top:8px">
        <thead>
          <tr style="border-bottom:1px solid var(--border)">
            <th style="padding:6px 14px;text-align:left;font-size:10px;font-weight:600;letter-spacing:0.1em;text-transform:uppercase;color:var(--text-muted);font-family:var(--font-mono)">Developer</th>
            <th style="padding:6px 14px;text-align:center;font-size:10px;font-weight:600;letter-spacing:0.1em;text-transform:uppercase;color:var(--text-muted);font-family:var(--font-mono)">Resolved</th>
            <th style="padding:6px 14px;text-align:center;font-size:10px;font-weight:600;letter-spacing:0.1em;text-transform:uppercase;color:var(--text-muted);font-family:var(--font-mono)">Avg time</th>
            <th style="padding:6px 14px;text-align:center;font-size:10px;font-weight:600;letter-spacing:0.1em;text-transform:uppercase;color:var(--text-muted);font-family:var(--font-mono)">Reopened</th>
          </tr>
        </thead>
        <tbody>${perfRows}</tbody>
      </table>
    </div>` : ''}

  </div>`;

  // Load Chart.js if not already present, then draw
  const drawCharts = () => {
    const textCol = 'rgba(156,163,175,0.8)';
    const gridCol = 'rgba(255,255,255,0.06)';
    const baseFont = { family: 'inherit', size: 11 };
    const noLeg  = { legend: { display: false } };
    const axisBase = (min0=true) => ({
      x: { ticks:{ color:textCol, font:baseFont }, grid:{ color:gridCol }, border:{ display:false } },
      y: { ticks:{ color:textCol, font:baseFont, precision:0 }, grid:{ color:gridCol }, border:{ display:false }, ...(min0?{min:0}:{}) }
    });

    if (document.getElementById('ttC1')) {
      new Chart(document.getElementById('ttC1'), {
        type: 'bar',
        data: { labels: statusChartLabels, datasets:[{ data: statusChartValues, backgroundColor: statusChartColors, borderRadius:8, borderSkipped:false }]},
        options: { responsive:true, maintainAspectRatio:false,
          scales: { ...axisBase(), x: { ticks:{ color:textCol, font:{ family:'inherit', size:12 } }, grid:{ display:false }, border:{ display:false } } },
          plugins: { ...noLeg, tooltip:{ callbacks:{ label: c => ` ${c.label}: ${c.raw}` } } }
        }
      });
    }

    if (document.getElementById('ttC2')) {
      new Chart(document.getElementById('ttC2'), {
        type: 'doughnut',
        data: { labels: prioLabels, datasets:[{ data: prioValues, backgroundColor: prioColors, borderWidth:2, borderColor:'var(--bg-card)', hoverOffset:5 }]},
        options: { responsive:true, maintainAspectRatio:false, cutout:'70%',
          plugins: { ...noLeg, tooltip:{ callbacks:{ label: c => {
            const totalCount = Math.max(statusChartValues[0], 1);
            return ` ${c.label}: ${c.raw} (${Math.round(c.raw/totalCount*100)}%)`;
          } } } }
        }
      });
    }

    if (document.getElementById('ttC3')) {
      new Chart(document.getElementById('ttC3'), {
        type: 'doughnut',
        data: { labels: prioLabels, datasets:[{ data: prioInProgressValues, backgroundColor: prioColors, borderWidth:2, borderColor:'var(--bg-card)', hoverOffset:5 }]},
        options: { responsive:true, maintainAspectRatio:false, cutout:'70%',
          plugins: { ...noLeg, tooltip:{ callbacks:{ label: c => ` ${c.label}: ${c.raw} (${Math.round(c.raw/Math.max(s.inProgress||wipCount,1)*100)}%)` } } }
        }
      });
    }

    if (document.getElementById('ttC4') && devTotalData.labels.length) {
      new Chart(document.getElementById('ttC4'), {
        type: 'bar',
        data: devTotalData,
        options: { indexAxis:'y', responsive:true, maintainAspectRatio:false,
          scales: {
            x: { stacked:true, ticks:{ color:textCol, font:baseFont, precision:0 }, grid:{ color:gridCol }, border:{ display:false }, min:0 },
            y: { stacked:true, ticks:{ color:textCol, font:baseFont }, grid:{ display:false }, border:{ display:false } }
          },
          plugins: { tooltip:{ callbacks:{ label: c => ` ${c.dataset.label}: ${c.raw}` } } }
        }
      });
    }

    if (document.getElementById('ttC5') && devInProgressData.labels.length) {
      new Chart(document.getElementById('ttC5'), {
        type: 'bar',
        data: devInProgressData,
        options: { indexAxis:'y', responsive:true, maintainAspectRatio:false,
          scales: {
            x: { stacked:true, ticks:{ color:textCol, font:baseFont, precision:0 }, grid:{ color:gridCol }, border:{ display:false }, min:0 },
            y: { stacked:true, ticks:{ color:textCol, font:baseFont }, grid:{ display:false }, border:{ display:false } }
          },
          plugins: { tooltip:{ callbacks:{ label: c => ` ${c.dataset.label}: ${c.raw}` } } }
        }
      });
    }

    if (document.getElementById('ttC6')) {
      new Chart(document.getElementById('ttC6'), {
        type: 'bar',
        data: { labels: ageBuckets.map(b => b.label), datasets:[{ data: agingValues, backgroundColor:'rgba(99,110,114,0.8)', borderRadius:6, borderSkipped:false }]},
        options: { responsive:true, maintainAspectRatio:false,
          scales: { ...axisBase(), x: { ticks:{ color:textCol, font:{ family:'inherit', size:12 } }, grid:{ display:false }, border:{ display:false } } },
          plugins: { ...noLeg, tooltip:{ callbacks:{ label: c => ` ${c.label}: ${c.raw} tickets` } } }
        }
      });
    }

    if (document.getElementById('ttC7') && modLabels.length) {
      new Chart(document.getElementById('ttC7'), {
        type: 'bar',
        data: { labels: modLabels, datasets:[{ data: modValues, backgroundColor:'rgba(245,166,35,0.75)', borderRadius:5, borderSkipped:false }]},
        options: { responsive:true, maintainAspectRatio:false,
          scales: axisBase(),
          plugins: { ...noLeg }
        }
      });
    }
  };

  if (window.Chart) {
    drawCharts();
  } else {
    const s = document.createElement('script');
    s.src = 'https://cdnjs.cloudflare.com/ajax/libs/Chart.js/4.4.1/chart.umd.js';
    s.onload = drawCharts;
    document.head.appendChild(s);
  }

  this.checkSLAAlerts();

  // Inject SLA Forecast widget if enabled (async, non-blocking)
  if (this.featureFlags && this.featureFlags['SLA_PREDICTOR_ENABLED'] === 'true') {
    const container = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    if (container) {
      const forecastDiv = document.createElement('div');
      forecastDiv.style.marginTop = '16px';
      forecastDiv.style.maxWidth = '1200px';
      forecastDiv.style.margin = '16px auto 0';
      container.querySelector('.tt-dash-container')?.appendChild(forecastDiv);
      App.renderSLAForecastWidget(forecastDiv);
    }
  }
},


  // ============================================================
  // CREATE ISSUE
  // ============================================================

  async renderCreateIssue(params = {}) {
    const [devsRes, modulesRes] = await Promise.all([
      this.call('getDevelopers'),
      this.call('getModules')
    ]);
    
    const devOptions = (devsRes.success ? devsRes.developers : [])
      .map(d => `<option value="${d.email}">${d.name || d.email}</option>`).join('');
    
    const moduleOptions = (modulesRes.success ? modulesRes.modules : [])
      .map(m => `<option value="${m}">${m}</option>`).join('');
    
    const self_tpls = this.getIssueTemplates();
    const tplCards = self_tpls.map(function(t){ return '<div class="template-card" data-template-id="'+t.id+'" onclick="App.applyTemplate(this.dataset.templateId)"><div class="template-card-icon">'+t.icon+'</div><div class="template-card-name">'+t.name+'</div><div class="template-card-desc">'+t.desc+'</div></div>'; }).join('');
    document.getElementById('contentArea').innerHTML = `
      <div style="max-width:760px;margin:0 auto">
        <div class="card mb-16">
          <div class="card-title mb-12" style="font-size:12px;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.1em;color:var(--text-dim);font-family:var(--font-mono)">Choose Template</div>
          <div class="template-picker-grid">${tplCards}</div>
        </div>
        <div class="page-header">
          <div>
            <div class="page-header-title">Create New Issue</div>
            <div class="page-header-sub">Report a technical issue to the engineering team</div>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <div id="duplicateWarning" style="display:none" class="duplicate-alert">
          <div class="duplicate-alert-title">Warning: Possible Duplicate Issues Found</div>
          <div id="duplicateList"></div>
          <button class="btn-secondary btn-sm mt-8" onclick="document.getElementById('duplicateWarning').style.display='none'">Dismiss   Create Anyway</button>
        </div>
        
        <div class="card">
          <div class="form-grid">
            <div class="form-group">
              <label class="form-label">Issue Title *</label>
              <input type="text" id="issueTitle" class="form-input" placeholder="Brief descriptive title..."
                oninput="App.checkDuplicatesLive(this.value)">
            </div>

            <div class="form-group">
              <label class="form-label">Description *</label>
              <textarea id="issueDesc" class="form-textarea" style="min-height:120px"
                placeholder="Detailed description of the issue, steps to reproduce, expected vs actual behavior..."></textarea>
            </div>

            ${(this.featureFlags && this.featureFlags['AI_SMART_TRIAGE_ENABLED'] === 'true') ? `
            <div class="form-group">
              <button id="aiTriageBtn" class="btn-secondary btn-sm" type="button" onclick="App.requestAITriage()">✨ AI Suggest Priority &amp; Module</button>
              <div id="aiTriageChips"></div>
            </div>` : ''}

            <div class="form-grid form-grid-3">
              <div class="form-group">
                <label class="form-label">Priority *</label>
                <select id="issuePriority" class="form-select">
                  <option value="Low">Low</option>
                  <option value="Medium" selected>Medium</option>
                  <option value="High">High</option>
                  <option value="Critical">Critical</option>
                </select>
              </div>
              <div class="form-group">
                <label class="form-label">Module</label>
                <select id="issueModule" class="form-select">
                  <option value="">Select module...</option>
                  ${moduleOptions}
                </select>
              </div>
              <div class="form-group">
                <label class="form-label">Environment</label>
                <select id="issueEnv" class="form-select">
                  <option value="">Select env...</option>
                  <option value="Production">Production</option>
                  <option value="Staging">Staging</option>
                  <option value="Development">Development</option>
                  <option value="QA">QA</option>
                </select>
              </div>
            </div>
            
            <div class="form-grid form-grid-2">
              <div class="form-group">
                <label class="form-label">Assign Developer</label>
                <select id="issueAssignee" class="form-select">
                  <option value="">Unassigned (manual later)</option>
                  ${devOptions}
                </select>
              </div>
              <div class="form-group">
                <label class="form-label">Business Impact</label>
                <select id="issueImpact" class="form-select">
                  <option value="">Select impact...</option>
                  <option value="Revenue">Revenue Impact</option>
                  <option value="Customer">Customer Facing</option>
                  <option value="Internal">Internal Only</option>
                  <option value="Performance">Performance</option>
                  <option value="Security">Security</option>
                </select>
              </div>
            </div>
            
            <div class="form-group">
              <label class="form-label">Attachment</label>
              <div class="file-upload-area" id="uploadArea" onclick="document.getElementById('fileInput').click()">
                <div style="font-size:24px;margin-bottom:8px">Upload</div>
                <div>Click to upload or drag & drop</div>
                <div style="font-size:10px;margin-top:4px;color:var(--text-dim)">PNG, JPG, PDF, ZIP up to 10MB</div>
              </div>
              <input type="file" id="fileInput" style="display:none" onchange="App.handleFileUpload(this)">
              <div id="uploadStatus" style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-top:6px"></div>
              <input type="hidden" id="attachmentUrl" value="">
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <div style="display:flex;gap:10px;margin-top:16px;justify-content:flex-end">
          <button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.navigate('issue-list')">Cancel</button>
          <button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitCreateIssue()">
            Create Issue
          </button>
        </div>
      </div>`;
    
    // Setup drag and drop
    const uploadArea = document.getElementById('uploadArea');
    uploadArea.addEventListener('dragover', (e) => { e.preventDefault(); uploadArea.classList.add('drag-over'); });
    uploadArea.addEventListener('dragleave', () => uploadArea.classList.remove('drag-over'));
    uploadArea.addEventListener('drop', (e) => {
      e.preventDefault(); uploadArea.classList.remove('drag-over');
      if (e.dataTransfer.files[0]) this.handleFileUpload({ files: e.dataTransfer.files });
    });
  },

  async checkDuplicatesLive(title) {
    if (title.length < 8) return;
    clearTimeout(this._dupeTimeout);
    this._dupeTimeout = setTimeout(async () => {
      const result = await this.call('checkDuplicates', title);
      const warning = document.getElementById('duplicateWarning');
      const list = document.getElementById('duplicateList');
      if (result && result.length > 0) {
        list.innerHTML = result.map(d => 
          `<div class="duplicate-issue-link" onclick="App.navigate('issue-detail',{id:'${d.id}'})">${d.id}   ${d.title} <span style="color:var(--text-dim)">[${d.status}]</span></div>`
        ).join('');
        warning.style.display = 'block';
      } else {
        warning.style.display = 'none';
      }
    }, 600);
  },
  
  async handleFileUpload(input) {
    const file = input.files[0];
    if (!file) return;
    const status = document.getElementById('uploadStatus');
    status.textContent = 'Uploading...';
    
    const reader = new FileReader();
    reader.onload = async (e) => {
      const base64 = e.target.result.split(',')[1];
      const result = await this.call('uploadFile', file.name, file.type, base64);
      if (result.success) {
        document.getElementById('attachmentUrl').value = result.url;
        status.innerHTML = `Uploaded: <a href="${result.url}" target="_blank" style="color:var(--accent)">${file.name}</a>`;
      } else {
        status.textContent = 'Upload failed: ' + result.error;
      }
    };
    reader.readAsDataURL(file);
  },
  
  async submitCreateIssue() {
    const title = document.getElementById('issueTitle').value.trim();
    const desc = document.getElementById('issueDesc').value.trim();
    if (!title || !desc) { this.showToast('Title and Description are required', 'warning'); return; }
    
    const issueData = {
      title,
      description: desc,
      priority: document.getElementById('issuePriority').value,
      module: document.getElementById('issueModule').value,
      environment: document.getElementById('issueEnv').value,
      assignedTo: document.getElementById('issueAssignee').value,
      impact: document.getElementById('issueImpact').value,
      attachmentUrl: document.getElementById('attachmentUrl').value
    };
    
    this.showToast('Creating issue...', 'info');
    const result = await this.call('createIssue', issueData);
    
    if (result.success) {
      this.showToast(`Issue ${result.issueId} created successfully!`, 'success');
      this.navigate('issue-detail', { id: result.issueId });
    } else if (result.duplicates) {
      const warning = document.getElementById('duplicateWarning');
      const list = document.getElementById('duplicateList');
      list.innerHTML = result.duplicates.map(d => 
        `<div class="duplicate-issue-link" onclick="App.navigate('issue-detail',{id:'${d.id}'})">${d.id}   ${d.title}</div>`
      ).join('');
      warning.style.display = 'block';
      this.showToast('Possible duplicates detected. Dismiss to proceed.', 'warning');
    } else {
      this.showToast('Failed: ' + result.error, 'error');
    }
  },

  // ============================================================
  // ISSUE LIST
  // ============================================================

  async renderIssueList(myIssuesOnly = false) {
    const [issuesRes, devsRes, modulesRes] = await Promise.all([
      this.call('getIssues', myIssuesOnly ? { raisedBy: this.currentUser.email } : null),
      this.call('getDevelopers'),
      this.call('getModules')
    ]);

    if (issuesRes && !issuesRes.success) {
      const area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
      this.showPageError(area, issuesRes.error || 'Failed to load issues. Redeploy Code.gs and run initializeEverything().');
      return;
    }
    
    this.allIssues = issuesRes.success ? issuesRes.issues : [];
    this.users = devsRes.success ? devsRes.developers : [];
    this.modules = modulesRes.success ? modulesRes.modules : [];
    
    const devOptions = this.users.map(d => `<option value="${d.email}">${d.name || d.email}</option>`).join('');
    const modOptions = this.modules.map(m => `<option value="${m}">${m}</option>`).join('');
    
    document.getElementById('contentArea').innerHTML = `
      <div class="table-wrap">
        <div class="bulk-bar" id="bulkBar">
          <span class="bulk-count" id="bulkCount">0 selected</span>
          <button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.bulkUpdateStatus('Resolved')">Mark Resolved</button>
          <button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.bulkUpdateStatus('Closed')">Close</button>
          <button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.bulkChangePriority()">Priority</button>
          <button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.bulkAddTag()">Add tag</button>
          <button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.bulkAddComment()">Comment</button>
          <button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.bulkAssign()">Assign</button>
          <button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App._selectedIssues.clear();App._updateBulkBar()">Clear</button>
        </div>
        <div id="savedFiltersBar" style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:6px;flex-wrap:wrap;padding:8px 0;margin-bottom:4px;"></div>
        <div class="table-toolbar">
          <input class="search-input" type="text" placeholder="Search issues..." id="issueSearch" oninput="App.filterIssues()">
          <select class="filter-select" id="fStatus" onchange="App.filterIssues()">
            <option value="all">All Status</option>
            <option value="Open">Open</option>
            <option value="Acknowledged">Acknowledged</option>
            <option value="In Progress">In Progress</option>
            <option value="Testing">Testing</option>
            <option value="Blocked">Blocked</option>
            <option value="Need Info">Need Info</option>
            <option value="Resolved">Resolved</option>
            <option value="Closed">Closed</option>
            <option value="Reopened">Reopened</option>
          </select>
          <select class="filter-select" id="fPriority" onchange="App.filterIssues()">
            <option value="all">All Priority</option>
            <option value="Critical">Critical</option>
            <option value="High">High</option>
            <option value="Medium">Medium</option>
            <option value="Low">Low</option>
          </select>
          <select class="filter-select" id="fModule" onchange="App.filterIssues()">
            <option value="all">All Modules</option>
            ${modOptions}
          </select>
          <select class="filter-select" id="fDev" onchange="App.filterIssues()">
            <option value="all">All Developers</option>
            ${devOptions}
          </select>
          <input type="date" class="filter-select" id="fDateFrom" onchange="App.filterIssues()" placeholder="From">
          <input type="date" class="filter-select" id="fDateTo" onchange="App.filterIssues()" placeholder="To">
          <span id="issueCount" style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);font-family:var(--font-mono);margin-left:auto"></span>
        </div>
        <div id="issueTableBody"></div>
      </div>`;
    
    this.filterIssues();
    this.loadSavedFiltersBar();
  },

  async renderMyIssues() {
    document.getElementById('pageTitle').textContent = 'My Issues';
    return this.renderIssueList(true);
  },
  
  filterIssues() {
    const search = (document.getElementById('issueSearch')?.value || '').toLowerCase();
    const fStatus = document.getElementById('fStatus')?.value || 'all';
    const fPriority = document.getElementById('fPriority')?.value || 'all';
    const fModule = document.getElementById('fModule')?.value || 'all';
    const fDev = document.getElementById('fDev')?.value || 'all';
    const fFrom = document.getElementById('fDateFrom')?.value;
    const fTo = document.getElementById('fDateTo')?.value;
    
    let filtered = this.allIssues.filter(i => {
      if (fStatus !== 'all' && i.status !== fStatus) return false;
      if (fPriority !== 'all' && i.priority !== fPriority) return false;
      if (fModule !== 'all' && i.module !== fModule) return false;
      if (fDev !== 'all' && i.assignedTo !== fDev) return false;
      if (fFrom && new Date(i.createdDate) < new Date(fFrom)) return false;
      if (fTo && new Date(i.createdDate) > new Date(fTo + 'T23:59:59')) return false;
      if (search && !i.title.toLowerCase().includes(search) && !i.id.toLowerCase().includes(search) && !(i.module||'').toLowerCase().includes(search)) return false;
      return true;
    });
    
    document.getElementById('issueCount').textContent = `${filtered.length} issues`;
    
    const container = document.getElementById('issueTableBody');
    if (filtered.length === 0) {
      container.innerHTML = `<div class="empty-state"><div class="empty-state-icon">No Issues</div><p>No issues match your filters</p></div>`;
      return;
    }
    
    const rows = filtered.map(i => {
      const slaClass = i.slaBreached ? 'breach' : i.slaRisk ? 'risk' : 'ok';
      const slaText = i.slaBreached ? 'BREACHED' : `${i.slaHoursRemaining}h left`;
      return `
        <tr onclick="App.navigate('issue-detail', {id:'${i.id}'})" title="${i.title}">
          <td><input type="checkbox" class="issue-checkbox" data-issue-id="${i.id}" onchange="App.toggleIssueSelect('${i.id}', this)" onclick="event.stopPropagation()"></td>
          <td><span class="issue-id">${i.id}</span></td>
          <td style="max-width:280px"><div class="truncate">${i.title}</div></td>
          <td>${this.priorityBadge(i.priority)}</td>
          <td>
            <div class="status-picker-wrap">
              ${this.statusBadge(i.status)}
              <button class="status-change-btn" onclick="event.stopPropagation(); App.openStatusPicker('${i.id}', '${i.status}', this)">▾</button>
            </div>
          </td>
          <td style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted)">${i.module || '—'}</td>
          <td style="font-size:11px;font-family:var(--font-mono);color:var(--text-muted)">${this.shortEmail(i.assignedTo)}</td>
          <td><span class="sla-badge ${slaClass}">${slaText}</span></td>
          <td>${this.ageBadge(i.createdDate)}</td>
          <td onclick="event.stopPropagation()">${FollowUp.renderBtn(i.id)}</td>
        </tr>`;
    }).join('');
    
    container.innerHTML = `
      <div class="table-wrap">
        <table>
          <thead><tr>
            <th style="width:36px"><input type="checkbox" class="issue-checkbox" onchange="App.selectAllIssues(this)" title="Select all"></th>
            <th style="min-width:90px">ID</th>
            <th style="min-width:200px">Title</th>
            <th style="min-width:90px">Priority</th>
            <th style="min-width:120px">Status</th>
            <th style="min-width:80px">Module</th>
            <th style="min-width:100px">Assignee</th>
            <th style="min-width:100px">SLA</th>
            <th style="min-width:70px">Age ⏱</th>
            <th style="min-width:60px">🚩 FU</th>
          </tr></thead>
          <tbody>${rows}</tbody>
        </table>
      </div>`;
  },

  // ============================================================
  // ISSUE DETAIL
  // ============================================================
  
  async renderIssueDetail(issueId) {
    if (!issueId) { this.navigate('issue-list'); return; }
    
    const [issueRes, commentsRes, activityRes, devsRes] = await Promise.all([
      this.call('getIssueById', issueId),
      this.call('getComments', issueId),
      this.call('getActivityLog', issueId),
      this.call('getDevelopers')
    ]);
    
    if (!issueRes.success) { this.showToast('Issue not found', 'error'); this.navigate('issue-list'); return; }
    
    const i = issueRes.issue;
    document.getElementById('breadcrumb').textContent = `Issues / ${i.id}`;
    document.getElementById('pageTitle').textContent = i.id;
    
    const devOptions = (devsRes.success ? devsRes.developers : [])
      .map(d => `<option value="${d.email}" ${d.email===i.assignedTo?'selected':''}>${d.name||d.email}</option>`).join('');
    
    const slaClass = i.slaBreached ? 'breach' : i.slaRisk ? 'risk' : 'ok';
    const slaText = i.slaBreached 
      ? 'SLA BREACHED' 
      : `${i.slaHoursRemaining}h remaining (${i.slaHours}h SLA)`;
    
    const isAdmin = this.currentUser.role === 'Admin';
    const isDev = this.currentUser.role === 'Developer';
    const canChangeStatus = isAdmin || isDev || i.raisedBy === this.currentUser.email;

    const allStatuses = ['Open', 'WIP', 'Resolved', 'New Request', 'Release Required'];
    const statusOptions = allStatuses.map(s => `<option value="${s}" ${s===i.status?'selected':''}>${s}</option>`).join('');

    const comments = commentsRes.success ? commentsRes.comments : [];

    // Pre-compute flag-gated tab buttons (avoids nested-quote syntax errors inside template literals)
    const _ff = this.featureFlags || {};
    const timeTabBtn = _ff['TIME_TRACKING_ENABLED'] === 'true'
      ? `<button class="email-tab" id="tab-time" onclick="App.switchDetailTab('time','${i.id}')">Time</button>` : '';
    const linksTabBtn = _ff['ISSUE_LINKING_ENABLED'] === 'true'
      ? `<button class="email-tab" id="tab-links" onclick="App.switchDetailTab('links','${i.id}')">Links</button>` : '';
    const summariseBtn = (_ff['AI_COMMENT_SUMMARISER_ENABLED'] === 'true' && comments.length > 3)
      ? `<button class="btn-secondary" style="margin-bottom:10px;" onclick="App.summariseThread('${i.id}')">✨ Summarise Thread</button>` : '';
    const aiTriageCreateBtn = _ff['AI_SMART_TRIAGE_ENABLED'] === 'true'
      ? `<button id="aiTriageBtn" class="btn-secondary btn-sm" type="button" onclick="App.requestAITriage()">✨ AI Suggest</button>` : '';
    const commentHtml = comments.length > 0 ? comments.map(c => `
      <div class="comment-item">
        <div class="comment-avatar">${c.userEmail.charAt(0).toUpperCase()}</div>
        <div class="comment-body">
          <div class="comment-meta">
            <span class="comment-author">${c.userEmail}</span>
            <span>·</span>
            <span>${this.relativeTime(c.timestamp)}</span>
          </div>
          <div class="comment-text">${this.escapeHtml(c.comment)}</div>
        </div>
      </div>`).join('') : '<div class="text-muted" style="font-size:12px;padding:12px 0">No comments yet. Be the first to comment.</div>';
    
    const activities = activityRes.success ? activityRes.logs : [];
    const activityHtml = activities.slice(0,15).map(a => `
      <div class="activity-item">
        <div class="activity-dot"></div>
        <div class="activity-text"><strong>${a.action}</strong> by ${this.shortEmail(a.user)}</div>
        <div class="activity-time">${this.relativeTime(a.timestamp)}</div>
      </div>`).join('');
    
    const resTime = i.resolvedDate && i.createdDate 
      ? this.durationHours(i.createdDate, i.resolvedDate) + 'h to resolve'
      : ' ';

    document.getElementById('contentArea').innerHTML = `
      <div style="display:flex;gap:10px;margin-bottom:16px;align-items:center;flex-wrap:wrap">
        <button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.navigate('issue-list')">Back</button>
        ${canChangeStatus ? `<button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.showStatusModal('${i.id}', '${i.status}')">Update Status</button>` : ''}
        ${isAdmin ? `<button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.showAssignModal('${i.id}')">Reassign</button>` : ''}
        ${['Resolved','Closed'].includes(i.status) ? `<button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.showPostMortem('${i.id}')">Post-Mortem</button>` : ''}
        <button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.showDepsModal('${i.id}')">Dependencies</button>
        <button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.showLogTimeModal('${i.id}')">Log Time</button>
        <button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" id="watcherBtn" onclick="App.toggleWatcher('${i.id}')">Watch</button>
        <button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" style="background:var(--accent-dim);color:var(--accent);border-color:var(--border-accent)" onclick="AIAssist.open('${i.id}', '${this.escapeHtml(i.title)}')">AI</button>
        ${i.attachmentUrl ? `<a href="${i.attachmentUrl}" target="_blank" class="btn-secondary btn-sm">Attachment</a>` : ''}
        <button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.exportIssue('${i.id}')">Export</button>
        <button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.showPeerReviewModal('${i.id}')">Peer Review</button>
      </div>
      
      <div class="issue-detail-grid">
        <div class="issue-main">
          <div class="card">
            <div style="display:flex;align-items:flex-start;justify-content:space-between;gap:12px;margin-bottom:14px">
              <h2 class="issue-title-display">${this.escapeHtml(i.title)}</h2>
              <div style="flex-shrink:0">${this.priorityBadge(i.priority)}</div>
            </div>
            <div class="sla-countdown ${slaClass}">${slaText}</div>
            <hr class="divider">
            <div style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text-secondary);line-height:1.7;white-space:pre-wrap">${this.escapeHtml(i.description)}</div>
          </div>
          
          <!-- Tabbed: Comments | Email Thread | Activity | Time | Links -->
          <div class="card">
            <div class="email-tab-bar">
              <button class="email-tab active" id="tab-comments" onclick="App.switchDetailTab('comments','${i.id}')">Comments <span class="email-badge">${comments.length}</span></button>
              <button class="email-tab" id="tab-email" onclick="App.switchDetailTab('email','${i.id}')">Email Thread</button>
              <button class="email-tab" id="tab-activity" onclick="App.switchDetailTab('activity','${i.id}')">Activity</button>
              ${timeTabBtn}
              ${linksTabBtn}
            </div>

            <!-- Comments Tab -->
            <div id="tab-panel-comments">
              <div id="aiSummaryArea"></div>
              <div class="comment-thread mb-16">${commentHtml}</div>
              <div style="position:relative">
                <textarea id="commentInput" class="form-textarea" style="min-height:70px;width:100%;box-sizing:border-box" placeholder="Add a comment… type @ to mention someone"></textarea>
                <div id="mentionDropdown" style="display:none;position:absolute;bottom:100%;left:0;background:var(--bg-card);border:1px solid var(--border);border-radius:8px;z-index:200;min-width:220px;max-height:180px;overflow-y:auto;box-shadow:0 4px 16px rgba(0,0,0,0.3)"></div>
              </div>
              <div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:8px;justify-content:flex-end">
                ${summariseBtn}
                <button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitComment('${i.id}')">Post</button>
              </div>
            </div>

            <!-- Email Thread Tab -->
            <div id="tab-panel-email" style="display:none">
              <div id="emailThreadContainer">
                <div class="empty-state"><div class="empty-state-icon">Email</div><p>Click the Email Thread tab to load.</p></div>
              </div>
            </div>

            <!-- Activity Tab -->
            <div id="tab-panel-activity" style="display:none">
              <div class="activity-list">${activityHtml || '<p class="text-muted" style="font-size:12px">No activity yet</p>'}</div>
            </div>

            <!-- Time Tracking Tab -->
            <div id="tab-panel-time" style="display:none">
              <div id="timeLogsContainer"><p class="text-muted" style="font-size:12px">Loading...</p></div>
              <div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:12px;align-items:flex-end">
                <div style="flex:0 0 80px">
                  <label class="form-label" style="font-size:11px">Hours</label>
                  <input type="number" id="logHoursInput" class="form-input" min="0.5" step="0.5" value="1" style="width:100%">
                </div>
                <div style="flex:1">
                  <label class="form-label" style="font-size:11px">Note</label>
                  <input type="text" id="logNoteInput" class="form-input" placeholder="What did you work on?">
                </div>
                <button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitTimeLog('${i.id}')">Log</button>
              </div>
            </div>

            <!-- Issue Links Tab -->
            <div id="tab-panel-links" style="display:none">
              <div id="issueLinksContainer"><p class="text-muted" style="font-size:12px">Loading...</p></div>
              <div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:12px;align-items:flex-end">
                <select id="linkTypeSelect" class="form-select" style="flex:0 0 130px">
                  <option value="blocks">Blocks</option>
                  <option value="related">Related to</option>
                  <option value="duplicates">Duplicates</option>
                </select>
                <input type="text" id="linkTargetInput" class="form-input" placeholder="Issue ID (e.g. ISS-001)" style="flex:1">
                <button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitIssueLink('${i.id}')">Link</button>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="issue-sidebar">
          <div class="card">
            <div class="card-title mb-16">Issue Details</div>
            <div class="meta-list">
              <div class="meta-item">
                <div class="meta-key">Status</div>
                <div class="meta-value">${this.statusBadge(i.status)}</div>
              </div>
              <div class="meta-item">
                <div class="meta-key">Priority</div>
                <div class="meta-value">${this.priorityBadge(i.priority)}</div>
              </div>
              <div class="meta-item">
                <div class="meta-key">Module</div>
                <div class="meta-value">${i.module || ' '}</div>
              </div>
              <div class="meta-item">
                <div class="meta-key">Env</div>
                <div class="meta-value">${i.environment || ' '}</div>
              </div>
              <div class="meta-item">
                <div class="meta-key">Impact</div>
                <div class="meta-value">${i.impact || ' '}</div>
              </div>
              <div class="meta-item">
                <div class="meta-key">Raised By</div>
                <div class="meta-value mono" style="font-size:12px">${i.raisedBy}</div>
              </div>
              <div class="meta-item">
                <div class="meta-key">Assignee</div>
                <div class="meta-value mono" style="font-size:12px">${i.assignedTo || ' '}</div>
              </div>
              <div class="meta-item">
                <div class="meta-key">Created</div>
                <div class="meta-value mono" style="font-size:11px">${this.formatDate(i.createdDate)}</div>
              </div>
              <div class="meta-item">
                <div class="meta-key">Started</div>
                <div class="meta-value mono" style="font-size:11px">${this.formatDate(i.startedDate)}</div>
              </div>
              <div class="meta-item">
                <div class="meta-key">Resolved</div>
                <div class="meta-value mono" style="font-size:11px">${this.formatDate(i.resolvedDate)}</div>
              </div>
              <div class="meta-item">
                <div class="meta-key">Res. Time</div>
                <div class="meta-value mono" style="font-size:12px;color:var(--accent)">${resTime}</div>
              </div>
              <div class="meta-item">
                <div class="meta-key">⏱ Age</div>
                <div class="meta-value">${this.ageBadge(i.createdDate)}</div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
          <!-- Follow-up Tracker panel in issue detail -->
          <div class="card" style="margin-top:14px">
            <div class="card-header" style="margin-bottom:10px">
              <div class="card-title" style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px">
                🚩 Follow-ups
                <span class="fu-count-label" id="fuDetailCount" style="font-size:18px;font-weight:900;letter-spacing:-0.5px;color:var(--accent)">${FollowUp.count(i.id)}</span>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div class="fu-inline-panel">
              <button class="fu-inline-btn" onclick="FollowUp.openModal('${i.id}')">
                + Log / View Follow-ups
              </button>
              <div id="fuDetailHistory" style="max-height:200px;overflow-y:auto;display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:6px;margin-top:4px">
                ${FollowUp._historyHtml(FollowUp.get(i.id))}
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>`;

    // Initialize @mention autocomplete for the comments tab
    setTimeout(() => {
      if (this.featureFlags && this.featureFlags['COMMENT_MENTIONS_ENABLED'] === 'true') {
        App.initMentionAutocomplete(issueId);
      }
    }, 100);
  },

  async submitComment(issueId) {
    const input = document.getElementById('commentInput');
    const text = input.value.trim();
    if (!text) return;

    // Use mentions-aware backend if feature is enabled
    const fnName = (this.featureFlags && this.featureFlags['COMMENT_MENTIONS_ENABLED'] === 'true')
      ? 'addCommentWithMentions' : 'addComment';

    const result = await this.call(fnName, issueId, text);
    if (result.success) {
      this.showToast('Comment added', 'success');
      input.value = '';
      document.getElementById('mentionDropdown') && (document.getElementById('mentionDropdown').style.display = 'none');
      this.renderIssueDetail(issueId);
    } else {
      this.showToast('Failed: ' + result.error, 'error');
    }
  },
  
  showStatusModal(issueId, currentStatus) {
    const allStatuses = ['Open', 'WIP', 'Resolved', 'New Request', 'Release Required'];
    const options = allStatuses.map(s => `<option value="${s}" ${s===currentStatus?'selected':''}>${s}</option>`).join('');
    
    const html = `
      <div class="modal-overlay" onclick="if(event.target===this)this.remove()">
        <div class="modal">
          <div class="modal-header">
            <span class="modal-title">Update Issue Status</span>
            <button class="modal-close" onclick="this.closest('.modal-overlay').remove()">×</button>
          </div>
          <div class="modal-body">
            <div class="form-group">
              <label class="form-label">New Status</label>
              <select id="modalStatus" class="form-select">${options}</select>
            </div>
            <div class="form-group mt-16">
              <label class="form-label">Comment (optional)</label>
              <textarea id="modalComment" class="form-textarea" style="min-height:80px" placeholder="Add context about this status change..."></textarea>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div class="modal-footer">
            <button class="btn-secondary" onclick="this.closest('.modal-overlay').remove()">Cancel</button>
            <button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitStatusUpdate('${issueId}')">Update Status</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
    document.body.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', html);
  },
  
  async submitStatusUpdate(issueId) {
    const status = document.getElementById('modalStatus').value;
    const comment = document.getElementById('modalComment').value;
    const result = await this.call('updateIssueStatus', issueId, status, comment);
    if (result.success) {
      document.querySelector('.modal-overlay')?.remove();
      this.showToast(`Status updated to ${status}`, 'success');
      this.renderIssueDetail(issueId);
    } else {
      this.showToast('Failed: ' + result.error, 'error');
    }
  },
  
  showAssignModal(issueId) {
    this.call('getDevelopers').then(devsRes => {
      const options = (devsRes.success ? devsRes.developers : [])
        .map(d => `<option value="${d.email}">${d.name||d.email}</option>`).join('');
      
      const html = `
        <div class="modal-overlay" onclick="if(event.target===this)this.remove()">
          <div class="modal">
            <div class="modal-header">
              <span class="modal-title">Assign Developer</span>
              <button class="modal-close" onclick="this.closest('.modal-overlay').remove()">×</button>
            </div>
            <div class="modal-body">
              <div class="form-group">
                <label class="form-label">Select Developer</label>
                <select id="modalAssignee" class="form-select">
                  <option value="">Unassigned</option>${options}
                </select>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div class="modal-footer">
              <button class="btn-secondary" onclick="this.closest('.modal-overlay').remove()">Cancel</button>
              <button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitAssign('${issueId}')">Assign</button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>`;
      document.body.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', html);
    });
  },
  
  async submitAssign(issueId) {
    const dev = document.getElementById('modalAssignee').value;
    const result = await this.call('assignIssue', issueId, dev);
    if (result.success) {
      document.querySelector('.modal-overlay')?.remove();
      this.showToast('Issue assigned successfully', 'success');
      this.renderIssueDetail(issueId);
    } else {
      this.showToast('Failed: ' + result.error, 'error');
    }
  },

  // ============================================================
  // ADMIN PANEL
  // ============================================================

  async renderAdminPanel() {
    if (this.currentUser.role !== 'Admin') { this.showToast('Access denied', 'error'); this.navigate('dashboard'); return; }
    
    const statsRes = await this.call('getDashboardStats');
    const s = statsRes.success ? statsRes.stats : {};
    
    document.getElementById('contentArea').innerHTML = `
      <div class="page-header">
        <div>
          <div class="page-header-title">Admin Control Panel</div>
          <div class="page-header-sub">System overview and quick actions</div>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <div class="stats-grid">
        <div class="stat-card" style="--stat-color:var(--status-open)">
          <div class="stat-label">Total Issues</div>
          <div class="stat-value">${s.total||0}</div>
        </div>
        <div class="stat-card" style="--stat-color:var(--critical)">
          <div class="stat-label">Critical Open</div>
          <div class="stat-value">${s.critical||0}</div>
        </div>
        <div class="stat-card" style="--stat-color:var(--critical)">
          <div class="stat-label">SLA Breaches</div>
          <div class="stat-value">${s.slaBreached||0}</div>
        </div>
        <div class="stat-card" style="--stat-color:var(--low)">
          <div class="stat-label">Resolved</div>
          <div class="stat-value">${(s.resolved||0)+(s.closed||0)}</div>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <div class="grid-3">
        <div class="card" style="cursor:pointer" onclick="App.navigate('user-management')">
          <div style="font-size:32px;margin-bottom:12px">●</div>
          <div class="card-title">User Management</div>
          <div class="card-subtitle">Add, edit, deactivate users</div>
        </div>
        <div class="card" style="cursor:pointer" onclick="App.navigate('sla-settings')">
          <div style="font-size:32px;margin-bottom:12px">⏱</div>
          <div class="card-title">SLA Configuration</div>
          <div class="card-subtitle">Set SLA hours per priority</div>
        </div>
        <div class="card" style="cursor:pointer" onclick="App.navigate('system-settings')">
          <div style="font-size:32px;margin-bottom:12px">✹</div>
          <div class="card-title">System Settings</div>
          <div class="card-subtitle">Feature toggles & configuration</div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
  },

  // ============================================================
  // USER MANAGEMENT
  // ============================================================

  async renderUserManagement() {
    if (this.currentUser.role !== 'Admin') { this.showToast('Access denied', 'error'); return; }
    
    const result = await this.call('getUsers', false);
    const users = result.success ? result.users : [];
    
    const rows = users.map(u => `
      <tr>
        <td class="mono" style="font-size:11px">${u.email}</td>
        <td>${u.name}</td>
        <td>${u.team}</td>
        <td>${this.roleBadge(u.role)}</td>
        <td style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted)">${u.skill||' '}</td>
        <td style="font-size:12px;text-align:center">${u.maxTickets||10}</td>
        <td><span style="color:${u.active==='TRUE'||u.active===true?'var(--low)':'var(--critical)'};font-size:12px">${u.active==='TRUE'||u.active===true?'Active':'Inactive'}</span></td>
        <td>
          <button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.showEditUserModal(${JSON.stringify(u).replace(/"/g,'&quot;')})">Edit</button>
          <button class="btn-danger btn-sm" onclick="App.toggleUserActive('${u.id}', ${u.active==='TRUE'||u.active===true})">${u.active==='TRUE'||u.active===true?'Deactivate':'Activate'}</button>
        </td>
      </tr>`).join('');
    
    document.getElementById('contentArea').innerHTML = `
      <div class="page-header">
        <div>
          <div class="page-header-title">User Management</div>
          <div class="page-header-sub">${users.length} users registered</div>
        </div>
        <button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.showAddUserModal()">+ Add User</button>
      </div>
      
      <div class="table-wrap">
        <table>
          <thead><tr>
            <th>Email</th><th>Name</th><th>Team</th><th>Role</th>
            <th>Skills</th><th>Max Tickets</th><th>Status</th><th>Actions</th>
          </tr></thead>
          <tbody>${rows || '<tr><td colspan="8" style="text-align:center;padding:20px;color:var(--text-muted)">No users found</td></tr>'}</tbody>
        </table>
      </div>`;
  },
  
  showAddUserModal() {
    const html = `
      <div class="modal-overlay" onclick="if(event.target===this)this.remove()">
