                <label class="form-label">Slack User ID</label>
                <input id="uSlack" class="form-input" placeholder="U01ABCDEF">
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div class="modal-footer">
            <button class="btn-secondary" onclick="this.closest('.modal-overlay').remove()">Cancel</button>
            <button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitAddUser()">Add User</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
    document.body.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', html);
  },
  
  async submitAddUser() {
    const userData = {
      name: document.getElementById('uName').value.trim(),
      email: document.getElementById('uEmail').value.trim(),
      role: document.getElementById('uRole').value,
      team: document.getElementById('uTeam').value.trim(),
      skill: document.getElementById('uSkill').value.trim(),
      maxTickets: document.getElementById('uMax').value,
      slackId: document.getElementById('uSlack').value.trim()
    };
    if (!userData.name || !userData.email) { this.showToast('Name and email required', 'warning'); return; }
    
    const result = await this.call('addUser', userData);
    if (result.success) {
      document.querySelector('.modal-overlay')?.remove();
      this.showToast('User added successfully', 'success');
      this.renderUserManagement();
    } else {
      this.showToast('Failed: ' + result.error, 'error');
    }
  },
  
  showEditUserModal(user) {
    const html = `
      <div class="modal-overlay" onclick="if(event.target===this)this.remove()">
        <div class="modal">
          <div class="modal-header">
            <span class="modal-title">Edit User: ${user.name}</span>
            <button class="modal-close" onclick="this.closest('.modal-overlay').remove()">×</button>
          </div>
          <div class="modal-body">
            <div class="form-grid">
              <div class="form-group">
                <label class="form-label">Full Name</label>
                <input id="euName" class="form-input" value="${user.name||''}">
              </div>
              <div class="form-grid form-grid-2">
                <div class="form-group">
                  <label class="form-label">Role</label>
                  <select id="euRole" class="form-select">
                    ${['Admin','Developer','CS','Sales','QA','Product'].map(r => `<option ${r===user.role?'selected':''}>${r}</option>`).join('')}
                  </select>
                </div>
                <div class="form-group">
                  <label class="form-label">Team</label>
                  <input id="euTeam" class="form-input" value="${user.team||''}">
                </div>
              </div>
              <div class="form-grid form-grid-2">
                <div class="form-group">
                  <label class="form-label">Skill</label>
                  <input id="euSkill" class="form-input" value="${user.skill||''}">
                </div>
                <div class="form-group">
                  <label class="form-label">Max Tickets</label>
                  <input id="euMax" type="number" class="form-input" value="${user.maxTickets||10}">
                </div>
              </div>
            </div>
          </div>
          <div class="modal-footer">
            <button class="btn-secondary" onclick="this.closest('.modal-overlay').remove()">Cancel</button>
            <button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitEditUser('${user.id}')">Save Changes</button>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
    document.body.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', html);
  },
  
  async submitEditUser(userId) {
    const userData = {
      name: document.getElementById('euName').value.trim(),
      role: document.getElementById('euRole').value,
      team: document.getElementById('euTeam').value.trim(),
      skill: document.getElementById('euSkill').value.trim(),
      maxTickets: document.getElementById('euMax').value
    };
    const result = await this.call('updateUser', userId, userData);
    if (result.success) {
      document.querySelector('.modal-overlay')?.remove();
      this.showToast('User updated', 'success');
      this.renderUserManagement();
    } else {
      this.showToast('Failed: ' + result.error, 'error');
    }
  },
  
  async toggleUserActive(userId, currentlyActive) {
    if (!confirm(`${currentlyActive ? 'Deactivate' : 'Activate'} this user?`)) return;
    const result = await this.call('updateUser', userId, { active: !currentlyActive });
    if (result.success) {
      this.showToast('User status updated', 'success');
      this.renderUserManagement();
    } else {
      this.showToast('Failed: ' + result.error, 'error');
    }
  },

  // ============================================================
  // SLA SETTINGS
  // ============================================================

  async renderSLASettings() {
    if (this.currentUser.role !== 'Admin') { this.showToast('Access denied', 'error'); return; }
    
    const result = await this.call('getSLAConfig');
    const config = result.success ? result.config : { Critical:2, High:6, Medium:24, Low:48 };
    
    const priorities = ['Critical', 'High', 'Medium', 'Low'];
    const rows = priorities.map(p => `
      <div class="meta-item" style="align-items:center">
        <div class="meta-key">${this.priorityBadge(p)}</div>
        <div class="meta-value">
          <div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px">
            <input type="number" id="sla_${p}" class="form-input" style="width:100px" value="${config[p]||24}">
            <span class="mono" style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted)">hours</span>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>`).join('');
    
    document.getElementById('contentArea').innerHTML = `
      <div style="max-width:540px">
        <div class="page-header">
          <div>
            <div class="page-header-title">SLA Configuration</div>
            <div class="page-header-sub">Set resolution time targets per priority level</div>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="card">
          <div class="meta-list">${rows}</div>
          <hr class="divider">
          <div style="display:flex;justify-content:flex-end">
            <button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.saveSLAConfig()">Save SLA Settings</button>
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <div class="card mt-16">
          <div class="card-title mb-8">How SLA Works</div>
          <div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);line-height:1.7">
            <p>SLA countdown starts when an issue is created.</p>
            <p>If not resolved within the configured hours, the issue is flagged as SLA Breached.</p>
            <p>Email and Slack alerts are sent automatically when SLA is breached (if enabled).</p>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
  },
  
  async saveSLAConfig() {
    const priorities = ['Critical', 'High', 'Medium', 'Low'];
    this.showToast('Saving SLA config...', 'info');
    
    for (const p of priorities) {
      const hours = parseInt(document.getElementById('sla_' + p).value);
      await this.call('updateSLAConfig', p, hours);
    }
    this.showToast('SLA configuration saved!', 'success');
  },

  // ============================================================
  // SYSTEM SETTINGS
  // ============================================================

  async renderSystemSettings() {
    if (this.currentUser.role !== 'Admin') { this.showToast('Access denied', 'error'); return; }
    
    const [settingsRes, modulesRes] = await Promise.all([
      this.call('getSettings'),
      this.call('getModules')
    ]);
    
    const settings = settingsRes.success ? settingsRes.settings : {};
    const modules = modulesRes.success ? modulesRes.modules : [];
    
    const toggles = [
      { key: 'AUTO_ASSIGN_ENABLED', name: 'Auto Ticket Assignment', desc: 'Automatically assign tickets to developers based on skill and workload. Manual assignment remains available.' },
      { key: 'SLA_RISK_ALERTS_ENABLED', name: 'SLA Risk Alerts', desc: 'Send email and Slack alerts when tickets are approaching or have breached SLA deadlines.' },
      { key: 'DUPLICATE_DETECTION_ENABLED', name: 'Duplicate Issue Detection', desc: 'Check for similar open issues when creating a new issue and warn the user.' },
      { key: 'BUG_HEATMAP_ENABLED', name: 'Bug Heatmap Analytics', desc: 'Show a heatmap chart on the dashboard displaying which modules have the most issues.' },
      { key: 'DEV_PERFORMANCE_ANALYTICS_ENABLED', name: 'Developer Performance Analytics', desc: 'Show performance metrics for developers including resolution times and reopened rates.' },
      { key: 'DAILY_ENGINEERING_REPORT_ENABLED', name: 'Daily Engineering Digest', desc: 'Send a daily summary email to admins at 8am with key issue metrics.' }
    ];
    
    const toggleHtml = toggles.map(t => `
      <div class="toggle-row">
        <div class="toggle-info">
          <div class="toggle-name">${t.name}</div>
          <div class="toggle-desc">${t.desc}</div>
        </div>
        <label class="toggle-switch">
          <input type="checkbox" id="toggle_${t.key}" ${settings[t.key]==='true'?'checked':''}
            onchange="App.saveSetting('${t.key}', this.checked ? 'true' : 'false')">
          <span class="toggle-slider"></span>
        </label>
      </div>`).join('');
    
    document.getElementById('contentArea').innerHTML = `
      <div class="page-header">
        <div>
          <div class="page-header-title">System Settings</div>
          <div class="page-header-sub">Feature toggles and system configuration</div>
        </div>
      </div>
      
      <div class="grid-2">
        <div>
          <div class="card mb-16">
            <div class="card-title mb-16">Feature Toggles</div>
            ${toggleHtml}
          </div>
        </div>
        
        <div>
          <div class="card mb-16">
            <div class="card-title mb-16">Slack Integration</div>
            <div class="form-group">
              <label class="form-label">Slack Webhook URL</label>
              <input id="slackWebhook" class="form-input" type="url" 
                placeholder="https://hooks.slack.com/services/..." 
                value="${settings.SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL||''}">
            </div>
            <div style="margin-top:12px;text-align:right">
              <button class="btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="App.saveSlackWebhook()">Save Webhook</button>
            </div>
          </div>

          <div class="card mb-16">
            <div class="card-header">
              <span class="card-title">Gemini AI</span>
              <span class="card-subtitle mono" style="color:var(--low);font-size:11px">' + (AI.getGeminiKey() ? '● Active' : '○ Not configured') + '</span>
            </div>
            <div class="form-group">
              <label class="form-label">Gemini API Key</label>
              <input id="geminiKeySettings" class="form-input" type="password"
                placeholder="AIzaSy..."
                value="' + (AI.getGeminiKey() ? '••••••••••••••' : '') + '">
              <div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-top:5px">
                Get a free key at <a href="https://aistudio.google.com" target="_blank" style="color:var(--accent)">aistudio.google.com</a> → API Keys. Stored locally in your browser only.
              </div>
            </div>
            <div style="margin-top:12px;display:flex;gap:8px;justify-content:flex-end">
              <button class="btn-danger btn-sm" onclick="App.clearGeminiKey()">Clear Key</button>
              <button class="btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="App.saveGeminiKeyFromSettings()">Save Key</button>
            </div>
          </div>
          
          <div class="card">
            <div class="card-title mb-16">Module Configuration</div>
            <div class="form-group">
              <label class="form-label">Modules (comma-separated)</label>
              <textarea id="modulesList" class="form-textarea" style="min-height:100px">${modules.join(', ')}</textarea>
            </div>
            <div style="margin-top:12px;text-align:right">
              <button class="btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="App.saveModules()">Save Modules</button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      </div>`;
  },
  
  async saveSetting(key, value) {
    const result = await this.call('updateSetting', key, value);
    if (result.success) {
      this.showToast(`${key} ${value === 'true' ? 'enabled' : 'disabled'}`, 'success');
    } else {
      this.showToast('Failed to save setting', 'error');
    }
  },
  
  async saveSlackWebhook() {
    const url = document.getElementById('slackWebhook').value.trim();
    const result = await this.call('updateSetting', 'SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL', url);
    if (result.success) this.showToast('Slack webhook saved', 'success');
    else this.showToast('Failed to save webhook', 'error');
  },
  

  // ============================================================
  // ISSUE DETAIL EMAIL THREAD TAB
  // ============================================================

  renderEmailThread: async function(issueId) {
    var self = this;
    var container = document.getElementById('emailThreadContainer');
    if (!container) return;
    container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><div class="empty-state-icon">&#x231B;</div><p>Loading email thread...</p></div>';

    var timelineResult = await self.callAsync('getEmailTimeline', issueId);
    var summaryResult  = await self.callAsync('getEmailSummary', issueId);
    var partResult     = await self.callAsync('getEmailParticipants', issueId);

    var messages      = (timelineResult && timelineResult.success) ? timelineResult.messages : [];
    var extraction    = (summaryResult && summaryResult.success)   ? summaryResult.extraction : null;
    var participants  = (partResult && partResult.success)         ? partResult.participants : [];

    var html = '';

    // AI Summary Card
    if (extraction) {
      var sentClass = extraction.sentiment || 'Neutral';
      html += '<div class="ai-email-summary">';
      html += '<div class="ai-email-summary-header">';
      html += '<div class="ai-email-summary-title">&#x2736; AI Email Intelligence</div>';
      html += '<span class="ai-sentiment ' + sentClass + '">' + sentClass + '</span>';
      html += '</div>';
      if (extraction.summary) {
        html += '<p style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text-secondary);line-height:1.6;margin:0 0 12px;">' + self._esc(extraction.summary) + '</p>';
      }

      html += '<div class="ai-extraction-grid">';

      if (extraction.decisions && extraction.decisions.length) {
        html += '<div class="ai-extraction-block">';
        html += '<div class="ai-extraction-label">&#x2714; Decisions</div>';
        extraction.decisions.forEach(function(d) {
          html += '<div class="ai-extraction-item"><div class="ai-extraction-dot" style="background:var(--low)"></div>' + App._esc(d) + '</div>';
        });
        html += '</div>';
      }

      if (extraction.actionItems && extraction.actionItems.length) {
        html += '<div class="ai-extraction-block">';
        html += '<div class="ai-extraction-label">&#x25B6; Action Items</div>';
        extraction.actionItems.forEach(function(a) {
          var text = (a.person ? a.person + ': ' : '') + (a.action || a);
          html += '<div class="ai-extraction-item"><div class="ai-extraction-dot" style="background:var(--accent)"></div>' + App._esc(text) + '</div>';
        });
        html += '</div>';
      }

      if (extraction.blockers && extraction.blockers.length) {
        html += '<div class="ai-extraction-block">';
        html += '<div class="ai-extraction-label">Blockers</div>';
        extraction.blockers.forEach(function(b) {
          html += '<div class="ai-extraction-item"><div class="ai-extraction-dot" style="background:var(--critical)"></div>' + App._esc(b) + '</div>';
        });
        html += '</div>';
      }

      if (extraction.rootCause) {
        html += '<div class="ai-extraction-block">';
        html += '<div class="ai-extraction-label">&#x1F50D; Root Cause</div>';
        html += '<div class="ai-extraction-item"><div class="ai-extraction-dot"></div>' + App._esc(extraction.rootCause) + '</div>';
        html += '</div>';
      }

      html += '</div>'; // grid

      if (extraction.suggestedStatus) {
        html += '<div class="ai-status-suggestion">';
        html += '<span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--accent)">&#x2736;</span>';
        html += '<span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-primary)">AI suggests status: <strong>' + extraction.suggestedStatus + '</strong></span>';
        html += '<button class="btn-primary btn-sm" style="margin-left:auto" onclick="App.applyAISuggestedStatus(\'' + issueId + '\',\'' + extraction.suggestedStatus + '\')">Apply</button>';
        html += '</div>';
      }

      html += '</div>'; // ai-email-summary
    }

    // Participants
    if (participants.length) {
      html += '<div class="email-participants">';
      html += '<span style="font-size:10px;font-family:var(--font-mono);color:var(--text-dim);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.08em;margin-right:8px;">Participants</span>';
      participants.forEach(function(p) {
        html += '<div class="participant-chip"><div class="participant-chip-dot"></div>' + App._esc(p) + '</div>';
      });
      html += '</div>';
    }

    // Messages
    if (messages.length === 0) {
      html += '<div class="empty-state"><div class="empty-state-icon">Email</div><p>No email replies captured yet.</p><p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim)">Replies to the issue notification email will appear here automatically.</p></div>';
    } else {
      messages.forEach(function(msg) {
        var initial = (msg.senderName || msg.sender || '?')[0].toUpperCase();
        var timeStr = msg.timestamp ? new Date(msg.timestamp).toLocaleString() : '';
        html += '<div class="email-message">';
        html += '<div class="email-message-header">';
        html += '<div class="email-avatar">' + initial + '</div>';
        html += '<div><div class="email-sender">' + App._esc(msg.senderName || msg.sender) + '</div>';
        html += '<div class="email-sender-addr">' + App._esc(msg.sender) + '</div></div>';
        html += '<div class="email-timestamp">' + timeStr + '</div>';
        html += '</div>';
        if (msg.aiTags && msg.aiTags.length) {
          msg.aiTags.forEach(function(tag) { html += '<span class="email-tag">' + App._esc(tag) + '</span>'; });
          html += '<br>';
        }
        html += '<div class="email-body">' + App._esc(msg.body || '') + '</div>';
        html += '</div>';
      });
    }

    container.innerHTML = html;
  },

  applyAISuggestedStatus: async function(issueId, status) {
    var self = this;
    var r = await self.callAsync('updateIssueStatus', issueId, status, 'Status updated based on AI email thread analysis.');
    if (r && r.success) {
      self.showToast('Status updated to ' + status, 'success');
      self.navigate('issue-detail', { id: issueId });
    } else {
      self.showToast('Failed: ' + (r ? r.error : 'unknown'), 'error');
    }
  },

  renderAIIntelligence: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('AI Intelligence', 'Admin / AI Intelligence');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><div class="empty-state-icon">&#x2736;</div><p>Loading AI Intelligence...</p></div>';

    var historyResult, rulesResult, statusResult, settingsResult;
    try {
      historyResult  = await self.callAsync('getAIQueryHistory', 50);
      rulesResult    = await self.callAsync('getInboundRules');
      statusResult   = await self.callAsync('getGeminiStatus');
      settingsResult = await self.callAsync('getSettings');
    } catch(e) {
      self.showPageError(area, 'AI Intelligence failed: ' + e.message + '. Redeploy Code.gs and run initializeAll().');
      return;
    }
    if (historyResult && !historyResult.success && historyResult.error) {
      self.showPageError(area, historyResult.error + '   Redeploy Code.gs and run initializeAll().');
      return;
    }

    var queries = (historyResult && historyResult.success) ? historyResult.queries : [];
    var rules   = (rulesResult && rulesResult.success) ? rulesResult.rules : [];
    var geminiOk = statusResult && statusResult.configured;
    var settings = (settingsResult && settingsResult.success) ? settingsResult.settings : {};

    var html = '<div style="max-width:900px">';

    // Gemini Status + Key
    html += '<div class="ai-admin-section">';
    html += '<div class="ai-admin-section-title">&#x2736; Gemini AI Backend</div>';
    html += '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;margin-bottom:14px;">';
    html += '<div class="status-dot ' + (geminiOk ? 'active' : '') + '"></div>';
    html += '<span style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text-secondary);">' + (geminiOk ? 'API key configured   AI running on backend' : 'No API key   set below to enable backend AI') + '</span>';
    html += '</div>';
    html += '<div class="form-grid-2">';
    html += '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Gemini API Key</label>';
    html += '<input id="geminiBackendKey" class="form-input" type="password" placeholder="AIzaSy...">';
    html += '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);margin-top:4px;">Stored securely in Script Properties   never exposed to browser.</div></div>';
    html += '<div class="form-group" style="display:flex;align-items:flex-end;padding-bottom:2px;">';
    html += '<button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.saveGeminiBackendKey()">Save Key</button></div>';
    html += '</div></div>';

    // Email Watch Settings
    html += '<div class="ai-admin-section">';
    html += '<div class="ai-admin-section-title">Email Thread Watching</div>';
    html += '<div class="form-grid-2" style="margin-bottom:14px;">';
    html += '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Thread Watch (outbound replies)</label>';
    html += '<select id="emailWatchToggle" class="form-select" onchange="App.saveEmailSetting(\'EMAIL_WATCH_ENABLED\',this.value)">';
    html += '<option value="true"' + (settings.EMAIL_WATCH_ENABLED === 'true' ? ' selected' : '') + '>Enabled</option>';
    html += '<option value="false"' + (settings.EMAIL_WATCH_ENABLED !== 'true' ? ' selected' : '') + '>Disabled</option>';
    html += '</select></div>';
    html += '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Inbound Email Triage</label>';
    html += '<select id="triageToggle" class="form-select" onchange="App.saveEmailSetting(\'EMAIL_TRIAGE_ENABLED\',this.value)">';
    html += '<option value="true"' + (settings.EMAIL_TRIAGE_ENABLED === 'true' ? ' selected' : '') + '>Enabled</option>';
    html += '<option value="false"' + (settings.EMAIL_TRIAGE_ENABLED !== 'true' ? ' selected' : '') + '>Disabled</option>';
    html += '</select></div>';
    html += '</div>';
    html += '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Gmail Label to Watch (inbound triage)</label>';
    html += '<input id="triageLabel" class="form-input" value="' + (settings.EMAIL_TRIAGE_LABEL || 'TechTrack-Inbox') + '" placeholder="TechTrack-Inbox">';
    html += '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);margin-top:4px;">Create this label in Gmail and move emails here to auto-triage. Leave blank to auto-detect from inbox.</div></div>';
    html += '<div style="text-align:right;margin-top:8px;"><button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.saveTriageLabel()">Save Settings</button></div>';
    html += '</div>';

    // Inbound Rules
    html += '<div class="ai-admin-section">';
    html += '<div class="ai-admin-section-title" style="justify-content:space-between;">&#x25B6; Inbound Email Rules <button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.showAddRuleModal()">+ Add Rule</button></div>';
    if (rules.length === 0) {
      html += '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);">No rules yet. Rules let you auto-assign priority, module, or assignee based on sender domain, sender email, or subject keywords.</p>';
    } else {
      html += '<div>';
      rules.forEach(function(r) {
        html += '<div class="rule-row">';
        html += '<span style="font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);width:80px;">' + r.matchField + '</span>';
        html += '<span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-primary);flex:1;">' + App._esc(r.matchValue) + '</span>';
        html += '<span class="badge priority-' + (r.priority||'medium').toLowerCase() + '">' + (r.priority||' ') + '</span>';
        html += '<span style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-muted);font-family:var(--font-mono);">' + (r.module||' ') + '</span>';
        html += '<button class="btn-danger btn-sm" onclick="App.deleteRule(\'' + r.id + '\')">&#x2715;</button>';
        html += '</div>';
      });
      html += '</div>';
    }
    html += '</div>';

    // AI Query History
    html += '<div class="ai-admin-section">';
    html += '<div class="ai-admin-section-title">&#x1F4CB; AI Query History</div>';
    if (queries.length === 0) {
      html += '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);">No queries yet. Use the AI command bar (&#x2318;K) to ask questions.</p>';
    } else {
      queries.slice(0, 20).forEach(function(q) {
        html += '<div class="ai-query-row">';
        html += '<span class="ai-query-intent">' + (q.intent||'?') + '</span>';
        html += '<span style="flex:1;color:var(--text-secondary);">' + App._esc(q.query) + '</span>';
        html += '<span style="color:var(--text-dim);font-size:11px;font-family:var(--font-mono);">' + (q.userEmail||'') + '</span>';
        html += '<span style="color:var(--text-dim);font-size:11px;font-family:var(--font-mono);margin-left:10px;">' + (q.timestamp ? new Date(q.timestamp).toLocaleDateString() : '') + '</span>';
        html += '</div>';
      });
    }
    html += '</div>';

    html += '</div>'; // max-width wrapper

    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

    if (r && r.success) {
      self.showToast('&#x2736; Gemini backend key saved!', 'success');
      document.getElementById('geminiBackendKey').value = '';
      self.renderAIIntelligence();
    } else {
      self.showToast('Error: ' + (r ? r.error : 'unknown'), 'error');
    }
  },

  showAddRuleModal: function() {
    var modal = document.getElementById('modal');
    var body  = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (!modal || !body) return;
    body.innerHTML =
      '<h3 style="margin:0 0 16px;color:var(--text-primary);">Add Inbound Email Rule</h3>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Match Field</label>' +
      '<select id="ruleField" class="form-select"><option value="sender">Sender Email</option><option value="domain">Sender Domain</option><option value="subject">Subject Contains</option></select></div>' +

      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Override Priority</label><select id="rulePriority" class="form-select"><option value="">  no override  </option><option>Critical</option><option>High</option><option>Medium</option><option>Low</option></select></div>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Override Module</label><input id="ruleModule" class="form-input" placeholder="API, Auth, etc."></div>' +

      '<button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitRule()">Add Rule</button></div>';
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
  },

  submitRule: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var rule = {
      matchField: (document.getElementById('ruleField') || {}).value,
      matchValue: ((document.getElementById('ruleValue') || {}).value || '').trim(),
      priority:   (document.getElementById('rulePriority') || {}).value,
      module:     ((document.getElementById('ruleModule') || {}).value || '').trim(),
      assignTo:   ((document.getElementById('ruleAssign') || {}).value || '').trim()
    };
    if (!rule.matchValue) { self.showToast('Match value required', 'warning'); return; }
    var r = await self.callAsync('saveInboundRule', rule);
    if (r && r.success) {
      self.closeModal();
      self.showToast('Rule added', 'success');
      self.renderAIIntelligence();
    } else {
      self.showToast('Error: ' + (r ? r.error : 'unknown'), 'error');
    }
  },

  deleteRule: async function(ruleId) {
    var self = this;
    if (!confirm('Delete this rule?')) return;
    var r = await self.callAsync('deleteInboundRule', ruleId);
    if (r && r.success) {
      self.showToast('Rule deleted', 'info');
      self.renderAIIntelligence();
    }
  },

  // Helper: callAsync wraps google.script.run in a promise
  callAsync: function(fn, arg1, arg2, arg3) {
    return new Promise(function(resolve) {
      var t = setTimeout(function() {
        resolve({ success: false, error: fn + ' timed out. Check Spreadsheet ID in Code.gs.' });
      }, 15000);
      var runner = google.script.run
        .withSuccessHandler(function(r) { clearTimeout(t); resolve(r || { success: false }); })
        .withFailureHandler(function(e) { clearTimeout(t); resolve({ success: false, error: e.message || 'Script error' }); });
      if (arg3 !== undefined) runner[fn](arg1, arg2, arg3);
      else if (arg2 !== undefined) runner[fn](arg1, arg2);
      else if (arg1 !== undefined || arguments.length >= 2) runner[fn](arg1);
      else runner[fn]();
    });
  },

  _esc: function(str) {
    if (!str) return '';
    return String(str)
      .replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;')
      .replace(/"/g,'&quot;').replace(/'/g,'&#039;');
  },


  // ============================================================
  // KANBAN BOARD
  // ============================================================


  // ============================================================
  // QUICK CAPTURE (floating button + keyboard shortcut Q)
  // ============================================================
  showQuickCapture: function() {
    var modal = document.getElementById('modal');
    var body  = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (!modal || !body) return;
    body.innerHTML =
      '<h3 style="margin:0 0 4px;color:var(--text-primary);">&#x2726; Quick Capture</h3>' +
      '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-bottom:14px;">Describe the issue in plain English   AI will fill the rest</p>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><textarea id="qcInput" class="form-textarea" style="min-height:90px;" placeholder="e.g. Login crashes on Safari iOS when user has 2FA enabled   affects all CS accounts"></textarea></div>' +
      '<div id="qcPreview" style="display:none"></div>' +
      '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:12px;justify-content:flex-end;">' +
      '<button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Cancel</button>' +
      '<button class="btn-secondary" id="qcParseBtn" onclick="App.parseQuickCapture()">&#x2736; Parse with AI</button>' +
      '<button class="btn-primary" id="qcSubmitBtn" style="display:none" onclick="App.submitQuickCapture()">Create Issue</button>' +
      '</div>';
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
    setTimeout(function() { var el = document.getElementById('qcInput'); if(el) el.focus(); }, 100);
  },

  parseQuickCapture: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var text = (document.getElementById('qcInput')||{}).value||'';
    if (!text.trim()) { self.showToast('Describe the issue first','warning'); return; }
    var btn = document.getElementById('qcParseBtn');
    if (btn) btn.textContent = '&#x2736; Parsing...';
    var r = await self.callAsync('processAIQuery', 'create: ' + text);
    if (btn) btn.textContent = '&#x2736; Parse with AI';
    var preview = document.getElementById('qcPreview');
    var submitBtn = document.getElementById('qcSubmitBtn');
    if (!preview) return;
    var parsed = (r && r.success && r.result && r.result.create) ? r.result.create : null;
    if (!parsed) {
      // fallback: use text as title
      parsed = { title: text, description: text, priority: 'Medium', module: '', environment: '', impact: '' };
    }
    self._qcData = parsed;
    var pColors = { Critical:'var(--critical)', High:'var(--high)', Medium:'var(--accent)', Low:'var(--low)' };
    preview.style.display = 'block';
    preview.innerHTML =
      '<div class="ai-confirm-form">' +
      '<div class="ai-confirm-row"><div class="ai-confirm-key">Title</div>' +
      '<input class="ai-confirm-edit" id="qcTitle" value="' + self._esc(parsed.title||text) + '"></div>' +
      '<div class="ai-confirm-row"><div class="ai-confirm-key">Description</div>' +
      '<input class="ai-confirm-edit" id="qcDesc" value="' + self._esc(parsed.description||text) + '"></div>' +
      '<div class="ai-confirm-row"><div class="ai-confirm-key">Priority</div>' +
      '<select class="ai-confirm-edit" id="qcPriority">' +
      ['Critical','High','Medium','Low'].map(function(p){ return '<option'+(p===(parsed.priority||'Medium')?' selected':'')+'>'+p+'</option>'; }).join('') +
      '</select></div>' +
      '<div class="ai-confirm-row"><div class="ai-confirm-key">Module</div>' +
      '<input class="ai-confirm-edit" id="qcModule" value="' + self._esc(parsed.module||'') + '"></div>' +
      '</div>';
    if (submitBtn) submitBtn.style.display = 'inline-flex';
  },

  submitQuickCapture: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var issueData = {
      title:       ((document.getElementById('qcTitle')||{}).value||'').trim(),
      description: (document.getElementById('qcDesc')||{}).value||'',
      priority:    (document.getElementById('qcPriority')||{}).value||'Medium',
      module:      (document.getElementById('qcModule')||{}).value||''
    };
    if (!issueData.title) { self.showToast('Title required','warning'); return; }
    var r = await self.callAsync('createIssue', issueData);
    if (r && r.success) {
      self.closeModal();
      self.showToast('&#x2726; ' + r.issueId + ' created!','success');
      App.navigate('issue-detail', { id: r.issueId });
    } else {
      self.showToast('Error: '+(r?r.error:'unknown'),'error');
    }
  },

  // ============================================================
  // KEYBOARD SHORTCUTS
  // ============================================================
  initKeyboardShortcuts: function() {
        document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
      // Skip if typing in an input/textarea
      var tag = (e.target||{}).tagName||'';
      if (['INPUT','TEXTAREA','SELECT'].includes(tag)) return;
      if (e.metaKey || e.ctrlKey || e.altKey) return;
      switch(e.key) {
        case 'q': case 'Q': e.preventDefault(); self.showQuickCapture(); break;
        case 'n': case 'N': e.preventDefault(); self.navigate('create-issue'); break;
        case 'k': case 'K': e.preventDefault(); self.navigate('kanban'); break;
        case 'd': case 'D': e.preventDefault(); self.navigate('dashboard'); break;
        case 'l': case 'L': e.preventDefault(); self.navigate('issue-list'); break;
        case '/': e.preventDefault();
          var bar = document.getElementById('aiBar');
          if (bar) bar.focus();
          break;
        case 'Escape':
          self.closeModal();
          AI.close();
          break;
        case '?':
          self.showKeyboardHelp();
          break;
      }
    });
  },

  showKeyboardHelp: function() {
    var modal = document.getElementById('modal');
    var body  = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (!modal||!body) return;
    var shortcuts = [
      ['Q','Quick capture new issue'],['N','New issue (full form)'],
      ['D','Go to Dashboard'],['L','Go to Issue List'],['K','Go to Kanban'],
      ['/','Focus AI command bar'],['Esc','Close modal / AI panel'],['?','Show this help'],
    ];
    body.innerHTML = '<h3 style="margin:0 0 16px;color:var(--text-primary);">Keyboard Shortcuts</h3>' +
      '<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:1fr 1fr;gap:8px;">' +
      shortcuts.map(function(s){
        return '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;padding:6px 0;">' +
          '<span class="kbd">' + s[0] + '</span>' +
          '<span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-secondary);">' + s[1] + '</span></div>';
      }).join('') +
      '</div><div style="text-align:right;margin-top:16px;"><button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Close</button></div>';
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
  },

  // ============================================================
  // ESCALATION RULES PAGE
  // ============================================================
  renderEscalations: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('Escalation Rules','Admin / Escalations');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Loading...</p></div>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('getEscalationRules');
    if (!r||!r.success) { self.showPageError(area, r&&r.error?r.error:'Failed'); return; }
    var rules = r.rules||[];
        var html = '<div style="max-width:800px">';
    html += '<div class="card mb-16">';
    html += '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-bottom:14px;">Auto-escalate issues that stay open too long. Actions: notify escalation lead via email + Slack, or bump priority.</p>';
    html += '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-bottom:16px;">' +
      '<button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.showAddEscalationModal()">+ Add Rule</button>' +
      '<button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.callAsync(\'runEscalationCheck\').then(function(){App.showToast(\'Escalation check ran\',\'success\');})">Run Now</button></div>';
    if (rules.length === 0) {
      html += '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim);">No rules yet.</p>';
    } else {
      rules.forEach(function(r) {
        html += '<div class="rule-row">';
        html += '<span class="badge priority-'+r.priority.toLowerCase()+'" style="flex-shrink:0;">'+r.priority+'</span>';
        html += '<span style="flex:1;font-size:12px;color:var(--text-secondary);">After <strong style="color:var(--text-primary);">'+r.hoursToEscalate+'h</strong> → notify <strong style="color:var(--text-primary);">'+(r.escalateTo||'Slack only')+'</strong></span>';
        html += '<span style="font-size:10px;font-family:var(--font-mono);color:var(--text-dim);">'+r.action+'</span>';
        html += '<span style="width:8px;height:8px;border-radius:50%;background:'+(r.active?'var(--low)':'var(--border)')+';" title="'+(r.active?'Active':'Inactive')+'"></span>';
        html += '<button class="btn-danger btn-sm" onclick="App.deleteEscRule(\''+r.id+'\')">&#x2715;</button>';
        html += '</div>';
      });
    }
    html += '</div></div>';
    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

  showAddEscalationModal: function() {
    var modal = document.getElementById('modal');
    var body  = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (!modal||!body) return;
    body.innerHTML = '<h3 style="margin:0 0 16px;color:var(--text-primary);">Add Escalation Rule</h3>' +
      '<div class="form-grid-2"><div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Priority</label>' +
      '<select id="escPriority" class="form-select"><option>Critical</option><option>High</option><option>Medium</option><option>Low</option></select></div>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Escalate After (hours)</label>' +
      '<input id="escHours" class="form-input" type="number" value="4" min="1"></div></div>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Notify Email</label>' +
      '<input id="escEmail" class="form-input" placeholder="lead@company.com"></div>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Action</label>' +
      '<select id="escAction" class="form-select"><option value="notify">Notify only</option><option value="bump-priority">Bump priority</option></select></div>' +
      '<div style="text-align:right;margin-top:16px;"><button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Cancel</button> ' +
      '<button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitEscalation()">Add Rule</button></div>';
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
  },

  submitEscalation: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var rule = {
      priority: (document.getElementById('escPriority')||{}).value||'Critical',
      hoursToEscalate: parseInt((document.getElementById('escHours')||{}).value||4),
      escalateTo: (document.getElementById('escEmail')||{}).value||'',
      action: (document.getElementById('escAction')||{}).value||'notify'
    };
    var r = await self.callAsync('saveEscalationRule', rule);
    if (r&&r.success) { self.closeModal(); self.showToast('Rule added','success'); self.renderEscalations(); }
    else self.showToast('Error: '+(r?r.error:'unknown'),'error');
  },

  deleteEscRule: async function(id) {
    var self = this;
    if (!confirm('Delete this escalation rule?')) return;
    var r = await self.callAsync('deleteEscalationRule', id);
    if (r&&r.success) { self.showToast('Deleted','info'); self.renderEscalations(); }
  },

  // ============================================================
  // RECURRING TEMPLATES PAGE
  // ============================================================
  renderRecurring: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('Recurring Templates','Admin / Recurring');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Loading...</p></div>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('getRecurringTemplates');
    if (!r||!r.success) { self.showPageError(area, r&&r.error?r.error:'Failed'); return; }
    var templates = r.templates||[];
        var html = '<div style="max-width:800px"><div class="card">';
    html += '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:14px;">' +
      '<span class="card-title">Recurring Issue Templates</span>' +
      '<button class="btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="App.showAddTemplateModal()">+ Add Template</button></div>';
    html += '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-bottom:14px;">Issues auto-created on schedule. Good for weekly maintenance tasks, security scans, and recurring checks.</p>';
    if (templates.length === 0) {
      html += '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim);">No recurring templates yet.</p>';
    } else {
      templates.forEach(function(t) {
        var next = t.nextRun ? new Date(t.nextRun).toLocaleDateString() : ' ';
        html += '<div class="template-row">';
        html += '<span style="flex:1;font-size:13px;color:var(--text-primary);font-weight:500;">'+self._esc(t.title)+'</span>';
        html += '<span class="schedule-badge">'+t.schedule+'</span>';
        html += '<span class="badge priority-'+(t.priority||'medium').toLowerCase()+'">'+(t.priority||'Medium')+'</span>';
        html += '<span style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);font-family:var(--font-mono);">next: '+next+'</span>';
        html += '<span style="width:8px;height:8px;border-radius:50%;background:'+(t.active?'var(--low)':'var(--border)')+'"></span>';
        html += '<button class="btn-danger btn-sm" onclick="App.deleteTemplate(\''+t.id+'\')">&#x2715;</button>';
        html += '</div>';
      });
    }
    html += '</div></div>';
    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

  showAddTemplateModal: function() {
    var modal = document.getElementById('modal');
    var body  = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (!modal||!body) return;
    body.innerHTML = '<h3 style="margin:0 0 16px;color:var(--text-primary);">Add Recurring Template</h3>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Issue Title</label><input id="tplTitle" class="form-input" placeholder="Weekly DB backup verification"></div>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Description</label><textarea id="tplDesc" class="form-textarea" style="min-height:60px;" placeholder="Check backup logs and verify integrity..."></textarea></div>' +
      '<div class="form-grid-3"><div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Schedule</label>' +
      '<select id="tplSchedule" class="form-select"><option value="daily">Daily</option><option value="weekday">Weekdays</option><option value="weekly" selected>Weekly</option><option value="monthly">Monthly</option></select></div>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Priority</label>' +
      '<select id="tplPriority" class="form-select"><option>Critical</option><option>High</option><option selected>Medium</option><option>Low</option></select></div>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Module</label><input id="tplModule" class="form-input" placeholder="DevOps"></div></div>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Auto-assign To (email)</label><input id="tplAssign" class="form-input" placeholder="dev@company.com"></div>' +
      '<div style="text-align:right;margin-top:16px;"><button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Cancel</button> ' +
      '<button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitTemplate()">Create Template</button></div>';
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
  },

  submitTemplate: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var tpl = {
      title:       (document.getElementById('tplTitle')||{}).value||'',
      description: (document.getElementById('tplDesc')||{}).value||'',
      schedule:    (document.getElementById('tplSchedule')||{}).value||'weekly',
      priority:    (document.getElementById('tplPriority')||{}).value||'Medium',
      module:      (document.getElementById('tplModule')||{}).value||'',
      assignTo:    (document.getElementById('tplAssign')||{}).value||''
    };
    if (!tpl.title) { self.showToast('Title required','warning'); return; }
    var r = await self.callAsync('saveRecurringTemplate', tpl);
    if (r&&r.success) { self.closeModal(); self.showToast('Template created','success'); self.renderRecurring(); }
    else self.showToast('Error: '+(r?r.error:'unknown'),'error');
  },

  deleteTemplate: async function(id) {
    var self = this;
    if (!confirm('Delete this template?')) return;
    var r = await self.callAsync('deleteRecurringTemplate', id);
    if (r&&r.success) { self.showToast('Deleted','info'); self.renderRecurring(); }
  },

  renderIntegrations: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('Integrations','Admin / Integrations');

    var settingsR = await self.callAsync('getSettings');

    var s = (settingsR&&settingsR.success) ? settingsR.settings : {};
    var calOk = calR&&calR.configured;
        var html = '<div style="max-width:800px">';

    // Google Calendar
    html += '<div class="ai-admin-section">';
    html += '<div class="ai-admin-section-title">&#x1F4C5; Google Calendar Sync</div>';

    html += '<div class="status-dot '+(calOk?'active':'')+'"></div>';

    html += '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Your Webhook URL (Apps Script deployment URL)</label>';

    html += '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);margin-top:6px;">In GitHub: Repo Settings → Webhooks → Add webhook → Content type: application/json → Events: Push</div>';
    html += '</div>';

    // Slack
    html += '<div class="ai-admin-section">';
    html += '<div class="ai-admin-section-title">&#x1F4AC; Slack Integration</div>';
    html += '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Slack Webhook URL</label>';

    html += '<div style="margin-top:8px;"><button class="btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="App.saveSlackInt()">Save Webhook</button></div></div>';

    html += '<div class="form-grid-2"><div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Webhook URL</label>';
