    html += '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Alert Level</label>';
    html += '<select id="whLevel" class="form-select"><option value="false" '+(s.WEBHOOK_CRITICAL_ONLY!=='true'?'selected':'')+'>All Issues</option><option value="true" '+(s.WEBHOOK_CRITICAL_ONLY==='true'?'selected':'')+'>Critical Only</option></select></div></div>';
    html += '<div style="margin-top:8px;"><button class="btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="App.saveWebhook()">Save</button></div></div>';

    html += '</div>';
    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

  saveCalendar: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var id = ((document.getElementById('calId')||{}).value||'').trim();
    await self.callAsync('updateSetting','GOOGLE_CALENDAR_ID', id||'false');
    self.showToast('Calendar ID saved','success');
    self.renderIntegrations();
  },

  saveSlackInt: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var url = ((document.getElementById('slackWh')||{}).value||'').trim();
    await self.callAsync('updateSetting','SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL', url||'false');
    self.showToast('Slack webhook saved','success');
  },

  saveWebhook: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var url   = ((document.getElementById('whUrl')||{}).value||'').trim();
    var level = (document.getElementById('whLevel')||{}).value||'false';
    await self.callAsync('updateSetting','WEBHOOK_ALERT_URL', url||'false');
    await self.callAsync('updateSetting','WEBHOOK_CRITICAL_ONLY', level);
    self.showToast('Webhook settings saved','success');
  },

  // ============================================================
  // SPRINT VELOCITY PAGE
  // ============================================================
  renderVelocity: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('Sprint Velocity','Sprints / Velocity');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Calculating velocity...</p></div>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('getSprintVelocity');
    if (!r||!r.success) { self.showPageError(area, r&&r.error?r.error:'Failed'); return; }
    var velocity = r.velocity||[];
        var html = '<div style="max-width:700px"><div class="card">';
    html += '<div class="card-title mb-16">Sprint Completion Rate</div>';
    if (velocity.length === 0) {
      html += '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);">No sprints with issues yet. Create sprints and assign issues to track velocity.</p>';
    } else {
      velocity.forEach(function(v) {
        html += '<div class="velocity-bar-row">';
        html += '<div class="velocity-label" title="'+self._esc(v.sprintName||v.sprintId)+'">'+self._esc(v.sprintName||v.sprintId)+'</div>';
        html += '<div class="velocity-bar-wrap"><div class="velocity-bar-fill" style="width:'+v.completionRate+'%"></div></div>';
        html += '<div class="velocity-pct">'+v.completionRate+'%</div>';
        html += '<div style="font-size:10px;font-family:var(--font-mono);color:var(--text-dim);width:80px;text-align:right;">'+v.resolved+'/'+v.total+' done</div>';
        html += '</div>';
      });
      // Summary stats
      var avgCompletion = Math.round(velocity.reduce(function(a,v){ return a+v.completionRate; },0)/velocity.length);
      html += '<div style="margin-top:16px;padding-top:12px;border-top:1px solid var(--border);display:flex;gap:24px;">';
      html += '<div><div style="font-size:22px;font-weight:800;color:var(--text-primary);">'+avgCompletion+'%</div><div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text-dim);font-family:var(--font-mono);text-transform:uppercase;">Avg Completion</div></div>';
      html += '<div><div style="font-size:22px;font-weight:800;color:var(--text-primary);">'+velocity.length+'</div><div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text-dim);font-family:var(--font-mono);text-transform:uppercase;">Sprints</div></div>';
      html += '</div>';
    }
    html += '</div></div>';
    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

  // ============================================================
  // PENDING REVIEWS PAGE
  // ============================================================
  renderPendingReviews: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('Pending Reviews','My Issues / Reviews');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Loading reviews...</p></div>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('getPendingReviews');
    if (!r||!r.success) { self.showPageError(area, r&&r.error?r.error:'Failed'); return; }
    var reviews = r.reviews||[];
        var html = '<div style="max-width:700px"><div class="card">';
    html += '<div class="card-title mb-16">Peer Reviews Awaiting Your Approval</div>';
    if (reviews.length === 0) {
      html += '<div class="empty-state"><div class="empty-state-icon">&#x2714;</div><p>No pending reviews. You\'re all caught up!</p></div>';
    } else {
      reviews.forEach(function(rev) {
        html += '<div class="review-card review-pending">';
        html += '<div style="flex:1"><div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:var(--text-primary);">'+self._esc(rev.issueId)+'</div>';
        html += '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-muted);">Requested by '+self._esc(rev.requestedBy)+' · '+new Date(rev.requestedAt).toLocaleDateString()+'</div></div>';
        html += '<button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.navigate(\'issue-detail\',{id:\''+rev.issueId+'\'})">View Issue</button>';
        html += '<button class="btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="App.approveReview(\''+rev.id+'\')">Approve</button>';
        html += '<button class="btn-danger btn-sm" onclick="App.rejectReview(\''+rev.id+'\')">Reject</button>';
        html += '</div>';
      });
    }
    html += '</div></div>';
    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

  approveReview: async function(reviewId) {
    var self = this;
    var comment = prompt('Add an approval comment (optional):') || '';
    var r = await self.callAsync('submitPeerReview', reviewId, 'Approved', comment);
    if (r&&r.success) { self.showToast('Review approved   issue resolved','success'); self.renderPendingReviews(); }
    else self.showToast('Error: '+(r?r.error:'unknown'),'error');
  },

  rejectReview: async function(reviewId) {
    var self = this;
    var comment = prompt('Reason for rejection:');
    if (!comment) return;
    var r = await self.callAsync('submitPeerReview', reviewId, 'Rejected', comment);
    if (r&&r.success) { self.showToast('Review rejected','info'); self.renderPendingReviews(); }
    else self.showToast('Error: '+(r?r.error:'unknown'),'error');
  },

  // ============================================================
  // PDF / HTML EXPORT
  // ============================================================
  exportIssue: async function(issueId) {
    var self = this;
    self.showToast('Generating export...','info');
    var r = await self.callAsync('exportIssueToPDF', issueId);
    if (r&&r.success) {
      self.showToast('Export ready   opening in Drive','success');
      window.open(r.url, '_blank');
    } else {
      self.showToast('Export failed: '+(r?r.error:'unknown'),'error');
    }
  },

  exportDashboard: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.showToast('Generating dashboard report...','info');
    var r = await self.callAsync('exportDashboardReport', null);
    if (r&&r.success) {
      self.showToast('Report ready   opening in Drive','success');
      window.open(r.url, '_blank');
    } else {
      self.showToast('Export failed: '+(r?r.error:'unknown'),'error');
    }
  },

  // ============================================================
  // GIT COMMITS tab in issue detail
  // ============================================================
  renderCommits: async function(issueId) {
    var self = this;
    var container = document.getElementById('commitsContainer');
    if (!container) return;
    container.innerHTML = '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);">Loading commits...</p>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('getIssueCommits', issueId);
    var commits = (r&&r.success) ? r.commits : [];
        if (commits.length === 0) {
      container.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state" style="padding:20px;">' +
        '<div class="empty-state-icon">&#x2731;</div>' +
        '<p>No commits linked yet.</p>' +
        '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim);">Link commits by mentioning TECH-XXXX in commit messages via the GitHub webhook.</p></div>';
      return;
    }
    var html = '';
    commits.forEach(function(c) {
      html += '<div class="commit-badge" style="display:flex;width:100%;box-sizing:border-box;">';
      html += '<span class="commit-sha">'+(c.sha||'').substring(0,7)+'</span>';
      html += '<span class="commit-msg">'+self._esc((c.message||'').substring(0,80))+'</span>';
      html += '<span style="color:var(--text-dim);font-size:10px;">'+self._esc(c.author||'')+'</span>';
      if (c.url) html += '<a href="'+c.url+'" target="_blank" style="color:var(--accent);font-size:10px;">&#x2197;</a>';
      html += '</div>';
    });
    container.innerHTML = html;
  },

  // ============================================================
  // PEER REVIEW REQUEST from issue detail
  // ============================================================
  showPeerReviewModal: async function(issueId) {
    var self = this;
    var usersR = await self.callAsync('getUsers', true);
    var users = (usersR&&usersR.success) ? usersR.users.filter(function(u){ return u.role==='Developer'||u.role==='Admin'; }) : [];
    var modal = document.getElementById('modal');
    var body  = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (!modal||!body) return;
    var opts = users.map(function(u){ return '<option value="'+u.email+'">'+self._esc(u.name||u.email)+'</option>'; }).join('');
    body.innerHTML = '<h3 style="margin:0 0 14px;color:var(--text-primary);">Request Peer Review</h3>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Select Reviewer</label>' +
      '<select id="reviewerSel" class="form-select">'+opts+'</select></div>' +
      '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);">The reviewer will be notified by email and can approve or reject the resolution.</p>' +
      '<div style="text-align:right;margin-top:14px;"><button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Cancel</button> ' +
      '<button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitReviewRequest(\''+issueId+'\')">Send Request</button></div>';
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
  },

  submitReviewRequest: async function(issueId) {
    var self = this;
    var email = (document.getElementById('reviewerSel')||{}).value||'';
    if (!email) { self.showToast('Select a reviewer','warning'); return; }
    var r = await self.callAsync('requestPeerReview', issueId, email);
    if (r&&r.success) { self.closeModal(); self.showToast('Review request sent to '+email,'success'); }
    else self.showToast('Error: '+(r?r.error:'unknown'),'error');
  },

  showDepsModal: async function(issueId) {
    var self = this;
    var modal = document.getElementById('modal');
    var body  = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (!modal||!body) return;
    body.innerHTML = '<p style="color:var(--text-muted);">Loading dependencies...</p>';
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
    var r = await self.callAsync('getIssueDependencies', issueId);
    var deps = (r && r.success) ? r : { blockedBy:[], blocks:[] };
        var html = '<h3 style="margin:0 0 16px;color:var(--text-primary);">Dependencies   ' + issueId + '</h3>';
    html += '<div class="form-group"><div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.1em;color:var(--text-dim);font-family:var(--font-mono);margin-bottom:8px;">BLOCKED BY</div>';
    if (deps.blockedBy && deps.blockedBy.length) {
      deps.blockedBy.forEach(function(id){ html += '<div class="dep-badge" style="margin-bottom:4px;" data-navid="'+self._esc(id)+'">&#x25FC; '+self._esc(id)+'</div><br>'; });
    } else { html += '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim);">Not blocked by any issue.</p>'; }
    html += '</div><div class="form-group"><div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.1em;color:var(--text-dim);font-family:var(--font-mono);margin-bottom:8px;">BLOCKS</div>';
    if (deps.blocks && deps.blocks.length) {
      deps.blocks.forEach(function(id){ html += '<div class="dep-badge" style="margin-bottom:4px;" data-navid="'+self._esc(id)+'">&#x25FC; '+self._esc(id)+'</div><br>'; });
    } else { html += '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim);">Does not block any issue.</p>'; }
    html += '</div><div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Add Blocker (Issue ID)</label>';
    html += '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;"><input id="depInput" class="form-input" placeholder="TECH-0001"></div></div>';
    html += '<div style="text-align:right;margin-top:12px;"><button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Close</button> ';
    html += '<button class="btn-primary" id="addDepBtn">Add Dependency</button></div>';
    body.innerHTML = html;
    // Wire dep badge clicks via data attributes
    setTimeout(function() {
      document.querySelectorAll('.dep-badge[data-navid]').forEach(function(el) {
        el.addEventListener('click', function() {
          var id = el.getAttribute('data-navid');
          App.closeModal();
          App.navigate('issue-detail', { id: id });
        });
      });
      var addBtn = document.getElementById('addDepBtn');
      if (addBtn) addBtn.addEventListener('click', function() { App.addDep(issueId); });
    }, 50);
  },

  addDep: async function(issueId) {
    var self = this;
    var blocker = ((document.getElementById('depInput')||{}).value||'').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!blocker) { self.showToast('Enter an issue ID','warning'); return; }
    var r = await self.callAsync('addDependency', issueId, blocker);
    if (r && r.success) { self.showToast('Dependency added','success'); self.showDepsModal(issueId); }
    else self.showToast('Error: '+(r?r.error:'unknown'),'error');
  },

  renderKanban: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('Kanban Board', 'Issues / Kanban');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Loading board...</p></div>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('getKanbanData');
    if (!r || !r.success) { self.showPageError(area, r && r.error ? r.error : 'getKanbanData failed. Redeploy Code.gs and run initializeAll().'); return; }
    self._kanbanFilter = self._kanbanFilter || { search:'', module:'all', priority:'all' };
    var colColors = { Open:'var(--text-muted)', Acknowledged:'var(--accent)', 'In Progress':'var(--high)', Testing:'var(--low)', Resolved:'var(--low)', Closed:'var(--text-dim)', Blocked:'var(--critical)', 'Need Info':'var(--high)', Reopened:'var(--critical)' };
    var modules = [];
    Object.values(r.board).flat().forEach(function(i) { if (i.module && !modules.includes(i.module)) modules.push(i.module); });
    modules.sort();

    var html = '<div style="display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:10px;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:14px;">';
    html += '<div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);">Drag cards to move status • click any card to open issue</div>';
    html += '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;flex-wrap:wrap;align-items:center;">';
    html += '<input class="search-input" type="text" placeholder="Search Kanban..." id="kanbanSearch" value="' + self._esc(self._kanbanFilter.search) + '" oninput="App.kanbanSearch(this.value)">';
    html += '<select class="filter-select" id="kanbanModule" onchange="App.kanbanFilter()"><option value="all">All Modules</option>' + modules.map(function(m){ return '<option value="' + m + '"' + (self._kanbanFilter.module === m ? ' selected' : '') + '>' + m + '</option>'; }).join('') + '</select>';
    html += '<select class="filter-select" id="kanbanPriority" onchange="App.kanbanFilter()">';
    html += '<option value="all">All Priority</option><option value="Critical">Critical</option><option value="High">High</option><option value="Medium">Medium</option><option value="Low">Low</option></select>';
    html += '<button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.navigate(\'issue-list\')">List View</button>';
    html += '</div></div>';
    html += '<div class="kanban-board">';
    r.columns.forEach(function(col) {
      var cards = (r.board[col] || []).filter(function(i) {
        if (self._kanbanFilter.search && (i.title || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(self._kanbanFilter.search.toLowerCase()) === -1 && (i.id || '').toLowerCase().indexOf(self._kanbanFilter.search.toLowerCase()) === -1) return false;
        if (self._kanbanFilter.module !== 'all' && i.module !== self._kanbanFilter.module) return false;
        if (self._kanbanFilter.priority !== 'all' && i.priority !== self._kanbanFilter.priority) return false;
        return true;
      });
      html += '<div class="kanban-col" ondragover="App.allowKanbanDrop(event)" ondrop="App.dropKanbanCard(event,\'' + col + '\')">';
      html += '<div class="kanban-col-header">';
      html += '<span class="kanban-col-title" style="color:' + (colColors[col]||'var(--text-muted)') + '">' + col + '</span>';
      html += '<span class="kanban-col-count">' + cards.length + '</span></div>';
      html += '<div class="kanban-cards">';
      if (cards.length === 0) {
        html += '<div class="kanban-empty">Empty</div>';
      }
      cards.forEach(function(i) {
        html += '<div class="kanban-card' + (i.slaBreached ? ' kanban-card-breached' : '') + '" draggable="true" ondragstart="App.startKanbanDrag(event,\'' + i.id + '\')" ondragend="App.endKanbanDrag(event)" onclick="App.navigate(\'issue-detail\',{id:\'' + i.id + '\'})">';
        html += '<div class="kanban-card-id">' + i.id + '</div>';
        html += '<div class="kanban-card-title">' + self._esc(i.title) + '</div>';
        html += '<div class="kanban-card-footer">';
        html += '<span class="badge-status ' + i.status.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g,'-') + '" style="font-size:10px;padding:3px 8px;">' + i.priority + '</span>';
        if (i.module) html += '<span class="kanban-card-module">' + i.module + '</span>';
        if (i.slaBreached) html += '<span class="kanban-card-sla">SLA!</span>';
        /* Age badge on card */
        var ageDays = i.createdDate ? Math.floor((Date.now()-new Date(i.createdDate))/86400000) : 0;
        var ageCls  = ageDays<=3?'age-fresh':ageDays<=7?'age-normal':ageDays<=14?'age-aging':ageDays<=29?'age-old':'age-stale';
        html += '<span class="age-badge '+ageCls+' kanban-card-age" title="'+ageDays+' days since raised">⏱ '+(ageDays===0?'today':ageDays+'d')+'</span>';
        /* Follow-up dot on card */
        var fuN = FollowUp.count(i.id);
        html += '<span class="kanban-fu-dot" title="'+(fuN>0?fuN+' follow-up(s)':'Log follow-up')+'" onclick="event.stopPropagation();FollowUp.openModal(\''+i.id+'\')">'+(fuN>0?'🚩 '+fuN:'🚩')+'</span>';
        html += '</div></div>';
      });
      html += '</div></div>';
    });
    html += '</div>';
    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

  startKanbanDrag: function(event, issueId) {
    event.dataTransfer.setData('text/plain', issueId);
    event.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'move';
    event.currentTarget.classList.add('dragging');
  },

  endKanbanDrag: function(event) {
    event.currentTarget.classList.remove('dragging');
  },

  allowKanbanDrop: function(event) {
    event.preventDefault();
    event.currentTarget.classList.add('kanban-drop-target');
  },

  dropKanbanCard: async function(event, targetStatus) {
    event.preventDefault();
    event.currentTarget.classList.remove('kanban-drop-target');
    var issueId = event.dataTransfer.getData('text/plain');
    if (!issueId || !targetStatus) return;
    await this.moveKanbanCard(issueId, targetStatus);
  },

  moveKanbanCard: async function(issueId, targetStatus) {
    var self = this;
    self.showToast('Moving ' + issueId + ' to ' + targetStatus + '...', 'info');
    var response = await self.callAsync('updateIssueStatus', issueId, targetStatus, 'Moved on kanban board');
    if (response && response.success) {
      self.showToast(issueId + ' moved to ' + targetStatus, 'success');
      self.renderKanban();
    } else {
      self.showToast('Failed to move ' + issueId + ': ' + (response ? response.error : 'unknown'), 'error');
    }
  },

  kanbanSearch: function(value) {
    this._kanbanFilter = this._kanbanFilter || { search:'', module:'all', priority:'all' };
    this._kanbanFilter.search = value || '';
    this.renderKanban();
  },

  kanbanFilter: function() {
    this._kanbanFilter = this._kanbanFilter || { search:'', module:'all', priority:'all' };
    this._kanbanFilter.module = document.getElementById('kanbanModule')?.value || 'all';
    this._kanbanFilter.priority = document.getElementById('kanbanPriority')?.value || 'all';
    this.renderKanban();
  },

  // ============================================================
  // SPRINTS
  // ============================================================
  renderSprints: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('Sprints', 'Issues / Sprints');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Loading sprints...</p></div>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('getSprints');
    var sprints = (r && r.success) ? r.sprints : [];
        var html = '<div style="display:flex;gap:10px;margin-bottom:20px;align-items:center;">';
    html += '<button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.showCreateSprintModal()">+ New Sprint</button>';
    html += '<button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.renderBurndown(null)">View Burndown</button></div>';
    if (sprints.length === 0) {
      html += '<div class="empty-state"><div class="empty-state-icon">&#x25B7;</div><p>No sprints yet. Create your first sprint to start organizing issues.</p></div>';
    } else {
      html += '<div class="grid-2">';
      sprints.forEach(function(s) {
        var start = s.startDate ? new Date(s.startDate).toLocaleDateString() : ' ';
        var end = s.endDate ? new Date(s.endDate).toLocaleDateString() : ' ';
        html += '<div class="card">';
        html += '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:10px;">';
        html += '<span style="font-size:14px;font-weight:700;color:var(--text-primary);">' + self._esc(s.name) + '</span>';
        html += '<span class="badge" style="background:var(--low-dim);color:var(--low)">' + (s.status||'Active') + '</span></div>';
        if (s.goal) html += '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-bottom:10px;">' + self._esc(s.goal) + '</p>';
        html += '<div style="display:flex;gap:16px;font-size:11px;font-family:var(--font-mono);color:var(--text-dim);">';
        html += '<span>' + start + ' → ' + end + '</span></div>';
        html += '<div style="margin-top:12px;display:flex;gap:8px;">';
        html += '<button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.renderBurndown(\'' + s.id + '\')">Burndown</button>';
        html += '<button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.navigate(\'issue-list\')">Issues</button></div>';
        html += '</div>';
      });
      html += '</div>';
    }
    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

  showCreateSprintModal: function() {
    var modal = document.getElementById('modal');
    var body = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (!modal || !body) return;
    var today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
    var twoWeeks = new Date(Date.now() + 14*24*3600000).toISOString().split('T')[0];
    body.innerHTML =
      '<h3 style="margin:0 0 16px;color:var(--text-primary);">Create Sprint</h3>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Sprint Name</label><input id="sprintName" class="form-input" placeholder="Sprint 1   Auth Overhaul"></div>' +
      '<div class="form-grid-2"><div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Start Date</label><input id="sprintStart" class="form-input" type="date" value="' + today + '"></div>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">End Date</label><input id="sprintEnd" class="form-input" type="date" value="' + twoWeeks + '"></div></div>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Sprint Goal (optional)</label><input id="sprintGoal" class="form-input" placeholder="Complete auth module refactor"></div>' +
      '<div style="text-align:right;margin-top:16px;"><button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Cancel</button> <button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitSprint()">Create Sprint</button></div>';
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
  },

  submitSprint: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var data = {
      name: (document.getElementById('sprintName')||{}).value||'',
      startDate: (document.getElementById('sprintStart')||{}).value||'',
      endDate: (document.getElementById('sprintEnd')||{}).value||'',
      goal: (document.getElementById('sprintGoal')||{}).value||''
    };
    if (!data.name) { self.showToast('Sprint name required','warning'); return; }
    var r = await self.callAsync('createSprint', data);
    if (r && r.success) { self.closeModal(); self.showToast('Sprint created','success'); self.renderSprints(); }
    else self.showToast('Error: '+(r?r.error:'unknown'),'error');
  },

  renderBurndown: async function(sprintId) {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('Burndown Chart', 'Sprints / Burndown');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Generating burndown...</p></div>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('getBurndownData', sprintId || null);
    if (!r || !r.success) { area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Failed to load data</p></div>'; return; }
    var days = r.burndown || [];
    if (days.length === 0) { area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>No data available</p></div>'; return; }
    var max = Math.max.apply(null, days.map(function(d){return d.remaining;})) || 1;
    var barW = Math.floor(580 / days.length) - 4;
    var html = '<div class="card"><div class="card-title mb-16">Issue Burndown   Last 14 Days</div>';
    html += '<div style="display:flex;align-items:flex-end;gap:4px;height:200px;padding:0 8px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);border-left:1px solid var(--border);">';
    days.forEach(function(d) {
      var h = Math.round((d.remaining / max) * 180);
      var label = d.date.split('-').slice(1).join('/');
      html += '<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;align-items:center;flex:1;gap:2px;">';
      html += '<div style="font-size:9px;font-family:var(--font-mono);color:var(--text-dim);">' + d.remaining + '</div>';
      html += '<div style="width:100%;background:var(--accent);border-radius:3px 3px 0 0;height:' + h + 'px;min-height:2px;"></div>';
      html += '<div style="font-size:8px;font-family:var(--font-mono);color:var(--text-dim);transform:rotate(-45deg);margin-top:4px;white-space:nowrap;">' + label + '</div>';
      html += '</div>';
    });
    html += '</div></div>';
    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

  // ============================================================
  // ANALYTICS PAGE
  // ============================================================
  renderAnalytics: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('Analytics', 'Admin / Analytics');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Crunching numbers...</p></div>';
        var mttrR = await self.callAsync('getMTTRStats');
    var patR = await self.callAsync('getRecurringPatterns');
    var burnR = await self.callAsync('getBurndownData', null);
    var html = '<div style="max-width:900px">';

    // MTTR by priority
    html += '<div class="analytics-grid">';
    if (mttrR && mttrR.success) {
      html += '<div class="analytics-card"><div class="analytics-card-title">MTTR by Priority (avg hours)</div>';
      var pColors = { Critical:'var(--critical)', High:'var(--high)', Medium:'var(--accent)', Low:'var(--low)' };
      ['Critical','High','Medium','Low'].forEach(function(p) {
        var val = mttrR.priorityMTTR ? (mttrR.priorityMTTR[p] || 0) : 0;
        html += '<div class="mttr-row">';
        html += '<span style="width:8px;height:8px;border-radius:50%;background:' + (pColors[p]||'var(--text-dim)') + ';flex-shrink:0;display:inline-block;"></span>';
        html += '<span class="mttr-key">' + p + '</span>';
        html += '<span class="mttr-val">' + val + 'h</span></div>';
      });
      html += '<div style="margin-top:10px;font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);font-family:var(--font-mono);">' + (mttrR.totalResolved||0) + ' issues resolved total</div>';
      html += '</div>';

      // MTTR by module
      html += '<div class="analytics-card"><div class="analytics-card-title">MTTR by Module (avg hours)</div>';
      var modules = mttrR.moduleMTTR ? Object.keys(mttrR.moduleMTTR).sort(function(a,b){ return mttrR.moduleMTTR[b] - mttrR.moduleMTTR[a]; }) : [];
      modules.slice(0,6).forEach(function(m) {
        var val = mttrR.moduleMTTR[m];
        html += '<div class="mttr-row"><span class="mttr-key">' + self._esc(m) + '</span><span class="mttr-val">' + val + 'h</span></div>';
      });
      html += '</div>';
    }
    html += '</div>';

    // Burndown mini chart
    if (burnR && burnR.success && burnR.burndown && burnR.burndown.length) {
      html += '<div class="analytics-card" style="margin-bottom:16px;"><div class="analytics-card-title">14-Day Issue Trend</div>';
      var days = burnR.burndown;
      var mx = Math.max.apply(null, days.map(function(d){return d.remaining;})) || 1;
      html += '<div style="display:flex;align-items:flex-end;gap:3px;height:80px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);">';
      days.forEach(function(d) {
        var bh = Math.round((d.remaining/mx)*70);
        html += '<div style="flex:1;background:var(--accent-dim);border-radius:2px 2px 0 0;height:' + bh + 'px;min-height:2px;" title="' + d.date + ': ' + d.remaining + ' issues"></div>';
      });
      html += '</div></div>';
    }

    // AI Recurring patterns
    if (patR && patR.success && patR.patterns && patR.patterns.length) {
      html += '<div class="card"><div class="card-title mb-16">&#x2736; AI Recurring Patterns</div>';
      if (patR.insight) html += '<div class="ai-email-summary" style="margin-bottom:14px;"><p style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text-secondary);margin:0;">'+self._esc(patR.insight)+'</p></div>';
      patR.patterns.forEach(function(p) {
        html += '<div class="pattern-card">';
        html += '<div class="pattern-title">' + self._esc(p.title) + '</div>';
        html += '<div class="pattern-desc">' + self._esc(p.description) + '</div>';
        html += '<div class="pattern-tags">';
        if (p.frequency) html += '<span class="badge" style="background:var(--accent-dim);color:var(--accent);">' + self._esc(p.frequency) + '</span>';
        (p.modules||[]).forEach(function(m){ html += '<span class="badge">' + self._esc(m) + '</span>'; });
        html += '</div>';
        if (p.suggestion) html += '<div style="margin-top:8px;font-size:11px;color:var(--accent);font-family:var(--font-mono);">&#x2736; ' + self._esc(p.suggestion) + '</div>';
        html += '</div>';
      });
      html += '</div>';
    } else if (patR && patR.success) {
      html += '<div class="card"><div class="card-title mb-16">&#x2736; AI Recurring Patterns</div>';
      html += '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);">' + (patR.message || 'Patterns will appear after more issues are logged.') + '</p></div>';
    }

    html += '</div>';
    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

  // ============================================================
  // WORKLOAD BALANCER
  // ============================================================
  renderWorkload: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('Workload Balancer', 'Admin / Workload');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Loading workload data...</p></div>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('getWorkloadData');
    if (!r || !r.success) { self.showPageError(area, r && r.error ? r.error : 'Backend call failed. Redeploy Code.gs and run initializeAll().'); return; }
        var workload = r.workload || [];
    workload.sort(function(a,b){ return b.loadScore - a.loadScore; });
    var html = '<div style="margin-bottom:14px;display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;">';
    html += '<span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);">Sorted by load score. Click a dev to reassign their issues.</span>';
    html += '</div><div class="workload-grid">';
    workload.forEach(function(dev) {
      var pct = Math.min(100, Math.round((dev.total / (dev.maxTickets||10)) * 100));
      var overloaded = dev.total >= dev.maxTickets;
      var warning = pct >= 70;
      var initial = (dev.name || dev.email || '?')[0].toUpperCase();
      html += '<div class="workload-card">';
      html += '<div class="workload-header">';
      html += '<div class="workload-avatar">' + initial + '</div>';
      html += '<div style="flex:1"><div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:var(--text-primary);">' + self._esc(dev.name||dev.email) + '</div>';
      html += '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);font-family:var(--font-mono);">' + self._esc(dev.email) + '</div></div>';
      if (overloaded) html += '<span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--critical);font-weight:700;font-family:var(--font-mono);">FULL</span>';
      html += '</div>';
      html += '<div class="workload-bar-wrap"><div class="workload-bar' + (overloaded?' overloaded':warning?' warning':'') + '" style="width:' + pct + '%"></div></div>';
      html += '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;font-size:11px;font-family:var(--font-mono);color:var(--text-dim);margin-bottom:10px;">';
      html += '<span>' + dev.total + '/' + dev.maxTickets + ' issues</span>';
      html += '<span style="color:' + (dev.critical?'var(--critical)':'var(--text-dim)') + '">' + (dev.critical?dev.critical+' critical':'') + '</span></div>';
      html += '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;">';
      if (dev.breached) html += '<span style="font-size:11px;color:var(--critical);"> ' + dev.breached + ' SLA breach</span>';
      html += '</div>';
      if (dev.issues && dev.issues.length) {
        html += '<div style="margin-top:10px;border-top:1px solid var(--border);padding-top:8px;">';
        dev.issues.slice(0,3).forEach(function(i) {
          html += '<div style="font-size:11px;padding:3px 0;color:var(--text-secondary);display:flex;gap:6px;">';
          html += '<span style="color:var(--accent);font-family:var(--font-mono);">' + i.id + '</span>';
          html += '<span style="flex:1;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;white-space:nowrap;">' + self._esc(i.title) + '</span></div>';
        });
        if (dev.issues.length > 3) html += '<div style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text-dim);margin-top:4px;">+' + (dev.issues.length-3) + ' more</div>';
        html += '</div>';
      }
      html += '</div>';
    });
    html += '</div>';
    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

  // ============================================================
  // ON-CALL SCHEDULE
  // ============================================================
  renderOnCall: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('On-Call Schedule', 'Admin / On-Call');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Loading...</p></div>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('getOnCallSchedule');
    var curR = await self.callAsync('getCurrentOnCall');
    var schedule = (r && r.success) ? r.schedule : [];
    var current = curR && curR.success ? curR.onCall : null;
        var html = '<div style="max-width:700px">';
    // Current on-call
    html += '<div class="card mb-16"><div class="card-title mb-12">Currently On-Call</div>';
    if (current) {
      html += '<div class="oncall-badge">&#x25CF; ' + self._esc(current.name||current.email) + '   until ' + new Date(current.endDate).toLocaleDateString() + '</div>';
    } else {
      html += '<p style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text-muted);">No one is currently scheduled. Critical issues will not be auto-assigned.</p>';
    }
    html += '</div>';
    // Add entry
    html += '<div class="card mb-16"><div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:14px;"><span class="card-title">Schedule</span><button class="btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="App.showAddOnCallModal()">+ Add Entry</button></div>';
    if (schedule.length === 0) {
      html += '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);">No schedule entries yet.</p>';
    } else {
      schedule.forEach(function(s) {
        var now = new Date();
        var isActive = now >= new Date(s.startDate) && now <= new Date(s.endDate);
        html += '<div class="rule-row">';
        if (isActive) html += '<span style="width:8px;height:8px;border-radius:50%;background:var(--low);flex-shrink:0;"></span>';
        else html += '<span style="width:8px;height:8px;border-radius:50%;background:var(--border);flex-shrink:0;"></span>';
        html += '<span style="flex:1;font-size:13px;color:var(--text-primary);">' + self._esc(s.name||s.email) + '</span>';
        html += '<span style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);font-family:var(--font-mono);">' + new Date(s.startDate).toLocaleDateString() + ' → ' + new Date(s.endDate).toLocaleDateString() + '</span>';
        html += '</div>';
      });
    }
    html += '</div></div>';
    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

  showAddOnCallModal: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var usersR = await self.callAsync('getUsers', true);
    var users = (usersR && usersR.success) ? usersR.users : [];
    var opts = users.map(function(u){ return '<option value="' + u.email + '" data-name="' + u.name + '">' + (u.name||u.email) + '</option>'; }).join('');
    var modal = document.getElementById('modal');
    var body = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (!modal||!body) return;
    var today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
    var week = new Date(Date.now()+7*24*3600000).toISOString().split('T')[0];
    body.innerHTML = '<h3 style="margin:0 0 16px;color:var(--text-primary);">Add On-Call Entry</h3>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Team Member</label><select id="ocUser" class="form-select">' + opts + '</select></div>' +
      '<div class="form-grid-2"><div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">From</label><input id="ocStart" class="form-input" type="date" value="' + today + '"></div>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">To</label><input id="ocEnd" class="form-input" type="date" value="' + week + '"></div></div>' +
      '<div style="text-align:right;margin-top:16px;"><button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Cancel</button> <button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitOnCall()">Save</button></div>';
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
  },

  submitOnCall: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var sel = document.getElementById('ocUser');
    var email = sel ? sel.value : '';
    var name = sel ? (sel.options[sel.selectedIndex]||{}).getAttribute('data-name')||'' : '';
    var entry = { email, name, startDate: (document.getElementById('ocStart')||{}).value||'', endDate: (document.getElementById('ocEnd')||{}).value||'' };
    if (!email) { self.showToast('Select a team member','warning'); return; }
    var r = await self.callAsync('saveOnCallEntry', entry);
    if (r && r.success) { self.closeModal(); self.showToast('On-call entry saved','success'); self.renderOnCall(); }
    else self.showToast('Error: '+(r?r.error:'unknown'),'error');
  },

  // ============================================================
  // CUSTOM FIELDS
  // ============================================================
  renderCustomFields: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('Custom Fields', 'Admin / Custom Fields');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Loading...</p></div>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('getCustomFields');
    var fields = (r && r.success) ? r.fields : [];
        var typeLabel = { text:'Text', number:'Number', dropdown:'Dropdown', date:'Date', checkbox:'Checkbox' };
    var html = '<div style="max-width:700px"><div class="card">';
    html += '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:16px;">';
    html += '<span class="card-title">Custom Issue Fields</span>';
    html += '<button class="btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="App.showAddFieldModal()">+ Add Field</button></div>';
    html += '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-bottom:14px;">Custom fields appear on all issue forms and detail pages.</p>';
    if (fields.length === 0) {
      html += '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim);">No custom fields yet.</p>';
    } else {
      fields.forEach(function(f) {
        html += '<div class="custom-field-row">';
        html += '<span style="flex:1;font-size:13px;color:var(--text-primary);font-weight:500;">' + self._esc(f.name) + '</span>';
        html += '<span style="font-size:11px;font-family:var(--font-mono);color:var(--text-muted);">' + (typeLabel[f.type]||f.type) + '</span>';
        if (f.required) html += '<span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--critical);">Required</span>';
        if (f.options && f.options.length) html += '<span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text-dim);">' + f.options.join(', ') + '</span>';
        html += '<button class="btn-danger btn-sm" onclick="App.deleteField(\'' + f.id + '\')">&#x2715;</button>';
        html += '</div>';
      });
    }
    html += '</div></div>';
    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

  showAddFieldModal: function() {
    var modal = document.getElementById('modal');
    var body = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (!modal||!body) return;
    body.innerHTML = '<h3 style="margin:0 0 16px;color:var(--text-primary);">Add Custom Field</h3>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Field Name</label><input id="cfName" class="form-input" placeholder="Customer Impact Score"></div>' +
      '<div class="form-grid-2"><div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Type</label>' +
      '<select id="cfType" class="form-select" onchange="App.toggleFieldOptions(this.value)">' +
      '<option value="text">Text</option><option value="number">Number</option><option value="dropdown">Dropdown</option><option value="date">Date</option><option value="checkbox">Checkbox</option></select></div>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label"><input type="checkbox" id="cfRequired"> Required</label></div></div>' +
      '<div class="form-group" id="cfOptionsGroup" style="display:none"><label class="form-label">Options (comma-separated)</label><input id="cfOptions" class="form-input" placeholder="Low, Medium, High, Critical"></div>' +
      '<div style="text-align:right;margin-top:16px;"><button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Cancel</button> <button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitField()">Add Field</button></div>';
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
  },

  toggleFieldOptions: function(type) {
    var g = document.getElementById('cfOptionsGroup');
    if (g) g.style.display = type === 'dropdown' ? 'block' : 'none';
  },

  submitField: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var name = (document.getElementById('cfName')||{}).value||'';
    var type = (document.getElementById('cfType')||{}).value||'text';
    var required = !!(document.getElementById('cfRequired')||{}).checked;
    var optStr = (document.getElementById('cfOptions')||{}).value||'';
    var options = optStr ? optStr.split(',').map(function(o){return o.trim();}) : [];
    if (!name) { self.showToast('Field name required','warning'); return; }
    var r = await self.callAsync('saveCustomField', { name, type, required, options });
    if (r && r.success) { self.closeModal(); self.showToast('Custom field added','success'); self.renderCustomFields(); }
    else self.showToast('Error: '+(r?r.error:'unknown'),'error');
  },

  deleteField: async function(fieldId) {
    var self = this;
    if (!confirm('Delete this custom field? Values on existing issues will be lost.')) return;
    var r = await self.callAsync('deleteCustomField', fieldId);
    if (r && r.success) { self.showToast('Field deleted','info'); self.renderCustomFields(); }
    else self.showToast('Error: '+(r?r.error:'unknown'),'error');
  },

  // ============================================================
  // RELEASE NOTES
  // ============================================================
  renderReleaseNotes: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('Release Notes', 'Admin / Release Notes');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Loading...</p></div>';
        var fromDate = new Date(Date.now() - 7*24*3600000).toISOString().split('T')[0];
    var toDate   = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
    var html = '<div style="max-width:800px">';
    html += '<div class="card mb-16"><div class="card-title mb-12">Generate Release Notes</div>';
    html += '<div class="form-grid-2">';
    html += '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">From Date</label><input id="rnFrom" class="form-input" type="date" value="' + fromDate + '"></div>';
    html += '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">To Date</label><input id="rnTo" class="form-input" type="date" value="' + toDate + '"></div></div>';
    html += '<div style="margin-top:12px;"><button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.generateReleaseNotes()">&#x2736; Generate with AI</button></div></div>';
    html += '<div id="rnOutput"></div></div>';
    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

  generateReleaseNotes: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var from = (document.getElementById('rnFrom')||{}).value;
    var to   = (document.getElementById('rnTo')||{}).value;
    var out  = document.getElementById('rnOutput');
    if (!out) return;
    out.innerHTML = '<div class="card"><p style="color:var(--text-muted);">&#x2736; AI is generating release notes...</p></div>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('generateReleaseNotes', from, to);
    if (!r || !r.success) { out.innerHTML = '<div class="card"><p style="color:var(--critical);">Error: ' + self._esc(r ? r.error : 'unknown') + '</p></div>'; return; }
    if (!r.notes) { out.innerHTML = '<div class="card"><p style="color:var(--text-muted);">' + (r.message||'No resolved issues in this period.') + '</p></div>'; return; }
    var n = r.notes;
        var html = '<div class="card">';
    html += '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;margin-bottom:16px;">';
    html += '<span class="release-badge">' + self._esc(n.version||'v1.0.0') + '</span>';
    html += '<span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);">' + (n.releaseDate||'') + '</span>';
    html += '<span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);">' + r.issueCount + ' issues included</span></div>';
    if (n.summary) html += '<p style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text-secondary);margin-bottom:16px;line-height:1.6;">' + self._esc(n.summary) + '</p>';
    if (n.highlights && n.highlights.length) {
      html += '<div class="release-section"><div class="analytics-card-title">Highlights</div>';
      n.highlights.forEach(function(h){ html += '<div class="ai-extraction-item"><div class="ai-extraction-dot"></div>' + self._esc(h) + '</div>'; });
      html += '</div>';
    }
    if (n.bugFixes && n.bugFixes.length) {
      html += '<div class="release-section"><div class="analytics-card-title">Bug Fixes</div>';
      n.bugFixes.forEach(function(f){
        html += '<div class="release-item"><span class="release-item-id">' + self._esc(f.id||'') + '</span><span style="color:var(--text-secondary);">' + self._esc(f.description||'') + '</span></div>';
      });
      html += '</div>';
    }
    if (n.improvements && n.improvements.length) {
      html += '<div class="release-section"><div class="analytics-card-title">Improvements</div>';
      n.improvements.forEach(function(i){
        html += '<div class="release-item"><span class="release-item-id" style="color:var(--text-muted);">' + self._esc(i.module||'') + '</span><span style="color:var(--text-secondary);">' + self._esc(i.description||'') + '</span></div>';
      });
      html += '</div>';
    }
    html += '</div>';
    out.innerHTML = html;
  },

  // ============================================================
  // AUDIT TRAIL
  // ============================================================
  renderAuditTrail: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('Audit Trail', 'Admin / Audit Trail');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Loading audit log...</p></div>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('getAuditTrail', {});
    if (!r || !r.success) { self.showPageError(area, r && r.error ? r.error : 'getAuditTrail failed. Admin role required. Redeploy Code.gs if needed.'); return; }
    var logs = r.logs || [];
        var html = '<div style="max-width:900px"><div class="card">';
    html += '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:16px;"><span class="card-title">Full Audit Trail</span>';
    html += '<span style="font-size:11px;font-family:var(--font-mono);color:var(--text-dim);">' + logs.length + ' entries</span></div>';
    if (logs.length === 0) {
      html += '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);">No audit entries yet.</p>';
    } else {
      logs.slice(0,100).forEach(function(l) {
        html += '<div class="ai-query-row">';
        html += '<span style="font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:10px;color:var(--accent);width:90px;flex-shrink:0;">' + self._esc(l.issueId||'SYSTEM') + '</span>';
        html += '<span style="flex:1;color:var(--text-secondary);font-size:12px;">' + self._esc(l.action||'') + '</span>';
        html += '<span style="color:var(--text-dim);font-size:11px;font-family:var(--font-mono);">' + self._esc(l.user||'') + '</span>';
        html += '<span style="color:var(--text-dim);font-size:10px;font-family:var(--font-mono);margin-left:10px;flex-shrink:0;">' + (l.timestamp ? new Date(l.timestamp).toLocaleString() : '') + '</span>';
        html += '</div>';
      });
    }
    html += '</div></div>';
    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

  // ============================================================
  // POST-MORTEM (called from issue detail)
  // ============================================================
  showPostMortem: async function(issueId) {
    var self = this;
    var modal = document.getElementById('modal');
    var body  = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (!modal||!body) return;
    body.innerHTML = '<p style="color:var(--text-muted);">&#x2736; Checking for existing post-mortem...</p>';
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
    var existing = await self.callAsync('getPostMortem', issueId);
        if (existing && existing.success && existing.postMortem) {
      self.renderPostMortemContent(body, existing.postMortem, existing.generatedAt);
    } else {
      body.innerHTML = '<h3 style="margin:0 0 12px;color:var(--text-primary);">Generate Post-Mortem</h3>' +
        '<p style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-bottom:16px;">AI will analyze the issue, comments, email thread, and activity log to generate a structured post-mortem.</p>' +
        '<div style="text-align:right;"><button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Cancel</button> ' +
        '<button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.runGeneratePostMortem(\'' + issueId + '\')">&#x2736; Generate</button></div>';
    }
  },

  runGeneratePostMortem: async function(issueId) {
    var self = this;
    var body = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (body) body.innerHTML = '<p style="color:var(--text-muted);">&#x2736; AI is writing post-mortem...</p>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('generatePostMortem', issueId);
    if (!r || !r.success) { if (body) body.innerHTML = '<p style="color:var(--critical);">Error: ' + self._esc(r?r.error:'unknown') + '</p>'; return; }
    var body2 = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (body2) this.renderPostMortemContent(body2, r.postMortem, new Date().toISOString());
    self.showToast('Post-mortem generated!','success');
  },

  renderPostMortemContent: function(container, pm, generatedAt) {
    if (!pm) return;
        var sevColors = { 'P1-Critical':'var(--critical)', 'P2-High':'var(--high)', 'P3-Medium':'var(--accent)', 'P4-Low':'var(--low)' };
    var html = '<div style="max-height:70vh;overflow-y:auto;">';
    html += '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;margin-bottom:16px;">';
    html += '<h3 style="margin:0;color:var(--text-primary);flex:1;">' + self._esc(pm.title||'Post-Mortem') + '</h3>';
    if (pm.severity) html += '<span style="color:' + (sevColors[pm.severity]||'var(--text-dim)') + ';font-size:12px;font-weight:700;">' + pm.severity + '</span>';
    html += '</div>';
    if (pm.summary) { html += '<div class="pm-section"><div class="pm-section-title">Summary</div><p style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text-secondary);line-height:1.6;">' + self._esc(pm.summary) + '</p></div>'; }
    if (pm.rootCause) { html += '<div class="pm-section"><div class="pm-section-title">Root Cause</div><p style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text-secondary);line-height:1.6;">' + self._esc(pm.rootCause) + '</p></div>'; }
    if (pm.impact) { html += '<div class="pm-section"><div class="pm-section-title">Impact</div><p style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text-secondary);line-height:1.6;">' + self._esc(pm.impact) + '</p></div>'; }
    if (pm.timeline && pm.timeline.length) {
      html += '<div class="pm-section"><div class="pm-section-title">Timeline</div><div class="pm-timeline">';
      pm.timeline.forEach(function(t){ html += '<div class="pm-timeline-item"><div class="pm-timeline-time">' + self._esc(t.time||'') + '</div><div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-secondary);">' + self._esc(t.event||'') + '</div></div>'; });
      html += '</div></div>';
    }
    if (pm.actionItems && pm.actionItems.length) {
      html += '<div class="pm-section"><div class="pm-section-title">Action Items</div>';
      pm.actionItems.forEach(function(a){ html += '<div class="pm-action-item"><div class="ai-extraction-dot" style="background:var(--accent);margin-top:2px;"></div><div><strong style="color:var(--text-primary);">' + self._esc(a.owner||'Team') + ':</strong> <span style="color:var(--text-secondary);">' + self._esc(a.action||'') + '</span>' + (a.deadline?' <span style="color:var(--text-dim);font-family:var(--font-mono);font-size:10px;">'+self._esc(a.deadline)+'</span>':'') + '</div></div>'; });
      html += '</div>';
    }
    if (pm.preventionMeasures && pm.preventionMeasures.length) {
      html += '<div class="pm-section"><div class="pm-section-title">Prevention Measures</div>';
      pm.preventionMeasures.forEach(function(p){ html += '<div class="ai-extraction-item"><div class="ai-extraction-dot" style="background:var(--low);"></div>' + self._esc(p) + '</div>'; });
      html += '</div>';
    }
    if (generatedAt) html += '<div style="margin-top:16px;font-size:10px;color:var(--text-dim);font-family:var(--font-mono);">Generated at ' + new Date(generatedAt).toLocaleString() + '</div>';
    html += '</div><div style="text-align:right;margin-top:12px;"><button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Close</button></div>';
    container.innerHTML = html;
  },

  // ============================================================
  // SAVED FILTERS UI (shown in issue list)
  // ============================================================
  loadSavedFiltersBar: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var r = await self.callAsync('getSavedFilters');
    var filters = (r && r.success) ? r.filters : [];
    var bar = document.getElementById('savedFiltersBar');
    if (!bar) return;
    if (filters.length === 0) { bar.style.display = 'none'; return; }
    bar.style.display = 'flex';
        var html = '<span style="font-size:10px;font-family:var(--font-mono);color:var(--text-dim);margin-right:8px;">SAVED:</span>';
    filters.forEach(function(f) {
      html += '<div class="saved-filter-chip" onclick="App.applySavedFilter(' + JSON.stringify(f.filters) + ')">' + self._esc(f.name) + '</div>';
    });
    html += '<button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" style="margin-left:auto" onclick="App.saveCurrentFilter()">Save Filter</button>';
    bar.innerHTML = html;
  },

  applySavedFilter: function(filtersObj) {
    self.issueFilters = Object.assign(self.issueFilters, filtersObj);
    self.renderIssueList();
  },

  saveCurrentFilter: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var name = prompt('Name this filter:');
    if (!name) return;
    var r = await self.callAsync('saveFilter', name, self.issueFilters, false);
    if (r && r.success) self.showToast('Filter saved: ' + name, 'success');
  },


  // ============================================================
  // SKELETON LOADERS
  // ============================================================
  skeletonDashboard: function() {
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    if (!area) return;
    var cards = '';
    for (var i = 0; i < 6; i++) {
      cards += '<div class="skel-card skeleton" style="height:100px"></div>';
    }
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="stats-grid">' + cards + '</div>' +
      '<div class="grid-2" style="margin-top:16px"><div class="skel-card skeleton" style="height:200px"></div><div class="skel-card skeleton" style="height:200px"></div></div>';
  },

  skeletonList: function() {
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    if (!area) return;
    var rows = '';
    for (var i = 0; i < 8; i++) {
      rows += '<div class="skeleton skel-line w-full" style="height:44px;margin-bottom:6px;border-radius:8px;"></div>';
    }
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="skeleton skel-title"></div>' + rows;
  },

  // ============================================================
  // ENHANCED TOAST (with progress bar)
  // ============================================================
  showToast: function(message, type, duration) {
    var self = this;
    type = type || 'info';
    duration = duration || 3500;
    var container = document.getElementById('toastContainer');
    if (!container) {
      container = document.createElement('div');
      container.id = 'toastContainer';
      container.className = 'toast-container';
      document.body.appendChild(container);
    }
    var icons = { success: '✓', error: '✕', warning: '⚠', info: 'ℹ' };
    var toast = document.createElement('div');
    toast.className = 'toast ' + type;
    toast.innerHTML =
      '<div class="toast-row">' +
        '<span style="font-size:14px;flex-shrink:0;">' + (icons[type]||'ℹ') + '</span>' +
        '<span style="flex:1;font-size:13px;">' + message + '</span>' +
        '<button onclick="this.closest(\'.toast\').remove()" style="background:none;border:none;color:var(--text-dim);cursor:pointer;font-size:14px;padding:0 0 0 8px;flex-shrink:0;">&#x2715;</button>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<div class="toast-progress"><div class="toast-progress-bar" id="tpb' + Date.now() + '"></div></div>';
    container.appendChild(toast);

    // Animate progress bar
    var pbId = toast.querySelector('[id^="tpb"]');
    if (pbId) {
      pbId.style.width = '100%';
      pbId.style.transition = 'width ' + duration + 'ms linear';
      setTimeout(function() { if (pbId) pbId.style.width = '0%'; }, 50);
    }

    // Auto-dismiss
    setTimeout(function() {
      toast.style.opacity = '0';
      toast.style.transform = 'translateX(16px)';
      toast.style.transition = 'opacity 0.3s, transform 0.3s';
      setTimeout(function() { if (toast.parentNode) toast.remove(); }, 320);
    }, duration);

    // Push to notification centre
    if (type === 'success' || type === 'error') {
      Notif.push(message.replace(/<[^>]+>/g,''), type);
    }
  },

  // ============================================================
  // ANIMATED STAT COUNTER
  // ============================================================
  animateCounter: function(el, target) {
    if (!el) return;
    var start = 0;
    var duration = 800;
    var startTime = null;
    function step(ts) {
      if (!startTime) startTime = ts;
      var progress = Math.min((ts - startTime) / duration, 1);
      var ease = 1 - Math.pow(1 - progress, 3);
      el.textContent = Math.round(start + (target - start) * ease);
      if (progress < 1) requestAnimationFrame(step);
    }
    requestAnimationFrame(step);
  },

  // ============================================================
  // HEATMAP BUILDER (for dashboard)
  // ============================================================
  buildHeatmap: function(issues) {
    var today = new Date();
    var days = [];
    for (var d = 89; d >= 0; d--) {
      var date = new Date(today);
      date.setDate(date.getDate() - d);
      days.push(date.toISOString().split('T')[0]);
    }
    var counts = {};
    issues.forEach(function(i) {
      var day = (i.createdDate || '').split('T')[0];
      if (day) counts[day] = (counts[day] || 0) + 1;
    });
    var max = Math.max.apply(null, Object.values(counts).concat([1]));
    var html = '<div class="heatmap-grid">';
    days.forEach(function(day) {
      var c = counts[day] || 0;
      var level = c === 0 ? '' : c <= max*0.2 ? 'h1' : c <= max*0.4 ? 'h2' : c <= max*0.6 ? 'h3' : c <= max*0.8 ? 'h4' : 'h5';
      html += '<div class="heatmap-cell ' + level + '" title="' + day + ': ' + c + ' issues"></div>';
    });
    html += '</div>';
    return html;
  },

  // ============================================================
  // ISSUE TEMPLATES (create issue page)
  // ============================================================
  getIssueTemplates: function() {
    return [
      {
        id: 'blank', icon: '&#x2610;', name: 'Blank', desc: 'Start fresh',
        fields: {}
      },
      {
        id: 'bug', icon: '&#x1F41B;', name: 'Bug Report', desc: 'Something is broken',
        fields: { priority: 'High', module: 'UI',
          description: 'Steps to Reproduce:\n1. \n2. \n3. \n\nExpected Behaviour:\n\nActual Behaviour:\n\nEnvironment:\n' }
      },
      {
        id: 'hotfix', icon: '&#x1F525;', name: 'Hotfix', desc: 'Critical production fix',
        fields: { priority: 'Critical', environment: 'Production', impact: 'Revenue',
          description: 'Production Issue:\n\nImpact:\n- Users affected:\n- Revenue impact:\n\nTemporary Workaround:\n\nProposed Fix:\n' }
      },
      {
        id: 'feature', icon: '&#x2605;', name: 'Feature Request', desc: 'New functionality',
        fields: { priority: 'Medium',
          description: 'User Story:\nAs a [role], I want [feature] so that [benefit].\n\nAcceptance Criteria:\n- [ ] \n- [ ] \n\nDesign Notes:\n' }
      },
      {
        id: 'security', icon: '&#x1F512;', name: 'Security', desc: 'Vulnerability or breach',
        fields: { priority: 'Critical', impact: 'Security', module: 'Authentication',
          description: 'Vulnerability Type:\n\nSeverity:\n\nSteps to Reproduce (DO NOT share publicly):\n\nAffected Systems:\n\nRemediation Plan:\n' }
      },
      {
        id: 'perf', icon: '&#x26A1;', name: 'Performance', desc: 'Slowness or degradation',
        fields: { priority: 'High', impact: 'Customer',
          description: 'Performance Issue:\n\nBaseline (before):\nCurrent (after):\n\nAffected Users/Endpoints:\n\nProfiling Data:\n' }
      }
    ];
  },

  applyTemplate: function(templateId) {
    var tpls = self.getIssueTemplates();
    var tpl = tpls.find(function(t){ return t.id === templateId; });
    if (!tpl) return;
    document.querySelectorAll('.template-card').forEach(function(c){
      c.classList.toggle('selected', c.dataset.templateId === templateId);
    });
    Object.keys(tpl.fields).forEach(function(field) {
      var el = document.getElementById('issue' + field.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + field.slice(1));
      if (!el) el = document.getElementById(field);
      if (el) el.value = tpl.fields[field];
    });
  },

  // ============================================================
  // INLINE STATUS CHANGE in issue list
  // ============================================================
  openStatusPicker: function(issueId, currentStatus, btnEl) {
    // Close any open pickers first
    document.querySelectorAll('.status-picker-dropdown.open').forEach(function(d){
      d.classList.remove('open');
    });
    var statuses = ['Open','Acknowledged','In Progress','Devlopment Required','Testing','Release required','Resolved','Closed'];
    var dd = document.createElement('div');
    dd.className = 'status-picker-dropdown open';
    statuses.forEach(function(s) {
      var opt = document.createElement('div');
      opt.className = 'status-pick-opt';
      opt.innerHTML = '<span style="width:8px;height:8px;border-radius:50%;background:var(--status-' + s.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g,'-') + ',var(--text-dim));flex-shrink:0;"></span>' + s;
      opt.onclick = function(e) {
        e.stopPropagation();
        App.inlineStatusChange(issueId, s);
        dd.remove();
      };
      dd.appendChild(opt);
    });
    btnEl.style.position = 'relative';
    btnEl.appendChild(dd);
    setTimeout(function() {
      document.addEventListener('click', function handler() {
        dd.remove();
        document.removeEventListener('click', handler);
      }, { once: true });
    }, 0);
  },

  inlineStatusChange: async function(issueId, newStatus) {
    var self = this;
    // Optimistic update
    var badge = document.querySelector('[data-issue-id="' + issueId + '"] .badge-status');
    if (badge) {
      badge.textContent = newStatus;
      badge.className = 'badge-status ' + newStatus.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g,'-');
      badge.closest('tr') && badge.closest('tr').classList.add('optimistic-update');
    }
    var r = await self.callAsync('updateIssueStatus', issueId, newStatus, '');
    if (r && r.success) {
      self.showToast('Status → ' + newStatus, 'success');
      Notif.push('Issue ' + issueId + ' status changed to ' + newStatus, 'info', issueId);
      // Refresh the issues cache
      self.allIssues = self.allIssues.map(function(i) {
        return i.id === issueId ? Object.assign({}, i, { status: newStatus }) : i;
      });
    } else {
      self.showToast('Failed: ' + (r ? r.error : 'unknown'), 'error');
      self.renderIssueList(); // revert by re-rendering
    }
  },

  // ============================================================
  // BULK ACTIONS
  // ============================================================
  _selectedIssues: new Set(),

  toggleIssueSelect: function(issueId, checkbox) {
    if (checkbox.checked) {
      this._selectedIssues.add(issueId);
    } else {
      this._selectedIssues.delete(issueId);
    }
    this._updateBulkBar();
  },

  selectAllIssues: function(checkbox) {
    var checkboxes = document.querySelectorAll('.issue-checkbox[data-issue-id]');
    checkboxes.forEach(function(cb) {
      cb.checked = checkbox.checked;
      if (checkbox.checked) App._selectedIssues.add(cb.dataset.issueId);
      else App._selectedIssues.delete(cb.dataset.issueId);
    });
    this._updateBulkBar();
  },

  _updateBulkBar: function() {
    var bar = document.getElementById('bulkBar');
    var count = document.getElementById('bulkCount');
    if (!bar) return;
    var n = this._selectedIssues.size;
    bar.classList.toggle('active', n > 0);
    if (count) count.textContent = n + ' selected';
  },

  bulkUpdateStatus: async function(status) {
    var self = this;
    if (!self._selectedIssues.size) return;
    if (!confirm('Update ' + self._selectedIssues.size + ' issues to "' + status + '"?')) return;
    var ids = Array.from(self._selectedIssues);
        self.showToast('Updating ' + ids.length + ' issues...', 'info');
    for (var i = 0; i < ids.length; i++) {
      await self.callAsync('updateIssueStatus', ids[i], status, '');
    }
    self._selectedIssues.clear();
    self.showToast('Updated ' + ids.length + ' issues to ' + status, 'success');
    self.renderIssueList();
  },

  openModal: function(title, contentHtml) {
    var modal = document.getElementById('modal');
    var titleEl = document.getElementById('modal-title');
    var body = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (!modal || !titleEl || !body) return;
    titleEl.textContent = title;
    body.innerHTML = contentHtml;
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
  },

  bulkAssign: async function() {
    var self = this;
    if (!self._selectedIssues.size) return;
    var ids = Array.from(self._selectedIssues);
    var body = '<p style="margin:0 0 12px;color:var(--text-muted);">Assign ' + ids.length + ' selected issues to a developer.</p>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Developer email</label>' +
      '<input id="bulkAssignEmail" class="form-input" placeholder="dev@example.com"></div>' +
      '<div style="text-align:right;margin-top:16px">' +
      '<button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Cancel</button> ' +
      '<button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitBulkAssign()">Assign</button></div>';
    self.openModal('Bulk Assign', body);
  },

  submitBulkAssign: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var email = (document.getElementById('bulkAssignEmail')||{}).value.trim();
    if (!email) { self.showToast('Enter an email address', 'warning'); return; }
    var ids = Array.from(self._selectedIssues);
    self.closeModal();
    self.showToast('Assigning ' + ids.length + ' issues...', 'info');
    for (var i = 0; i < ids.length; i++) {
      await self.callAsync('assignIssue', ids[i], email);
    }
    self._selectedIssues.clear();
    self.showToast('Assigned ' + ids.length + ' issues to ' + email, 'success');
    self.renderIssueList();
  },

  bulkChangePriority: async function() {
    var self = this;
    if (!self._selectedIssues.size) return;
    var ids = Array.from(self._selectedIssues);
    var body = '<p style="margin:0 0 12px;color:var(--text-muted);">Select the new priority for ' + ids.length + ' issues.</p>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Priority</label>' +

        '<option value="Critical">Critical</option>' +
        '<option value="High">High</option>' +
        '<option value="Medium">Medium</option>' +
        '<option value="Low">Low</option>' +
      '</select></div>' +
      '<div style="text-align:right;margin-top:16px">' +
      '<button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Cancel</button> ' +
      '<button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitBulkPriority()">Update priority</button></div>';
    self.openModal('Bulk Priority Update', body);
  },

  submitBulkPriority: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var priority = (document.getElementById('bulkPrioritySelect')||{}).value;
    if (!priority) { self.showToast('Select a priority', 'warning'); return; }
    var ids = Array.from(self._selectedIssues);
    self.closeModal();
    self.showToast('Updating priority for ' + ids.length + ' issues...', 'info');
    for (var i = 0; i < ids.length; i++) {
      await self.callAsync('updateIssuePriority', ids[i], priority);
    }
    self._selectedIssues.clear();
    self.showToast('Priority updated for ' + ids.length + ' issues', 'success');
    self.renderIssueList();
  },

  bulkAddTag: async function() {
    var self = this;
    if (!self._selectedIssues.size) return;
    var ids = Array.from(self._selectedIssues);
    var body = '<p style="margin:0 0 12px;color:var(--text-muted);">Add a tag to ' + ids.length + ' selected issues.</p>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Tag label</label>' +
      '<input id="bulkTagInput" class="form-input" placeholder="customer"></div>' +

      '<button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitBulkTag()">Add tag</button></div>';
    self.openModal('Bulk Tag Add', body);
  },

  submitBulkTag: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var tag = ((document.getElementById('bulkTagInput')||{}).value || '').trim().toLowerCase();
    var color = (document.getElementById('bulkTagColor')||{}).value || '#534AB7';
    if (!tag) { self.showToast('Enter a tag label', 'warning'); return; }
    var ids = Array.from(self._selectedIssues);
    self.closeModal();
    self.showToast('Adding tag to ' + ids.length + ' issues...', 'info');
    for (var i = 0; i < ids.length; i++) {
      await self.callAsync('addIssueTag', ids[i], tag, color);
    }
    self._selectedIssues.clear();
    self.showToast('Tag added to ' + ids.length + ' issues', 'success');
    self.renderIssueList();
  },

  bulkAddComment: async function() {
    var self = this;
    if (!self._selectedIssues.size) return;
    var ids = Array.from(self._selectedIssues);
    var body = '<p style="margin:0 0 12px;color:var(--text-muted);">Add a comment to ' + ids.length + ' selected issues.</p>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Comment</label>' +
      '<textarea id="bulkCommentInput" class="form-input" style="min-height:140px;resize:vertical;" placeholder="Write a message that will be added to each selected issue."></textarea></div>' +
