      '<button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitBulkComment()">Add comment</button></div>';
    self.openModal('Bulk Comment Preview', body);
  },

  submitBulkComment: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var comment = (document.getElementById('bulkCommentInput')||{}).value.trim();
    if (!comment) { self.showToast('Enter a comment', 'warning'); return; }
    var ids = Array.from(self._selectedIssues);
    self.closeModal();
    self.showToast('Adding comment to ' + ids.length + ' issues...', 'info');
    for (var i = 0; i < ids.length; i++) {
      await self.callAsync('addComment', ids[i], comment);
    }
    self._selectedIssues.clear();
    self.showToast('Comments added to ' + ids.length + ' issues', 'success');
    self.renderIssueList();
  },

  // ============================================================
  // TIME TRACKING
  // ============================================================
  showLogTimeModal: function(issueId) {
    var modal = document.getElementById('modal');
    var body  = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (!modal || !body) return;
    body.innerHTML =
      '<h3 style="margin:0 0 14px;color:var(--text-primary);">Log Time   ' + issueId + '</h3>' +
      '<div class="form-grid-2">' +
        '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Hours Spent</label>' +
        '<input id="logHours" class="form-input" type="number" min="0.5" max="24" step="0.5" value="1" placeholder="1.5"></div>' +
        '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Date</label>' +
        '<input id="logDate" class="form-input" type="date" value="' + new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0] + '"></div>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Work Note</label>' +
      '<input id="logNote" class="form-input" placeholder="What did you work on?"></div>' +
      '<div style="text-align:right;margin-top:14px;">' +
        '<button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Cancel</button> ' +
        '<button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitTimeLog(\'' + issueId + '\')">Log Time</button>' +
      '</div>';
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
  },

  submitTimeLog: async function(issueId) {
    var self = this;
    var hours = parseFloat((document.getElementById('logHours')||{}).value || 0);
    var note  = (document.getElementById('logNote')||{}).value || '';
    var date  = (document.getElementById('logDate')||{}).value || new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
    if (!hours || hours <= 0) { self.showToast('Enter valid hours','warning'); return; }
    var r = await self.callAsync('logTime', issueId, hours, note, date);
    if (r && r.success) {
      self.closeModal();
      self.showToast(hours + 'h logged on ' + issueId, 'success');
    } else {
      // Graceful fallback   add as comment
      var commentText = '[Time Log] ' + hours + 'h on ' + date + (note ? ': ' + note : '');
      await self.call('addComment', issueId, commentText);
      self.closeModal();
      self.showToast(hours + 'h logged as comment', 'success');
    }
  },

  // ============================================================
  // WATCHERS / SUBSCRIBE
  // ============================================================
  toggleWatcher: async function(issueId) {
    var self = this;
    var email = App.currentUser ? App.currentUser.email : '';
    if (!email) return;
    var r = await self.callAsync('toggleWatcher', issueId, email);
    var btn = document.getElementById('watcherBtn');
    if (r && r.success) {
      var watching = r.watching;
      if (btn) {
        btn.className = 'watcher-chip ' + (watching ? 'watching' : '');
        btn.innerHTML = watching ? 'Watching' : 'Watch';
      }
      self.showToast(watching ? 'Watching this issue' : 'Unwatched', 'info');
    }
  },

  // ============================================================
  // MOBILE NAV ACTIVE STATE
  // ============================================================
  updateMobileNav: function(page) {
    document.querySelectorAll('.mobile-nav-item[data-page]').forEach(function(btn) {
      btn.classList.toggle('active', btn.dataset.page === page);
    });
  },



  // ============================================================
  // ISSUE TAGS
  // ============================================================
  renderTagsRow: function(tags, issueId, editable) {
    var self = this;
    var pills = (tags||[]).map(function(t){
      return '<span class="tag-pill" style="background:' + t.color + '22;color:' + t.color + ';border:1px solid ' + t.color + '44">'
        + self._esc(t.label)
        + (editable ? '<button class="tag-remove" onclick="App.removeTag(\'' + t.id + '\',\'' + issueId + '\')" title="Remove">&times;</button>' : '')
        + '</span>';
    }).join('');
    if (!editable) return '<div class="tags-row">' + pills + '</div>';
    return '<div class="tags-row">' + pills
      + '<input class="tag-add-input" id="tagInput_' + issueId + '" placeholder="+ tag" maxlength="20"'
      + ' onkeydown="if(event.key===\'Enter\'||event.key===\',\'){event.preventDefault();App.addTagFromInput(\'' + issueId + '\')}">'
      + '</div>';
  },

  addTagFromInput: async function(issueId) {
    var self = this;
    var el = document.getElementById('tagInput_' + issueId);
    var label = (el ? el.value.replace(',','') : '').trim().toLowerCase();
    if (!label) return;
    var colors = ['#534AB7','#0F6E56','#993C1D','#185FA5','#854F0B','#993556'];
    var color = colors[label.charCodeAt(0) % colors.length];
    var r = await self.callAsync('addIssueTag', issueId, label, color);
    if (r && r.success) {
      if (el) el.value = '';
      self.showToast('Tag added', 'success');
      self.renderIssueDetail(issueId);
    }
  },

  removeTag: async function(tagId, issueId) {
    var self = this;
    var r = await self.callAsync('removeIssueTag', tagId);
    if (r && r.success) self.renderIssueDetail(issueId);
  },

  // ============================================================
  // ISSUE VOTING
  // ============================================================
  voteOnIssue: async function(issueId, btn) {
    var self = this;
    var r = await self.callAsync('voteIssue', issueId);
    if (r && r.success) {
      var countEl = btn ? btn.querySelector('.vote-count') : document.querySelector('[data-vote-id="' + issueId + '"] .vote-count');
      if (countEl) {
        var cur = parseInt(countEl.textContent) || 0;
        countEl.textContent = r.voted ? cur + 1 : Math.max(0, cur - 1);
      }
      if (btn) btn.classList.toggle('voted', r.voted);
      self.showToast(r.voted ? 'Upvoted' : 'Vote removed', 'info');
    }
  },

  // ============================================================
  // CO-ASSIGNEES
  // ============================================================
  showCoAssignModal: async function(issueId) {
    var self = this;
    var modal = document.getElementById('modal');
    var body  = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (!modal || !body) return;
    var usersR = await self.callAsync('getUsers', true);
    var coR    = await self.callAsync('getCoAssignees', issueId);
    var users = (usersR && usersR.success) ? usersR.users : [];
    var co    = (coR && coR.success) ? coR.coAssignees : [];
    var opts = users.map(function(u){ return '<option value="' + u.email + '">' + self._esc(u.name||u.email) + ' (' + u.role + ')</option>'; }).join('');
    body.innerHTML = '<h3 style="margin:0 0 14px;color:var(--text-primary)">Co-Assignees   ' + issueId + '</h3>'
      + '<div style="margin-bottom:12px">' + (co.length ? co.map(function(e){ return '<span class="co-assignee-chip">' + self._esc(e) + '<button class="rm" onclick="App.removeCoAssignee(\'' + issueId + '\',\'' + e + '\',this)">×</button></span>'; }).join('') : '<span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim)">No co-assignees yet</span>') + '</div>'
      + '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Add co-assignee</label>'
      + '<select id="coAssignSel" class="form-select"><option value="">Select person</option>' + opts + '</select></div>'
      + '<div style="text-align:right;margin-top:12px"><button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Close</button> <button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.addCoAssigneeSubmit(\'' + issueId + '\')">Add</button></div>';
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
  },

  addCoAssigneeSubmit: async function(issueId) {
    var self = this;
    var el = document.getElementById('coAssignSel');
    var email = el ? el.value : '';
    if (!email) return;
    var r = await self.callAsync('addCoAssignee', issueId, email);
    if (r && r.success) { self.closeModal(); self.showToast('Co-assignee added', 'success'); self.renderIssueDetail(issueId); }
    else self.showToast('Failed: ' + (r ? r.error : 'unknown'), 'error');
  },

  removeCoAssignee: async function(issueId, email, btn) {
    var self = this;
    var r = await self.callAsync('removeCoAssignee', issueId, email);
    if (r && r.success) {
      self.showToast('Removed', 'info');
      var chip = btn ? btn.closest('.co-assignee-chip') : null;
      if (chip) chip.remove();
    }
  },

  // ============================================================
  // DUE DATE
  // ============================================================
  showDueDateModal: async function(issueId) {
    var self = this;
    var modal = document.getElementById('modal');
    var body  = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (!modal || !body) return;
    body.innerHTML = '<h3 style="margin:0 0 14px;color:var(--text-primary)">Set Due Date</h3>'
      + '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Due Date</label>'
      + '<input id="dueDateInput" type="date" class="form-input" value="' + new Date(Date.now()+7*24*3600000).toISOString().split('T')[0] + '">'
      + '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);margin-top:4px">A reminder email will be sent 24 hours before the due date</div></div>'
      + '<div style="text-align:right;margin-top:14px"><button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Cancel</button> <button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.saveDueDate(\'' + issueId + '\')">Save</button></div>';
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
  },

  saveDueDate: async function(issueId) {
    var self = this;
    var el = document.getElementById('dueDateInput');
    var date = el ? el.value : '';
    if (!date) return;
    var r = await self.callAsync('setIssueDueDate', issueId, date);
    if (r && r.success) { self.closeModal(); self.showToast('Due date set', 'success'); self.renderIssueDetail(issueId); }
    else self.showToast('Failed: ' + (r ? r.error : 'unknown'), 'error');
  },

  // ============================================================
  // AI TRIAGE ON CREATE
  // ============================================================
  runAITriage: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var title = (document.getElementById('issueTitle')||{}).value||'';
    var desc  = (document.getElementById('issueDesc')||{}).value||'';
    if (!title.trim()) { self.showToast('Enter a title first', 'warning'); return; }
    var btn = document.getElementById('aiTriageBtn');
    if (btn) { btn.disabled = true; btn.textContent = '&#x2736; Analysing...'; }
    var r = await self.callAsync('getAITriage', title, desc);
    if (btn) { btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = '&#x2736; AI Triage'; }
    if (!r || !r.success) { self.showToast('AI unavailable', 'warning'); return; }
    var t = r.triage;
    var card = document.getElementById('aiTriageCard');
    if (card) {
      card.style.display = 'block';
      card.innerHTML = '<div class="ai-triage-title">&#x2736; AI Triage Suggestion</div>'
        + (t.priority ? '<div class="ai-triage-row"><span style="color:var(--text-dim);width:80px">Priority</span><span class="badge priority-'+(t.priority||'').toLowerCase()+'">' + t.priority + '</span><button class="ai-triage-apply" onclick="App.applyTriagePriority(\'' + t.priority + '\')">Apply</button></div>' : '')
        + (t.module ? '<div class="ai-triage-row"><span style="color:var(--text-dim);width:80px">Module</span><span>' + self._esc(t.module) + '</span><button class="ai-triage-apply" onclick="App.applyTriageModule(\'' + t.module + '\')">Apply</button></div>' : '')
        + (t.suggestedAssignee ? '<div class="ai-triage-row"><span style="color:var(--text-dim);width:80px">Assignee</span><span>' + self._esc(t.suggestedAssignee) + '</span><button class="ai-triage-apply" onclick="App.applyTriageAssignee(\'' + t.suggestedAssignee + '\')">Apply</button></div>' : '')
        + (t.reasoning ? '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-top:8px;font-style:italic">' + self._esc(t.reasoning) + '</div>' : '')
        + (t.tags && t.tags.length ? '<div class="ai-triage-row" style="margin-top:6px"><span style="color:var(--text-dim);width:80px">Tags</span><span>' + t.tags.map(function(tag){ return '<span style="background:var(--accent-dim);color:var(--accent);padding:1px 7px;border-radius:999px;font-size:10px;margin-right:3px">'+self._esc(tag)+'</span>'; }).join('') + '</span></div>' : '');
    }
  },

  applyTriagePriority: function(p) { var el = document.getElementById('issuePriority'); if (el) { el.value = p; this.showToast('Priority set to ' + p, 'info'); } },
  applyTriageModule:   function(m) { var el = document.getElementById('issueModule');   if (el) { el.value = m; this.showToast('Module set to ' + m, 'info'); } },
  applyTriageAssignee: function(e) { var el = document.getElementById('issueAssignee'); if (el) { el.value = e; this.showToast('Assignee set', 'info'); } },

  // ============================================================
  // CONTEXT MENU
  // ============================================================
  initContextMenu: function() {
    var self = this;
    var menu = document.getElementById('contextMenu');
    if (!menu) return;
    document.addEventListener('contextmenu', function(e) {
      var row = e.target.closest('[data-issue-id]');
      if (!row) return;
      e.preventDefault();
      var id = row.dataset.issueId;
      self._ctxIssueId = id;
      menu.style.left = Math.min(e.clientX, window.innerWidth-200) + 'px';
      menu.style.top  = Math.min(e.clientY, window.innerHeight-200) + 'px';
      menu.classList.add('open');
    });
    document.addEventListener('click', function() { menu.classList.remove('open'); });
    document.getElementById('cmOpen').onclick    = function() { if (self._ctxIssueId) self.navigate('issue-detail', { id: self._ctxIssueId }); };
    document.getElementById('cmCopyId').onclick  = function() { if (self._ctxIssueId) { navigator.clipboard.writeText(self._ctxIssueId).catch(function(){}); self.showToast(self._ctxIssueId + ' copied', 'success'); } };
    document.getElementById('cmStatus').onclick  = function() { if (self._ctxIssueId) self.openStatusPicker(self._ctxIssueId, '', document.querySelector('[data-issue-id="' + self._ctxIssueId + '"]') || document.body); };
    document.getElementById('cmAssign').onclick  = function() { if (self._ctxIssueId) self.showAssignModal(self._ctxIssueId); };
    document.getElementById('cmPin').onclick     = function() { if (self._ctxIssueId) self.togglePin(self._ctxIssueId); };
    document.getElementById('cmVote').onclick    = function() { if (self._ctxIssueId) self.voteOnIssue(self._ctxIssueId, null); };
  },

  copyIssueId: function(id) {
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(id).then(function(){ }).catch(function(){});
    this.showToast(id + ' copied to clipboard', 'success');
  },

  // ============================================================
  // ANNOUNCEMENTS
  // ============================================================
  loadAnnouncements: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var r = await self.callAsync('getAnnouncements');
    var area = document.getElementById('announcementArea');
    if (!area || !r || !r.success || !r.announcements.length) return;
    var dismissed = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('tt_dismissed_ann') || '[]');
    var active = r.announcements.filter(function(a){ return dismissed.indexOf(a.id) === -1; });
    if (!active.length) return;
    area.innerHTML = active.map(function(a) {
      return '<div class="announcement-banner ' + (a.type||'info') + '">'
        + '<span>' + self._esc(a.message) + '</span>'
        + '<button class="ann-dismiss" onclick="App.dismissAnn(\'' + a.id + '\')" title="Dismiss">&#x2715;</button>'
        + '</div>';
    }).join('');
  },

  dismissAnn: function(id) {
    var dismissed = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('tt_dismissed_ann') || '[]');
    dismissed.push(id);
    localStorage.setItem('tt_dismissed_ann', JSON.stringify(dismissed));
    var area = document.getElementById('announcementArea');
    if (area) {
      var banners = area.querySelectorAll('.announcement-banner');
      banners.forEach(function(b) { if (b.querySelector('[onclick*="' + id + '"]')) b.remove(); });
    }
  },

  showAnnouncementModal: function() {
    var modal = document.getElementById('modal');
    var body  = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (!modal || !body) return;
    body.innerHTML = '<h3 style="margin:0 0 14px;color:var(--text-primary)">Post Announcement</h3>'
      + '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Message</label>'
      + '<textarea id="annMsg" class="form-textarea" style="min-height:80px" placeholder="Deploy scheduled for 2pm today. Expected downtime: 10 minutes."></textarea></div>'
      + '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Type</label>'
      + '<select id="annType" class="form-select"><option value="info">Info</option><option value="warning">Warning</option><option value="critical">Critical</option></select></div>'
      + '<div style="text-align:right;margin-top:14px"><button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Cancel</button> <button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.submitAnnouncement()">Post</button></div>';
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
  },

  submitAnnouncement: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var msg  = (document.getElementById('annMsg')||{}).value||'';
    var type = (document.getElementById('annType')||{}).value||'info';
    if (!msg.trim()) { self.showToast('Message required', 'warning'); return; }
    var r = await self.callAsync('saveAnnouncement', msg, type);
    if (r && r.success) { self.closeModal(); self.showToast('Announcement posted', 'success'); self.loadAnnouncements(); }
    else self.showToast('Failed', 'error');
  },

  // ============================================================
  // AI SPRINT PLANNER PAGE
  // ============================================================
  renderSprintPlanner: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('AI Sprint Planner', 'Sprints / AI Planner');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div style="max-width:700px"><div class="card"><div class="card-title mb-12">&#x2736; AI Sprint Planner</div>'
      + '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-bottom:16px">Tell Gemini your team\'s total sprint capacity and it will recommend which open issues to include, in priority order.</p>'
      + '<div class="form-grid-2 mb-16"><div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Total Sprint Capacity (hours)</label><input id="sprintCapacity" class="form-input" type="number" value="80" min="1"></div></div>'
      + '<button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.runAISprintPlanner()">&#x2736; Generate Sprint Plan</button>'
      + '<div id="sprintPlanResult" style="margin-top:16px"></div></div></div>';
  },

  runAISprintPlanner: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var cap = parseInt((document.getElementById('sprintCapacity')||{}).value||80);
    var result = document.getElementById('sprintPlanResult');
    if (result) result.innerHTML = '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted)">&#x2736; Gemini is planning your sprint...</p>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('getAISprintPlan', cap);
    if (!r || !r.success || !r.plan) { if (result) result.innerHTML = '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--critical)">AI unavailable. Set a Gemini API key in Settings → AI & Gemini.</p>'; return; }
    var p = r.plan;
    var html = '<div class="card-title mb-12">Recommended Sprint (' + (p.totalEstimatedHours||'?') + 'h of ' + cap + 'h)</div>';
    if (p.advice) html += '<div class="ai-issue-summary-card" style="margin-bottom:12px"><span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-secondary)">' + self._esc(p.advice) + '</span></div>';
    if (p.sprintIssues && p.sprintIssues.length) {
      html += (p.sprintIssues||[]).map(function(i,idx) {
        return '<div class="flag-row"><div class="flag-info"><div class="flag-name"><span style="font-family:var(--font-mono);color:var(--accent);font-size:11px">' + i.id + '</span></div><div class="flag-desc">' + self._esc(i.reason||'') + '</div></div><span style="font-size:11px;font-family:var(--font-mono);color:var(--text-dim)">' + (i.estimatedHours||'?') + 'h</span></div>';
      }).join('');
    }
    if (result) result.innerHTML = html;
  },

  // ============================================================
  // LEADERBOARD PAGE
  // ============================================================
  renderLeaderboard: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('Dev Leaderboard', 'Analytics / Leaderboard');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Loading...</p></div>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('getDevLeaderboard');
    if (!r || !r.success) { self.showPageError(area, r && r.error ? r.error : 'Failed'); return; }
    var medals = ['&#x1F947;','&#x1F948;','&#x1F949;'];
    var html = '<div style="max-width:600px"><div class="card"><div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:16px"><span class="card-title">This Month\'s Leaderboard</span><span style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);font-family:var(--font-mono)">Since ' + r.period + '</span></div>';
    r.board.forEach(function(dev, idx) {
      html += '<div class="leaderboard-row">'
        + '<div class="leaderboard-rank">' + (medals[idx] || (idx+1)) + '</div>'
        + '<div class="leaderboard-name">' + self._esc(dev.name) + '</div>'
        + '<div class="leaderboard-stat" title="Issues resolved">' + dev.resolved + ' resolved</div>'
        + '<div class="leaderboard-stat" style="min-width:80px" title="Avg hours to resolve">' + dev.avgHours + 'h avg</div>'
        + '</div>';
    });
    if (!r.board.length) html += '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim)">No resolved issues this month yet.</p>';
    html += '</div></div>';
    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

  // ============================================================
  // CFD CHART PAGE
  // ============================================================
  renderCFD: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('Cumulative Flow', 'Analytics / CFD');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Loading CFD data...</p></div>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('getCFDData');
    if (!r || !r.success) { self.showPageError(area, r && r.error ? r.error : 'Failed'); return; }
    var days = r.daily; var statuses = r.statuses;
    var colors = { 'Open':'var(--critical)','In Progress':'var(--high)','Testing':'var(--accent)','Resolved':'var(--low)','Closed':'var(--text-dim)' };
    area.innerHTML = '<div style="max-width:900px"><div class="card"><div class="card-title mb-16">Cumulative Flow Diagram   last 30 days</div>'
      + '<div id="cfdCanvas" style="height:220px;position:relative;overflow:hidden;background:var(--bg-elevated);border-radius:8px;padding:10px">'
      + '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);text-align:center;margin-top:80px">CFD chart renders here   connect Chart.js for full visualisation</div>'
      + '</div>'
      + '<div style="display:flex;gap:16px;flex-wrap:wrap;margin-top:12px">'
      + statuses.map(function(s){ var c=colors[s]||'var(--text-dim)'; return '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:5px;font-size:11px;color:var(--text-secondary)"><div style="width:10px;height:10px;border-radius:2px;background:'+c+';flex-shrink:0"></div>' + s + '</div>'; }).join('')
      + '</div></div></div>';
  },

  // ============================================================
  // ISSUE FORECASTING PAGE
  // ============================================================
  renderForecast: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('Issue Forecast', 'Analytics / Forecast');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Calculating forecast...</p></div>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('forecastResolution', 30);
    if (!r || !r.success) { self.showPageError(area, r && r.error ? r.error : 'Failed'); return; }
    var pct = r.openCount > 0 ? Math.round((r.resolvedByTarget / r.openCount) * 100) : 100;
    var html = '<div style="max-width:700px">'
      + '<div class="card mb-16 forecast-hero">'
      + '<div class="forecast-big" style="color:' + (pct >= 80 ? 'var(--low)' : pct >= 50 ? 'var(--accent)' : 'var(--critical)') + '">' + pct + '%</div>'
      + '<div style="font-size:14px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-top:6px">of open issues resolved in 30 days</div>'
      + '<div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim);font-family:var(--font-mono);margin-top:4px">at current rate of ' + r.dailyRate + ' issues/day</div>'
      + '</div>'
      + '<div class="grid-3">'
      + '<div class="stat-card-animated"><div class="stat-number">' + r.openCount + '</div><div class="stat-label">Open Now</div></div>'
      + '<div class="stat-card-animated"><div class="stat-number">' + r.resolvedByTarget + '</div><div class="stat-label">Resolved by ' + new Date(Date.now()+30*24*3600000).toLocaleDateString() + '</div></div>'
      + '<div class="stat-card-animated"><div class="stat-number">' + r.daysToResolveAll + '</div><div class="stat-label">Days to Clear Backlog</div></div>'
      + '</div></div>';
    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

  // ============================================================
  // REPEAT OFFENDERS PAGE
  // ============================================================
  renderRepeatOffenders: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('Repeat Offenders', 'Analytics / Repeat Offenders');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Loading...</p></div>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('getRepeatOffenders');
    if (!r || !r.success) { self.showPageError(area, r && r.error ? r.error : 'Failed'); return; }
    var offenders = r.offenders || [];
    var html = '<div style="max-width:700px"><div class="card">';
    html += '<div class="card-title mb-4">Repeat Offenders</div>';
    html += '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-bottom:14px">Issues that have been reopened 2 or more times. These often indicate incomplete fixes or unclear requirements.</p>';
    if (!offenders.length) {
      html += '<div class="empty-state-v2"><div class="empty-icon-ring">&#x2714;</div><div class="empty-title">No repeat offenders</div><div class="empty-subtitle">All issues have been closed cleanly.</div></div>';
    } else {
      offenders.forEach(function(i) {
        html += '<div class="flag-row">'
          + '<div class="flag-info"><div class="flag-name">'
          + '<span style="font-family:var(--font-mono);color:var(--accent);font-size:11px;cursor:pointer" onclick="App.navigate(\'issue-detail\',{id:\'' + i.id + '\'})">' + i.id + '</span> ' + self._esc(i.title.substring(0,50))
          + '</div><div class="flag-desc">' + i.priority + ' · ' + i.status + ' · ' + (i.module||'?') + '</div></div>'
          + '<span class="regression-badge">&#x21BA; ' + i.reopenCount + 'x</span>'
          + '</div>';
      });
    }
    html += '</div></div>';
    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

  // ============================================================
  // FIRST RESPONSE STATS PAGE
  // ============================================================
  renderFirstResponse: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('First Response Time', 'Analytics / First Response');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Calculating...</p></div>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('getFirstResponseStats');
    if (!r || !r.success) { self.showPageError(area, r && r.error ? r.error : 'Failed'); return; }
    var html = '<div style="max-width:700px">'
      + '<div class="card mb-16" style="text-align:center;padding:28px">'
      + '<div style="font-size:56px;font-weight:800;color:var(--text-primary);letter-spacing:-3px;line-height:1">' + r.avgHours + 'h</div>'
      + '<div style="font-size:14px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-top:6px">Average first response time</div>'
      + '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);font-family:var(--font-mono);margin-top:3px">Based on ' + r.sampleSize + ' issues</div>'
      + '</div>'
      + '<div class="card"><div class="card-title mb-12">By Developer</div>';
    Object.entries(r.byDev || {}).sort(function(a,b){ return a[1]-b[1]; }).forEach(function(entry) {
      html += '<div class="leaderboard-row"><div class="leaderboard-name">' + self._esc(entry[0]) + '</div><div class="leaderboard-stat">' + entry[1] + 'h</div></div>';
    });
    if (!Object.keys(r.byDev||{}).length) html += '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim)">No data yet.</p>';
    html += '</div></div>';
    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

  // ============================================================
  // AI ESCALATION DRAFTER on issue detail
  // ============================================================
  showEscalationDraft: async function(issueId) {
    var self = this;
    var modal = document.getElementById('modal');
    var body  = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (!modal||!body) return;
    body.innerHTML = '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted)">&#x2736; Gemini is drafting the escalation email...</p>';
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
    var r = await self.callAsync('draftEscalationEmail', issueId);
    if (!r || !r.success) { body.innerHTML = '<p style="color:var(--critical)">AI unavailable. Please set a Gemini key in Settings.</p><div style="text-align:right;margin-top:12px"><button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Close</button></div>'; return; }
    var d = r.draft;
    body.innerHTML = '<h3 style="margin:0 0 12px;color:var(--text-primary)">Escalation Email Draft</h3>'
      + '<div class="form-group mb-8"><label class="form-label">Subject</label><input class="form-input" value="' + self._esc(d.subject||'') + '" id="escSubject"></div>'
      + '<div class="form-group mb-12"><label class="form-label">Body</label><textarea class="form-textarea" style="min-height:140px" id="escBody">' + self._esc(d.body||'') + '</textarea></div>'
      + (d.keyPoints && d.keyPoints.length ? '<div style="margin-bottom:12px">' + d.keyPoints.map(function(p){ return '<div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-secondary);padding:3px 0">• ' + self._esc(p) + '</div>'; }).join('') + '</div>' : '')
      + '<div style="text-align:right"><button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Cancel</button> <button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.sendEscalationEmail()">Send Email</button></div>';
  },

  sendEscalationEmail: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var subject = (document.getElementById('escSubject')||{}).value||'';
    var body    = (document.getElementById('escBody')||{}).value||'';
    if (!subject || !body) return;
    self.closeModal();
    self.showToast('Escalation email copied   paste into your email client', 'info');
    try { await navigator.clipboard.writeText('Subject: ' + subject + '\n\n' + body); } catch(e) {}
  },

  // ============================================================
  // AI ROOT CAUSE CLUSTERING
  // ============================================================
  renderRootCauseClusters: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.setPage('Root Cause Clusters', 'Analytics / Root Causes');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>&#x2736; Gemini is analysing patterns...</p></div>';
    var r = await self.callAsync('getRootCauseClusters');
    if (!r || !r.success) { self.showPageError(area, r && r.error ? r.error : 'Failed'); return; }
    var html = '<div style="max-width:800px">';
    if (r.overallPattern) html += '<div class="ai-issue-summary-card mb-16"><div class="ai-issue-summary-header"><span style="font-size:16px">&#x2736;</span><span class="ai-issue-summary-title">This Week\'s Pattern</span></div><p style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text-secondary)">' + self._esc(r.overallPattern) + '</p></div>';
    if (!r.clusters || !r.clusters.length) {
      html += '<div class="empty-state-v2"><div class="empty-icon-ring">&#x2714;</div><div class="empty-title">No clusters found</div><div class="empty-subtitle">Need at least 3 issues in the last 7 days for clustering.</div></div>';
    } else {
      r.clusters.forEach(function(c) {
        html += '<div class="card mb-12"><div class="card-title mb-8">' + self._esc(c.theme||'Cluster') + '</div>'
          + '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-secondary);margin-bottom:8px">' + self._esc(c.description||'') + '</p>'
          + '<div style="display:flex;flex-wrap:wrap;gap:4px;margin-bottom:8px">' + (c.issueIds||[]).map(function(id){ return '<span style="background:var(--accent-dim);color:var(--accent);padding:2px 8px;border-radius:4px;font-size:11px;font-family:var(--font-mono);cursor:pointer" onclick="App.navigate(\'issue-detail\',{id:\'' + id + '\'})">' + id + '</span>'; }).join('') + '</div>'
          + (c.recommendation ? '<div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--low);font-style:italic">&#x2726; ' + self._esc(c.recommendation) + '</div>' : '')
          + '</div>';
      });
    }
    html += '</div>';
    area.innerHTML = html;
  },

  // ============================================================
  // AI RETROSPECTIVE
  // ============================================================
  showRetroModal: async function(sprintId) {
    var self = this;
    var modal = document.getElementById('modal');
    var body  = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (!modal||!body) return;
    body.innerHTML = '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted)">&#x2736; Writing your retrospective...</p>';
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
    var r = await self.callAsync('generateSprintRetrospective', sprintId||null);
    if (!r || !r.success) { body.innerHTML = '<p style="color:var(--critical)">AI unavailable.</p><div style="text-align:right;margin-top:10px"><button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Close</button></div>'; return; }
    var rr = r.retro; var s = r.stats;
    body.innerHTML = '<h3 style="margin:0 0 4px;color:var(--text-primary)">&#x2736; Sprint Retrospective</h3>'
      + '<p style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);font-family:var(--font-mono);margin-bottom:14px">' + s.resolved + '/' + s.total + ' resolved · ' + s.breached + ' SLA breaches</p>'
      + (rr.highlights ? '<p style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text-secondary);margin-bottom:14px;font-style:italic">' + self._esc(rr.highlights) + '</p>' : '')
      + '<div class="form-grid-2">'
      + '<div><div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.08em;color:var(--low);margin-bottom:6px">What went well</div>' + (rr.wentWell||[]).map(function(w){ return '<div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-secondary);padding:3px 0">&#x2714; ' + self._esc(w) + '</div>'; }).join('') + '</div>'
      + '<div><div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.08em;color:var(--high);margin-bottom:6px">Needs improvement</div>' + (rr.needsImprovement||[]).map(function(w){ return '<div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-secondary);padding:3px 0">&#x25B6; ' + self._esc(w) + '</div>'; }).join('') + '</div>'
      + '</div>'
      + (rr.actionItems && rr.actionItems.length ? '<div style="margin-top:12px"><div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:.08em;color:var(--accent);margin-bottom:6px">Action items</div>' + rr.actionItems.map(function(a){ return '<div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-secondary);padding:3px 0">&#x2726; ' + self._esc(a) + '</div>'; }).join('') + '</div>' : '')
      + '<div style="text-align:right;margin-top:16px"><button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.closeModal()">Close</button></div>';
  },

  // ============================================================
  // QA SIGN-OFF
  // ============================================================
  showQASignoff: async function(issueId) {
    var self = this;
    var modal = document.getElementById('modal');
    var body  = document.getElementById('modal-body');
    if (!modal||!body) return;
    body.innerHTML = '<h3 style="margin:0 0 14px;color:var(--text-primary)">QA Sign-Off   ' + issueId + '</h3>'
      + '<div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">QA Notes (optional)</label><textarea id="qaNote" class="form-textarea" style="min-height:70px" placeholder="Tested on Chrome, Firefox, Safari. Regression check passed."></textarea></div>'
      + '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:16px"><button class="qa-signoff-btn qa-reject" onclick="App.submitQASignoff(\'' + issueId + '\',false)">&#x2715; Reject</button><button class="qa-signoff-btn qa-approve" onclick="App.submitQASignoff(\'' + issueId + '\',true)">&#x2714; Approve &amp; Resolve</button><button class="btn-secondary" style="margin-left:auto" onclick="App.closeModal()">Cancel</button></div>';
    modal.style.display = 'flex';
  },

  submitQASignoff: async function(issueId, approved) {
    var self = this;
    var note = (document.getElementById('qaNote')||{}).value||'';
    var r = await self.callAsync('submitQASignoff', issueId, approved, note);
    if (r && r.success) {
      self.closeModal();
      self.showToast(approved ? 'QA approved   issue resolved' : 'QA rejected', approved ? 'success' : 'info');
      self.renderIssueDetail(issueId);
    } else {
      self.showToast('Failed: ' + (r ? r.error : 'unknown'), 'error');
    }
  },

  // ============================================================
  // REGRESSION TRACKER
  // ============================================================
  toggleRegression: async function(issueId, btn) {
    var self = this;
    var cur = btn && btn.classList.contains('active');
    var r = await self.callAsync('markAsRegression', issueId, !cur);
    if (r && r.success) {
      if (btn) btn.classList.toggle('active', !cur);
      self.showToast(!cur ? 'Marked as regression' : 'Regression flag removed', 'info');
    }
  },


  closeModal: function() {
    var m = document.getElementById('modal');
    if (m) { m.style.display = 'none'; }
    // Also close any dynamic modal-overlay divs
    document.querySelectorAll('.modal-overlay:not(#modal)').forEach(function(el){ el.remove(); });
  },


  // ============================================================
  // UNIFIED ADMIN SETTINGS   renderAdminSettings
  // ============================================================
  renderAdminSettings: async function(initialTab) {
    var self = this;
    if (!self.currentUser || self.currentUser.role !== 'Admin') {
      self.showToast('Admin access required', 'error');
      self.navigate('dashboard');
      return;
    }
    self.setPage('Settings', 'Admin / Settings');
    var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Loading settings...</p></div>';

    // Fetch all data in parallel
    var flagsR, settingsR, modulesR, slaR, geminiR, historyR, rulesR, fieldsR, escR, recR, ocR;
    try {
      var results = await Promise.all([
        self.callAsync('getAllFeatureFlags'),
        self.callAsync('getSettings'),
        self.callAsync('getModules'),
        self.callAsync('getSLAConfig'),
        self.callAsync('getGeminiStatus'),
        self.callAsync('getAIQueryHistory', 10),
        self.callAsync('getInboundRules'),
        self.callAsync('getCustomFields'),
        self.callAsync('getEscalationRules'),
        self.callAsync('getRecurringTemplates'),
        self.callAsync('getOnCallSchedule')
      ]);
      flagsR=results[0]; settingsR=results[1]; modulesR=results[2]; slaR=results[3];
      geminiR=results[4]; historyR=results[5]; rulesR=results[6]; fieldsR=results[7];
      escR=results[8]; recR=results[9]; ocR=results[10];
    } catch(e) {
      self.showPageError(area, 'Settings load failed: ' + e.message);
      return;
    }

    var flags    = (flagsR && flagsR.success)    ? flagsR.flags    : {};
    var settings = (settingsR && settingsR.success) ? settingsR.settings : {};
    var modules  = (modulesR && modulesR.success) ? modulesR.modules : [];
    var sla      = (slaR && slaR.success)        ? slaR.config     : {};
    var geminiOk = geminiR && geminiR.configured;
    var queries  = (historyR && historyR.success) ? historyR.queries : [];
    var inboundRules = (rulesR && rulesR.success) ? rulesR.rules    : [];
    var customFields = (fieldsR && fieldsR.success) ? fieldsR.fields  : [];
    var escRules = (escR && escR.success)         ? escR.rules      : [];
    var recTpls  = (recR && recR.success)         ? recR.templates  : [];
    var oncall   = (ocR && ocR.success)           ? ocR.schedule    : [];

    //  TAB DEFINITIONS —
    var tabGroups = [
      { label: 'Configuration', tabs: [
        { id:'features',  icon:'&#x2726;', label:'Feature Flags' },
        { id:'sla',       icon:'&#x23F1;', label:'SLA Rules' },
        { id:'modules',   icon:'&#x25A6;', label:'Modules' },
      ]},
      { label: 'Notifications', tabs: [
        { id:'notif',     icon:'&#x1F514;', label:'Channels' },

      { label: 'Developer', tabs: [

        { id:'ai_log',    icon:'&#x2630;', label:'AI Query Log', count: queries.length },

    //  FEATURE FLAGS HTML —

      }).join('') : '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim)">No rules yet.</p>') +
      '<div style="text-align:right;margin-top:12px"><button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.saveTriageLabelAdmin()">Save Label</button></div>';

    //  CUSTOM FIELDS HTML 
    var typeLabel = {text:'Text',number:'Number',dropdown:'Dropdown',date:'Date',checkbox:'Checkbox'};
    var fieldsHtml = '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:12px">' +
      '<span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted)">' + customFields.length + ' custom fields defined</span>' +
      '<button class="btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="App.showAddFieldModal()">+ Add Field</button></div>' +
      (customFields.length ? customFields.map(function(f) {
        return '<div class="flag-row"><div class="flag-info"><div class="flag-name">' + esc(f.name) + '</div>' +
          '<div class="flag-desc">Type: ' + (typeLabel[f.type]||f.type) + (f.required?' · Required':'') + (f.options&&f.options.length?' · Options: '+esc(f.options.join(', ')):'') + '</div></div>' +
          '<button class="btn-danger btn-sm" onclick="App.deleteFieldAndRefresh(\'' + f.id + '\')">&#x2715;</button></div>';
      }).join('') : '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim)">No custom fields yet. Add one above.</p>');

    //  ESCALATIONS HTML 
    var escHtml = '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-bottom:12px">' +
      '<button class="btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="App.showAddEscalationModal()">+ Add Rule</button>' +
      '<button class="btn-secondary btn-sm" onclick="App.callAsync(\'runEscalationCheck\').then(function(){App.showToast(\'Escalation check ran\',\'success\');})">Run Now</button></div>' +
      '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-bottom:12px">Auto-escalate issues that stay open too long   notify leads or auto-bump priority.</p>' +

          '<div class="flag-desc">Notify: ' + (r.escalateTo||'Slack only') + ' · Action: ' + (r.action||'notify') + '</div></div>' +
          '<span class="flag-status ' + (r.active?'on':'off') + '">' + (r.active?'ON':'OFF') + '</span>' +

    //  RECURRING HTML 
    var recHtml = '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:12px">' +
      '<span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted)">' + recTpls.length + ' templates</span>' +
      '<button class="btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="App.showAddTemplateModal()">+ Add Template</button></div>' +
      (recTpls.length ? recTpls.map(function(t) {
        return '<div class="flag-row"><div class="flag-info"><div class="flag-name">' + esc(t.title) + '</div>' +
          '<div class="flag-desc">Schedule: ' + t.schedule + ' · Priority: ' + (t.priority||'Medium') + ' · Next: ' + (t.nextRun?new Date(t.nextRun).toLocaleDateString():' ') + '</div></div>' +
          '<span class="flag-status ' + (t.active?'on':'off') + '">' + (t.active?'ON':'OFF') + '</span>' +
          '<button class="btn-danger btn-sm" onclick="App.deleteTemplate(\'' + t.id + '\')">&#x2715;</button></div>';
      }).join('') : '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim)">No recurring templates yet.</p>');

    //  ON-CALL HTML 
    var ocHtml = '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:12px">' +
      '<span style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-muted)">' + oncall.length + ' schedule entries</span>' +
      '<button class="btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="App.showAddOnCallModal()">+ Add Entry</button></div>' +

          '</div>';
      }).join('') : '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim)">No on-call schedule entries yet.</p>');

    //  MODULE HEALTH HTML (skeleton, loads async) 
    var healthHtml = '<div id="healthContent"><div class="empty-state"><p>Loading health scores...</p></div></div>';

    //  SLA REPORT HTML (skeleton, loads async) —
    var slaReportHtml = '<div id="slaReportContent"><div class="empty-state"><p>Calculating compliance...</p></div></div>';

    //  INTEGRATIONS HTML —
    var intHtml = [
      {label:'Google Calendar ID',       id:'int_calId',     key:'GOOGLE_CALENDAR_ID',  ph:'yourname@gmail.com or calendar-id@group.calendar.google.com', desc:'Calendar ID from Google Calendar Settings   SLA deadlines sync as events'},
      {label:'Zapier / Make Webhook URL',id:'int_zapier',    key:'ZAPIER_WEBHOOK_URL',  ph:'https://hooks.zapier.com/...', desc:'Receives a JSON POST on issue create, update, resolve'},
      {label:'GitHub Webhook URL',       id:'int_github',    key:'_READONLY',           ph:'', desc:'Use your Apps Script deployment URL as the GitHub webhook target. Set Content-Type: application/json. Commits mentioning TECH-XXXX auto-link.', readonly:true},
    ].map(function(f) {
      var v = f.readonly ? '' : (settings[f.key] && settings[f.key] !== 'false' ? esc(settings[f.key]) : '');
      return '<div class="form-group mb-16"><label class="form-label">' + f.label + '</label>' +
        '<input id="' + f.id + '" class="form-input" ' + (f.readonly?'readonly style="color:var(--text-dim);font-size:11px" value="Your Apps Script deployment URL"':'type="url" placeholder="'+f.ph+'" value="'+v+'"') + '>' +
        '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-dim);margin-top:3px">' + f.desc + '</div></div>';
    }).join('') +
    '<div style="text-align:right"><button class="btn-primary" onclick="App.saveIntegrationsFromAdmin()">Save</button></div>';

    //  AI LOG HTML —
    var logHtml = queries.length ? queries.map(function(q) {
      return '<div style="padding:10px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border)">' +
        '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:4px">' +
        '<span style="font-size:10px;font-family:var(--font-mono);color:var(--text-dim)">' + new Date(q.timestamp).toLocaleString() + '</span>' +
        '<span style="font-size:10px;color:var(--text-dim)">' + esc(q.userEmail||'') + '</span></div>' +
        '<div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-primary)">' + esc((q.query||'').substring(0,120)) + '</div>' +
        '</div>';
    }).join('') : '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim)">No AI queries yet.</p>';

    //  ADVANCED HTML —
    var advHtml = '<div class="flag-row mb-8">' +
      '<div class="flag-info"><div class="flag-name">Auto-close after N days Resolved</div><div class="flag-desc">Issues in Resolved status auto-close after this many days</div></div>' +
      '<input type="number" id="adv_closeDays" class="form-input" style="width:80px;text-align:center" min="1" max="90" value="' + (settings.AUTO_CLOSE_DAYS||14) + '">' +
      '</div>' +
      '<div style="text-align:right;margin-top:8px;margin-bottom:24px"><button class="btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="App.saveAdvancedFromAdmin()">Save</button></div>' +

      '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;flex-wrap:wrap">' +
      '<button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.callAsync(\'initializeAllPhases\').then(function(r){App.showToast(r&&r.success?\'All sheets initialized\':\'Failed: \'+(r&&r.error||\'?\'),r&&r.success?\'success\':\'error\');})">&#x2730; Init All Sheets</button>' +
      '<button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.callAsync(\'setupAllTriggersV4\').then(function(r){App.showToast(r&&r.success?\'All triggers set\':\'Failed\',r&&r.success?\'success\':\'error\');})">&#x23F1; Reset Triggers</button>' +
      '<button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.navigate(\'audit-trail\')">&#x2637; View Audit Trail</button>' +
      '<button class="btn-secondary" onclick="App.exportDashboard()">&#x2197; Export Dashboard Report</button>' +
      '</div>';

    //  BUILD SIDEBAR —
    var sidebarHtml = tabGroups.map(function(g) {
      return '<div class="admin-tab-group-label">' + g.label + '</div>' +
        g.tabs.map(function(t) {
          return '<div class="admin-tab" data-atab="' + t.id + '" onclick="App.switchAdminTab(\'' + t.id + '\')">' +
            '<span class="admin-tab-icon">' + t.icon + '</span>' + t.label +
            (t.count ? '<span class="admin-tab-badge">' + t.count + '</span>' : '') +
            '</div>';
        }).join('');
    }).join('');

    //  BUILD SECTIONS 
    var sections = [
      {id:'features',    title:'Feature Flags',          desc:'Enable or disable any feature platform-wide. Changes take effect immediately.',  html:flagsHtml},
      {id:'sla',         title:'SLA Rules',               desc:'Set resolution time targets per priority level. SLA countdown starts at issue creation.', html:slaHtml},
      {id:'modules',     title:'Module Configuration',    desc:'Comma-separated list of modules used in your system.',  html:modulesHtml},
      {id:'notif',       title:'Notification Channels',   desc:'Configure Slack, Google Chat, and webhook alert destinations.',  html:notifHtml},
      {id:'ai',          title:'AI & Gemini Settings',    desc:'Configure Gemini API keys and view AI usage history.',  html:aiHtml},
      {id:'email',       title:'Email Triage',            desc:'Auto-create issues from Gmail. Set up inbound routing rules.',  html:emailHtml},
      {id:'fields',      title:'Custom Fields',           desc:'Define extra fields that appear on every issue.',  html:fieldsHtml},
      {id:'escalations', title:'Escalation Rules',        desc:'Auto-escalate issues that stay open too long.',  html:escHtml},
      {id:'recurring',   title:'Recurring Templates',     desc:'Auto-create issues on a schedule.',  html:recHtml},
      {id:'oncall',      title:'On-Call Schedule',        desc:'Define who is on-call and when.',  html:ocHtml},
      {id:'health',      title:'Module Health Scores',    desc:'Health grades (A–F) for each module based on open issues, critical count, and SLA breaches.',  html:healthHtml},
      {id:'sla_report',  title:'SLA Compliance Report',   desc:'Percentage of issues resolved within SLA over the last 30 days.',  html:slaReportHtml},
      {id:'integrations',title:'External Integrations',   desc:'Google Calendar sync, Zapier webhooks, and GitHub commit linking.',  html:intHtml},
      {id:'ai_log',      title:'AI Query Log',            desc:'Recent queries sent to Gemini through TechTrack.',  html:logHtml},
      {id:'advanced',    title:'Advanced Settings',       desc:'System actions and advanced configuration.',  html:advHtml},
    ];

      return '<div class="admin-section" id="asec_' + s.id + '">' +

    area.innerHTML = '<div class="admin-layout">' +
      '<div class="admin-sidebar">' +

        sidebarHtml +
      '</div>' +
      '<div class="admin-content" id="adminContent">' + sectionsHtml + '</div>' +
