    // Activate initial tab
    var startTab = initialTab || 'features';
    self.switchAdminTab(startTab);

    // Lazy-load health and SLA report when those tabs are shown
    self._adminHealthLoaded = false;
    self._adminSLALoaded = false;
  },

  switchAdminTab: function(tabId) {
    var self = this;
    document.querySelectorAll('.admin-tab').forEach(function(t) {
      t.classList.toggle('active', t.dataset.atab === tabId);
    });
    document.querySelectorAll('.admin-section').forEach(function(s) {
      s.classList.toggle('active', s.id === 'asec_' + tabId);
    });
    // Lazy-load heavy tabs
    if (tabId === 'health' && !self._adminHealthLoaded) {
      self._adminHealthLoaded = true;
      self.callAsync('getModuleHealthScores').then(function(r) {
        var el = document.getElementById('healthContent');
        if (!el) return;
        if (!r || !r.success || !r.scores.length) { el.innerHTML = '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim)">No module data yet.</p>'; return; }
        var html = '<div class="health-grid">';
        r.scores.forEach(function(s) {
          html += '<div class="health-card">' +
            '<div class="health-grade ' + s.grade + '">' + s.grade + '</div>' +
            '<div class="health-module">' + self._esc(s.module) + '</div>' +
            '<div class="health-meta">' + s.open + ' open · ' + s.resolved + ' resolved' + (s.critical?' · <span style="color:var(--critical)">' + s.critical + ' critical</span>':'') + '</div>' +
            '</div>';
        });
        html += '</div>';
        el.innerHTML = html;
      });
    }
    if (tabId === 'sla_report' && !self._adminSLALoaded) {
      self._adminSLALoaded = true;
      var t30 = new Date(Date.now()-30*24*3600000).toISOString().split('T')[0];
      var today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
      self.callAsync('getSLAComplianceReport', t30, today).then(function(r) {
        var el = document.getElementById('slaReportContent');
        if (!el) return;
        if (!r || !r.success) { el.innerHTML = '<p style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-dim)">No data.</p>'; return; }
        var pColors = {Critical:'var(--critical)',High:'var(--high)',Medium:'var(--accent)',Low:'var(--low)'};
        var color = r.compliancePct>=80?'var(--low)':r.compliancePct>=60?'var(--accent)':'var(--critical)';
        el.innerHTML = '<div class="compliance-hero">' +
          '<div class="compliance-pct" style="color:' + color + '">' + r.compliancePct + '%</div>' +
          '<div class="compliance-label">SLA Compliance   last 30 days</div>' +
          '<div class="compliance-sub">' + r.withinSLA + ' within SLA · ' + r.breached + ' breached · ' + r.total + ' total</div>' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div style="max-width:500px;margin:0 auto">' +
          ['Critical','High','Medium','Low'].map(function(p) {
            var d = r.byPriority[p] || {compliance:100,total:0};
            return '<div class="flag-row"><div class="flag-info"><div class="flag-name" style="color:' + (pColors[p]||'') + '">' + p + '</div><div class="flag-desc">' + d.total + ' issues in range</div></div>' +
              '<span class="flag-status ' + (d.compliance>=80?'on':'off') + '">' + d.compliance + '%</span></div>';
          }).join('') + '</div>';
      });
    }
  },

  toggleFeatureFlag: async function(key, enabled) {
    var self = this;
    var badge = document.getElementById('fs_' + key);
    if (badge) { badge.textContent = enabled ? 'ON' : 'OFF'; badge.className = 'flag-status ' + (enabled?'on':'off'); }
    var r = await self.callAsync('updateSetting', key, enabled ? 'true' : 'false');
    if (r && r.success) {
      // Update local cache
      if (!self.featureFlags) self.featureFlags = {};
      self.featureFlags[key] = enabled ? 'true' : 'false';
      self.showToast((enabled ? 'Enabled: ' : 'Disabled: ') + key.replace(/_/g,' '), enabled ? 'success' : 'info');
    } else {
      self.showToast('Failed to update setting', 'error');
    }
    // Update nav visibility based on flags
    self.applyFeatureFlags();
  },

  applyFeatureFlags: async function() {
    var self = this;
    // Prefer already-loaded flags from init(); only re-fetch if not available
    if (!self.featureFlags || Object.keys(self.featureFlags).length === 0) {
      var r = await self.callAsync('getAllFeatureFlags');
      if (r && r.success) self.featureFlags = r.flags;
    }
    var flags = self.featureFlags || {};
    // Hide/show nav items based on flags
    var navMap = {
      'KANBAN_ENABLED':              '[data-page="kanban"]',
      'SPRINTS_ENABLED':             '[data-page="sprints"]',
      'VELOCITY_ENABLED':            '[data-page="velocity"]',
      'WORKLOAD_ENABLED':            '[data-page="workload"]',
      'WORKLOAD_BOARD_ENABLED':      '[data-page="workload-board"]',
      'ONCALL_ENABLED':              '[data-page="oncall"]',
      'CUSTOM_FIELDS_ENABLED':       '[data-page="custom-fields"]',
      'RELEASE_NOTES_ENABLED':       '[data-page="release-notes"]',
      'ESCALATION_RULES_ENABLED':    '[data-page="escalations"]',
      'RECURRING_TEMPLATES_ENABLED': '[data-page="recurring"]',
      'AUDIT_TRAIL_ENABLED':         '[data-page="audit-trail"]',
      'ANALYTICS_ENABLED':           '[data-page="analytics"]',
      'CEO_DASHBOARD_ENABLED':       '[data-page="leadership"]',
    };
    Object.keys(navMap).forEach(function(flag) {
      var enabled = flags[flag] === 'true' || flags[flag] === true;
      var els = document.querySelectorAll(navMap[flag]);
      els.forEach(function(el) {
        el.style.display = enabled ? '' : 'none';
        // CEO dashboard only for Admins
        if (flag === 'CEO_DASHBOARD_ENABLED' && self.currentUser && self.currentUser.role !== 'Admin') {
          el.style.display = 'none';
        }
      });
    });

    // Mobile nav
    if (flags['MOBILE_NAV_ENABLED'] === 'true') {
      self.initMobileNav();
    }
  },

  saveSLAFromAdmin: async function() {
    var self = this;
    for (var p of ['Critical','High','Medium','Low']) {
      var el = document.getElementById('sla_' + p);
      if (el) await self.callAsync('updateSLAConfig', p, parseInt(el.value)||24);
    }
    self.showToast('SLA rules saved', 'success');
  },

  saveModulesFromAdmin: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var el = document.getElementById('admin_modules') || document.getElementById('modulesList');
    if (!el) return;
    var mods = el.value.split(',').map(function(m){return m.trim();}).filter(Boolean);
    var r = await self.callAsync('updateModules', mods);
    r && r.success ? self.showToast('Modules saved', 'success') : self.showToast('Failed', 'error');
  },

  saveNotifChannels: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var fields = [
      {id:'notif_slack',     key:'SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL'},
      {id:'notif_gchat',     key:'GOOGLE_CHAT_WEBHOOK'},
      {id:'notif_wa',        key:'WEBHOOK_ALERT_URL'},
      {id:'notif_threshold', key:'WEBHOOK_CRITICAL_ONLY'},
    ];
    for (var i=0; i<fields.length; i++) {
      var el = document.getElementById(fields[i].id);
      if (el) await self.callAsync('updateSetting', fields[i].key, el.value||'false');
    }
    self.showToast('Notification channels saved', 'success');
  },

  saveBrowserGeminiKey: function() {
    var el = document.getElementById('ai_localKey');
    if (!el || !el.value || el.value.startsWith('••')) { this.showToast('Enter a valid key','warning'); return; }
    AI.setGeminiKey(el.value.trim());
    this.showToast('Browser Gemini key saved','success');
    el.value = '••••••••';
  },

  saveTriageLabelAdmin: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var el = document.getElementById('email_label');
    if (el) await self.callAsync('updateSetting', 'EMAIL_TRIAGE_LABEL', el.value||'TechTrack-Inbox');
    self.showToast('Triage label saved', 'success');
  },

  saveIntegrationsFromAdmin: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var fields = [
      {id:'int_calId',   key:'GOOGLE_CALENDAR_ID'},
      {id:'int_zapier',  key:'ZAPIER_WEBHOOK_URL'},
    ];
    for (var i=0; i<fields.length; i++) {
      var el = document.getElementById(fields[i].id);
      if (el) await self.callAsync('updateSetting', fields[i].key, el.value||'false');
    }
    self.showToast('Integration settings saved', 'success');
  },

  saveAdvancedFromAdmin: async function() {
    var self = this;
    var el = document.getElementById('adv_closeDays');
    if (el) await self.callAsync('updateSetting', 'AUTO_CLOSE_DAYS', el.value||'14');
    self.showToast('Advanced settings saved', 'success');
  },

  deleteFieldAndRefresh: async function(fieldId) {
    var self = this;
    if (!confirm('Delete this custom field?')) return;
    var r = await self.callAsync('deleteCustomField', fieldId);
    if (r && r.success) { self.showToast('Deleted', 'info'); self.renderAdminSettings('fields'); }
    else self.showToast('Failed', 'error');
  },

  exportCSV: async function() {
    var self = this;
    self.showToast('Generating CSV...','info');
    var r = await self.callAsync('exportIssuesCSV', null);
    if (!r || !r.success) { self.showToast('Failed: '+(r?r.error:'unknown'),'error'); return; }
    var blob = new Blob([atob(r.csv)], {type:'text/csv'});
    var url = URL.createObjectURL(blob);
    var a = document.createElement('a');
    a.href = url; a.download = 'techtrack-issues-'+new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0]+'.csv';
    a.click(); URL.revokeObjectURL(url);
    self.showToast('Downloaded '+r.count+' issues','success');
  },

  togglePin: async function(issueId) {
    var self = this;
    var r = await self.callAsync('togglePinnedIssue', issueId);
    if (r && r.success) {
      self.showToast(r.pinned?'Issue pinned':'Unpinned','success');
      var btn = document.querySelector('[data-pin-id="'+issueId+'"]');
      if (btn) btn.style.color = r.pinned ? 'var(--accent)' : '';
    }
  },


  switchDetailTab: function(tab, issueId) {
    var tabs = ['comments', 'email', 'activity', 'time', 'links'];
    tabs.forEach(function(t) {
      var btn = document.getElementById('tab-' + t);
      var panel = document.getElementById('tab-panel-' + t);
      if (btn) btn.classList.toggle('active', t === tab);
      if (panel) panel.style.display = t === tab ? 'block' : 'none';
    });
    if (tab === 'email') {
      App.renderEmailThread(issueId);
    }
    if (tab === 'time') {
      App.loadTimeLogs(issueId);
    }
    if (tab === 'links') {
      App.loadIssueLinks(issueId);
    }
    // Init @mention handler when comments tab is active
    if (tab === 'comments') {
      App.initMentionAutocomplete(issueId);
    }
  },

  saveGeminiKeyFromSettings() {
    const input = document.getElementById('geminiKeySettings');
    const key = input?.value?.trim();
    if (!key || key.startsWith('••')) { App.showToast('Enter a new key to update', 'warning'); return; }
    AI.setGeminiKey(key);
    App.showToast('Gemini API key saved!', 'success');
    App.renderSystemSettings();
  },

  clearGeminiKey() {
    if (!confirm('Remove your Gemini API key?')) return;
    try { localStorage.removeItem('tt_gemini_key'); } catch(e) {}
    App.showToast('Gemini key removed', 'info');
    App.renderSystemSettings();
  },

  async saveModules() {
    const raw = document.getElementById('modulesList').value;
    const modules = raw.split(',').map(m => m.trim()).filter(Boolean);
    const result = await self.call('updateModules', modules);
    if (result.success) self.showToast('Modules updated', 'success');
    else self.showToast('Failed to update modules', 'error');
  },

  // ============================================================
  // SLA ALERTS
  // ============================================================

  async checkSLAAlerts() {
    const result = await self.call('getIssues', null);
    if (!result.success) return;
    const breaches = result.issues.filter(i => i.slaBreached);
    const alertEl = document.getElementById('slaAlert');
    const countEl = document.getElementById('slaCount');
    if (breaches.length > 0) {
      alertEl.style.display = 'flex';
      countEl.textContent = breaches.length;
    } else {
      alertEl.style.display = 'none';
    }
  },

  // ============================================================
  // UTILITIES
  // ============================================================

  async call(fn, ...args) {
    return new Promise((resolve) => {
      // Per-call timeout: 15s   prevents silent hangs
      const t = setTimeout(() => {
        resolve({ success: false, error: `Call to ${fn} timed out. Check your Spreadsheet ID in Code.gs.` });
      }, 15000);

      google.script.run
        .withSuccessHandler((r) => { clearTimeout(t); resolve(r); })
        .withFailureHandler((err) => { clearTimeout(t); resolve({ success: false, error: err.message }); })
        [fn](...args);
    });
  },
  
  showError(msg) {
    document.getElementById('loading-screen').style.display = 'none';
    const screen = document.getElementById('error-screen');
    const msgEl = document.getElementById('error-message');
    screen.style.display = 'flex';
    // Replace newlines with <br> for multi-line messages
    msgEl.innerHTML = msg.replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
    // Add retry button if not already present
    if (!document.getElementById('retryBtn')) {
      const btn = document.createElement('button');
      btn.id = 'retryBtn';
      btn.className = 'btn-secondary';
      btn.style.marginTop = '20px';
      btn.textContent = '→ Retry';
      btn.onclick = () => location.reload();
      document.querySelector('.error-wrap').appendChild(btn);
    }
  },
  
  // showToast replaced by improved version above
  
  priorityBadge(priority) {
    const cls = (priority||'').toLowerCase();
    return `<span class="badge-priority ${cls}">${priority||' '}</span>`;
  },
  
  statusBadge(status) {
    const cls = (status||'').toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '-');
    return `<span class="badge-status ${cls}">${status||' '}</span>`;
  },
  
  roleBadge(role) {
    const colors = { Admin: 'var(--critical)', Developer: 'var(--accent)', CS: 'var(--status-ack)', Sales: 'var(--low)', QA: 'var(--status-testing)', Product: 'var(--status-open)' };
    return `<span style="font-size:11px;font-weight:600;color:${colors[role]||'var(--text-muted)'}">${role}</span>`;
  },
  
  shortEmail(email) {
    if (!email) return ' ';
    const parts = email.split('@');
    return parts[0].length > 12 ? parts[0].substring(0,12) + '…' : parts[0];
  },
  
  relativeTime(dateStr) {
    if (!dateStr) return ' ';
    const diff = Date.now() - new Date(dateStr);
    const mins = Math.floor(diff / 60000);
    if (mins < 60) return `${mins}m ago`;
    const hrs = Math.floor(mins / 60);
    if (hrs < 24) return `${hrs}h ago`;
    const days = Math.floor(hrs / 24);
    if (days < 30) return `${days}d ago`;
    return new Date(dateStr).toLocaleDateString();
  },
  
  formatDate(dateStr) {
    if (!dateStr) return ' ';
    return new Date(dateStr).toLocaleString('en', { 
      month: 'short', day: 'numeric', hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' 
    });
  },
  
  durationHours(from, to) {
    if (!from || !to) return ' ';
    return Math.round((new Date(to) - new Date(from)) / (1000 * 60 * 60));
  },

  /* ── Age since raised ── */
  ageDays(dateStr) {
    if (!dateStr) return 0;
    return Math.floor((Date.now() - new Date(dateStr)) / 86400000);
  },

  ageBadge(dateStr) {
    const d = this.ageDays(dateStr);
    const cls = d <= 3 ? 'age-fresh' : d <= 7 ? 'age-normal' : d <= 14 ? 'age-aging' : d <= 29 ? 'age-old' : 'age-stale';
    const label = d === 0 ? 'today' : d === 1 ? '1d' : `${d}d`;
    return `<span class="age-badge ${cls}" title="${d} days since raised">⏱ ${label}</span>`;
  },
  
  escapeHtml(str) {
    if (!str) return '';
    return str.replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;')
              .replace(/"/g,'&quot;').replace(/'/g,'&#039;');
  }
};

// Initialize on load
document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => App.init());

// ============================================================
// PHASE 5/6 — NEW FRONTEND FUNCTIONS
// ============================================================

// ─── Helper: render comment list with @mention highlighting ──
App.renderCommentList = function(comments) {
  if (!comments || comments.length === 0) {
    return '<div class="text-muted" style="font-size:12px;padding:12px 0">No comments yet. Be the first to comment.</div>';
  }
  return comments.map(function(c) {
    var highlighted = (c.comment || '').replace(
      /@([\w.]+)/g,
      '<strong style="color:var(--accent);">@$1</strong>'
    );
    return '<div class="comment-item">' +
      '<div class="comment-avatar">' + (c.userEmail||'?').charAt(0).toUpperCase() + '</div>' +
      '<div class="comment-body">' +
      '<div class="comment-meta"><span class="comment-author">' + (c.userEmail||'') + '</span>' +
      '<span>·</span><span>' + App.relativeTime(c.timestamp) + '</span></div>' +
      '<div class="comment-text">' + highlighted + '</div>' +
      '</div></div>';
  }).join('');
};

// ─── @Mention autocomplete ────────────────────────────────────
App.initMentionAutocomplete = function(issueId) {
  var textarea = document.getElementById('commentInput');
  var dropdown = document.getElementById('mentionDropdown');
  if (!textarea || !dropdown) return;
  if (textarea._mentionInit) return; // already initialized
  textarea._mentionInit = true;

  textarea.addEventListener('input', function() {
    var val = textarea.value;
    var cursorPos = textarea.selectionStart;
    var textBefore = val.substring(0, cursorPos);
    var mentionMatch = textBefore.match(/@([\w.]*)$/);
    if (!mentionMatch) { dropdown.style.display = 'none'; return; }
    var query = mentionMatch[1].toLowerCase();
    var users = App.users || [];
    var filtered = users.filter(function(u) {
      return u.name.toLowerCase().includes(query) || u.email.toLowerCase().includes(query);
    }).slice(0, 8);
    if (filtered.length === 0) { dropdown.style.display = 'none'; return; }
    dropdown.innerHTML = filtered.map(function(u) {
      var handle = u.name.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '.');
      return '<div class="mention-item" style="padding:8px 12px;cursor:pointer;font-size:12px;color:var(--text-primary);" ' +
        'onmouseover="this.style.background=\'var(--bg-elevated)\'" onmouseout="this.style.background=\'\'" ' +
        'onclick="App.insertMention(\'' + handle + '\', \'' + issueId + '\')"><strong>@' + handle + '</strong> · ' + u.name + '</div>';
    }).join('');
    dropdown.style.display = 'block';
  });

  textarea.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
    if (e.key === 'Escape') dropdown.style.display = 'none';
  });

  document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    if (!textarea.contains(e.target) && !dropdown.contains(e.target)) dropdown.style.display = 'none';
  }, { once: false });
};

App.insertMention = function(handle, issueId) {
  var textarea = document.getElementById('commentInput');
  var dropdown = document.getElementById('mentionDropdown');
  if (!textarea) return;
  var val = textarea.value;
  var cursorPos = textarea.selectionStart;
  var textBefore = val.substring(0, cursorPos);
  var newTextBefore = textBefore.replace(/@[\w.]*$/, '@' + handle + ' ');
  textarea.value = newTextBefore + val.substring(cursorPos);
  textarea.selectionStart = textarea.selectionEnd = newTextBefore.length;
  textarea.focus();
  if (dropdown) dropdown.style.display = 'none';
};

// ─── Time Tracking: load and submit ──────────────────────────
App.loadTimeLogs = async function(issueId) {
  var container = document.getElementById('timeLogsContainer');
  if (!container) return;
  var r = await App.call('getTimeLogsForIssue', issueId);
  if (!r || !r.success) { container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted" style="font-size:12px">Failed to load time logs</p>'; return; }
  var logs = r.logs || [];
  var total = r.totalHours || 0;
  if (logs.length === 0) {
    container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted" style="font-size:12px">No time logged yet.</p>';
    return;
  }
  container.innerHTML = '<div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:700;color:var(--text-primary);margin-bottom:10px">Total: ' + total + 'h</div>' +
    logs.map(function(l) {
      return '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;padding:6px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);font-size:12px;">' +
        '<span style="color:var(--accent);font-weight:700;font-family:var(--font-mono);">' + l.hours + 'h</span>' +
        '<span style="color:var(--text-secondary);">' + (l.userEmail||'') + '</span>' +
        '<span style="flex:1;color:var(--text-muted);">' + (l.note||'') + '</span>' +
        '<span style="color:var(--text-dim);font-family:var(--font-mono);">' + App.relativeTime(l.loggedAt) + '</span>' +
        '</div>';
    }).join('');
};

App.submitTimeLog = async function(issueId) {
  var hrs = parseFloat(document.getElementById('logHoursInput')?.value || 0);
  var note = document.getElementById('logNoteInput')?.value || '';
  if (!hrs || hrs <= 0) { App.showToast('Enter valid hours', 'warning'); return; }
  var r = await App.call('logTime', issueId, hrs, note);
  if (r && r.success) {
    App.showToast('Logged ' + hrs + 'h', 'success');
    document.getElementById('logHoursInput') && (document.getElementById('logHoursInput').value = '1');
    document.getElementById('logNoteInput') && (document.getElementById('logNoteInput').value = '');
    App.loadTimeLogs(issueId);
  } else {
    App.showToast('Failed: ' + (r && r.error || 'unknown'), 'error');
  }
};

// ─── Issue Linking: load and submit ──────────────────────────
App.loadIssueLinks = async function(issueId) {
  var container = document.getElementById('issueLinksContainer');
  if (!container) return;
  var r = await App.call('getIssueLinks', issueId);
  if (!r || !r.success) { container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted" style="font-size:12px">Failed to load links</p>'; return; }
  var links = r.links || [];
  if (links.length === 0) { container.innerHTML = '<p class="text-muted" style="font-size:12px">No linked issues.</p>'; return; }
  var grouped = {};
  links.forEach(function(l) {
    var type = l.issueId === issueId ? l.linkType : 'blocked-by';
    if (type === 'blocks' && l.issueId !== issueId) type = 'blocked-by';
    if (!grouped[type]) grouped[type] = [];
    var related = l.issueId === issueId ? l.targetId : l.issueId;
    grouped[type].push({ depId: l.id, relatedId: related, createdAt: l.createdAt });
  });
  container.innerHTML = Object.keys(grouped).map(function(type) {
    return '<div style="margin-bottom:12px;"><div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;color:var(--text-dim);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.1em;margin-bottom:6px;">' + type + '</div>' +
      grouped[type].map(function(l) {
        return '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;padding:4px 0;font-size:12px;">' +
          '<span class="issue-id" onclick="App.navigate(\'issue-detail\',{id:\'' + l.relatedId + '\'})" style="cursor:pointer;">' + l.relatedId + '</span>' +
          '<button class="btn-danger btn-sm" style="padding:2px 6px;font-size:10px;" onclick="App.removeIssueLink(\'' + l.depId + '\',\'' + issueId + '\')">×</button>' +
          '</div>';
      }).join('') + '</div>';
  }).join('');
};

App.submitIssueLink = async function(issueId) {
  var targetId = (document.getElementById('linkTargetInput')?.value || '').trim();
  var linkType = document.getElementById('linkTypeSelect')?.value || 'related';
  if (!targetId) { App.showToast('Enter a target issue ID', 'warning'); return; }
  var r = await App.call('linkIssues', issueId, targetId, linkType);
  if (r && r.success) {
    App.showToast('Issues linked', 'success');
    document.getElementById('linkTargetInput') && (document.getElementById('linkTargetInput').value = '');
    App.loadIssueLinks(issueId);
  } else {
    App.showToast('Failed: ' + (r && r.error || 'unknown'), 'error');
  }
};

App.removeIssueLink = async function(depId, issueId) {
  var r = await App.call('removeIssueLink', depId);
  if (r && r.success) { App.showToast('Link removed', 'info'); App.loadIssueLinks(issueId); }
  else App.showToast('Failed', 'error');
};

// ─── AI Thread Summariser ─────────────────────────────────────
App.summariseThread = async function(issueId) {
  var area = document.getElementById('aiSummaryArea');
  if (!area) return;
  area.innerHTML = '<div class="skeleton" style="height:80px;border-radius:8px;margin-bottom:10px;"></div>';
  var r = await App.call('summariseIssueThread', issueId);
  if (!r || !r.success) { area.innerHTML = '<p style="color:var(--critical);font-size:12px">AI failed: ' + (r&&r.error||'unknown') + '</p>'; return; }
  var s = r.summary || {};
  var summary = typeof s === 'string' ? { summary: s } : s;
  area.innerHTML = '<div style="background:var(--bg-elevated);border-left:3px solid var(--accent);border-radius:0 8px 8px 0;padding:12px 16px;margin-bottom:12px;">' +
    '<div style="font-size:11px;font-weight:700;color:var(--accent);text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.1em;margin-bottom:8px;">✨ AI Thread Summary</div>' +
    '<p style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text-primary);margin:0 0 8px;">' + (summary.summary||'') + '</p>' +
    (summary.decisions&&summary.decisions.length ? '<div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-secondary);"><strong>Decisions:</strong> ' + summary.decisions.join(' · ') + '</div>' : '') +
    (summary.actionItems&&summary.actionItems.length ? '<div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--text-secondary);margin-top:4px;"><strong>Action items:</strong> ' + summary.actionItems.join(' · ') + '</div>' : '') +
    (summary.blockers&&summary.blockers.length&&summary.blockers[0] ? '<div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--critical);margin-top:4px;">⚠️ Blockers: ' + summary.blockers.join(', ') + '</div>' : '') +
    (summary.suggestedNextStep ? '<div style="font-size:12px;color:var(--accent);margin-top:6px;">→ ' + summary.suggestedNextStep + '</div>' : '') +
    '</div>';
};

// ─── Workload Board ───────────────────────────────────────────
App.renderWorkloadBoard = async function() {
  var self = App;
  var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
  if (!(self.featureFlags && self.featureFlags['WORKLOAD_BOARD_ENABLED'] === 'true')) {
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Workload Board is disabled. Enable WORKLOAD_BOARD_ENABLED in Admin › Settings › Features.</p></div>';
    return;
  }
  area.innerHTML = '<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fill,minmax(300px,1fr));gap:14px;">' +
    [1,2,3].map(function(){return '<div class="skeleton" style="height:220px;border-radius:14px"></div>';}).join('') + '</div>';
  var r = await App.call('getDevWorkloadBoard');
  if (!r || !r.success) { App.showPageError(area, r&&r.error||'Failed to load workload data'); return; }
  var board = r.board || [];
  if (board.length === 0) { area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>No developer data found.</p></div>'; return; }
  area.innerHTML = '<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(auto-fill,minmax(300px,1fr));gap:14px;">' +
    board.map(function(dev) {
      var capColor = dev.capacityPct > 85 ? 'var(--critical)' : dev.capacityPct > 60 ? 'var(--accent)' : 'var(--low)';
      var barBg = dev.capacityPct > 85 ? '#ff475733' : dev.capacityPct > 60 ? '#f5a62333' : '#2ed57333';
      var topIssues = (dev.issues || []).slice(0,3).map(function(i) {
        return '<div style="padding:3px 0;font-size:11px;color:var(--text-secondary);cursor:pointer;" onclick="App.navigate(\'issue-detail\',{id:\'' + i.id + '\'})">' +
          '<span class="issue-id" style="font-size:10px;">' + i.id + '</span> ' + (i.title||'').substring(0,40) + '</div>';
      }).join('');
      return '<div class="card" style="border-color:' + (dev.slaAtRisk > 0 ? 'var(--critical-dim)' : 'var(--border)') + ';">' +
        '<div style="display:flex;align-items:flex-start;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:12px;">' +
        '<div><div style="font-size:14px;font-weight:700;color:var(--text-primary);">' + (dev.name||dev.email) + '</div>' +
        '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-top:2px;">' + (dev.team||'') + (dev.skill ? ' · ' + dev.skill : '') + '</div></div>' +
        (dev.slaAtRisk > 0 ? '<span style="background:#ff475733;color:var(--critical);border:1px solid var(--critical-dim);border-radius:999px;padding:2px 8px;font-size:10px;font-weight:700;">' + dev.slaAtRisk + ' SLA</span>' : '') +
        '</div>' +
        '<div style="margin-bottom:12px;">' +
        '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;font-size:11px;margin-bottom:4px;">' +
        '<span style="color:var(--text-muted);">Capacity</span>' +
        '<span style="font-weight:700;color:' + capColor + ';">' + dev.openCount + ' / ' + dev.maxTickets + ' (' + dev.capacityPct + '%)</span></div>' +
        '<div style="height:8px;border-radius:4px;background:var(--bg-elevated);overflow:hidden;">' +
        '<div style="height:100%;width:' + dev.capacityPct + '%;background:' + capColor + ';border-radius:4px;transition:width 0.3s;"></div></div>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div style="display:flex;gap:12px;font-size:11px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-bottom:12px;">' +
        '<span>🔴 ' + dev.critical + ' critical</span>' +
        '<span>✅ ' + dev.resolvedTotal + ' resolved</span>' +
        (dev.avgMTTRHours ? '<span>⏱ ' + dev.avgMTTRHours + 'h avg</span>' : '') +
        '</div>' +
        (topIssues ? '<div style="border-top:1px solid var(--border);padding-top:8px;">' + topIssues + '</div>' : '') +
        '</div>';
    }).join('') + '</div>';
};

// ─── Leadership Dashboard ─────────────────────────────────────
App.renderLeadershipDashboard = async function() {
  var self = App;
  var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
  if (!self.currentUser || self.currentUser.role !== 'Admin') {
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Admin access required.</p></div>'; return;
  }
  if (!(self.featureFlags && self.featureFlags['CEO_DASHBOARD_ENABLED'] === 'true')) {
    area.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state"><p>Leadership Dashboard is disabled. Enable CEO_DASHBOARD_ENABLED in Admin › Settings › Features.</p></div>'; return;
  }
  area.innerHTML = '<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(4,1fr);gap:14px;margin-bottom:20px;">' +
    [1,2,3,4].map(function(){return '<div class="skeleton" style="height:88px;border-radius:14px"></div>';}).join('') + '</div>';
  var r = await App.call('getCEODashboardData');
  if (!r || !r.success) { App.showPageError(area, r&&r.error||'Failed'); return; }
  var s = r.snapshot || {};
  var mh = r.moduleHealth || [];
  var mttr = r.avgMTTR || {};
  var compliance = r.slaCompliance;
  var weekTrend = s.newThisWeek > s.newLastWeek ? '▲' : s.newThisWeek < s.newLastWeek ? '▼' : '–';
  var trendColor = s.newThisWeek > s.newLastWeek ? 'var(--critical)' : 'var(--low)';
  var cards = [
    { label: 'Open Critical', value: s.openCritical || 0, sub: 'active issues', color: 'var(--critical)' },
    { label: 'SLA Compliance', value: compliance !== null && compliance !== undefined ? compliance + '%' : '—', sub: 'last 30 days', color: compliance >= 90 ? 'var(--low)' : 'var(--accent)' },
    { label: 'Resolved This Week', value: s.resolvedThisWeek || 0, sub: 'last 7 days', color: 'var(--low)' },
    { label: 'New This Week', value: (s.newThisWeek || 0) + ' ' + weekTrend, sub: 'vs ' + (s.newLastWeek||0) + ' last week', color: trendColor }
  ];
  var kpiHtml = '<div style="display:grid;grid-template-columns:repeat(4,1fr);gap:14px;margin-bottom:20px;">' +
    cards.map(function(c) {
      return '<div class="card" style="text-align:center;">' +
        '<div style="font-size:28px;font-weight:800;color:' + c.color + ';line-height:1;">' + c.value + '</div>' +
        '<div style="font-size:13px;font-weight:600;color:var(--text-primary);margin-top:4px;">' + c.label + '</div>' +
        '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-top:2px;">' + c.sub + '</div>' +
        '</div>';
    }).join('') + '</div>';
  var mhGrade = function(score) {
    if (score >= 90) return {g:'A',c:'var(--low)'}; if (score >= 75) return {g:'B',c:'#74b9ff'};
    if (score >= 60) return {g:'C',c:'var(--accent)'}; if (score >= 45) return {g:'D',c:'var(--high)'}; return {g:'F',c:'var(--critical)'};
  };
  var mhHtml = mh.length ? '<div class="card" style="margin-bottom:16px;"><div class="card-title mb-16">Module Health</div>' +
    '<table style="width:100%;font-size:12px;"><thead><tr><th style="text-align:left;color:var(--text-muted);">Module</th><th style="text-align:right;color:var(--text-muted);">Score</th><th style="text-align:right;color:var(--text-muted);">Grade</th></tr></thead><tbody>' +
    mh.map(function(m) {
      var gd = mhGrade(m.score || m.healthScore || 0);
      return '<tr><td style="padding:6px 0;">' + (m.module||m.name||'') + '</td>' +
        '<td style="text-align:right;font-family:var(--font-mono);">' + (m.score||m.healthScore||0) + '</td>' +
        '<td style="text-align:right;"><span style="font-weight:700;color:' + gd.c + ';">' + gd.g + '</span></td></tr>';
    }).join('') + '</tbody></table></div>' : '';
  var mttrKeys = ['Critical','High','Medium','Low'];
  var mttrHtml = '<div class="card"><div class="card-title mb-16">Avg MTTR by Priority</div>' +
    mttrKeys.map(function(p) {
      var val = mttr[p] || 0;
      var maxVal = Math.max.apply(null, mttrKeys.map(function(k){return mttr[k]||0;})) || 1;
      var pct = Math.round((val / maxVal) * 100);
      var pColors = {Critical:'var(--critical)',High:'var(--high)',Medium:'var(--accent)',Low:'var(--low)'};
      return '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:12px;margin-bottom:10px;">' +
        '<span style="width:60px;font-size:12px;color:' + (pColors[p]||'') + ';font-weight:600;">' + p + '</span>' +
        '<div style="flex:1;height:12px;background:var(--bg-elevated);border-radius:6px;overflow:hidden;">' +
        '<div style="height:100%;width:' + pct + '%;background:' + (pColors[p]||'var(--accent)') + ';border-radius:6px;"></div></div>' +
        '<span style="width:50px;font-size:11px;font-family:var(--font-mono);color:var(--text-muted);text-align:right;">' + val + 'h</span>' +
        '</div>';
    }).join('') + '</div>';
  area.innerHTML = kpiHtml + mhHtml + mttrHtml;
};

// ─── Mobile Navigation ────────────────────────────────────────
App.initMobileNav = function() {
  var sidebar = document.getElementById('sidebar');
  var topbar = document.getElementById('topbar') || document.querySelector('.topbar');
  if (!sidebar || !topbar) return;
  if (document.getElementById('hamburgerBtn')) return; // already set up

  // Inject hamburger button into topbar
  var btn = document.createElement('button');
  btn.id = 'hamburgerBtn';
  btn.className = 'topbar-hamburger';
  btn.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Toggle menu');
  btn.innerHTML = '<span></span><span></span><span></span>';
  topbar.insertBefore(btn, topbar.firstChild);

  // Overlay element
  var overlay = document.createElement('div');
  overlay.id = 'sidebarOverlay';
  overlay.style.cssText = 'display:none;position:fixed;inset:0;background:rgba(0,0,0,0.45);z-index:299;';
  document.body.appendChild(overlay);

  btn.addEventListener('click', function() {
    sidebar.classList.toggle('open');
    overlay.style.display = sidebar.classList.contains('open') ? 'block' : 'none';
  });
  overlay.addEventListener('click', function() {
    sidebar.classList.remove('open');
    overlay.style.display = 'none';
  });
  // Close sidebar on nav item click (mobile)
  sidebar.querySelectorAll('.nav-item').forEach(function(item) {
    item.addEventListener('click', function() {
      sidebar.classList.remove('open');
      overlay.style.display = 'none';
    });
  });
};

// ─── SLA Countdown (client-side badge helper) ─────────────────
App.renderSLACountdown = function(issue) {
  if (!App.featureFlags || App.featureFlags['SLA_COUNTDOWN_DISPLAY_ENABLED'] !== 'true') return '';
  if (['Resolved','Closed'].includes(issue.status)) return '';
  var hrs = issue.slaHoursRemaining;
  var total = issue.slaHours || 24;
  var pct = total > 0 ? (hrs / total) : 1;
  var color, label;
  if (issue.slaBreached) { color = 'var(--critical)'; label = 'SLA BREACHED'; }
  else if (pct < 0.2) { color = 'var(--critical)'; label = Math.round(hrs) + 'h left'; }
  else if (pct < 0.5) { color = 'var(--accent)'; label = Math.round(hrs) + 'h left'; }
  else { color = 'var(--low)'; label = Math.round(hrs) + 'h left'; }
  return '<span style="font-size:10px;font-weight:600;color:' + color + ';font-family:var(--font-mono);">' + label + '</span>';
};

// ─── SLA Risk Forecast widget (Dashboard addition) ────────────
App.renderSLAForecastWidget = async function(containerEl) {
  if (!App.featureFlags || App.featureFlags['SLA_PREDICTOR_ENABLED'] !== 'true') return;
  if (!containerEl) return;
  containerEl.innerHTML = '<div class="skeleton" style="height:160px;border-radius:14px;"></div>';
  var r = await App.call('predictSLABreaches');
  if (!r || !r.success || !r.predictions || r.predictions.length === 0) {
    containerEl.innerHTML = '<div class="card"><div class="card-title mb-8">SLA Risk Forecast</div><p class="text-muted" style="font-size:12px;">No at-risk issues detected.</p></div>';
    return;
  }
  containerEl.innerHTML = '<div class="card"><div class="card-title mb-12">⚠️ SLA Risk Forecast</div>' +
    r.predictions.slice(0, 8).map(function(p) {
      var rColor = p.riskScore >= 90 ? 'var(--critical)' : p.riskScore >= 70 ? 'var(--accent)' : 'var(--text-muted)';
      return '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:8px;padding:5px 0;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);font-size:11px;">' +
        '<span class="issue-id" onclick="App.navigate(\'issue-detail\',{id:\'' + p.issueId + '\'})" style="cursor:pointer;">' + p.issueId + '</span>' +
        '<span style="flex:1;color:var(--text-secondary);overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;white-space:nowrap;">' + p.title + '</span>' +
        '<div style="width:40px;height:6px;border-radius:3px;background:var(--bg-elevated);overflow:hidden;flex-shrink:0;">' +
        '<div style="height:100%;width:' + p.riskScore + '%;background:' + rColor + ';"></div></div>' +
        '<span style="font-family:var(--font-mono);font-weight:700;color:' + rColor + ';width:30px;text-align:right;">' + p.riskScore + '</span>' +
        '</div>';
    }).join('') + '</div>';
};

// ─── AI Issue Suggestions (New Issue form) ─────────────────────
App.requestAITriage = async function() {
  if (!App.featureFlags || App.featureFlags['AI_SMART_TRIAGE_ENABLED'] !== 'true') return;
  var title = (document.getElementById('issueTitle') || document.getElementById('newIssueTitle') || {}).value || '';
  var desc = (document.getElementById('issueDescription') || document.getElementById('newIssueDesc') || {}).value || '';
  if (!title.trim()) { App.showToast('Enter a title first', 'warning'); return; }
  var btn = document.getElementById('aiTriageBtn');
  if (btn) { btn.textContent = '⏳ Analysing...'; btn.disabled = true; }
  var r = await App.call('getAIIssueSuggestions', title, desc);
  if (btn) { btn.textContent = '✨ AI Suggest'; btn.disabled = false; }
  if (!r || !r.success) { App.showToast('AI triage failed: ' + (r&&r.error||''), 'error'); return; }
  var s = r.suggestions || {};
  var chips = document.getElementById('aiTriageChips');
  if (!chips) return;
  var conf = s.confidence ? Math.round(s.confidence * 100) + '% conf' : '';
  chips.innerHTML = '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;flex-wrap:wrap;margin-top:8px;">' +
    (s.priority ? '<span class="badge" style="cursor:pointer;" onclick="App.acceptAITriage(\'priority\',\'' + s.priority + '\')" title="Click to apply">' + s.priority + ' priority</span>' : '') +
    (s.module ? '<span class="badge" style="cursor:pointer;background:var(--bg-elevated);" onclick="App.acceptAITriage(\'module\',\'' + s.module + '\')" title="Click to apply">' + s.module + '</span>' : '') +
    (conf ? '<span class="badge" style="background:transparent;border-color:var(--border);">' + conf + '</span>' : '') +
    '</div>' +
    (s.impact ? '<div style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-muted);margin-top:4px;">' + s.impact + '</div>' : '');
};

App.acceptAITriage = function(field, value) {
  if (field === 'priority') {
    var sel = document.getElementById('issuePriority') || document.getElementById('newIssuePriority');
    if (sel) sel.value = value;
  } else if (field === 'module') {
    var mod = document.getElementById('issueModule') || document.getElementById('newIssueModule');
    if (mod) { mod.value = value; }
  }
  App.showToast('Applied AI suggestion: ' + value, 'success');
};

// ─── Bulk Actions (Phase 5 additions) ────────────────────────
App.bulkUpdateIssuesPhase5 = async function(action, value) {
  if (!App._selectedIssues || App._selectedIssues.size === 0) { App.showToast('No issues selected', 'warning'); return; }
  var ids = Array.from(App._selectedIssues);
  var r = await App.call('bulkUpdateIssues', ids, action, value);
  if (r && r.success) {
    App.showToast('Updated ' + r.updated + ' issues', 'success');
    App._selectedIssues.clear();
    App._updateBulkBar();
    App.renderIssueList();
  } else {
    App.showToast('Bulk update failed: ' + (r&&r.error||''), 'error');
  }
};


// ============================================================
// TECHTRACK UI/UX ENHANCEMENT SUITE v2.0
// Slide Panel · Keyboard Shortcuts · Saved Views · Compact Mode
// SLA Bars · Inline Edit · Activity Timeline · Enhanced Filters

// ─── HELPER UTILITIES ──────────────────────────────────────────
App._esc = function(s) {
  return String(s||'').replace(/&/g,'&amp;').replace(/</g,'&lt;').replace(/>/g,'&gt;').replace(/"/g,'&quot;');
};
App._relTime = function(d) {
  if (!d) return '—';
  var dt = new Date(d); if (isNaN(dt)) return d;
  var diff = Date.now() - dt, m = Math.floor(diff/60000);
  if (m < 1) return 'just now';
  if (m < 60) return m + 'm ago';
  var h = Math.floor(m/60); if (h < 24) return h + 'h ago';
  var days = Math.floor(h/24); if (days < 7) return days + 'd ago';
  return dt.toLocaleDateString();
};
App._computeSLA = function(issue) {
  if (!issue || !issue.CreatedDate || !issue.SLAHours) return null;
  if (['Resolved','Closed'].includes(issue.Status)) return null;
  var created = new Date(issue.CreatedDate);
  var slaMs = parseFloat(issue.SLAHours) * 3600000;
  var deadline = new Date(created.getTime() + slaMs);
  var now = new Date();
  var elapsed = now - created;
  var pct = Math.round((elapsed / slaMs) * 100);
  var remaining = deadline - now;
  var hLeft = Math.round(remaining / 3600000);
  var status, label;
  if (remaining < 0) { status = 'breach'; label = 'SLA Breached'; }
  else if (pct >= 75) { status = 'risk'; label = hLeft + 'h left'; }
  else { status = 'ok'; label = hLeft + 'h left'; }
  return { pct: Math.min(pct, 100), status, label };
};
App.copyTicketId = function(id, btn) {
  var copy = function(t) {
    if (navigator.clipboard) { navigator.clipboard.writeText(t); }
    else { var ta = document.createElement('textarea'); ta.value = t; document.body.appendChild(ta); ta.select(); document.execCommand('copy'); document.body.removeChild(ta); }
    App.showToast('Copied: ' + t, 'success');
    if (btn) { var o = btn.textContent; btn.textContent = '✓'; btn.classList.add('tt-copied'); setTimeout(function(){ btn.textContent = o; btn.classList.remove('tt-copied'); }, 1500); }
  };
  copy(id);
};

// ─── SLIDE PANEL ───────────────────────────────────────────────
var SlidePanel = {
  _open: false,
  _currentId: null,
  _fromPanel: false,

  open: function(issueId) {
    this._currentId = issueId;
    this._open = true;
    var panel = document.getElementById('slidePanel');
    var overlay = document.getElementById('slidePanelOverlay');
    if (panel) panel.classList.add('open');
    if (overlay) overlay.classList.add('open');
    document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
    this._load(issueId);
  },

  close: function() {
    this._open = false;
    this._currentId = null;
    var panel = document.getElementById('slidePanel');
    var overlay = document.getElementById('slidePanelOverlay');
    if (panel) panel.classList.remove('open');
    if (overlay) overlay.classList.remove('open');
    document.body.style.overflow = '';
  },

  _load: async function(issueId) {
    var body = document.getElementById('slidePanelBody');
    var idEl = document.getElementById('slidePanelId');
    var titleEl = document.getElementById('slidePanelTitle');
    if (!body) return;
    body.innerHTML = '<div class="slide-panel-loading"><div class="slide-panel-spinner"></div>Loading issue…</div>';
    if (idEl) idEl.textContent = issueId;
    try {
      var r = await App.callAsync('getIssueById', issueId);
      if (!r || !r.success || !r.issue) {
        body.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state-v3"><div class="es-graphic">&#x26A0;</div><div class="es-title">Issue not found</div><div class="es-subtitle">This issue may have been deleted or you may not have access.</div></div>';
        return;
      }
      var issue = r.issue;
      if (idEl) idEl.textContent = issue.IssueID || issueId;
      if (titleEl) titleEl.textContent = issue.Title || 'Untitled';
      body.innerHTML = SlidePanel._renderBody(issue);
    } catch(e) {
      body.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-state-v3"><div class="es-graphic">&#x26A0;</div><div class="es-title">Error loading</div><div class="es-subtitle">' + (e.message||'Unknown error') + '</div></div>';
    }
  },

  _renderBody: function(issue) {
    var sla = App._computeSLA(issue);
    var slaBar = sla ? '<div class="sla-bar-wrap" style="margin-top:10px"><div class="sla-bar-track"><div class="sla-bar-fill ' + sla.status + '" style="width:' + sla.pct + '%"></div></div><div class="sla-bar-label ' + sla.status + '">' + sla.label + '</div></div>' : '';
    var sm = {'Open':'open','Acknowledged':'acknowledged','In Progress':'in-progress','Testing':'testing','Resolved':'resolved','Closed':'closed','Blocked':'blocked','Need Info':'need-info','Reopened':'open'};
    var sc = sm[issue.Status] || 'open';
    var pc = (issue.Priority||'').toLowerCase();
    var desc = issue.Description ? '<div class="card" style="padding:16px;margin-top:12px"><div class="section-title">Description</div><div style="font-size:13px;color:var(--text-secondary);line-height:1.7;white-space:pre-wrap">' + App._esc(issue.Description) + '</div></div>' : '';
    return '<div style="display:flex;flex-direction:column;gap:12px">'
      + '<div class="card" style="padding:16px">'
      + '<div class="issue-title-display" style="font-size:17px;margin-bottom:10px">' + App._esc(issue.Title||'') + '</div>'
      + '<div style="display:flex;gap:7px;flex-wrap:wrap;margin-bottom:10px">'
      + '<span class="badge-priority ' + pc + '">' + (issue.Priority||'—') + '</span>'
      + '<span class="badge-status ' + sc + '">' + (issue.Status||'—') + '</span>'
      + (issue.Module ? '<span class="tag-chip">' + App._esc(issue.Module) + '</span>' : '')
      + '</div>'
      + slaBar
      + '</div>'
      + '<div class="card" style="padding:16px"><div class="section-title">Details</div><div class="meta-list">'
      + '<div class="meta-item"><span class="meta-key">Reporter</span><span class="meta-value">' + App._esc(issue.RaisedBy||'—') + '</span></div>'
      + '<div class="meta-item"><span class="meta-key">Assigned</span><span class="meta-value">' + App._esc(issue.AssignedTo||'Unassigned') + '</span></div>'
      + '<div class="meta-item"><span class="meta-key">Created</span><span class="meta-value">' + App._relTime(issue.CreatedDate) + '</span></div>'
      + (issue.Environment ? '<div class="meta-item"><span class="meta-key">Env</span><span class="meta-value">' + App._esc(issue.Environment) + '</span></div>' : '')
      + (issue.Impact ? '<div class="meta-item"><span class="meta-key">Impact</span><span class="meta-value">' + App._esc(issue.Impact) + '</span></div>' : '')
      + '</div></div>'
      + desc
      + '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;margin-top:4px">'
      + '<button class="btn-primary" style="flex:1" onclick="SlidePanel.openFull()">Open Full Detail &#x2197;</button>'
      + '<button class="btn-secondary" onclick="SlidePanel.close()">Close</button>'
      + '</div></div>';
  },

  copyId: function() {
    var idEl = document.getElementById('slidePanelId');
    var id = idEl ? idEl.textContent : this._currentId;
    if (!id || id === '—') return;
    App.copyTicketId(id, idEl);
  },

  openFull: function() {
    if (!this._currentId) return;
    var id = this._currentId;
    this._fromPanel = true;
    this.close();
    setTimeout(function() {
      App.navigate('issue-detail', { id: id });
      SlidePanel._fromPanel = false;
    }, 50);
  }
};

// ─── NAVIGATE PATCH (slide panel intercept) ─────────────────────
(function() {
  var _orig = App.navigate.bind(App);
  App.navigate = function(page, params) {
    // Intercept issue-detail navigation from list context → show slide panel
    if (page === 'issue-detail' && params && params.id && !SlidePanel._fromPanel) {
      var contentArea = document.getElementById('contentArea');
      var hasTable = contentArea && contentArea.querySelector('tbody tr');
      if (hasTable) {
        SlidePanel.open(params.id);
        return;
      }
    }
    _orig(page, params);
  };
})();

// ─── KEYBOARD SHORTCUTS ─────────────────────────────────────────
var Keyboard = {
  init: function() {
    document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
      var tag = (document.activeElement || {}).tagName || '';
      var isInput = ['INPUT','TEXTAREA','SELECT'].includes(tag);
      var isCE = document.activeElement && document.activeElement.contentEditable === 'true';

      if (e.key === 'Escape') {
        Search.close();
        SlidePanel.close();
        Keyboard._closeKbdHelp();
        if (isInput) document.activeElement.blur();
        return;
      }

      if (isInput || isCE) return;

      if (e.key === 'c' || e.key === 'C') {
        if (!e.ctrlKey && !e.metaKey && !e.altKey) { e.preventDefault(); App.navigate('create-issue'); }
      } else if (e.key === '/') {
        e.preventDefault(); Search.open();
      } else if (e.key === 'f' || e.key === 'F') {
        if (!e.ctrlKey && !e.metaKey) { e.preventDefault(); Keyboard._toggleFilter(); }
      } else if (e.key === '?') {
        e.preventDefault(); Keyboard._toggleKbdHelp();
      } else if ((e.key === 'k' || e.key === 'K') && (e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey)) {
        e.preventDefault();
        var bar = document.getElementById('aiBar');
        if (bar) { bar.focus(); bar.select(); }
      }
    });
  },

  _toggleFilter: function() {
    var exp = document.querySelector('.filter-bar-expanded');
    if (exp) {
      exp.classList.toggle('open');
      var btn = document.querySelector('[data-filter-toggle]');
      if (btn) btn.classList.toggle('active');
    }
  },

  _toggleKbdHelp: function() {
    var o = document.getElementById('kbdOverlay');
    if (o) o.classList.toggle('open');
  },

  _closeKbdHelp: function() {
    var o = document.getElementById('kbdOverlay');
    if (o) o.classList.remove('open');
  }
};

// ─── SAVED VIEWS ────────────────────────────────────────────────
var SavedViews = {
  _key: 'tt_saved_views',
  _custom: [],
  _defaults: [
    { id: 'all',      name: 'All Issues',       icon: '≡',  filters: {} },
    { id: 'critical', name: 'Critical & High',  icon: '⚠',  filters: { priority: 'Critical' } },
    { id: 'my-open',  name: 'My Open Issues',   icon: '👤', filters: { mine: true } },
    { id: 'sla-risk', name: 'SLA at Risk',      icon: '⏱', filters: { sla: 'risk' } },
    { id: 'blocked',  name: 'Blocked Issues',   icon: '🚫', filters: { status: 'Blocked' } }
  ],

  init: function() {
    try { this._custom = JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem(this._key) || '[]'); } catch(e) { this._custom = []; }
  },

  getAll: function() { return this._defaults.concat(this._custom); },

  save: function(name, filters) {
    var v = { id: 'v_' + Date.now(), name: name, icon: '⭐', filters: filters };
    this._custom.push(v);
    localStorage.setItem(this._key, JSON.stringify(this._custom));
    App.showToast('View saved: ' + name, 'success');
    return v;
  },

  delete: function(id) {
    this._custom = this._custom.filter(function(v){ return v.id !== id; });
    localStorage.setItem(this._key, JSON.stringify(this._custom));
  },

  apply: function(id) {
    var view = this.getAll().find(function(v){ return v.id === id; });
    if (!view) return;
    App.showToast('View: ' + view.name, 'info');
    // Apply basic filters if on issue list
    var statusSel = document.getElementById('filterStatus');
    var prioSel = document.getElementById('filterPriority');
    if (view.filters.priority && prioSel) prioSel.value = view.filters.priority;
    if (view.filters.status && statusSel) statusSel.value = view.filters.status;
    // Trigger filter change
    var evt = new Event('change', { bubbles: true });
    if (statusSel) statusSel.dispatchEvent(evt);
    if (prioSel) prioSel.dispatchEvent(evt);
  },

  renderDropdown: function(containerId) {
    var c = document.getElementById(containerId);
    if (!c) return;
    var views = this.getAll();
    var items = views.map(function(v) {
      return '<div class="saved-view-item" onclick="SavedViews.apply(\'' + v.id + '\');document.querySelector(\'.saved-views-dropdown\').classList.remove(\'open\');document.querySelector(\'.saved-views-btn\').classList.remove(\'open\')">'
        + '<span>' + v.icon + '</span>'
        + '<span>' + App._esc(v.name) + '</span>'
        + (!v.id.startsWith('v_') ? '' : '<button class="saved-view-delete" onclick="event.stopPropagation();SavedViews.delete(\'' + v.id + '\');SavedViews.renderDropdown(\'' + containerId + '\')">&#x2715;</button>')
        + '</div>';
    }).join('');
    c.innerHTML = items + '<div class="saved-views-save-btn" onclick="SavedViews._promptSave(\'' + containerId + '\')">+ Save current filters</div>';
  },

  _promptSave: function(containerId) {
    var name = prompt('Name this view:');
    if (!name || !name.trim()) return;
    // Collect current filters
    var f = {};
    var s = document.getElementById('filterStatus'); if (s && s.value) f.status = s.value;
    var p = document.getElementById('filterPriority'); if (p && p.value) f.priority = p.value;
    this.save(name.trim(), f);
    this.renderDropdown(containerId);
    document.querySelector('.saved-views-dropdown') && document.querySelector('.saved-views-dropdown').classList.remove('open');
  },

  toggle: function(btnEl, dropEl) {
    btnEl.classList.toggle('open');
    dropEl.classList.toggle('open');
  }
};

// ─── COMPACT MODE ────────────────────────────────────────────────
var CompactMode = {
  _active: false,
  init: function() {
    this._active = localStorage.getItem('tt_compact') === '1';
    this.apply();
  },
  toggle: function() {
    this._active = !this._active;
    localStorage.setItem('tt_compact', this._active ? '1' : '0');
    this.apply();
    var btn = document.querySelector('.compact-toggle');
    if (btn) { btn.classList.toggle('active', this._active); btn.textContent = this._active ? '⊟ Compact' : '⊞ Compact'; }
  },
  apply: function() {
    var tbl = document.querySelector('table');
    if (tbl) tbl.classList.toggle('tt-compact', this._active);
  }
};

// ─── ROW PREVIEW BUTTONS ─────────────────────────────────────────
App._injectPreviewButtons = function() {
  document.querySelectorAll('tbody tr').forEach(function(row) {
    if (row.querySelector('.row-preview-btn')) return;
    var onclk = row.getAttribute('onclick') || '';
    var m = onclk.match(/id\s*:\s*['"]([^'"]+)['"]/);
    if (!m) return;
    var id = m[1];
    row.dataset.ttId = id;
    var lastTd = row.querySelector('td:last-child');
    if (!lastTd) return;
    // Wrap last td content
    var btn = document.createElement('button');
    btn.className = 'row-preview-btn';
    btn.title = 'Quick preview';
    btn.textContent = 'Preview';
    btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) { e.stopPropagation(); SlidePanel.open(id); });
    lastTd.appendChild(btn);
    // Copy ID button on issue-id cell
    var idCell = row.querySelector('.issue-id');
    if (idCell && !idCell.querySelector('.copy-id-btn')) {
      var copyBtn = document.createElement('button');
      copyBtn.className = 'copy-id-btn';
      copyBtn.title = 'Copy ID';
      copyBtn.textContent = '⎘';
      copyBtn.addEventListener('click', function(e) { e.stopPropagation(); App.copyTicketId(id, copyBtn); });
      idCell.appendChild(copyBtn);
    }
  });
  CompactMode.apply();
};

// ─── ACTIVITY TIMELINE RENDERER ──────────────────────────────────
App.renderActivityTimeline = function(activities) {
  if (!activities || !activities.length) return '<div class="empty-state-v3"><div class="es-graphic">&#x1F4CB;</div><div class="es-title">No activity yet</div></div>';
  var typeMap = { 'created':'created','assigned':'assigned','status':'status','comment':'comment','resolved':'resolved','closed':'closed','blocked':'blocked' };
  return '<div class="activity-timeline">'
    + activities.map(function(a) {
      var action = (a.Action||a.action||'').toLowerCase();
      var dotType = Object.keys(typeMap).find(function(k){ return action.includes(k); }) || 'status';
      var text = (a.Action||a.action||'Activity recorded');
      var user = a.User || a.user || '';
      var time = App._relTime(a.Timestamp || a.timestamp);
      return '<div class="timeline-item">'
        + '<div class="timeline-dot ' + dotType + '"></div>'
        + '<div class="timeline-action">'
        + (user ? '<strong>' + App._esc(user.split('@')[0]) + '</strong> ' : '')
        + App._esc(text)
        + '</div>'
        + '<div class="timeline-time">' + time + '</div>'
        + '</div>';
    }).join('')
    + '</div>';
};

// ─── SLA BAR RENDERER ────────────────────────────────────────────
App.renderSLABar = function(issue) {
  var sla = App._computeSLA(issue);
  if (!sla) return ((['Resolved','Closed'].includes(issue.Status)) ? '<span class="sla-badge ok">&#x2713; Resolved</span>' : '—');
  return '<div class="sla-bar-wrap">'
    + '<div class="sla-bar-track"><div class="sla-bar-fill ' + sla.status + '" style="width:' + sla.pct + '%"></div></div>'
    + '<div class="sla-bar-label ' + sla.status + '">' + sla.label + '</div>'
    + '</div>';
};

// ─── EMPTY STATE RENDERER ────────────────────────────────────────
App.renderEmptyState = function(icon, title, subtitle, actionLabel, actionFn) {
  return '<div class="empty-state-v3">'
    + '<div class="es-graphic">' + icon + '</div>'
    + '<div class="es-title">' + title + '</div>'
    + '<div class="es-subtitle">' + subtitle + '</div>'
    + (actionLabel ? '<div class="es-action"><button class="btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="' + actionFn + '">' + actionLabel + '</button></div>' : '')
    + '</div>';
};

// ─── MUTATION OBSERVER for table rows ────────────────────────────
(function() {
  var observer = new MutationObserver(function(mutations) {
    var hasNew = mutations.some(function(m) {
      return Array.from(m.addedNodes).some(function(n){ return n.nodeType === 1 && (n.tagName === 'TR' || n.querySelector && n.querySelector('tr')); });
    });
    if (hasNew) {
      setTimeout(function() { App._injectPreviewButtons(); CompactMode.apply(); }, 80);
    }
  });
  var contentArea = document.getElementById('contentArea');
  if (contentArea) observer.observe(contentArea, { childList: true, subtree: true });
})();
