// ─── TOP PROGRESS BAR ──────────────────────────────────────────
var ProgressBar = {
  _el: null,
  _t: null,
  init: function() { this._el = document.getElementById('ttProgressBar'); },
  start: function() {
    if (!this._el) return;
    clearTimeout(this._t);
    this._el.className = 'tt-progress-bar loading';
  },
  done: function() {
    if (!this._el) return;
    this._el.className = 'tt-progress-bar done';
    this._t = setTimeout(function() {
      if (ProgressBar._el) ProgressBar._el.className = 'tt-progress-bar';
    }, 400);
  }
};

// Patch App.navigate to trigger progress bar
(function() {
  var _orig = App.navigate.bind(App);
  App.navigate = function(page, params) {
    ProgressBar.start();
    var r = _orig(page, params);
    setTimeout(function() { ProgressBar.done(); }, 600);
    return r;
  };
})();

// ─── PAGE TRANSITIONS ──────────────────────────────────────────
(function() {
  var _origInner = Object.getOwnPropertyDescriptor(Element.prototype, 'innerHTML');
  var contentArea = document.getElementById('contentArea');
  if (contentArea) {
    var observer2 = new MutationObserver(function() {
      contentArea.classList.remove('tt-page-enter');
      void contentArea.offsetWidth; // reflow
      contentArea.classList.add('tt-page-enter');
    });
    observer2.observe(contentArea, { childList: true });
  }
})();

// ─── COMMAND PALETTE ───────────────────────────────────────────
var CmdPalette = {
  _open: false,
  _sel: 0,
  _items: [],

  open: function() {
    this._open = true;
    var overlay = document.getElementById('cmdOverlay');
    var input = document.getElementById('cmdInput');
    if (overlay) overlay.classList.add('open');
    if (input) { input.value = ''; input.focus(); }
    this._sel = 0;
    this._loadDefaults();
  },

  close: function() {
    this._open = false;
    var overlay = document.getElementById('cmdOverlay');
    if (overlay) overlay.classList.remove('open');
  },

  run: function(action) {
    this.close();
    switch(action) {
      case 'create':       App.navigate('create-issue'); break;
      case 'dashboard':    App.navigate('dashboard'); break;
      case 'kanban':       App.navigate('kanban'); break;
      case 'my-issues':    App.navigate('my-issues'); break;
      case 'issue-list':   App.navigate('issue-list'); break;
      case 'focus':        FocusMode.toggle(); break;
      case 'theme':        Themes.toggle(); break;
      case 'filter-critical':
        App.navigate('issue-list');
        setTimeout(function() {
          var p = document.getElementById('filterPriority');
          if (p) { p.value = 'Critical'; p.dispatchEvent(new Event('change', {bubbles:true})); }
        }, 400);
        break;
      case 'compact':      CompactMode.toggle(); break;
      case 'shortcuts':    Keyboard._toggleKbdHelp(); break;
      default:
        if (action.startsWith('issue:')) {
          var id = action.replace('issue:','');
          SlidePanel.open(id);
        } else {
          App.navigate(action);
        }
    }
  },

  _loadDefaults: function() {
    var results = document.getElementById('cmdResults');
    if (!results) return;
    // Keep existing default HTML — only override when query typed
  },

  search: async function(query) {
    if (!query.trim()) { this._loadDefaults(); return; }
    var results = document.getElementById('cmdResults');
    if (!results) return;

    var lq = query.toLowerCase();
    // Quick nav matches
    var navItems = [
      { title:'Dashboard', sub:'Overview & KPIs', action:'dashboard', icon:'⌂' },
      { title:'All Issues', sub:'Browse issue list', action:'issue-list', icon:'≡' },
      { title:'Kanban Board', sub:'Drag-drop workflow', action:'kanban', icon:'▦' },
      { title:'My Issues', sub:'Your assigned issues', action:'my-issues', icon:'👤' },
      { title:'Create Ticket', sub:'Report a new issue', action:'create', icon:'+' },
      { title:'Focus Mode', sub:'Hide sidebar', action:'focus', icon:'◎' },
      { title:'Switch Theme', sub:'Change color theme', action:'theme', icon:'◑' },
      { title:'Keyboard Shortcuts', sub:'View all shortcuts', action:'shortcuts', icon:'⌨' },
      { title:'Compact Mode', sub:'Toggle table density', action:'compact', icon:'⊟' }
    ];
    var matched = navItems.filter(function(n){ return n.title.toLowerCase().includes(lq) || n.sub.toLowerCase().includes(lq); });

    // Search issues in cache
    var issueMatches = [];
    if (App.allIssues && App.allIssues.length) {
      App.allIssues.forEach(function(iss) {
        var score = 0;
        if ((iss.IssueID||'').toLowerCase().includes(lq)) score += 100;
        if ((iss.Title||'').toLowerCase().includes(lq)) score += 50;
        if ((iss.Description||'').toLowerCase().includes(lq)) score += 10;
        if (score > 0) issueMatches.push({ iss: iss, score: score });
      });
      issueMatches.sort(function(a,b){ return b.score - a.score; });
      issueMatches = issueMatches.slice(0, 6);
    }

    var html = '';
    if (matched.length) {
      html += '<div class="cmd-section-label">Navigation</div>';
      matched.slice(0,5).forEach(function(n, i) {
        html += '<div class="cmd-item' + (i===0&&!issueMatches.length?' selected':'') + '" onclick="CmdPalette.run(\'' + n.action + '\')">'
          + '<div class="cmd-item-icon">' + n.icon + '</div>'
          + '<div class="cmd-item-body"><div class="cmd-item-title">' + App._esc(n.title) + '</div><div class="cmd-item-sub">' + App._esc(n.sub) + '</div></div>'
          + '</div>';
      });
    }
    if (issueMatches.length) {
      html += '<div class="cmd-section-label">Issues</div>';
      issueMatches.forEach(function(m, i) {
        var iss = m.iss;
        var pc = (iss.Priority||'').toLowerCase();
        html += '<div class="cmd-item' + (i===0&&!matched.length?' selected':'') + '" onclick="CmdPalette.run(\'issue:' + iss.IssueID + '\')">'
          + '<div class="cmd-item-icon"><span class="priority-dot ' + pc + '"></span></div>'
          + '<div class="cmd-item-body"><div class="cmd-item-title">' + App._esc(iss.Title||'Untitled') + '</div><div class="cmd-item-sub">' + (iss.IssueID||'') + ' · ' + (iss.Status||'') + '</div></div>'
          + '</div>';
      });
    }
    if (!html) html = '<div class="cmd-empty">No results for "<strong>' + App._esc(query) + '</strong>"</div>';
    results.innerHTML = html;
  },

  _handleKey: function(e) {
    if (!CmdPalette._open) return;
    var items = document.querySelectorAll('#cmdResults .cmd-item');
    if (!items.length) return;
    if (e.key === 'ArrowDown') {
      e.preventDefault();
      CmdPalette._sel = (CmdPalette._sel + 1) % items.length;
    } else if (e.key === 'ArrowUp') {
      e.preventDefault();
      CmdPalette._sel = (CmdPalette._sel - 1 + items.length) % items.length;
    } else if (e.key === 'Enter') {
      e.preventDefault();
      var sel = items[CmdPalette._sel];
      if (sel) sel.click();
      return;
    }
    items.forEach(function(el, i) { el.classList.toggle('selected', i === CmdPalette._sel); });
    var sel = items[CmdPalette._sel];
    if (sel) sel.scrollIntoView({ block: 'nearest' });
  },

  init: function() {
    var overlay = document.getElementById('cmdOverlay');
    var input   = document.getElementById('cmdInput');
    if (overlay) overlay.addEventListener('click', function(e) { if (e.target === overlay) CmdPalette.close(); });
    if (input) {
      input.addEventListener('input', function() { CmdPalette.search(this.value); });
      input.addEventListener('keydown', CmdPalette._handleKey);
    }
    document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
      var tag = (document.activeElement||{}).tagName||'';
      var isInput = ['INPUT','TEXTAREA','SELECT'].includes(tag);
      if ((e.key === 'p' || e.key === 'P') && (e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey)) {
        e.preventDefault(); CmdPalette.open();
      }
      if (e.key === 'Escape' && CmdPalette._open) CmdPalette.close();
    });
  }
};

// ─── STATS BAR ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
var StatsBar = {
  load: async function() {
    var el = document.getElementById('tsRefresh');
    if (el) { el.style.opacity = '0.4'; }
    try {
      var r = await App.callAsync('getDashboardStats');
      if (r && r.success && r.stats) {
        var s = r.stats;
        var open = document.getElementById('tsOpen');
        var wip  = document.getElementById('tsWip');
        var crit = document.getElementById('tsCritical');
        var sla  = document.getElementById('tsSla');
        if (open) open.textContent = (s.open !== undefined ? s.open : (s.total||'—'));
        if (wip)  wip.textContent  = (s.inProgress !== undefined ? s.inProgress : '—');
        if (crit) crit.textContent = s.critical || '0';
        if (sla)  sla.textContent  = s.slaBreached || '0';
        // Update critical badge
        var badge = document.getElementById('criticalBadge');
        var bc    = document.getElementById('criticalBadgeCount');
        if (badge && bc) {
          var critCount = parseInt(s.critical||0);
          bc.textContent = critCount;
          badge.classList.toggle('hidden', critCount === 0);
        }
        // Update sidebar badges
        SidebarBadges.update(s);
      }
    } catch(e) { /* silent fail */ }
    if (el) { el.style.opacity = ''; }
  }
};

// ─── SIDEBAR NAV BADGES ────────────────────────────────────────
var SidebarBadges = {
  update: function(stats) {
    // Show total open on "All Issues" nav item
    var allIssuesNav = document.querySelector('.nav-item[data-page="issue-list"]');
    if (allIssuesNav && !allIssuesNav.querySelector('.nav-badge')) {
      var badge = document.createElement('span');
      badge.className = 'nav-badge';
      badge.id = 'navBadgeAll';
      allIssuesNav.appendChild(badge);
    }
    var nb = document.getElementById('navBadgeAll');
    if (nb && stats) {
      var open = (stats.open !== undefined ? stats.open : 0);
      nb.textContent = open > 99 ? '99+' : open;
      nb.className = 'nav-badge' + (stats.critical > 0 ? ' urgent' : '');
    }
  }
};

// ─── FOCUS MODE ────────────────────────────────────────────────
var FocusMode = {
  _active: false,
  toggle: function() {
    this._active = !this._active;
    document.body.classList.toggle('focus-mode', this._active);
    var btn = document.getElementById('focusModeBtn');
    if (btn) {
      btn.textContent = this._active ? '◉ Unfocus' : '◎ Focus';
      btn.classList.toggle('active', this._active);
    }
    var stats = document.getElementById('topbarStats');
    if (stats) stats.classList.toggle('sidebar-collapsed', this._active);
    App.showToast(this._active ? 'Focus mode on' : 'Focus mode off', 'info');
  }
};

// ─── CARD VIEW ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
var CardView = {
  _active: false,
  _key: 'tt_card_view',

  init: function() {
    this._active = localStorage.getItem(this._key) === '1';
  },

  toggle: function() {
    this._active = !this._active;
    localStorage.setItem(this._key, this._active ? '1' : '0');
    // Re-render issue list
    if (App.renderIssueList) App.renderIssueList();
    App.showToast(this._active ? 'Card view' : 'Table view', 'info');
  },

  renderGrid: function(issues) {
    if (!issues || !issues.length) return App.renderEmptyState('&#x1F4CB;', 'No issues found', 'Try adjusting your filters or create a new ticket.', 'Create Ticket', "App.navigate('create-issue')");
    var html = '<div class="issue-card-grid">';
    issues.forEach(function(iss) {
      var pc = (iss.Priority||'').toLowerCase();
      var sm = {'Open':'open','Acknowledged':'acknowledged','In Progress':'in-progress','Testing':'testing','Resolved':'resolved','Closed':'closed','Blocked':'blocked'};
      var sc = sm[iss.Status] || 'open';
      var sla = App._computeSLA(iss);
      var slaHtml = sla ? '<div class="issue-card-sla"><div class="sla-bar-track" style="height:3px"><div class="sla-bar-fill ' + sla.status + '" style="width:' + sla.pct + '%"></div></div></div>' : '';
      var initials = (iss.AssignedTo||'?').split('@')[0].slice(0,2).toUpperCase();
      html += '<div class="issue-card priority-' + pc + '" onclick="SlidePanel.open(\'' + iss.IssueID + '\')">'
        + '<div class="issue-card-top">'
        + '<span class="issue-card-id">' + App._esc(iss.IssueID||'') + '</span>'
        + '<div class="issue-card-badges"><span class="badge-priority ' + pc + '">' + (iss.Priority||'') + '</span><span class="badge-status ' + sc + '">' + (iss.Status||'') + '</span></div>'
        + '</div>'
        + '<div class="issue-card-title">' + App._esc(iss.Title||'Untitled') + '</div>'
        + (iss.Description ? '<div class="issue-card-desc">' + App._esc(iss.Description) + '</div>' : '')
        + slaHtml
        + '<div class="issue-card-footer">'
        + '<div class="issue-card-assignee"><div class="issue-card-avatar-sm">' + initials + '</div>' + App._esc((iss.AssignedTo||'Unassigned').split('@')[0]) + '</div>'
        + '<div class="issue-card-date">' + App._relTime(iss.CreatedDate) + '</div>'
        + '</div>'
        + '</div>';
    });
    return html + '</div>';
  }
};

// ─── STATUS STEPPER RENDERER ───────────────────────────────────
App.renderStatusStepper = function(currentStatus, issueId) {
  var steps = ['Open','Acknowledged','In Progress','Testing','Resolved','Closed'];
  var blocked = currentStatus === 'Blocked';
  var ci = steps.indexOf(currentStatus);
  if (ci < 0) ci = 0;
  var html = '<div class="status-stepper" style="margin-bottom:14px">';
  if (blocked) {
    html += '<div class="stepper-step active" style="color:var(--critical);background:var(--critical-dim);flex:1;justify-content:center"><span class="step-dot" style="background:var(--critical)"></span>Blocked</div></div>';
    return html;
  }
  steps.forEach(function(s, i) {
    var cls = i < ci ? 'done' : i === ci ? 'active' : 'future';
    var statusKey = s.replace(' ','+');
    html += '<div class="stepper-step ' + cls + '" onclick="App.updateIssueStatus && App.updateIssueStatus(\'' + issueId + '\',\'' + s + '\')" title="Set status: ' + s + '">'
      + '<span class="step-dot"></span>'
      + s + '</div>';
  });
  return html + '</div>';
};

// ─── QUICK FILTER PILLS RENDERER ──────────────────────────────
App.renderQuickFilters = function(containerId, issues) {
  var c = document.getElementById(containerId);
  if (!c) return;
  var total  = issues.length;
  var open   = issues.filter(function(i){ return i.Status==='Open'; }).length;
  var wip    = issues.filter(function(i){ return i.Status==='In Progress'; }).length;
  var blk    = issues.filter(function(i){ return i.Status==='Blocked'; }).length;
  var crit   = issues.filter(function(i){ return i.Priority==='Critical'; }).length;
  var slaAt  = issues.filter(function(i){ var s=App._computeSLA(i); return s&&(s.status==='risk'||s.status==='breach'); }).length;
  var user   = (App.currentUser||{}).email||'';
  var mine   = issues.filter(function(i){ return i.AssignedTo===user; }).length;

  c.innerHTML = '<div class="quick-filter-row" id="qfRow">'
    + '<span class="quick-filter-row-label">Filter</span>'
    + '<span class="qf-pill qf-all active" onclick="QF.apply(\'all\',this)">All <span class="qf-count">' + total + '</span></span>'
    + '<span class="qf-pill qf-open" onclick="QF.apply(\'open\',this)">Open <span class="qf-count">' + open + '</span></span>'
    + '<span class="qf-pill qf-wip" onclick="QF.apply(\'wip\',this)">WIP <span class="qf-count">' + wip + '</span></span>'
    + (blk ? '<span class="qf-pill qf-blocked" onclick="QF.apply(\'blocked\',this)">Blocked <span class="qf-count">' + blk + '</span></span>' : '')
    + '<span class="qf-pill qf-critical" onclick="QF.apply(\'critical\',this)">Critical <span class="qf-count">' + crit + '</span></span>'
    + (slaAt ? '<span class="qf-pill qf-sla" onclick="QF.apply(\'sla\',this)">SLA Risk <span class="qf-count">' + slaAt + '</span></span>' : '')
    + (mine ? '<span class="qf-pill qf-mine" onclick="QF.apply(\'mine\',this)">Mine <span class="qf-count">' + mine + '</span></span>' : '')
    + '<span class="qf-spacer"></span>'
    + '</div>';
};

// Quick filter applier
var QF = {
  _current: 'all',
  apply: function(type, el) {
    this._current = type;
    // Update pill active state
    document.querySelectorAll('.qf-pill').forEach(function(p){ p.classList.remove('active'); });
    if (el) el.classList.add('active');
    // Apply filter to table/card rows
    var rows = document.querySelectorAll('tbody tr');
    var cards = document.querySelectorAll('.issue-card');
    var user = (App.currentUser||{}).email||'';
    function show(el, visible) { el.style.display = visible ? '' : 'none'; }
    rows.forEach(function(row) {
      var status   = (row.dataset.status||row.querySelector('.badge-status')||{textContent:''}).textContent || row.dataset.status || '';
      var priority = (row.querySelector('.badge-priority')||{textContent:''}).textContent;
      var assignee = row.dataset.assignee || '';
      var slaEl    = row.querySelector('.sla-bar-fill');
      var slaRisk  = slaEl && (slaEl.classList.contains('risk') || slaEl.classList.contains('breach'));
      var vis = QF._match(type, status, priority, assignee, slaRisk, user);
      show(row, vis);
    });
    cards.forEach(function(card) {
      var statusEl   = card.querySelector('.badge-status');
      var priorityEl = card.querySelector('.badge-priority');
      var status   = statusEl   ? statusEl.textContent.trim()   : '';
      var priority = priorityEl ? priorityEl.textContent.trim() : '';
      var vis = QF._match(type, status, priority, '', false, user);
      show(card, vis);
    });
  },
  _match: function(type, status, priority, assignee, slaRisk, user) {
    switch(type) {
      case 'all':      return true;
      case 'open':     return status === 'Open';
      case 'wip':      return status === 'In Progress';
      case 'blocked':  return status === 'Blocked';
      case 'critical': return priority === 'Critical';
      case 'sla':      return slaRisk;
      case 'mine':     return assignee === user || assignee.includes(user.split('@')[0]);
      default:         return true;
    }
  }
};

// ─── ARROW KEY TABLE NAVIGATION ────────────────────────────────
var ArrowNav = {
  _focused: -1,
  init: function() {
    document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
      var tag = (document.activeElement||{}).tagName||'';
      if (['INPUT','TEXTAREA','SELECT'].includes(tag)) return;
      var rows = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('tbody tr:not([style*="display: none"])'));
      if (!rows.length) return;
      if (e.key === 'ArrowDown') {
        e.preventDefault();
        ArrowNav._focused = Math.min(ArrowNav._focused + 1, rows.length - 1);
        ArrowNav._highlight(rows);
      } else if (e.key === 'ArrowUp') {
        e.preventDefault();
        ArrowNav._focused = Math.max(ArrowNav._focused - 1, 0);
        ArrowNav._highlight(rows);
      } else if (e.key === 'Enter' && ArrowNav._focused >= 0) {
        var row = rows[ArrowNav._focused];
        if (row) row.click();
      } else if (e.key === 'p' && !e.ctrlKey && !e.metaKey && ArrowNav._focused >= 0) {
        // P key = preview focused row
        var row = rows[ArrowNav._focused];
        if (row) {
          var onclk = row.getAttribute('onclick') || '';
          var m = onclk.match(/id\s*:\s*['"]([^'"]+)['"]/);
          if (m) SlidePanel.open(m[1]);
        }
      }
    });
  },
  _highlight: function(rows) {
    rows.forEach(function(r, i) {
      r.classList.toggle('tt-arrow-focus', i === ArrowNav._focused);
      if (i === ArrowNav._focused) {
        r.style.outline = '2px solid var(--accent)';
        r.style.outlineOffset = '-2px';
        r.scrollIntoView({ block: 'nearest', behavior: 'smooth' });
      } else {
        r.style.outline = '';
      }
    });
  }
};

// ─── SHIFT+CLICK RANGE SELECT ──────────────────────────────────
(function() {
  var _lastChecked = null;
  document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    var cb = e.target.closest('input[type="checkbox"]');
    if (!cb || !cb.closest('tbody')) return;
    if (e.shiftKey && _lastChecked && _lastChecked !== cb) {
      var rows = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('tbody tr'));
      var a = rows.findIndex(function(r){ return r.contains(_lastChecked); });
      var b = rows.findIndex(function(r){ return r.contains(cb); });
      if (a >= 0 && b >= 0) {
        var lo = Math.min(a,b), hi = Math.max(a,b);
        for (var i=lo; i<=hi; i++) {
          var tcb = rows[i].querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
          if (tcb) tcb.checked = true;
        }
      }
    }
    _lastChecked = cb;
  });
})();

// ─── CONFETTI ON RESOLVE ───────────────────────────────────────
App._celebrate = function() {
  var colors = ['#f5a623','#2ed573','#a29bfe','#74b9ff','#fd79a8','#ff6b35'];
  for (var i = 0; i < 28; i++) {
    (function(delay) {
      setTimeout(function() {
        var el = document.createElement('div');
        el.className = 'tt-confetti-piece';
        el.style.cssText = 'left:' + (40+Math.random()*20) + 'vw;top:' + (30+Math.random()*20) + 'vh;background:' + colors[Math.floor(Math.random()*colors.length)] + ';animation-duration:' + (0.6+Math.random()*0.6) + 's';
        document.body.appendChild(el);
        setTimeout(function(){ el.remove(); }, 1400);
      }, delay);
    })(i * 40);
  }
};

// ─── SCROLL TO TOP ─────────────────────────────────────────────
(function() {
  var main = document.querySelector('.main-content') || window;
  var btn = document.getElementById('scrollTopBtn');
  var scrollEl = document.querySelector('.main-content') || document.documentElement;
  if (!btn) return;
  function onScroll() {
    btn.classList.toggle('visible', scrollEl.scrollTop > 300);
  }
  scrollEl.addEventListener('scroll', onScroll, { passive: true });
})();

// ─── RESIZABLE SLIDE PANEL ─────────────────────────────────────
(function() {
  var panel  = document.getElementById('slidePanel');
  if (!panel) return;
  var handle = document.createElement('div');
  handle.className = 'slide-panel-resize-handle';
  panel.insertBefore(handle, panel.firstChild);
  var dragging = false, startX = 0, startW = 0;
  handle.addEventListener('mousedown', function(e) {
    dragging = true; startX = e.clientX; startW = panel.offsetWidth;
    panel.classList.add('resizing');
    document.body.style.userSelect = 'none';
  });
  document.addEventListener('mousemove', function(e) {
    if (!dragging) return;
    var diff = startX - e.clientX;
    var newW = Math.max(340, Math.min(window.innerWidth * 0.85, startW + diff));
    panel.style.width = newW + 'px';
  });
  document.addEventListener('mouseup', function() {
    if (!dragging) return;
    dragging = false;
    panel.classList.remove('resizing');
    document.body.style.userSelect = '';
  });
})();

// ─── GROUPED TABLE HEADER TOGGLE ──────────────────────────────
App._initGroupHeaders = function() {
  document.querySelectorAll('.group-header').forEach(function(h) {
    h.addEventListener('click', function() {
      var next = h.nextElementSibling;
      if (!next) return;
      h.classList.toggle('collapsed');
      next.classList.toggle('collapsed');
    });
  });
};

// ─── SLIDE PANEL TABS ─────────────────────────────────────────
SlidePanel._renderBodyWithTabs = function(issue) {
  var id = issue.IssueID;
  return '<div class="sp-tabs">'
    + '<div class="sp-tab active" onclick="SlidePanel._showTab(this,\'overview\',\'' + id + '\')">Overview</div>'
    + '<div class="sp-tab" onclick="SlidePanel._showTab(this,\'activity\',\'' + id + '\')">Activity</div>'
    + '</div>'
    + '<div id="spTabContent" style="flex:1;overflow-y:auto;padding:18px">' + SlidePanel._renderBody(issue) + '</div>';
};

SlidePanel._showTab = async function(tabEl, tab, issueId) {
  document.querySelectorAll('.sp-tab').forEach(function(t){ t.classList.remove('active'); });
  tabEl.classList.add('active');
  var content = document.getElementById('spTabContent');
  if (!content) return;
  if (tab === 'overview') {
    var r = await App.callAsync('getIssueById', issueId);
    if (r && r.success) content.innerHTML = SlidePanel._renderBody(r.issue);
  } else if (tab === 'activity') {
    content.innerHTML = '<div style="padding:4px">Loading…</div>';
    var r2 = await App.callAsync('getActivityLog', issueId);
    var acts = (r2 && r2.success && r2.log) ? r2.log : [];
    content.innerHTML = App.renderActivityTimeline(acts);
  }
};

// Override SlidePanel._load to use tabbed body
SlidePanel._load = async function(issueId) {
  var body = document.getElementById('slidePanelBody');
  var idEl = document.getElementById('slidePanelId');
  var titleEl = document.getElementById('slidePanelTitle');
  if (!body) return;
  body.innerHTML = '<div class="slide-panel-loading"><div class="slide-panel-spinner"></div>Loading…</div>';
  body.style.padding = '0';
  body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
  body.style.display = 'flex';
  body.style.flexDirection = 'column';
  if (idEl) idEl.textContent = issueId;
  try {
    var r = await App.callAsync('getIssueById', issueId);
    if (!r || !r.success || !r.issue) {
      body.innerHTML = App.renderEmptyState('&#x26A0;','Issue not found','This issue may have been deleted.','','');
      return;
    }
    var issue = r.issue;
    if (idEl) idEl.textContent = issue.IssueID || issueId;
    if (titleEl) titleEl.textContent = issue.Title || 'Untitled';
    body.innerHTML = SlidePanel._renderBodyWithTabs(issue);
  } catch(e) {
    body.innerHTML = App.renderEmptyState('&#x26A0;','Error loading','Please try again.','','');
  }
};

// ─── INITIALISE ALL ENHANCEMENTS ─────────────────────────────────
(function initEnhancements() {
  var ready = function() {
    Keyboard.init();
    SavedViews.init();
    CompactMode.init();

    // FAB tooltip
    var fab = document.getElementById('quickCaptureFab');
    if (fab) fab.setAttribute('title', 'Create Ticket  [C]');

    // Slide panel overlay click to close
    var overlay = document.getElementById('slidePanelOverlay');
    if (overlay) overlay.addEventListener('click', function() { SlidePanel.close(); });

    // Keyboard overlay click-outside to close
    var kbdOverlay = document.getElementById('kbdOverlay');
    if (kbdOverlay) kbdOverlay.addEventListener('click', function(e) { if (e.target === kbdOverlay) Keyboard._closeKbdHelp(); });

    // Close notif panel on outside click
    document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
      var wrap = document.getElementById('notifWrap');
      if (wrap && !wrap.contains(e.target)) {
        var panel = document.getElementById('notifPanel');
        if (panel) panel.classList.remove('open');
      }
      // Close saved-views dropdowns
      document.querySelectorAll('.saved-views-dropdown.open').forEach(function(d) {
        var btn = d.previousElementSibling;
        if (btn && !btn.contains(e.target) && !d.contains(e.target)) {
          d.classList.remove('open');
          if (btn) btn.classList.remove('open');
        }
      });
    });

    // Patch Notif.toggle to use CSS class instead of inline display
    if (window.Notif && Notif.toggle) {
      Notif.toggle = function() {
        var panel = document.getElementById('notifPanel');
        if (panel) {
          panel.classList.toggle('open');
          Notif._render && Notif._render();
        }
      };
    }

    // ── Wave 2 inits ──
    ProgressBar.init();
    CmdPalette.init();
    ArrowNav.init();
    CardView.init();

    // Stats bar — load after App fully initialised
    setTimeout(function() { StatsBar.load(); }, 1200);

    // Patch App.updateIssueStatus to trigger confetti on Resolved
    if (App.updateIssueStatus) {
      var _origUpdateStatus = App.updateIssueStatus.bind(App);
      App.updateIssueStatus = async function(issueId, newStatus, comment) {
        var r = await _origUpdateStatus(issueId, newStatus, comment);
        if (newStatus === 'Resolved' || newStatus === 'Closed') App._celebrate();
        return r;
      };
    }

    // Extend Keyboard to handle Ctrl+P for command palette
    // (already handled in CmdPalette.init)

    // Topbar stats bar sidebar offset sync
    var sidebarEl = document.getElementById('sidebar');
    if (sidebarEl) {
      var _sbObserver = new MutationObserver(function() {
        var collapsed = sidebarEl.classList.contains('collapsed');
        var statsBar = document.getElementById('topbarStats');
        if (statsBar) statsBar.classList.toggle('sidebar-collapsed', collapsed);
      });
      _sbObserver.observe(sidebarEl, { attributes: true, attributeFilter: ['class'] });
    }

    // Inject preview buttons once list is ready
    setTimeout(function() { App._injectPreviewButtons(); }, 800);

    // Reload stats on navigate
    var _origNavFinal = App.navigate.bind(App);
    App._statsNavPatch = true; // guard against re-patching
  };

  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() { setTimeout(ready, 400); });
  } else {
    setTimeout(ready, 400);
  }
})();

// WAVE 3 FEATURES — New JavaScript Modules

// ── NOTIFICATION CENTER ───────────────────────────────────────────
const NotifCenter = {
  _items: [],
  _filter: 'all',

  open: function() {
    var drawer = document.getElementById('notifCenterDrawer');
    if (drawer) drawer.classList.add('open');
    this.load();
  },

  close: function() {
    var drawer = document.getElementById('notifCenterDrawer');
    if (drawer) drawer.classList.remove('open');
  },

  filter: function(type, btn) {
    this._filter = type;
    document.querySelectorAll('.notif-center-drawer .notif-tab').forEach(function(t) { t.classList.remove('active'); });
    if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
    this._render();
  },

  load: async function() {
    var list = document.getElementById('notifCenterList');
    if (!list) return;
    list.innerHTML = '<div class="notif-empty" style="color:var(--text-muted);">Loading...</div>';
    try {
      var r = await App.callAsync('getNotifications', {});
      if (r && r.success && r.notifications) {
        this._items = r.notifications;
      } else {
        this._items = this._localItems();
      }
    } catch(e) {
      this._items = this._localItems();
    }
    this._render();
    this._updateBell();
  },

  _localItems: function() {
    return JSON.parse(localStorage.getItem('tt_notifications') || '[]');
  },

  _saveLocal: function() {
    localStorage.setItem('tt_notifications', JSON.stringify(this._items.slice(0, 50)));
  },

  push: function(title, desc, type, issueId) {
    var item = {
      id: Date.now() + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2),
      title: title, desc: desc, type: type || 'info',
      issueId: issueId || '', time: new Date().toISOString(), read: false
    };
    this._items.unshift(item);
    this._saveLocal();
    this._render();
    this._updateBell();
    App.showToast('🔔 ' + title, 'info');
  },

  markAllRead: function() {
    this._items.forEach(function(n) { n.read = true; });
    this._saveLocal();
    this._render();
    this._updateBell();
  },

  markRead: function(id) {
    var item = this._items.find(function(n) { return n.id === id; });
    if (item) item.read = true;
    this._saveLocal();
    this._updateBell();
  },

  _updateBell: function() {
    var unread = this._items.filter(function(n) { return !n.read; }).length;
    var badge = document.getElementById('notifCount');
    if (badge) {
      badge.textContent = unread > 99 ? '99+' : unread;
      badge.style.display = unread > 0 ? 'flex' : 'none';
    }
  },

  _render: function() {
    var list = document.getElementById('notifCenterList');
    if (!list) return;
    var self = this;
    var items = this._items.filter(function(n) {
      if (self._filter === 'unread') return !n.read;
      if (self._filter === 'assigned') return n.type === 'assigned';
      if (self._filter === 'sla') return n.type === 'sla';
      if (self._filter === 'mention') return n.type === 'mention';
      return true;
    });
    if (items.length === 0) {
      list.innerHTML = '<div class="notif-empty">✓ All caught up!</div>';
      return;
    }
    var iconMap = { assigned: '👤', sla: '⏰', mention: '💬', resolved: '✅', info: '🔔', critical: '🚨' };
    var bgMap = { assigned: 'rgba(56,189,248,0.15)', sla: 'rgba(255,71,87,0.15)', mention: 'rgba(162,155,254,0.15)', resolved: 'rgba(46,213,115,0.15)', info: 'rgba(245,166,35,0.15)', critical: 'rgba(255,71,87,0.15)' };
    list.innerHTML = items.map(function(n) {
      return '<div class="notif-item' + (n.read ? '' : ' unread') + '" onclick="NotifCenter._click(\'' + n.id + '\',\'' + (n.issueId||'') + '\')">' +
        '<div class="notif-item-icon" style="background:' + (bgMap[n.type]||bgMap.info) + '">' + (iconMap[n.type]||'🔔') + '</div>' +
        '<div class="notif-item-body">' +
        '<div class="notif-item-title">' + App._esc(n.title) + '</div>' +
        '<div class="notif-item-desc">' + App._esc(n.desc||'') + '</div>' +
        '<div class="notif-item-time">' + App.relativeTime(n.time) + '</div>' +
        '</div></div>';
    }).join('');
  },

  _click: function(id, issueId) {
    this.markRead(id);
    this._render();
    if (issueId) {
      this.close();
      App.navigate('issue-detail', { id: issueId });
    }
  }
};

// Patch the notification bell to open NotifCenter drawer
(function patchNotifBell() {
  var bell = document.getElementById('notifBell') || document.querySelector('.notif-bell-btn');
  if (bell) {
    bell.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
      e.stopPropagation();
      NotifCenter.open();
    }, true);
  }
  setTimeout(function() { NotifCenter.load(); }, 2000);
})();


// ── ISSUE TAB BAR ─────────────────────────────────────────────────
const IssueTabBar = {
  _tabs: [], // [{id, title}]
  _active: null,

  init: function() {
    var bar = document.getElementById('issueTabBar');
    if (!bar) return;
    // Show bar only when there are tabs
    this._render();
  },

  open: function(issueId, title) {
    var exists = this._tabs.find(function(t) { return t.id === issueId; });
    if (!exists) {
      this._tabs.push({ id: issueId, title: title || issueId });
      if (this._tabs.length > 8) this._tabs.shift(); // max 8 tabs
    }
    this._active = issueId;
    this._render();
  },

  close: function(issueId, event) {
    if (event) event.stopPropagation();
    this._tabs = this._tabs.filter(function(t) { return t.id !== issueId; });
    if (this._active === issueId) {
      this._active = this._tabs.length > 0 ? this._tabs[this._tabs.length - 1].id : null;
      if (this._active) App.navigate('issue-detail', { id: this._active });
    }
    this._render();
  },

  _render: function() {
    var bar = document.getElementById('issueTabBar');
    if (!bar) return;
    var self = this;
    if (this._tabs.length === 0) { bar.style.display = 'none'; return; }
    bar.style.display = 'flex';
    bar.innerHTML = this._tabs.map(function(t) {
      var isActive = t.id === self._active;
      return '<div class="issue-tab' + (isActive ? ' active' : '') + '" onclick="IssueTabBar._activate(\'' + t.id + '\')">' +
        '<span class="issue-tab-id">' + App._esc(t.id) + '</span>' +
        '<span class="issue-tab-title">' + App._esc((t.title||'').slice(0,28)) + '</span>' +
        '<button class="issue-tab-close" onclick="IssueTabBar.close(\'' + t.id + '\',event)">×</button>' +
        '</div>';
    }).join('');
  },

  _activate: function(issueId) {
    this._active = issueId;
    this._render();
    App.navigate('issue-detail', { id: issueId });
  }
};


// ── QUICK FILTERS ROW ──────────────────────────────────────────────
const QuickFilters = {
  _active: null,
  _counts: {},

  init: function(counts) {
    this._counts = counts || {};
  },

  render: function(containerId) {
    var container = document.getElementById(containerId);
    if (!container) return;
    var self = this;
    var filters = [
      { key: 'my-issues',   label: 'My Issues',     icon: '👤' },
      { key: 'critical',    label: 'Critical',       icon: '🔴' },
      { key: 'sla-breach',  label: 'SLA Breach',     icon: '⏰' },
      { key: 'unassigned',  label: 'Unassigned',     icon: '⚡' },
      { key: 'open',        label: 'Open',           icon: '●' },
      { key: 'wip',         label: 'In Progress',    icon: '▶' },
    ];
    container.innerHTML = '<div class="quick-filters-row">' +
      filters.map(function(f) {
        var cnt = self._counts[f.key] || '';
        return '<button class="quick-filter-btn' + (self._active === f.key ? ' active' : '') + '" onclick="QuickFilters.apply(\'' + f.key + '\',this)">' +
          f.icon + ' ' + f.label +
          (cnt ? '<span class="qf-count">' + cnt + '</span>' : '') +
          '</button>';
      }).join('') +
      (self._active ? '<button class="quick-filter-btn" onclick="QuickFilters.clear()" style="margin-left:auto;">× Clear</button>' : '') +
      '</div>';
  },

  apply: function(key, btn) {
    if (this._active === key) { this.clear(); return; }
    this._active = key;
    document.querySelectorAll('.quick-filter-btn').forEach(function(b) { b.classList.remove('active'); });
    if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
    App._applyQuickFilter && App._applyQuickFilter(key);
  },

  clear: function() {
    this._active = null;
    App._clearQuickFilter && App._clearQuickFilter();
  }
};

// Patch App to support quick filters
App._applyQuickFilter = function(key) {
  var userEmail = App._currentUser && App._currentUser.email;
  var filters = {
    'my-issues': function(i) { return i.assignedTo === userEmail || i.raisedBy === userEmail; },
    'critical': function(i) { return i.priority === 'Critical'; },
    'sla-breach': function(i) { return i.slaBreached; },
    'unassigned': function(i) { return !i.assignedTo; },
    'open': function(i) { return i.status === 'Open'; },
    'wip': function(i) { return i.status === 'WIP'; }
  };
  var fn = filters[key];
  if (!fn) return;
  var rows = document.querySelectorAll('tbody tr[data-issue-id]');
  rows.forEach(function(r) {
    var id = r.getAttribute('data-issue-id');
    var issue = App._lastIssues && App._lastIssues.find(function(i) { return i.id === id; });
    if (issue) r.style.display = fn(issue) ? '' : 'none';
  });
};

App._clearQuickFilter = function() {
  var rows = document.querySelectorAll('tbody tr[data-issue-id]');
  rows.forEach(function(r) { r.style.display = ''; });
};


// ── BATCH OPERATIONS ──────────────────────────────────────────────
const BatchOps = {
  _selected: new Set(),
  _issues: [],

  init: function(issues) {
    this._issues = issues || [];
    this._selected.clear();
  },

  toggle: function(issueId, checkbox) {
    if (checkbox && checkbox.checked) {
      this._selected.add(issueId);
    } else {
      this._selected.delete(issueId);
    }
    this._updateToolbar();
  },

  selectAll: function(checkbox) {
    var rows = document.querySelectorAll('tbody tr[data-issue-id]');
    var self = this;
    rows.forEach(function(r) {
      var id = r.getAttribute('data-issue-id');
      var cb = r.querySelector('input[type="checkbox"]');
      if (checkbox.checked) {
        self._selected.add(id);
        if (cb) cb.checked = true;
      } else {
        self._selected.delete(id);
        if (cb) cb.checked = false;
      }
    });
    this._updateToolbar();
  },

  _updateToolbar: function() {
    var bar = document.querySelector('.batch-toolbar');
    if (!bar) return;
    var count = this._selected.size;
    bar.classList.toggle('visible', count > 0);
    var cntEl = bar.querySelector('.batch-count');
    if (cntEl) cntEl.textContent = count + ' selected';
  },

  cancel: function() {
    this._selected.clear();
    document.querySelectorAll('tbody input[type="checkbox"]').forEach(function(cb) { cb.checked = false; });
    var hdr = document.querySelector('thead input[type="checkbox"]');
    if (hdr) hdr.checked = false;
    this._updateToolbar();
  },

  assignTo: async function() {
    if (this._selected.size === 0) return;
    var devs = await App.callAsync('getDevelopers', {});
    if (!devs || !devs.developers) return;
    var opts = devs.developers.map(function(d) { return '<option value="' + d.email + '">' + d.name + '</option>'; }).join('');
    var html = '<div class="modal-overlay" onclick="if(event.target===this)this.remove()">' +
      '<div class="modal"><div class="modal-header"><span class="modal-title">Assign ' + this._selected.size + ' Issues</span>' +
      '<button class="modal-close" onclick="this.closest(\'.modal-overlay\').remove()">×</button></div>' +
      '<div class="modal-body"><div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Assign To</label>' +
      '<select id="batchAssignee" class="form-select"><option value="">— Select Developer —</option>' + opts + '</select></div>' +
      '<div style="text-align:right;margin-top:16px;">' +
      '<button class="btn-primary" onclick="BatchOps._doAssign()">Assign</button></div></div></div></div>';
    document.body.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', html);
  },

  _doAssign: async function() {
    var sel = document.getElementById('batchAssignee');
    if (!sel || !sel.value) return;
    var email = sel.value;
    var ids = Array.from(this._selected);
    sel.closest('.modal-overlay').remove();
    App.showToast('Assigning ' + ids.length + ' issues...', 'info');
    var r = await App.callAsync('batchUpdateIssues', ids, { assignedTo: email });
    if (r && r.success) {
      App.showToast('Assigned ' + ids.length + ' issues ✓', 'success');
      this.cancel();
      App.navigate(App._currentPage || 'issue-list');
    } else {
      App.showToast('Batch assign failed', 'error');
    }
  },

  changePriority: async function() {
    if (this._selected.size === 0) return;
    var priorities = ['Critical','High','Medium','Low'];
    var opts = priorities.map(function(p) { return '<option value="' + p + '">' + p + '</option>'; }).join('');
    var html = '<div class="modal-overlay" onclick="if(event.target===this)this.remove()">' +
      '<div class="modal"><div class="modal-header"><span class="modal-title">Change Priority for ' + this._selected.size + ' Issues</span>' +
      '<button class="modal-close" onclick="this.closest(\'.modal-overlay\').remove()">×</button></div>' +
      '<div class="modal-body"><div class="form-group"><label class="form-label">Priority</label>' +
      '<select id="batchPriority" class="form-select">' + opts + '</select></div>' +
      '<div style="text-align:right;margin-top:16px;">' +
      '<button class="btn-primary" onclick="BatchOps._doPriority()">Update</button></div></div></div></div>';
    document.body.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', html);
  },

  _doPriority: async function() {
    var sel = document.getElementById('batchPriority');
    if (!sel) return;
    var priority = sel.value;
    var ids = Array.from(this._selected);
    sel.closest('.modal-overlay').remove();
    var r = await App.callAsync('batchUpdateIssues', ids, { priority: priority });
    if (r && r.success) {
      App.showToast('Updated priority for ' + ids.length + ' issues ✓', 'success');
      this.cancel();
      App.navigate(App._currentPage || 'issue-list');
    } else {
      App.showToast('Batch priority update failed', 'error');
    }
  },

  close: async function() {
    if (this._selected.size === 0) return;
    if (!confirm('Close ' + this._selected.size + ' issues?')) return;
    var ids = Array.from(this._selected);
    var r = await App.callAsync('batchUpdateIssues', ids, { status: 'Closed' });
    if (r && r.success) {
      App.showToast('Closed ' + ids.length + ' issues ✓', 'success');
      this.cancel();
      App.navigate(App._currentPage || 'issue-list');
    } else {
      App.showToast('Batch close failed', 'error');
    }
  }
};


// ── ISSUE CLONING ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
App.cloneIssue = async function(issueId) {
  App.showToast('Cloning issue...', 'info');
  var r = await App.callAsync('cloneIssue', issueId);
  if (r && r.success) {
    App.showToast('Cloned as ' + r.newIssueId + ' ✓', 'success');
    NotifCenter.push('Issue Cloned', 'New issue ' + r.newIssueId + ' created from ' + issueId, 'info', r.newIssueId);
    App.navigate('issue-detail', { id: r.newIssueId });
  } else {
    App.showToast('Clone failed: ' + (r && r.error || 'unknown'), 'error');
  }
};


// ── MARK AS DUPLICATE ──────────────────────────────────────────────
App.markDuplicate = function(issueId) {
  var html = '<div class="modal-overlay" onclick="if(event.target===this)this.remove()">' +
    '<div class="modal"><div class="modal-header"><span class="modal-title">Mark as Duplicate</span>' +
    '<button class="modal-close" onclick="this.closest(\'.modal-overlay\').remove()">×</button></div>' +
    '<div class="modal-body"><div class="form-group">' +
    '<label class="form-label">Original Issue ID (e.g. TECH-001)</label>' +
    '<input id="dupOriginalId" class="form-input" placeholder="TECH-001" style="text-transform:uppercase">' +
    '</div><div style="text-align:right;margin-top:16px;">' +
    '<button class="btn-secondary" onclick="this.closest(\'.modal-overlay\').remove()" style="margin-right:8px;">Cancel</button>' +
    '<button class="btn-primary" onclick="App._confirmDuplicate(\'' + issueId + '\')">Mark Duplicate</button>' +
    '</div></div></div></div>';
  document.body.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', html);
};

App._confirmDuplicate = async function(issueId) {
  var originalId = (document.getElementById('dupOriginalId')?.value || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  if (!originalId) { App.showToast('Enter original issue ID', 'warning'); return; }
  var modal = document.querySelector('.modal-overlay');
  if (modal) modal.remove();
  var r = await App.callAsync('markAsDuplicate', issueId, originalId);
  if (r && r.success) {
    App.showToast(issueId + ' marked as duplicate of ' + originalId + ' ✓', 'success');
    App.navigate('issue-list');
  } else {
    App.showToast('Failed: ' + (r && r.error || 'unknown'), 'error');
  }
};


// ── COPY ISSUE LINK ────────────────────────────────────────────────
App.copyIssueLink = function(issueId, btn) {
  var link = window.location.href.split('?')[0] + '?issue=' + issueId;
  if (navigator.clipboard) {
    navigator.clipboard.writeText(link).then(function() {
      App.showToast('Link copied to clipboard ✓', 'success');
      if (btn) { btn.classList.add('copied'); setTimeout(function() { btn.classList.remove('copied'); }, 2000); }
    });
  } else {
    var ta = document.createElement('textarea');
    ta.value = link; document.body.appendChild(ta); ta.select(); document.execCommand('copy'); document.body.removeChild(ta);
    App.showToast('Link copied ✓', 'success');
  }
};


// ── WATCH / SUBSCRIBE ──────────────────────────────────────────────
App.watchIssue = async function(issueId, btn) {
  var isWatching = btn && btn.classList.contains('watching');
  if (isWatching) {
    var r = await App.callAsync('removeWatcher', issueId, App._currentUser && App._currentUser.email);
    if (r && r.success) {
      if (btn) { btn.classList.remove('watching'); btn.innerHTML = '🔔 Watch'; }
      App.showToast('Unwatched issue', 'info');
    }
  } else {
    var r2 = await App.callAsync('addWatcher', issueId, App._currentUser && App._currentUser.email);
    if (r2 && r2.success) {
      if (btn) { btn.classList.add('watching'); btn.innerHTML = '🔔 Watching'; }
      App.showToast('Watching issue — you\'ll be notified of updates', 'success');
    }
  }
};


// ── TIME TRACKER TIMER ─────────────────────────────────────────────
const Timer = {
  _issueId: null,
  _startTime: null,
  _interval: null,

  start: function(issueId, btn) {
    if (this._interval) { this.stop(btn); return; }
    this._issueId = issueId;
    this._startTime = Date.now();
    if (btn) { btn.classList.add('running'); btn.innerHTML = '⏹ Stop Timer'; }
    var self = this;
    this._interval = setInterval(function() {
      var elapsed = Math.floor((Date.now() - self._startTime) / 1000);
      var h = Math.floor(elapsed / 3600).toString().padStart(2,'0');
      var m = Math.floor((elapsed % 3600) / 60).toString().padStart(2,'0');
      var s = (elapsed % 60).toString().padStart(2,'0');
      var display = document.querySelector('.timer-display');
      if (display) display.textContent = h + ':' + m + ':' + s;
    }, 1000);
    App.showToast('Timer started ▶', 'info');
  },

  stop: async function(btn) {
    if (!this._interval || !this._issueId) return;
    clearInterval(this._interval);
    this._interval = null;
    var elapsed = (Date.now() - this._startTime) / 3600000; // hours
    var hours = Math.round(elapsed * 100) / 100;
    if (btn) { btn.classList.remove('running'); btn.innerHTML = '▶ Start Timer'; }
    var display = document.querySelector('.timer-display');
    if (display) display.textContent = '00:00:00';
    if (hours >= 0.01) {
      var note = 'Tracked via timer';
      var r = await App.callAsync('logTime', this._issueId, hours, note);
      if (r && r.success) {
        App.showToast('Logged ' + hours + 'h via timer ✓', 'success');
        App.loadTimeLogs && App.loadTimeLogs(this._issueId);
      }
    }
    this._issueId = null;
    this._startTime = null;
  }
};


// ── INLINE TABLE EDITING ───────────────────────────────────────────
App.enableInlineEdit = function(issueId, field, currentValue, cell) {
  var options = field === 'status'
    ? ['Open','Acknowledged','WIP','Testing','Resolved','Closed','Blocked']
    : ['Critical','High','Medium','Low'];
  var sel = document.createElement('select');
  sel.className = 'inline-select';
  options.forEach(function(o) {
    var opt = document.createElement('option');
    opt.value = o; opt.textContent = o;
    if (o === currentValue) opt.selected = true;
    sel.appendChild(opt);
  });
  var original = cell.innerHTML;
  cell.innerHTML = '';
  cell.appendChild(sel);
  sel.focus();
  sel.addEventListener('change', async function() {
    var newVal = sel.value;
    cell.innerHTML = original;
    var fn = field === 'status' ? 'updateIssueStatus' : 'updateIssuePriority';
    var r = await App.callAsync(fn, issueId, newVal, '');
    if (r && r.success) {
      App.showToast(field + ' updated to ' + newVal + ' ✓', 'success');
      App.navigate(App._currentPage || 'issue-list');
    } else {
      App.showToast('Update failed', 'error');
    }
  });
  sel.addEventListener('blur', function() {
    setTimeout(function() { if (cell.contains(sel)) cell.innerHTML = original; }, 200);
  });
  sel.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) { if (e.key === 'Escape') { cell.innerHTML = original; } });
};


// ── KANBAN ENHANCEMENTS ────────────────────────────────────────────
const KanbanEnhance = {
  _swimlane: null, // null = no swimlanes, 'priority' or 'assignee'
  _cardSize: 'normal', // 'compact', 'normal', 'expanded'
  _wipLimits: { 'Open': 20, 'Acknowledged': 15, 'WIP': 10, 'Testing': 8 },

  setSwimlane: function(type) {
    this._swimlane = type;
    App.navigate('kanban');
  },

  setCardSize: function(size, btn) {
    this._cardSize = size;
    var board = document.querySelector('.kanban-board');
    if (board) {
      board.classList.remove('compact', 'expanded');
      if (size !== 'normal') board.classList.add(size);
    }
    document.querySelectorAll('.kanban-size-btn').forEach(function(b) { b.classList.remove('active'); });
    if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
  },

  getWipIndicator: function(colName, count) {
    var limit = this._wipLimits[colName] || 999;
    var pct = count / limit;
    var cls = pct >= 1 ? 'over' : (pct >= 0.8 ? 'warn' : 'ok');
    return '<span class="wip-indicator ' + cls + '">' + count + '/' + limit + '</span>';
  },

  quickCreate: function(status) {
    // Pre-fill the create-issue form with the given status
    App.navigate('create-issue');
    setTimeout(function() {
      var statusEl = document.getElementById('issueStatus') || document.querySelector('[name="status"]');
      if (statusEl) statusEl.value = status;
    }, 300);
  }
};


// ── THEMES ENHANCEMENTS ────────────────────────────────────────────
// Extend the existing Themes object
if (window.Themes) {
  Themes.setCustomAccent = function(color) {
    document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--accent', color);
    document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--accent-dim', color + '26');
    document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--accent-glow', color + '66');
    document.documentElement.style.setProperty('--border-accent', color + '4d');
    localStorage.setItem('tt_custom_accent', color);
  };

  Themes.setFontSize = function(size, btn) {
    document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-font-size', size);
    localStorage.setItem('tt_font_size', size);
    document.querySelectorAll('.kanban-size-btn[id^="font"]').forEach(function(b) { b.classList.remove('active'); });
    if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
  };

  Themes.toggleContrast = function(btn) {
    var html = document.documentElement;
    var current = html.getAttribute('data-contrast');
    if (current === 'high') {
      html.removeAttribute('data-contrast');
      if (btn) btn.classList.remove('active');
      localStorage.removeItem('tt_contrast');
    } else {
      html.setAttribute('data-contrast', 'high');
      if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
      localStorage.setItem('tt_contrast', 'high');
    }
  };

  Themes.toggleMotion = function(btn) {
    var html = document.documentElement;
    var current = html.getAttribute('data-motion');
    if (current === 'reduced') {
      html.removeAttribute('data-motion');
      if (btn) btn.classList.remove('active');
      localStorage.removeItem('tt_motion');
    } else {
      html.setAttribute('data-motion', 'reduced');
      if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
      localStorage.setItem('tt_motion', 'reduced');
    }
  };

  // Load saved preferences
  (function loadThemePrefs() {
    var accent = localStorage.getItem('tt_custom_accent');
    if (accent) Themes.setCustomAccent(accent);
    var fontSize = localStorage.getItem('tt_font_size');
    if (fontSize) {
      document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-font-size', fontSize);
      var btn = document.getElementById('font' + fontSize.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + fontSize.slice(1,2));
      if (btn) { document.querySelectorAll('[id^="font"]').forEach(function(b){b.classList.remove('active');}); btn.classList.add('active'); }
    }
    var contrast = localStorage.getItem('tt_contrast');
    if (contrast) document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-contrast', contrast);
    var motion = localStorage.getItem('tt_motion');
    if (motion) document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-motion', motion);
  })();
}


// ── ROW HOVER PREVIEW ──────────────────────────────────────────────
const RowPreview = {
  _tip: null,
  _timeout: null,

  init: function() {
    this._tip = document.getElementById('rowPreviewTip');
    var self = this;
    document.addEventListener('mouseover', function(e) {
      var row = e.target.closest('tbody tr[data-issue-id]');
      if (!row) { self.hide(); return; }
      var id = row.getAttribute('data-issue-id');
      clearTimeout(self._timeout);
      self._timeout = setTimeout(function() { self.show(id, e); }, 400);
    });
    document.addEventListener('mouseout', function(e) {
      var row = e.target.closest('tbody tr[data-issue-id]');
      if (!row) return;
      clearTimeout(self._timeout);
      setTimeout(function() { self.hide(); }, 200);
    });
  },

  show: function(issueId, e) {
    if (!this._tip) return;
    var issue = App._lastIssues && App._lastIssues.find(function(i) { return i.id === issueId; });
    if (!issue) return;
    var pBadge = '<span class="badge-priority ' + (issue.priority||'').toLowerCase() + '">' + (issue.priority||'') + '</span>';
    var sBadge = '<span class="badge-status ' + (issue.status||'').toLowerCase().replace(' ','-') + '">' + (issue.status||'') + '</span>';
    this._tip.innerHTML =
      '<div class="row-preview-id">' + App._esc(issue.id) + '</div>' +
      '<div class="row-preview-title">' + App._esc(issue.title) + '</div>' +
      '<div class="row-preview-desc">' + App._esc((issue.description||'').slice(0,120)) + (issue.description && issue.description.length > 120 ? '...' : '') + '</div>' +
      '<div class="row-preview-meta">' + pBadge + sBadge + '</div>';
    var x = Math.min(e.clientX + 16, window.innerWidth - 360);
    var y = Math.min(e.clientY + 16, window.innerHeight - 200);
    this._tip.style.left = x + 'px';
    this._tip.style.top = y + 'px';
    this._tip.classList.add('visible');
  },

  hide: function() {
    if (this._tip) this._tip.classList.remove('visible');
  }
};


// ── TAKE THIS BUTTON (Assign to Me) ───────────────────────────────
App.takeThisIssue = async function(issueId) {
  var email = App._currentUser && App._currentUser.email;
  if (!email) { App.showToast('Could not detect your account', 'error'); return; }
  var r = await App.callAsync('assignIssue', issueId, email);
  if (r && r.success) {
    App.showToast('Issue assigned to you ✓', 'success');
    NotifCenter.push('Took Issue', issueId + ' assigned to you', 'assigned', issueId);
    App.renderIssueDetail(issueId);
  } else {
    App.showToast('Failed: ' + (r && r.error || 'unknown'), 'error');
  }
};


// ── DRAFT AUTO-SAVE ────────────────────────────────────────────────
const DraftSave = {
  _key: 'tt_issue_draft',
  _fields: ['issueTitle','issueDescription','issueModule','issuePriority','issueEnvironment','issueImpact'],

  save: function() {
    var draft = {};
    this._fields.forEach(function(id) {
      var el = document.getElementById(id);
      if (el) draft[id] = el.value;
    });
    localStorage.setItem(this._key, JSON.stringify(draft));
  },

  load: function() {
    var raw = localStorage.getItem(this._key);
    if (!raw) return false;
    try {
      var draft = JSON.parse(raw);
      var hasData = false;
      this._fields.forEach(function(id) {
        var el = document.getElementById(id);
        if (el && draft[id]) { el.value = draft[id]; hasData = true; }
      });
      if (hasData) App.showToast('Draft restored ✓', 'info');
      return hasData;
    } catch(e) { return false; }
  },

  clear: function() {
    localStorage.removeItem(this._key);
  },

  attach: function() {
    var self = this;
    this._fields.forEach(function(id) {
      var el = document.getElementById(id);
      if (el) el.addEventListener('input', function() { self.save(); });
    });
    this.load();
  }
};


// ── EXTENDED KEYBOARD SHORTCUTS ────────────────────────────────────
(function extendKeyboard() {
  document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
    if (e.target.tagName === 'INPUT' || e.target.tagName === 'TEXTAREA' || e.target.isContentEditable) return;
    if (e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey || e.altKey) return;
    switch(e.key) {
      case 'D':
      case 'd':
        if (!e.shiftKey) return;
        App.navigate('dashboard');
        break;
      case 'K':
      case 'k':
        if (!e.shiftKey) return;
        App.navigate('kanban');
        break;
      case 'L':
      case 'l':
        if (!e.shiftKey) return;
        App.navigate('issue-list');
        break;
      case 'N':
      case 'n':
        if (!e.shiftKey) return;
        NotifCenter.open();
        break;
    }
  });
})();


// ── ISSUE AGE BADGE ────────────────────────────────────────────────
App.ageBadgeV2 = function(createdDate) {
  if (!createdDate) return '';
  var hours = (Date.now() - new Date(createdDate)) / 3600000;
  var days = Math.floor(hours / 24);
  if (days < 1) return '<span class="age-dot fresh">< 1d</span>';
  if (days < 3) return '<span class="age-dot warning">' + days + 'd</span>';
  if (days < 7) return '<span class="age-dot stale">' + days + 'd</span>';
  return '<span class="age-dot critical">' + days + 'd</span>';
};


// ── SLA LIVE COUNTDOWN ─────────────────────────────────────────────
App.slaCountdown = function(issue) {
  if (!issue) return '';
  if (issue.slaBreached) return '<span class="sla-countdown breached">⚠ Breached</span>';
  var h = issue.slaHoursRemaining;
  if (h === undefined || h === null) return '';
  var cls = h < issue.slaHours * 0.2 ? 'risk' : 'safe';
  var label = h < 24 ? Math.round(h) + 'h' : Math.round(h/24) + 'd';
  return '<span class="sla-countdown ' + cls + '">⏱ ' + label + '</span>';
};


// ── ISSUE HEATMAP ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
App.renderIssueHeatmap = async function(containerId) {
  var container = document.getElementById(containerId);
  if (!container) return;
  container.innerHTML = '<p style="color:var(--text-muted);font-size:12px;">Loading heatmap...</p>';
  var r = await App.callAsync('getIssueHeatmap', {});
  if (!r || !r.success) { container.innerHTML = '<p style="color:var(--text-muted);">Could not load heatmap.</p>'; return; }
  var data = r.data || {}; // { 'YYYY-MM-DD': count }
  var now = new Date();
  var cells = [];
  for (var i = 364; i >= 0; i--) {
    var d = new Date(now - i * 86400000);
    var key = d.toISOString().slice(0,10);
    var cnt = data[key] || 0;
    var clamped = Math.min(cnt, 5);
    cells.push('<div class="heatmap-cell" data-count="' + clamped + '" title="' + key + ': ' + cnt + ' issues"></div>');
  }
  container.innerHTML = '<div style="margin-bottom:8px;"><span style="font-size:11px;color:var(--text-muted);">Issue creation activity — last 12 months</span>' +
    '<span style="float:right;font-size:10px;color:var(--text-dim);">Less ⬜ ⬜ ⬜ ⬜ ⬜ More</span></div>' +
    '<div class="heatmap-grid">' + cells.join('') + '</div>';
};


// ── NOTIFICATION SETTINGS PAGE ─────────────────────────────────────
App.renderNotifSettings = function() {
  App.setPage('Notification Rules', 'Admin / Notification Rules');
  var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
  var rules = [
    { key: 'on_assign', label: 'Issue Assigned to Me', sub: 'When you are assigned a new issue', email: true, inapp: true, slack: false },
    { key: 'on_mention', label: 'Mentioned in Comment', sub: 'When someone @mentions you', email: false, inapp: true, slack: false },

    { key: 'on_status', label: 'Status Change on My Issues', sub: 'When issues you raised change status', email: false, inapp: true, slack: false },
    { key: 'on_comment', label: 'New Comment on My Issues', sub: 'When someone comments on your issues', email: false, inapp: true, slack: false },
    { key: 'on_resolve', label: 'Issue Resolved', sub: 'When an issue you raised is resolved', email: true, inapp: true, slack: false },
    { key: 'on_critical', label: 'Critical Issue Created', sub: 'Any new critical priority issue', email: true, inapp: true, slack: true },

  ];
  var savedKey = 'tt_notif_rules';
  var saved = {};

    '<div class="card">' +
    '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;justify-content:space-between;margin-bottom:16px;">' +
    '<span class="card-title">🔔 Notification Rules</span>' +
    '<button class="btn-primary btn-sm" onclick="App._saveNotifRules()">Save Preferences</button></div>' +
    '<div style="display:flex;gap:8px;padding-bottom:10px;border-bottom:1px solid var(--border);margin-bottom:4px;">' +
    '<span style="flex:1;font-size:10px;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;letter-spacing:0.08em;color:var(--text-dim);">Event</span>' +
    '<span style="width:60px;text-align:center;font-size:10px;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;color:var(--text-dim);">Email</span>' +
    '<span style="width:60px;text-align:center;font-size:10px;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;color:var(--text-dim);">In-App</span>' +
    '<span style="width:60px;text-align:center;font-size:10px;font-weight:700;text-transform:uppercase;color:var(--text-dim);">Slack</span>' +
    '</div>';
  rules.forEach(function(r) {
    var s = saved[r.key] || { email: r.email, inapp: r.inapp, slack: r.slack };
    html += '<div class="notif-rule-row">' +
      '<div class="notif-rule-label">' + r.label + '<div class="notif-rule-sub">' + r.sub + '</div></div>' +
      '<div style="width:60px;text-align:center;"><button class="notif-channel-btn' + (s.email ? ' on' : '') + '" id="nr_' + r.key + '_email" onclick="App._toggleNotifBtn(this)">Email</button></div>' +
      '<div style="width:60px;text-align:center;"><button class="notif-channel-btn' + (s.inapp ? ' on' : '') + '" id="nr_' + r.key + '_inapp" onclick="App._toggleNotifBtn(this)">App</button></div>' +
      '<div style="width:60px;text-align:center;"><button class="notif-channel-btn' + (s.slack ? ' on' : '') + '" id="nr_' + r.key + '_slack" onclick="App._toggleNotifBtn(this)">Slack</button></div>' +
      '</div>';
  });
  html += '</div></div>';
  area.innerHTML = html;
};

App._toggleNotifBtn = function(btn) {
  btn.classList.toggle('on');
};

App._saveNotifRules = function() {
  var rules = {};
  document.querySelectorAll('.notif-rule-row').forEach(function(row) {
    var emailBtn = row.querySelector('[id$="_email"]');
    var inappBtn = row.querySelector('[id$="_inapp"]');
    var slackBtn = row.querySelector('[id$="_slack"]');
    if (emailBtn) {
      var key = emailBtn.id.replace('nr_','').replace('_email','');
      rules[key] = { email: emailBtn.classList.contains('on'), inapp: inappBtn && inappBtn.classList.contains('on'), slack: slackBtn && slackBtn.classList.contains('on') };
    }
  });
  localStorage.setItem('tt_notif_rules', JSON.stringify(rules));
  App.showToast('Notification preferences saved ✓', 'success');
};


// ── BREADCRUMB HELPER ──────────────────────────────────────────────
App.setBreadcrumb = function(crumbs) {
  var el = document.querySelector('.breadcrumb, .breadcrumb-trail');
  if (!el) return;
  el.innerHTML = crumbs.map(function(c, i) {
    if (i === crumbs.length - 1) return '<span class="bc-current">' + App._esc(c.label) + '</span>';
    return '<span class="bc-link" onclick="App.navigate(\'' + c.page + '\')">' + App._esc(c.label) + '</span><span class="bc-sep"> › </span>';
  }).join('');
};


// ── INIT ALL WAVE 3 FEATURES ───────────────────────────────────────
(function initWave3() {
  var ready = function() {
    IssueTabBar.init();
    RowPreview.init();

    // Patch App.navigate to track issue tabs
    var _origNavigate = App.navigate && App.navigate.bind(App);
    if (_origNavigate) {
      App.navigate = function(page, params) {
        App._currentPage = page;
        if (page === 'issue-detail' && params && params.id) {
          IssueTabBar.open(params.id, params.title || params.id);
        }
        return _origNavigate(page, params);
      };
    }

    // Load NotifCenter after delay
    setTimeout(function() { NotifCenter.load(); }, 3000);

    // Attach draft save to create-issue page
    var origRenderCreate = App.renderCreateIssue;
    if (origRenderCreate) {
      App.renderCreateIssue = function() {
        origRenderCreate.call(App);
        setTimeout(function() { DraftSave.attach(); }, 300);
      };
    }

    // Patch issue creation to clear draft on success
    var origCreateIssue = App.createIssue;
    if (origCreateIssue) {
      App.createIssue = async function() {
        var r = await origCreateIssue.call(App);
        if (r && r.success) DraftSave.clear();
        return r;
      };
    }

    // Add keyboard shortcuts info
    setTimeout(function() {
      var kbdBody = document.getElementById('kbdBody');
      if (kbdBody) {
        kbdBody.innerHTML += '<div class="kbd-row"><span class="kbd-keys"><kbd>Shift+D</kbd></span><span class="kbd-desc">Go to Dashboard</span></div>' +
          '<div class="kbd-row"><span class="kbd-keys"><kbd>Shift+K</kbd></span><span class="kbd-desc">Go to Kanban</span></div>' +
          '<div class="kbd-row"><span class="kbd-keys"><kbd>Shift+L</kbd></span><span class="kbd-desc">Go to Issue List</span></div>' +
          '<div class="kbd-row"><span class="kbd-keys"><kbd>Shift+N</kbd></span><span class="kbd-desc">Open Notifications</span></div>';
      }
    }, 1500);
  };

  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() { setTimeout(ready, 600); });
  } else {
    setTimeout(ready, 600);
  }
})();

// NOVA THEME — JavaScript System

// ── THEME ROLLBACK ────────────────────────────────────────────────
const ThemeRollback = {
  _SNAP_KEY: 'tt_theme_snapshot',
  _DISMISSED: false,

  snapshot: function(currentTheme) {
    if (currentTheme && currentTheme !== 'nova') {
      localStorage.setItem(this._SNAP_KEY, currentTheme);
    }
  },

  restore: function() {
    var prev = localStorage.getItem(this._SNAP_KEY) || 'midnight';
    var picker = document.querySelector('[data-theme-pick="' + prev + '"]');
    if (window.Themes) Themes.set(prev, picker);
    this._dismissPill();
    App.showToast('Restored to ' + prev + ' theme ✓', 'success');
  },

  dismiss: function() {
    this._dismissPill();
  },

  _dismissPill: function() {
    this._DISMISSED = true;
    var pill = document.getElementById('novaRollbackPill');
    if (pill) {
      pill.style.animation = 'none';
      pill.style.transition = 'opacity 0.3s, transform 0.3s';
      pill.style.opacity = '0';
      pill.style.transform = 'translateX(-50%) translateY(20px)';
      setTimeout(function() { pill.style.display = 'none'; }, 300);
    }
  }
};

// Intercept Themes.set to snapshot before switching to nova or clarity
(function patchThemesForRollback() {
  var _origSet = window.Themes && Themes.set;
  if (!_origSet) { setTimeout(patchThemesForRollback, 500); return; }
  Themes.set = function(name, el) {
    var currentTheme = document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme');
    if (name === 'nova') {
      ThemeRollback.snapshot(currentTheme);
      ThemeRollback._DISMISSED = false;
    }
    if (name === 'clarity') {
      ClaritySystem.snapshot(currentTheme);
      ClaritySystem._dismissed = false;
    }
    // Hide the other pill when switching away
    if (name !== 'nova') ThemeRollback._dismissPill && ThemeRollback._dismissPill();
    if (name !== 'clarity') ClaritySystem.dismissPill && ClaritySystem.dismissPill();
    _origSet.call(Themes, name, el);
    if (name === 'nova') {
      setTimeout(function() { NovaSystem.init(); }, 100);
    }
    if (name === 'clarity') {
      setTimeout(function() { ClaritySystem.init(); }, 100);
    }
  };
})();


// ── NOVA SYSTEM ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
const NovaSystem = {
  _criticalCount: 0,
  _initialized: false,

  init: function() {
    if (document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') !== 'nova') return;
    this._addRippleToButtons();
    this._startAmbientReactor();
    this._patchCounters();
    this._injectSkeletonHelper();
    if (!this._initialized) {
      this._initialized = true;
    }
  },

  // ── LIQUID RIPPLE EFFECT ON ALL BUTTONS ─────────────────────────
  _addRippleToButtons: function() {
    document.querySelectorAll('.btn-primary, .btn-secondary, .btn-danger').forEach(function(btn) {
      if (btn.dataset.novaRipple) return;
      btn.dataset.novaRipple = '1';
      btn.style.position = 'relative';
      btn.style.overflow = 'hidden';
      btn.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
        var rect = btn.getBoundingClientRect();
        var ripple = document.createElement('span');
        ripple.className = 'nova-ripple';
        var size = Math.max(rect.width, rect.height);
        ripple.style.width = ripple.style.height = size + 'px';
        ripple.style.left = (e.clientX - rect.left - size/2) + 'px';
        ripple.style.top  = (e.clientY - rect.top  - size/2) + 'px';
        btn.appendChild(ripple);
        ripple.addEventListener('animationend', function() { ripple.remove(); });
      });
    });
    // Re-observe for dynamically added buttons
    if (!this._rippleObserver) {
      var self = this;
      this._rippleObserver = new MutationObserver(function() {
        if (document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'nova') {
          self._addRippleToButtons();
        }
      });
      this._rippleObserver.observe(document.body, { childList: true, subtree: true });
    }
  },

  // ── AMBIENT BACKGROUND REACTOR ───────────────────────────────────
  _startAmbientReactor: function() {
    var self = this;
    var check = function() {
      if (document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') !== 'nova') return;
      var criticals = document.querySelectorAll('[data-priority="Critical"]').length
        + document.querySelectorAll('.badge-priority.critical').length;
      if (criticals !== self._criticalCount) {
        self._criticalCount = criticals;
        document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-nova-alert', criticals > 0 ? 'critical' : 'clear');
      }
      setTimeout(check, 5000);
    };
    setTimeout(check, 2000);
  },

  // ── COUNT-UP ANIMATION FOR KPI NUMBERS ───────────────────────────
  _patchCounters: function() {
    var self = this;
    var patchEl = function(el) {
      if (el.dataset.novaCounter) return;
      var raw = el.textContent.trim();
      var num = parseInt(raw.replace(/[^0-9]/g,''), 10);
      if (isNaN(num) || num < 2) return;
      el.dataset.novaCounter = '1';
      el.textContent = '0';
      el.classList.add('nova-counter');
      var start = performance.now();
      var duration = Math.min(800, num * 40);
      var raf = function(now) {
        var pct = Math.min(1, (now - start) / duration);
        var eased = 1 - Math.pow(1 - pct, 3);
        el.textContent = Math.round(num * eased);
        if (pct < 1) requestAnimationFrame(raf);
        else el.textContent = raw;
      };
      requestAnimationFrame(raf);
    };
    // Patch metric values on page load and navigation
    var observe = function() {
      if (document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') !== 'nova') return;
      document.querySelectorAll('.metric-value, .stat-value, .kpi-value, [class*="big-number"]').forEach(patchEl);
    };
    setTimeout(observe, 800);
    var navObs = new MutationObserver(function(muts) {
      if (document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') !== 'nova') return;
      muts.forEach(function(m) {
        m.addedNodes.forEach(function(n) {
          if (n.nodeType !== 1) return;
          n.querySelectorAll && n.querySelectorAll('.metric-value,.stat-value,.kpi-value').forEach(patchEl);
        });
      });
    });
    navObs.observe(document.body, { childList: true, subtree: true });
  },

  // ── SKELETON SCREEN HELPER ────────────────────────────────────────
  _injectSkeletonHelper: function() {
    App.novaSkeletonTable = function(rows, cols) {
      if (document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') !== 'nova') return null;
      var widths = ['40%','60%','20%','15%','25%','30%'];
      var html = '<div style="padding:8px 0;">';
      for (var r = 0; r < (rows||6); r++) {
        html += '<div class="nova-skeleton-row">';
        for (var c = 0; c < (cols||5); c++) {
          html += '<div class="nova-skeleton nova-skeleton-text" style="width:' + widths[c % widths.length] + ';flex-shrink:0;"></div>';
        }
        html += '</div>';
      }
      html += '</div>';
      return html;
    };

    // Patch App's loading states to use skeleton when Nova is active
    var origLoad = App._showLoading;
    App._showLoading = function(area, label) {
      if (document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'nova' && area) {
        var skel = App.novaSkeletonTable(7, 5);
        if (skel) { area.innerHTML = '<div class="card" style="padding:16px;">' + skel + '</div>'; return; }
      }
      if (origLoad) origLoad.call(App, area, label);
    };
  }
};


// ── AUTO-INIT NOVA IF ALREADY SET ─────────────────────────────────
(function() {
  var ready = function() {
    if (document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'nova') {
      NovaSystem.init();
    }
  };
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() { setTimeout(ready, 400); });
  } else {
    setTimeout(ready, 400);
  }
})();

// WAVE 4 — Cross-Theme + Nova Extended JS
