// ── TOAST QUEUE v2 ────────────────────────────────────────────────
const ToastQueue = {
  _queue: [],
  _max: 4,
  _icons: { success:'✅', error:'❌', warning:'⚠️', info:'ℹ️' },
  _durations: { success:3500, error:6000, warning:4500, info:3000 },

  show: function(message, type, title) {
    type = type || 'info';
    var duration = this._durations[type] || 3500;
    var id = 'toast_' + Date.now() + '_' + Math.random().toString(36).slice(2,6);
    var container = document.getElementById('toastContainer');
    if (!container) return;

    // Remove oldest if over max
    var existing = container.querySelectorAll('.toast-v2');
    if (existing.length >= this._max) {
      this._remove(existing[0]);
    }

    var el = document.createElement('div');
    el.className = 'toast-v2 ' + type;
    el.id = id;
    el.innerHTML =
      '<span class="toast-v2-icon">' + (this._icons[type]||'🔔') + '</span>' +
      '<div class="toast-v2-body">' +
        (title ? '<div class="toast-v2-title">' + title + '</div>' : '') +
        '<div class="toast-v2-msg">' + message + '</div>' +
      '</div>' +
      '<button class="toast-v2-close" onclick="ToastQueue._remove(this.closest(\'.toast-v2\'))">×</button>' +
      '<div class="toast-v2-progress" style="animation-duration:' + duration + 'ms"></div>';
    container.appendChild(el);

    var self = this;
    setTimeout(function() { self._remove(el); }, duration);
  },

  _remove: function(el) {
    if (!el || el.classList.contains('removing')) return;
    el.classList.add('removing');
    setTimeout(function() { el && el.remove(); }, 220);
  }
};

// Patch App.showToast to use ToastQueue
(function patchShowToast() {
  var patch = function() {
    if (!window.App || !App.showToast) { setTimeout(patch, 300); return; }
    App.showToast = function(message, type, title) {
      ToastQueue.show(message, type, title);
    };
  };
  patch();
})();


// ── BUTTON LOADING STATES ─────────────────────────────────────────
App.btnLoading = function(btn, loading) {
  if (!btn) return;
  if (loading) {
    btn._origText = btn.innerHTML;
    btn.classList.add('btn-loading');
    btn.disabled = true;
  } else {
    btn.classList.remove('btn-loading');
    btn.disabled = false;
    if (btn._origText) btn.innerHTML = btn._origText;
  }
};

// Auto-apply loading to all form submit buttons
(function autoButtonLoading() {
  document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    var btn = e.target.closest('.btn-primary[type="submit"], .btn-primary[data-loading]');
    if (!btn) return;
    App.btnLoading(btn, true);
    setTimeout(function() { App.btnLoading(btn, false); }, 4000); // safety reset
  });
})();


// ── DENSITY TOGGLE ────────────────────────────────────────────────
const DensityToggle = {
  _current: 'default',

  set: function(density, btn) {
    this._current = density;
    var html = document.documentElement;
    html.removeAttribute('data-density');
    if (density !== 'default') html.setAttribute('data-density', density);
    document.querySelectorAll('.density-btn').forEach(function(b) { b.classList.remove('active'); });
    if (btn) btn.classList.add('active');
    localStorage.setItem('tt_density', density);
  },

  init: function() {
    var saved = localStorage.getItem('tt_density');
    if (saved && saved !== 'default') {
      document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-density', saved);
      this._current = saved;
    }
  },

  render: function(container) {
    if (!container) return;
    var self = this;
    container.innerHTML =
      '<div class="density-bar">' +
      ['compact','default','comfortable'].map(function(d) {
        var labels = { compact:'Compact', 'default':'Default', comfortable:'Cozy' };
        return '<button class="density-btn' + (self._current === d ? ' active' : '') + '" onclick="DensityToggle.set(\'' + d + '\',this)">' + labels[d] + '</button>';
      }).join('') +
      '</div>';
  }
};

DensityToggle.init();


// ── GOOD MORNING HEADER ───────────────────────────────────────────
App.renderGoodMorning = async function(containerId) {
  var container = document.getElementById(containerId);
  if (!container) return;

  var name = (App._currentUser && App._currentUser.name) || 'there';
  var firstName = name.split(' ')[0];
  var h = new Date().getHours();
  var greet = h < 12 ? 'Good morning' : h < 17 ? 'Good afternoon' : 'Good evening';
  var emoji = h < 12 ? '☀️' : h < 17 ? '🌤' : '🌙';

  // Build quick stats
  var stats = [];
  try {
    var r = await App.callAsync('getSummaryStats', {});
    if (r && r.success && r.stats) {
      var s = r.stats;
      stats = [
        { value: s.totalOpen || 0,       label: 'Open',       cls: '' },
        { value: s.byPriority.Critical||0,label: 'Critical',  cls: 'critical' },
        { value: s.slaBreached || 0,      label: 'SLA Risk',  cls: 'breach' },
        { value: s.resolvedThisWeek || 0, label: 'Resolved ↗',cls: 'resolved' }
      ];
    }
  } catch(e) {}

  var statsHtml = stats.map(function(s) {
    return '<div class="gm-stat ' + s.cls + '"><div class="gm-stat-value nova-counter">' + s.value + '</div><div class="gm-stat-label">' + s.label + '</div></div>';
  }).join('');

  // Build assigned/unread sub-line
  var sub = '';
  if (App._currentUser) {
    var assigned = stats[0] ? stats[0].value : '...';
    sub = 'You have <strong>' + (App._currentUser.assignedCount || '–') + '</strong> assigned issues';
    if (stats[1] && stats[1].value > 0) sub += ' · <strong style="color:var(--critical)">' + stats[1].value + ' critical</strong> need attention';
  }

  container.innerHTML =
    '<div class="gm-header">' +
      '<div>' +
        '<div class="gm-greeting">' + greet + ', <em>' + App._esc(firstName) + '</em> ' + emoji + '</div>' +
        (sub ? '<div class="gm-sub">' + sub + '</div>' : '') +
      '</div>' +
      (statsHtml ? '<div class="gm-stats">' + statsHtml + '</div>' : '') +
    '</div>';

  // Trigger count-up for Nova
  if (document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'nova') {
    setTimeout(function() { NovaSystem._patchCounters && NovaSystem._patchCounters(); }, 100);
  }
};


// ── KPI SPARKLINES ────────────────────────────────────────────────
App.renderSparkline = function(containerId, values, label) {
  var container = document.getElementById(containerId);
  if (!container || !values || !values.length) return;
  var max = Math.max.apply(null, values) || 1;
  var today = values[values.length - 1];
  var yesterday = values[values.length - 2] || 0;
  var trend = today > yesterday ? 'up' : today < yesterday ? 'down' : 'flat';
  var trendIcon = { up:'↑', down:'↓', flat:'→' }[trend];
  var pct = Math.round(Math.abs(today - yesterday) / (yesterday||1) * 100);

  var bars = values.slice(-14).map(function(v, i, arr) {
    var h = Math.round((v / max) * 100);
    var isToday = i === arr.length - 1;
    return '<div class="spark-bar' + (isToday ? ' today' : '') + '" style="height:' + Math.max(h, 8) + '%" title="' + v + '"></div>';
  }).join('');

  container.innerHTML =
    '<div class="sparkline-wrap">' + bars + '</div>' +
    '<div class="spark-trend ' + trend + '">' + trendIcon + ' ' + pct + '% vs yesterday</div>';
};

App.loadSparklines = async function() {
  try {
    var r = await App.callAsync('getIssueHeatmap', {});
    if (!r || !r.success || !r.data) return;
    var data = r.data;
    var vals = [];
    for (var i = 13; i >= 0; i--) {
      var d = new Date(Date.now() - i * 86400000);
      vals.push(data[d.toISOString().slice(0,10)] || 0);
    }
    App.renderSparkline('kpiSparklineNew', vals, 'New Issues');
    App.renderSparkline('kpiSparklineNew2', vals.map(function(v) { return Math.floor(v * 0.6); }), 'Resolved');
  } catch(e) {}
};


// ── PRIORITY VISUAL CARD SELECTOR ─────────────────────────────────
App.renderPriorityCards = function(containerId, inputId, defaultPriority) {
  var container = document.getElementById(containerId);
  if (!container) return;

  var priorities = [
    { key:'Critical', icon:'🔴', desc:'System down · customer impact' },
    { key:'High',     icon:'🟠', desc:'Major feature broken' },
    { key:'Medium',   icon:'🟡', desc:'Feature degraded, workaround exists' },
    { key:'Low',      icon:'🟢', desc:'Minor issue, no urgency' }
  ];

  var html = '<div class="priority-cards">';
  priorities.forEach(function(p) {
    var sel = (defaultPriority === p.key) ? ' selected' : '';
    html +=
      '<div class="priority-card ' + p.key.toLowerCase() + sel + '" onclick="App._selectPriorityCard(this,\'' + p.key + '\',\'' + (inputId||'issuePriority') + '\')">' +
      '<span class="pc-icon">' + p.icon + '</span>' +
      '<span class="pc-label">' + p.key + '</span>' +
      '<span class="pc-desc">' + p.desc + '</span>' +
      '</div>';
  });
  html += '</div>';
  container.innerHTML = html;
};

App._selectPriorityCard = function(card, priority, inputId) {
  var container = card.closest('.priority-cards');
  if (container) container.querySelectorAll('.priority-card').forEach(function(c) { c.classList.remove('selected'); });
  card.classList.add('selected');
  var inp = document.getElementById(inputId);
  if (inp) inp.value = priority;
  // Ripple effect
  if (document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'nova') {
    var ripple = document.createElement('div');
    ripple.className = 'nova-ripple';
    ripple.style.cssText = 'width:200px;height:200px;left:-60px;top:-60px;';
    card.appendChild(ripple);
    ripple.addEventListener('animationend', function() { ripple.remove(); });
  }
};

// Patch create-issue render to inject priority cards
(function patchCreateIssue() {
  var patch = function() {
    if (!window.App || !App.renderCreateIssue) { setTimeout(patch, 400); return; }
    var _orig = App.renderCreateIssue.bind(App);
    App.renderCreateIssue = function() {
      _orig();
      setTimeout(function() {
        var priorityGroup = document.querySelector('#issuePriority')?.closest('.form-group');
        if (!priorityGroup || document.getElementById('priorityCardsWrap')) return;
        var wrap = document.createElement('div');
        wrap.id = 'priorityCardsWrap';
        priorityGroup.appendChild(wrap);
        App.renderPriorityCards('priorityCardsWrap', 'issuePriority', 'Medium');
      }, 200);
    };
  };
  patch();
})();


// ── NOVA COMMAND CENTER ───────────────────────────────────────────
const CmdCenter = {
  open: async function() {
    var el = document.getElementById('novaCmdCenter');
    if (!el) return;
    el.classList.add('open');
    document.body.style.overflow = 'hidden';
    await this.load();
  },

  close: function() {
    var el = document.getElementById('novaCmdCenter');
    if (el) el.classList.remove('open');
    document.body.style.overflow = '';
  },

  load: async function() {
    var body = document.getElementById('cmdCenterBody');
    var meta = document.getElementById('cmdCenterMeta');
    if (!body) return;

    body.innerHTML = '<div class="nova-cmd-empty" style="grid-column:1/-1;">⚡ Loading critical issues...</div>';

    try {
      var r = await App.callAsync('getIssues', { priority: 'Critical' });
      var issues = (r && r.success && r.issues) ? r.issues.filter(function(i) {
        return !['Resolved','Closed'].includes(i.status);
      }) : [];

      if (meta) meta.textContent = issues.length + ' open critical issue' + (issues.length !== 1 ? 's' : '') + ' · ' + new Date().toLocaleTimeString();

      if (issues.length === 0) {
        body.innerHTML = '<div class="nova-cmd-empty" style="grid-column:1/-1;">✅ No open critical issues right now — great work!</div>';
        return;
      }

      body.innerHTML = issues.map(function(i, idx) {
        var slaLabel = i.slaBreached ? 'Breached' : (i.slaRisk ? 'At Risk ' + i.slaHoursRemaining + 'h' : i.slaHoursRemaining + 'h left');
        var slaCls   = i.slaBreached ? 'breached' : (i.slaRisk ? 'risk' : 'safe');
        var since    = i.createdDate ? App.relativeTime(i.createdDate) : '';
        return '<div class="nova-cmd-card" style="animation-delay:' + (idx * 0.05) + 's" onclick="CmdCenter.close();App.navigate(\'issue-detail\',{id:\'' + i.id + '\'})">' +
          '<div class="nova-cmd-card-id">' + App._esc(i.id) + '</div>' +
          '<div class="nova-cmd-card-title">' + App._esc(i.title) + '</div>' +
          '<div class="nova-cmd-card-meta">' +
          '<span class="nova-cmd-sla ' + slaCls + '">⏱ ' + App._esc(slaLabel) + '</span>' +
          (i.assignedTo ? '<span class="nova-cmd-card-assignee">→ ' + App._esc(i.assignedTo.split('@')[0]) + '</span>' : '<span class="nova-cmd-card-assignee" style="color:#ff4d6d;">⚡ Unassigned</span>') +
          '<span style="font-size:10px;color:rgba(164,159,200,0.4);font-family:var(--font-mono);">' + App._esc(since) + '</span>' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div style="margin-top:12px;display:flex;gap:8px;">' +
          '<button class="nova-cmd-open-btn" onclick="event.stopPropagation();App.takeThisIssue(\'' + i.id + '\')">⚡ Take This</button>' +
          '<button class="nova-cmd-open-btn" onclick="event.stopPropagation();CmdCenter.close();App.navigate(\'issue-detail\',{id:\'' + i.id + '\'})">→ Open</button>' +
          '</div>' +
          '</div>';
      }).join('');

    } catch(e) {
      body.innerHTML = '<div class="nova-cmd-empty" style="grid-column:1/-1;">Failed to load issues.</div>';
    }
  },

  updateTopbarBtn: function() {
    var btn = document.getElementById('cmdCenterBtn');
    if (!btn) return;
    var criticals = document.querySelectorAll('[data-priority="Critical"]').length;
    btn.classList.toggle('hidden', criticals === 0);
    if (criticals > 0) btn.innerHTML = '⚡ ' + criticals + ' Critical';
  }
};

// Keyboard shortcut: Ctrl+Shift+C = Command Center
document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
  if ((e.ctrlKey || e.metaKey) && e.shiftKey && e.key === 'C') {
    if (document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'nova') {
      e.preventDefault();
      CmdCenter.open();
    }
  }
  if (e.key === 'Escape') {
    var cc = document.getElementById('novaCmdCenter');
    if (cc && cc.classList.contains('open')) { CmdCenter.close(); }
  }
});


// ── NOVA BENTO DASHBOARD ──────────────────────────────────────────
App.renderNovaBentoDashboard = async function() {
  if (document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') !== 'nova') return false;

  var area = document.getElementById('contentArea');
  if (!area) return false;

  App.setPage && App.setPage('Dashboard', 'Overview');

  // Show skeleton while loading
  area.innerHTML =
    '<div class="nova-bento-grid" id="bentoDashboard">' +
      '<div class="nova-bento-cell bento-12x1"><div class="nova-skeleton" style="height:24px;width:40%;margin-bottom:8px;"></div><div class="nova-skeleton" style="height:12px;width:25%;"></div></div>' +
      '<div class="nova-bento-cell bento-3x1"><div class="nova-skeleton" style="height:40px;width:60%;margin-bottom:8px;"></div><div class="nova-skeleton" style="height:12px;width:40%;"></div></div>'.repeat(4) +
    '</div>';

  var r = await App.callAsync('getSummaryStats', {});
  var s = (r && r.success && r.stats) ? r.stats : {};
  var h = (r && r.success && r.heatmapVals) ? r.heatmapVals : [];

  var assignedIssues = [];
  try {
    var ai = await App.callAsync('getIssues', { assignedTo: App._currentUser && App._currentUser.email });
    if (ai && ai.success) assignedIssues = ai.issues.filter(function(i) { return !['Resolved','Closed'].includes(i.status); }).slice(0,4);
  } catch(e) {}

  area.innerHTML =
    '<div class="nova-bento-grid">' +

    // Row 1 — good morning full width
    '<div class="nova-bento-cell bento-12x1" style="padding:0;overflow:hidden;" id="bentogm"></div>' +

    // Row 2 — 4 KPI stats
    '<div class="nova-bento-cell bento-3x1">' +
      '<div class="bento-stat-label">Total Open</div>' +
      '<div class="bento-stat-num nova-counter">' + (s.totalOpen||0) + '</div>' +
      '<div class="bento-stat-trend flat">→ Active issues</div>' +
      '<div id="kpiSparklineNew" style="margin-top:6px;"></div>' +
    '</div>' +

    '<div class="nova-bento-cell bento-3x1 accent-red">' +
      '<div class="bento-stat-label">Critical</div>' +
      '<div class="bento-stat-num critical-color nova-counter">' + ((s.byPriority && s.byPriority.Critical)||0) + '</div>' +
      '<div class="bento-stat-trend up">↑ Need immediate attention</div>' +
    '</div>' +

    '<div class="nova-bento-cell bento-3x1 accent-pink">' +
      '<div class="bento-stat-label">SLA Breached</div>' +
      '<div class="bento-stat-num critical-color nova-counter">' + (s.slaBreached||0) + '</div>' +
      '<div class="bento-stat-trend ' + ((s.slaBreached||0) > 0 ? 'up' : 'down') + '">' + ((s.slaBreached||0) > 0 ? '↑ Needs action' : '↓ All on track') + '</div>' +
    '</div>' +

    '<div class="nova-bento-cell bento-3x1 accent-green">' +
      '<div class="bento-stat-label">Resolved This Week</div>' +
      '<div class="bento-stat-num resolved-color nova-counter">' + (s.resolvedThisWeek||0) + '</div>' +
      '<div class="bento-stat-trend down">↓ Great velocity</div>' +
    '</div>' +

    // Row 3 — My issues (8 wide) + Status breakdown (4 wide)
    '<div class="nova-bento-cell bento-8x2">' +
      '<div class="bento-stat-label" style="margin-bottom:12px;">My Assigned Issues</div>' +
      (assignedIssues.length === 0 ?
        '<div class="empty-state-v3" style="padding:20px;"><div class="es-icon">✅</div><div class="es-title" style="font-size:14px;">All clear!</div><div class="es-sub" style="font-size:12px;">No issues assigned to you.</div></div>' :
        assignedIssues.map(function(i) {
          var pCls = (i.priority||'').toLowerCase();
          return '<div style="display:flex;align-items:center;gap:10px;padding:8px 0;border-bottom:1px solid rgba(255,255,255,0.04);cursor:pointer;" onclick="App.navigate(\'issue-detail\',{id:\'' + i.id + '\'})">' +
            '<span class="issue-id" style="font-size:11px;flex-shrink:0;">' + App._esc(i.id) + '</span>' +
            '<span style="flex:1;font-size:13px;color:var(--text-primary);font-weight:500;white-space:nowrap;overflow:hidden;text-overflow:ellipsis;">' + App._esc(i.title) + '</span>' +
            '<span class="badge-priority ' + pCls + '">' + App._esc(i.priority) + '</span>' +
            App.slaCountdown(i) +
            '</div>';
        }).join('')) +
    '</div>' +

    '<div class="nova-bento-cell bento-4x2">' +
      '<div class="bento-stat-label" style="margin-bottom:12px;">Status Breakdown</div>' +
      (function() {
        var statuses = ['Open','WIP','Testing','Blocked'];
        var byStatus = s.byStatus || {};
        return statuses.map(function(st) {
          var cnt = byStatus[st] || 0;
          var total = s.totalOpen || 1;
          var pct = Math.round(cnt / total * 100);
          var colors = { Open:'var(--status-open)', WIP:'var(--accent)', Testing:'var(--status-testing)', Blocked:'var(--critical)' };
          return '<div style="margin-bottom:10px;">' +
            '<div style="display:flex;justify-content:space-between;font-size:11px;margin-bottom:4px;">' +
            '<span style="color:var(--text-secondary);">' + st + '</span>' +
            '<span style="color:var(--text-muted);font-family:var(--font-mono);">' + cnt + '</span>' +
            '</div>' +
            '<div style="height:4px;background:rgba(255,255,255,0.06);border-radius:999px;overflow:hidden;">' +
            '<div style="height:100%;width:' + pct + '%;background:' + colors[st] + ';border-radius:999px;box-shadow:0 0 6px ' + colors[st] + ';transition:width 0.6s ease;"></div>' +
            '</div></div>';
        }).join('');
      })() +
    '</div>' +

    '</div>'; // end bento grid

  // Load Good Morning header
  setTimeout(function() {
    App.renderGoodMorning('bentogm');
    App.loadSparklines();
    if (window.NovaSystem) NovaSystem._patchCounters();
    CmdCenter.updateTopbarBtn();
  }, 100);

  return true;
};

// Patch App.navigate to use bento dashboard when Nova is active
(function patchDashboardForNova() {
  var patch = function() {
    if (!window.App || !App.renderDashboard) { setTimeout(patch, 500); return; }
    var _orig = App.renderDashboard.bind(App);
    App.renderDashboard = async function() {
      var used = await App.renderNovaBentoDashboard();
      if (!used) _orig();
    };
  };
  patch();
})();


// ── ROW SELECTION HIGHLIGHT ───────────────────────────────────────
(function initRowSelection() {
  document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
    var row = e.target.closest('tbody tr[data-issue-id]');
    if (!row) return;
    var isCheckbox = e.target.type === 'checkbox';
    if (!isCheckbox) {
      var table = row.closest('table');
      if (table) table.querySelectorAll('tr.row-selected').forEach(function(r) { r.classList.remove('row-selected'); });
      row.classList.add('row-selected');
    }
  });
})();


// ── DENSITY TOGGLE IN TOOLBAR ─────────────────────────────────────
App._injectDensityToggle = function() {
  var toolbars = document.querySelectorAll('.table-toolbar');
  toolbars.forEach(function(tb) {
    if (tb.querySelector('.density-bar')) return;
    var wrap = document.createElement('div');
    wrap.style.cssText = 'margin-left:auto;';
    DensityToggle.render(wrap);
    tb.appendChild(wrap);
  });
};

// Patch navigate to inject density toggle after page render
(function patchNavigateDensity() {
  var patch = function() {
    if (!window.App || !App.navigate) { setTimeout(patch, 400); return; }
    var _orig = App.navigate.bind(App);
    App.navigate = function(page, params) {
      var r = _orig(page, params);
      setTimeout(function() { App._injectDensityToggle(); }, 600);
      return r;
    };
  };
  patch();
})();


// ── INIT WAVE 4 ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
(function initWave4() {
  var ready = function() {
    ToastQueue;  // init
    DensityToggle.init();

    // If nova is active, render bento dashboard
    if (document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'nova') {
      setTimeout(function() {
        CmdCenter.updateTopbarBtn();
        App.loadSparklines && App.loadSparklines();
      }, 2500);
    }

    // Add Command Center button to topbar
    var topbarActions = document.querySelector('.topbar-actions, .topbar-right');
    if (topbarActions && !document.getElementById('cmdCenterBtn')) {
      var btn = document.createElement('button');
      btn.id = 'cmdCenterBtn';
      btn.className = 'cmd-center-topbar-btn hidden';
      btn.onclick = function() { CmdCenter.open(); };
      btn.innerHTML = '⚡ Critical';
      btn.title = 'Nova Command Center  [Ctrl+Shift+C]';
      topbarActions.insertBefore(btn, topbarActions.firstChild);
    }

    // Update command center button count periodically
    setInterval(function() {
      if (document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') === 'nova') CmdCenter.updateTopbarBtn();
    }, 30000);
  };

  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() { setTimeout(ready, 700); });
  } else {
    setTimeout(ready, 700);
  }
})();

// ================================================================
// CLARITY THEME — JavaScript System
// ================================================================
const ClaritySystem = {
  _SNAP_KEY: 'tt_clarity_snapshot',
  _dismissed: false,

  snapshot: function(currentTheme) {
    if (currentTheme && currentTheme !== 'clarity') {
      localStorage.setItem(this._SNAP_KEY, currentTheme);
    }
  },

  restore: function() {
    var prev = localStorage.getItem(this._SNAP_KEY) || 'midnight';
    var picker = document.querySelector('[data-theme-pick="' + prev + '"]');
    if (window.Themes) Themes.set(prev, picker);
    this.dismissPill();
    if (window.App && App.showToast) App.showToast('Restored to ' + prev + ' theme ✓', 'success');
  },

  dismissPill: function() {
    this._dismissed = true;
    var pill = document.getElementById('clarityRollbackPill');
    if (pill) {
      pill.style.transition = 'opacity 0.3s, transform 0.3s';
      pill.style.opacity = '0';
      pill.style.transform = 'translateY(16px)';
      setTimeout(function() { if (pill) pill.style.display = 'none'; }, 300);
    }
  },

  init: function() {
    if (document.documentElement.getAttribute('data-theme') !== 'clarity') return;
    // Show the rollback pill if not dismissed
    if (!this._dismissed) {
      var pill = document.getElementById('clarityRollbackPill');
      if (pill) {
        pill.style.display = 'flex';
        pill.style.opacity = '1';
        pill.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
      }
    }
    // Ensure sidebar starts collapsed (icon-rail mode)
    var sidebar = document.querySelector('.sidebar');
    if (sidebar) {
      sidebar.classList.remove('expanded');
    }
    // Restore saved theme on load if clarity was active
    var savedTheme = localStorage.getItem('tt_theme');
    if (savedTheme === 'clarity') {
      var snapExists = localStorage.getItem(this._SNAP_KEY);
      if (!snapExists) {
        localStorage.setItem(this._SNAP_KEY, 'midnight');
      }
    }
  }
};

// Auto-init Clarity on page load if it was the last saved theme
(function initClarityOnLoad() {
  function check() {
    var saved = localStorage.getItem('tt_theme');
    if (saved === 'clarity') {
      ClaritySystem._dismissed = false;
      setTimeout(function() { ClaritySystem.init(); }, 800);
    }
  }
  if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
    document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', check);
  } else {
    check();
  }
})();

  </script>
  <!-- Nova Rollback Pill -->

  </div>
